
#Ōṃ Awiǥnamāstu#

#praŧamas saṙggaḥ#
<Āṙyyā>
! – – | – – | – – = :12: !
! – – | – – | – – | – – | = :18: !
! – – | – – | – – = :12: !
! – – | – – | ⏑ | – – | – = :15: !
%1/1/1.
hana sira ratu dibya rĕṅön, 
praśāsta riŋ rāt musuḥ nira praṇata, 
jaya paṇḍita riṅ aji kabèḥ, 
saŋ daśaraŧa nāma tamoli*1:1:1*

sira ta triwikramapita, 
pinakabapa ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu maŋ janma, 
Inaka nikaŋ ƀuwana kabèḥ,ya ta don ira nimitta niŋ janma*1:2:2*

guṇamānta saŋ daśaraŧa,wruḥ sira riŋ wéda ƀakti riŋ déwa,taṙ malupèŋ pitrĕpūja,māsiḥ ta sirèŋ swagotra kabèḥ*1:3:3*

rāgādi musuḥ maparö,riŋ hati ya toṅgwanya tan madoḥ riṅ awak,yékā tan hana ri sira,prawīra wihikan sirèŋ nīti*1:4:4*

kadi méǥa maŋhudanakĕn,paḍa nira yaṙ wèhakĕn nikaŋ dana,dīnānđa krĕpaṇa ya winèḥ,ṅūni-ṅūni ḍaṅhyaŋ ḍaṅ ācāṙyya*1:5:5*

mwaŋ satya ta sira mojar,riṅ anak kĕbi towi taṙ mrĕṣawāda,ṅūni-ṅūni yan ri para jana, 
priyahita sojaṙ nirātiśaya*1:6:6*

saꝑala sira rākṣakèŋ rāt,tuwi sira mitra hyaṅ indra ƀakti tĕmĕn,māhéśwara ta sira lanā,śiwaƀakti ginöŋ lanā ginawé*1:7:7*

Ikanaŋ đanuṙđara kabèḥ,kapwa ya ƀakti ri sira praṇata matwaŋ,kadi mawwata yaśa lanā,rūpanyan agöŋ ta kīṙti nira*1:8:8*

jñāna nira śudđa kadi wulan,parāṙŧa gumawé sukā niŋ ƀuwana,sākṣāt indra sira katon,tuhun hanèŋ ƀumi ƀéda nira*1:9:9*

Ikanaŋ pratāpa dumilaḥ,suka nikanaŋ rāt yatèka ginawénya,kadi bahni riŋ pahoman,dumilaḥ maṅdé suka nikaŋ rāt*1:10:10*

hana rājya tulya kéndran,kakwèhan saŋ mahāṙdđika suśīla,riṅ ayođyā suƀagèŋ rāt,yéka kaḍatwan niraŋ nrĕpati*1:11:11*

hayu niŋ swaṙgga tuwi masor,dé niṅ ayođyāpurātiśaya,suka nityakāla ménak,ri rĕŋrĕŋ towi riŋ lahru*1:12:12*

sakwèḥ nikaŋ mūlya kabèḥ,kanaka rajata lèn manik hana ṅkana,yāṅkĕn huntunya maputiḥ,gumuyu-guyuŋ swaṙgga kasoṙ dénya*1:13:13*

hana ta umaḥ kanaka maṇik,kinuliliṅan ikaŋ taman rāmya,warakanyakāmĕṅ-amĕŋ,warāpsāri tulya rin méru*1:14:14*

sꝑaṭika maṇik tamalah-alaḥ,satéja muṅgwiṅ umaḥ paniñjowan,kadi pwa gaṅga saka himawān,rūpanya katon sutéjāśrī*1:15:15*

suka trĕpti saŋ naréndra,ƀuktīkaŋ ƀoga tan papaḍa dibya,niṙƀaya tan hana katakut,sāmanta kabèḥ masö praṇata*1:16:16*

saŋ kékayī sumitrā,kośalyā ǥāra saŋ naréndra tiga,duṙggā gaṅga gorī,paḍa nira surūpa dibyaguṇa*1:17:17*

suꝁa saŋ naréndra makurĕn,dèwi nira kapwa yatna maniwi,tan hana māmbĕk iṙṣya,ri sira dèwi matūt katiga*1:18:18*

kadi haṙṣa saŋ mahāṙṣi,saktèn rĕk sāma lèn yajuṙwwéda,maṅkana saŋ daśaraŧa wèḥ,haṙṣa sira ta dé mahādèwī*1:19:19*

malawas sirāṙ papaṅguḥ,masnéha lawan mahādèwī,surasa saṅgama rinasan, 
rāgāliṅganācumbanādinya.

mahyūn ta sira maputrām,mānaka wètnyaṙ warĕg riŋ wiṣaya,malawas taṙ pānak ataḥ, 
mahyūn ta sirāgawéya yajña*1:20:20*

hana sira rĕṣyaśrĕṅga,praśāsta karĕṅö widagđa riŋ śāstra,tamoli ri yajña kabèḥ,Anuŋ makaꝑalaṅ anak dibya*1:21:21*

sira ta pinĕt naranāŧa,marā ry-ayođyā purohita ṅkāna,tātaṙ wihaŋ sira pinèt,pininta kasihan ta sirāyajñā*1:22:22*

saji niŋ yajña ta humaḍaŋ,śrī-wrĕkṣa samidđa puṣpa ganđa ꝑala,dađi ǥrĕta krĕṣṇatila mađu,mwaŋ kumƀa kuśāgra wrĕtti wĕtiḥ*1:23:23*

lumĕkas ta sira mahoma,prétādi piśāca rākṣasa minantran,ƀūta kabèh inilagakĕn,Asiŋ mamiǥnérikaŋ yajña*1:24:24*

sakalī kāraṇa ginawé,Āwāhana lèn pratiṣṭa sānniđya,paraméśwara inaṅĕn-aṅĕn,Umuṅgu riŋ kuṇḍa bahnimaya*1:25:25*

sāmpun ƀaṭāra Inĕnaḥ,tinitisakĕn taŋ miñak sasomyamaya,lawan ikaŋ krĕṣṇatila mađu,śrī-wrĕkṣa samidđa rowaŋnya*1:26:26*

saŋ hyaŋ kuṇḍa pinūjā,caru makuliliṅan samatsyamāṅsadađi,kalawan sĕkul niwédya,Inamĕs salwiṙ nikaŋ marasa*1:27:27*

ri sĕḍĕŋ saŋ hyaŋ dumilaḥ,niniwédyākĕn ikaŋ niwédya kabèḥ,Oṣađi lèn ꝑalamūla,mwaŋ kĕmbaŋ ganđa đūpādi*1:28:28*

sāmpun pwa sira pinūjā,binojanan saŋ mahāṙṣi paripūṙṇna,kalawan saŋ wiku sākṣī,winūṙṣitan dinakṣinān ta sira*1:29:29*

śésa mahāṙṣi mamījā,pūṙṇnāhuti dibya patyaganđarasa,ya ta pinaṅan kinabèhan,dé nira dèwī mahārāja*1:30:30*

nda tatīta kāla luṅhā,mānak tānakbi saŋ daśaraŧāsiḥ,saŋ rāmānak matuha,I sira mahādèwī kośalyā*1:31:31*

saŋ kékayī sira makānak,saŋ ƀarata ꝁyāti śakti dibyaguṇa,dèwī siraŋ sumitrā,lakṣmaṇa śatruǥna putra nira*1:32:32*

ri wĕtu nikaŋ putra kabèḥ,pinuluŋ ḍaŋ hyaŋ lawan ḍaṅ acāṙyya,paripūṙṇna sira pinūjā,binojanan dé mahārāja*1:33:33*

matuhānak naranāŧa,winara-waraḥ maṅajya wédāstra,ƀagawān wasiṣṫa maṅajar,nipuṇa wruḥ sirèŋ đanuṙwéda*1:34:34*

saŋ rāma sira winarahan,riṅ astra dé saŋ waṣiṣṭa taṙ malawas,kalawan antĕn ira katiga,prajñèŋ widyā kabèḥ wihikan*1:35:35*

sāwara-waraḥ mahāṙṣi,hĕnti kabèḥ tan paśéṣa kapwa tama,karĕṅö ta sira riŋ rāt,guṇāmānta suśīla śakti towi raray*1:36:36*

hana sira gađisutaṙṣi,yogīśwara lèn tapaswi rājāṙṣi,wiśwāmitra ṅaran nira,sira rumĕṅö śakti saŋ rāma*1:37:37*

patapan ira yā mananā,dé nikaŋ rākṣasa krūrakaṙmma,mahyun ta sira rinākṣā,patapan nira dé niraŋ rāma*1:38:38*

naranāŧa saŋ daśaraŧa,sira pinaran dé niraŋ mahāṙṣiwara,gorawa saŋ praƀu pinaran,praṇata manambaḥ sirānuŋsuŋ*1:39:39*

Apa don iraŋ saŋ mahāṙṣi,kita jaya riŋ mantra sidđa sākahyun,tatwa ya linolyanta lanā,yatikā mūlya riṅwaŋ kadi kita*1:40:40*

sumahuṙ ta saŋ mahāṙṣi,tan madwa wuwus naréndra yukti tĕmĕn,kami ikihĕn wiku hana matapa,jñāna lawan yoga mūlya juga*1:41:41*

Ikana kunaŋ dona mami,mamalakwa rinakṣā dé mahārāja,hana saṅhulun mayajña,ndan yālilaŋ rākṣasāmiǥné*1:42:42*

Ikana kunaŋ yan yogyā,saŋ rāma marā riṅ āśrāma maŋ­rakṣā,śāraṇa mamin wĕnaṅa,Umatyanaŋ rākṣasāmiǥné*1:43:43*

maṅkana liŋ mahāṙṣi,naréndra trĕṣṇa tĕmĕn ri saŋ rāma,ndā taṙ sahuṙ tumuṅkul,mojaṙ tā saŋ mahāṙṣi muwaḥ*1:44:44*

hé nāŧa saŋ daśaraŧa,nojaṙku rĕṅönta yatna pituhun ya,yan tan yogya kṣama ya,jāti niṅ aswī maminta kasiḥ*1:45:45*

nyā đaṙmma niŋ kadi kita,pinakaśaraṇa dé niraŋ tapaswi kabèḥ,salwīra niŋ katakuta,kita tāṅrākṣā ri duḥka kabèḥ*1:46:46*

nyā đaṙmma niŋ kadi kami,mawaraha kita riŋ sinaṅguhan đaṙmma,puṇya lawan pāpa kunaŋ,kami mawaraha ṅwaŋ kadi kitèŋ yukti*1:47:47*

brahmaṇa kṣatriyan padulur,jātinya parasparopasaṙppaṇa ya,wiku tan panāŧa ya hilaŋ,tan pawiku kunaŋ ratu wiśīṙṇna*1:48:48*

kalawan tamƀāra Iké,Apan mahāśakti rakwa saŋ rāma,yéki rānak śrī naranāŧa,tatan hana paḍa nira ri kaśaktin*1:49:49*

ya mataŋnya hé naréndra,haywa ta sandéha riṅ anak jayā,dānawa rākṣasa hilaṅa,praƀāwa saŋ rāma hétukanya*1:50:50*

nā liŋ mahāṙṣi mojar,Umĕnĕṅ ataḥ naréndra maṅĕn-aṅĕn,dolayamānacitta,képwan ta sira taṙ wĕnaŋ sumahur*1:51:51*

An lakwéki si rāma,lumagé muṅsuḥ mahāṙṣi riŋ patapan,pĕjahāwās ya kasāmbya,Apan raré tuwi tan wruḥ riŋ biṣama*1:52:52*

tuhu yan wruḥ ya riṅ astra,ndā tan tahu maŋlagé musuḥ biṣama,rakṣasa māyā ya kabèḥ,lāwan paracidra yan papraŋ*1:53:53*

yapwan wihaṅĕ mahāṙṣi,tak anumodā yaṙ paminta śaraṇa ṅké,krođā sirān salahasan,byakta kami kabèḥ śināpa nira*1:54:54*

ri huwus nirān māṅĕn-aṅĕn,sumahuṙ ta sirānumoda taṙ pamihaŋ,Om-om sājña mahāṙṣi,yan yogyā pwa ṅhulun śaraṇā*1:55:55*

bālaka raray mapuṅguŋ,tapwan papraŋ taman panon śatru,yapwan wĕnaṅāśaraṇā,sojaṙ mahāṙṣi tan wihaṅĕn*1:56:56*

dadi tuṣṭa saŋ mahāṙṣi,madĕg ta sira māmwit muliha śīǥra,saŋ rāma sira madandan,lumakwa marérikaŋ patapan*1:57:57*

saŋ lakṣmaṇa sira dibya,sira sasuka duḥka mwaŋ saŋ rāma,rumakĕt citta nira lanā,dadi ta sira tumūt marĕŋ patapan*1:58:58*

sira magawé pratiwimba,tuladana ikaŋ wwaṅ ulaḥ nirāṙ paniwi,sakwan saŋ rāma tumūt,taṙ dadi kantun asiŋ saparan*1:59:59*

{mālinī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
rahina ya sakatambé māwa taŋ déśa rāmya,lumaku ta sira kāliḥ sāmpun amwit manambaḥ,mamawa ta sira laṅkap Astra saṅhārarāja,Anakĕbi ri Ayođyā śoka monĕŋ manaḥnya*1:60:60*

katĕka nira lumakwāśānti saŋ Aṣṭaséni,paḍahi haji ya ginwal maṅgalā niŋ lumampaḥ,kumĕdut i-tĕṅĕnan māṙ bāhu saŋ rāmaƀadra,marahakĕna Alaḥ niŋ śatru tātan paśéṣa#

#dwitīyas saṙggaḥ#
<basantatilaka>:2
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :14:
^2/1/63.
kāwit śaratsamaya kāla nirāṙ para ṅkā,ṅ ton taŋ pradéśa ri hawan Ira kapwa rāmya,kwèḥ lwaḥ magöŋ katĕmu dé nira tīṙŧa dibya,Udyāna lèn talaga niṙɉara kapwa mahniŋ*2:1:61*

tuñjuŋ putiḥ pwa ya ta-tañjuṅ abaŋ sĕḍĕŋ rūm,kumbaŋnya ǥūṙṇnita maśabda humuŋ sadaṙppa,lèn mandamāmruta miriṙ ya suganđa māmbö,saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa rikaŋ kṣana tuṣṭa dénya*2:2:62*

kĕmbaŋ turut sisi rikaŋ padamāṙgga lumrā,saŋ rāmaƀadra manĕhĕṙ maṅalap ta kĕmbaŋ,mādyus sirācamana kapwa maśoca riŋ lwaḥ,ṅkāné śilātala jĕnĕk ta sirān pararyan*2:3:63*

Utꝑulla taŋ kumuda kapwa mĕkaṙ paḍābaŋ,ṙyyak-ṙyyak nikaŋ talaga yéka dumèḥ ya cāla,byaktan katon kadi dilaḥ niṅ apuy ya molaḥ,kumbaŋ ƀramanta I-ruhuṙnya Akĕn kukusnya*2:4:64*

rāmya ṅ-alas kadi mahā maṅilo tumuṅkul,cāyānya yèniṅĕt-iṅöt ya mawās rikaŋ lwaḥ,mèdī dĕlĕg Agul-agul magĕlis ya molaḥ,cāyālilaŋ malimunan makusut ya dénya*2:5:65*

tatkāla sāmpun umĕtu pwa ƀaṭāra suṙyya,rukṣékanaŋ kumuda śūnya hilaŋ hayunya,sakwèḥ nikaŋ kayu kadi pwa tumūt makiṅkiŋ,moni-ŋ manuk mawurahan kaharan taṅisnya*2:6:66*

mwaŋ lwiṙ nikaŋ kayu kadi pwa mahā padĕlwan,lāwan tikaŋ talaga kapwa sahaṙṣa kāliḥ,kĕmbaŋnya kapwa maputiḥ kaharan matanya,kumbaŋ Umandĕl ahirĕŋ ya ta tārakanya*2:7:67*

tuñjuŋ prakampita tinūb riṅ aṅin ya molaḥ,tulyānulak kadi mahā ri lakinya mélik,kumbaŋ marĕŋ kumuda ṅūni dumèḥ ya méwa,Iṙṣa swaƀāwa nikanaŋ wini ǥāra kāsiḥ*2:8:68*

ṅkānèṅ alas ƀramara matta maśabda mandra,nidraŋ kidaŋ kiniduṅan juga paŋhiḍĕpnya,caṇḍāla yékana manaḥnya luput pwa dénya,Āpan pijĕṙ ya rumĕṅö kalahaṅsa moni*2:9:69*

Ahniŋ maho talaga dibya makin ya saśrī,kātéjanaṇ sakĕna dé ni sĕnö hyaṅ aṙkka,sindūrawaṙṇna kadi lāka mabāŋ praƀanya,lwiṙnyan katon kadi ta téja tĕñuḥ dadi wway*2:10:70*

nāhan tinor ira rikaŋ wanadéśa rāmya,n ton taŋ gagā saꝑala dibya parinya wrĕdđi,kapwākiris wahu huwus winatun ya rāmya,saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa sahaṙṣa tumon ya saśrī*2:11:71*

wanwé gunuŋ-gunuṅ alĕmbu gawénya mahwan,yékā hawan Ira tinon ira taŋ palĕmbwan,gopāla yékana mamöḥ rikanaŋ praƀāta,mawwat miñak susu gawénya maré ry-ayođya*2:12:72*

gopāṅganânakĕbi saŋ makĕmit palĕmbwan,rārā gunuŋ duga-dugā sipi maryadanya,yaṙ ton sirāŋ humaliwat madulū rwa sānak,wiśwāsa yan wahu mulat sapi wèḥ wulatnya*2:13:73*

gambīra śabda nikanaŋ mamutĕṙ ya mandra,yāṅkĕn paḍahya nikanaŋ maṅinum magoṣṭi,sakwèḥ nikaŋ wwaṅ amutĕṙ maṅigèl jugānton,bāhunya kālih asiliḥ-silihan ya molaḥ*2:14:74*

daṙppā-ŋ kidaŋ ya makidaŋ-kidaṅan ya mādrĕs,wètnyān śaratsamaya kāla dumèḥ ya daṙppa,ṅkāné tĕgal-tĕgal awan mamaṅan-maṅan ya,saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa Alaḥ magiraŋ tumon ya*2:15:75*

śudđāputiḥ pwa ya ta méǥa magöŋ Akandĕl,Imbaŋ nikaŋ gunuṅ i-soṙ kahanannya lumra,dé niŋ Aṅin makin agöŋ ya makin ya māwān,lwiṙnyān katon kadi gunuŋ himawān apūṙwwa*2:16:76*

lèn siṅha muṅgu rikanaŋ giri pāṙśwa moni,śabdanya riŋ gagana mapratiśabda mādrĕs,sakrođa maŋdĕmaka liŋnya mulat tumĕṅha,Āḥ sihha mūḋa winaliŋnya musuḥnya monī*2:17:77*

riŋ paṙśwa lèn talaga rāmya tinon ira ṅkā,tuñjuŋ putiḥ juga sĕkaṙnya tatan hanābāŋ,tātan katon hana ta haṅsa putiḥ maṅumbaŋ,śabdanya mātra karĕṅö mrĕdu komalālwan*2:18:78*

sakwèḥ nikaŋ talaga tan hana tan patuñjuŋ,tuñjuŋnya tan hana kuraŋ paḍa mèsi kumbaŋ,kumbaŋnya kapwa muni tan hana tan paśabda,śabdanya kaṙṇnasuka tan hana tan manojña*2:19:79*

tatkāla yaṙ tĕka rikaŋ patapan mahāṙṣi,sakwèḥ niraŋ wiku tapaswi kabèḥ manuŋsuŋ,Ꜽṙśānti puṣpa ꝑalamūla suganđa đūpa,lèn wwaḥ sĕrĕḥ wway ininum panamuy mahāṙṣi*2:20:80*

sāmpun siromaṅan ikaŋ panamuy sutrĕpti,māmöŋ-mamöŋ sira rikaŋ patapan mahāṙṣi,wiśwāsa saŋ tapa kabèḥ paḍa gorawāṅliŋ,ménak ta Uṅgwan ira riŋ patapan wisāta*2:21:81*

māsiḥ ta saŋ rĕṣi mawèḥ ta sirāstra diwya,saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa parĕŋ winaraḥ maṅajya,widyātiduṙjjaya jayā wijayā jayantī,yékin pawèḥ ri sira dibya Amoǥaśakti*2:22:82*

sāmpun tikaŋ Aji kabèḥ tama dé nirāwās,māmöṅ-amöŋ sira rikaŋ wanadéśa rāmya,n-ton rākṣasī tĕka mamātyana donya tan lèn,wadwā nira-ŋ praƀu daśāsya si tāṭakākyā*2:23:83*

saŋ rāma yatna Inayat nira taŋ suđanwa,gaṇḍéwa dibya tumihaŋ warayaŋ malaṇḍĕp,tĕṅgĕknya yénarah-araḥ nira tan papiṅrwan,mūṙcꞓān tibā maguliṅan ta si tāṭakākyā*2:24:84*

sāmpun pĕjaḥ pwa ya sahaṙṣa ta saŋ mahāṙṣi,tātan hanaŋ ƀaya rikaŋ patapan samrĕdđi,māriŋ manuk muni mĕṅé matakut ya kasraŋ,dé niŋ mahāmuni raray muni yāmicāra*2:25:85*

ṅūnin hanékana si tāṭaka tāpa moni,moŋ mona muṅgu ri guhānya humīs awaknya,sihhomĕhaḥ ya malapākuru yaṙ mahuṅhaŋ,Aṅhiŋ warak juga warĕg rumuruk rikaŋ rwī*2:26:86*

sāmpun pĕjaḥ pwa katakutnya si tāṭakākyā,moŋ māri mabrata warĕg ya kĕnas kidaŋ kwèḥ,siṅhātisāhasa mahās riṅ alas madasyu,mattā-ŋ liman ya pinaṅanya labuḥ bratanya*2:27:87*

sakwèḥ niṅ oṣađi Anuŋ tinanĕm mahāṙṣi,mārin nanā saꝑala dibya parĕŋ ya mawwaḥ,poh ambawaŋ wawaṅ atöb ya kabèh umĕṇḍuḥ,lwiṙnyān katon kadi sumĕmbahakĕn ꝑalanya*2:28:88*

tatkāla yan rahayu ṅ-āśrama pūṙṇnawrĕdđi,saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa winūṙṣita dé mahāṙṣi,dinyūs inaṙgǥa sira muṅgu rikaŋ palaṅka,mojaṙ ta saŋ rĕṣi tumon sira dibyajāti*2:29:89*

hé rāma lakṣmaṇa Anāku nihan rĕṅönta,nārāyaṇāṅsa kita wiṣṇu Awakta jāti,sakwèḥ nikaŋ ƀuwana ṅūni đināraṇanta,rākṣanta yajña mami dènta kamīkyayajñā*2:30:90*

nā liŋ mahāṙṣi sumahuṙ ta sirā pinūjā,sojaṙ mahāṙṣi kita tan hana saṅśayanta,Āpan praƀāwa ni tapanta magöŋ Alaṅǥya,yékān dumèḥ kami jayā ri musuḥ mahāṙṣi*2:31:91*

nā liŋ niraŋ nrĕpasutottama rāmaƀadra,sāmbut taṅ āyuđa laras lawan astra dibya,maṅkat sirāṅuliliṅī patapan prayatna,saŋ lakṣmaṇéka n-aduluṙ nira kapwa saṅkĕp*2:32:92*

tatkāla saŋ rĕṣi kabèḥ ta winèḥ mamūjā,tandwa-ŋ musuḥ tĕka parĕŋ sumahab ya rodra,ṅkānèŋ laṅit kadi ta méǥa sĕḍĕŋ gumantuŋ,daŋṣṭrokarāla ya sihuŋnya kilat paḍanya*2:33:93*

saŋ lakṣmaṇékana wawaŋ Umulat tumĕṅha,wĕṇṭaŋ laras nira suđīra maṅékapāda,tātan salaḥ r-arah-araḥ ya riṅ aṙdđacandra,śiṙṇnāpasaḥ mati kabèḥnya taman paśéṣa*2:34:94*

tĕṇḍasnya ǥoratara rāhu paḍanya rodra,śabdanya ƀīṣaṇa rikaŋ gagaṇan paṅohan,lāwan Awaknya maṅawanđa tibā gumĕntĕr,sakwèḥ niraŋ tapa kabèḥ matakut tumon ya*2:35:95*

mārīca yékana tuhanya masö masĕṅhit,māyā yatéka pinasaŋnya masö tumandaŋ,saŋ rāma taṙ wiǥani śūra suđīra maṅsö,mojaṙ siraŋ nrĕpatiputra mahā marīkṣā*2:36:96*

mārīca mūḋa Apa donmu riṅ āśrama ṅké,kon māṅsabakṣaṇa ri saŋ wiku taṙ pamāṅsa,yapwan Ĕmās ya kaharĕpmu ri saŋ tapaswī,tan drĕbya saŋ wiku ṅaranya Atītaduḥka*2:37:97*

Ꜽ rāmaƀadra Atimūḋa dahat mapuṅguŋ,tātan Ĕmās pinakadon mami yan para ṅké,taṙ māṅsa tan Apa mahāṅraƀasā juga ṅké,đaṙmma swaƀāwa mami rākṣasa śatru niŋ rāt*2:38:98*

miǥnèṅ ayajña Umatī wiku tan padosa,nā đaṙmma niŋ Asura-rākṣasajanma jāti,mūṙkkātisāhasa mamañcana bañcanĕŋ rāt,krūra swaƀāwa mami tan hana sāđubudđi*2:39:99*

nyaŋ rāt kabèḥ ya raƀasāṅkwa taman paśéṣa,wèhĕnku taŋ ƀuwana dadya Alas ya śūnya,Āpan swaƀāwa mami rākṣasa sāhasèŋ rāt,nā liŋnya śīǥra sumahuṙ nrĕpaputra rāma*2:40:100*

yan rākṣasaprakrĕti duṣṭa ya tūtanamwa,jātinku śudđa karatun ya ta tūtanaṅkwa,sakwèḥ nikaŋ Ađama rākṣasa śatru niŋ rāt,tātan pataṅgwa sahananya ya patyanaṅkwa*2:41:101*

mārīca ko kalana mūḋa taman panoliḥ,Atyanta sāhasa rikèŋ patapan mahāṙṣi,ko tan pasāra trĕṇatulya ḍukut mahumpaŋ,méraŋ Aku g-lawana ko laku mūṙ saka ṅké*2:42:102*

nā liŋ nirār adĕgakĕn ta laras nirāgöŋ,bāyabya yéka pamanaḥ nira bāyu mādrĕs,mārīca rākṣasa kapuk juga tan pasāra,kontal katūb ya tamatan papuliḥ muliḥ ya*2:43:103*

sāmpun katūb kapalupuy pwa ya dé niṅ astra,Indrādi déwata sahaṙṣa manāđukāra,Ꜽ rāma hé daśaraŧātmaja sāđu dibya,nā liŋ nirāṅhudanakĕn sira puṣpawaṙṣa*2:44:104*

ménak manaḥ nira mahāmuni yan payajña,niṙwiǥna tan hana kuraŋ rikanaŋ pamūjā,lāwan ta yajña nira niṙmmala niṙwikāra,sāmpun mahoma Umuwaḥ ta mahāṙṣi mojar*2:45:105*

Ꜽ rāmaƀadra kita dibya Anugrahanta,ƀūlokapāla kita liṅkwiki yan hana ṅké,sāswaṙgga dé nikana taŋ prĕŧiwī hiḍĕpku,kabwat nikan hana ƀaṭāra śacīpati ṅké*2:46:106*

sakwèḥnyawakta katutuṙku tinonku maṅké,wiṣṇwaṅśa déwata kitānaku dibya śakti,riŋ pūṙwwakāla balirāja hilaŋ ya dènta,kṣīrodasāgara nahan pinutĕṙta ṅūni*2:47:107*

mwaŋ rāhu yékana cinakra gulūnya dènta,kwèḥ dꜽtya dānawa Anuŋ talu dènta ṅūni,prākkalpa dibya tĕmahanta warāharūpa,saŋ hyaŋ lĕmaḥ kalĕbu ṅūni đināraṇanta*2:48:108*

nyānuŋ rĕṅönta ratu saŋ janakojarĕṅkwa,mahyūn sirāgawaya yajña ta rakwa maṅké,lāwan swayambara nahan gawayĕn wanèhan,sītā Anak nira rarā waraṅĕn malakya*2:49:109*

ndā tan wĕlin riṅ upaƀoga lawan kaḍatwan,trꜽlokyarājya tuwi tan ya pamĕlya rīya,Aṅhiŋ wiśésa kaharĕpnya Anuŋ siwin ya,wwaŋ śaktimānta guṇamānta kulīṇajanma*2:50:110*

sītā sĕḍĕŋnya mĕtu ṅūni laras duluṙnya,gaṇḍéwa dibya yatikā pinakaryarinya,yapwan hanānuṅ umĕṭĕŋ ya mayat ya śaktya,ya swāmya saŋ janakarājasutā tatan lén*2:51:111*

ndan liṅku yogya kita milwa Ataḥ marā ṅkā,Aṅhiŋ kitékana Anuŋ wĕnaṅomayat ya,gaṇḍéwa yadyapin akas tikĕlā ta dènta,sītā Awās ya kita kéwala kahyunanya*2:52:112*

nā liŋ mahāṙṣi ri siraŋ nrĕpaputra kāliḥ,tātan wihaŋ sira parĕŋ ta masö manĕmbaḥ,sāmpun manĕmbah aduluṙ sira śīǥra luṅhā,saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa marèŋ mitilāđirājya*2:53:113*

tatkāla yaṙ tĕka rikaŋ pasaƀān saśoƀa,sök ǥora ǥūṙṇnita humuŋ tikanaŋ manonton,tonton ta rūpa nira saŋ nrĕpaputra kāliḥ,Āścaṙyya tékana manaḥnya wijaḥ ya mojar*2:54:114*

hyaŋ Aświno sira kunaŋ Umahas mara ṅké,hyaŋ kāmadéwa ta kunaŋ maduluṙ basanta,Ākāra Iṅgita sulakṣaṇa rūpa sampat,saŋ hyaŋ triwikrama kunaŋ Umahā katona*2:55:115*

nā liŋ nikaŋ wwaṅ umulat paḍa haṙṣacitta*2:56:116*
saŋ rāmadéwa pinujinya surūpa dibya,mojaṙ ta saŋ janakarāja mulat sahaṙṣa,saŋ rāmadéwa pinarīkṣa winèḥ ta laṅkap*2:57:117*

gaṇḍéwa dibya paṅalaḥ tripuréka ṅūni,laṅkap ƀaṭāra paraméśwara pūṙwwakāla,sakwèḥ niraŋ nrĕpati ta Umĕtĕŋ mayat ya,saŋ rāma kéwala Anuŋ tumikĕllakĕn ya*2:58:118*

sāmpun tikĕl pwa ya sahaṙṣa ta saŋ naréndra,tuṣṭāgiraŋ hati niraŋ janakāđirāja,dé niŋ praƀāwa nira saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma,mojaṙ ta saŋ janaka riŋ ƀaṭamantrimuꝁya*2:59:119*

saŋ rāma yogya rasikā ta siwīn i-sītā,sampat kulīna tuwi yowana śaktimānta,Undaŋ ta saŋ daśaraŧāt laku śīǥra méṅgal,saŋ rāmadéwa waraṅĕn ya ta pājaranta*2:60:120*

nā liŋ niraŋ janakarāja rikaŋ kinonkon,luṅhā ḍatĕŋ tumama mājar-ajaṙ ya wrĕtta,kagyat siraŋ daśaraŧān winaraḥ Inundaŋ,tātaṙ wihaŋ sira pinèt tĕka śīǥra méṅgal*2:61:121*

tatkāla yaṙ tĕka rikaŋ mitilāđirājya,maṅkat sagorawa siraŋ janakāṙ panuŋsuŋ,nānā prakāra panamuy pariƀoga yogya,mojaṙ ta saŋ janakarāja mulat sahaṙṣa*2:62:122*

hé nāŧa saŋ nrĕpati śūra mahāpraƀāwa,đaṙmmāṙŧa kāma gawayĕn tuwi dé naréndra,mitra hyaṅ indra kita déwata tulya sākṣāt,ƀāgyan tĕmĕn kami ḍatĕŋ naranāŧa maṅké*2:63:123*

rānak naréndra guṇamānta suśīla śakti,saŋ rāmadéwa tamatan papaḍérikaŋ rāt,sītā ya ƀaktya ri Anak naranāŧa tan lèn,nāhan prayojana naréndra pinèt marā ṅké*2:64:124*

nā liŋ niromĕtu ta saŋ wara rājakanyā,pahyas huwus hana kabèḥ masĕkaṙ suganđa,maṅsö manĕmbah i-siraŋ naranāŧa kāliḥ,lāwan siraŋ nrĕpatipūtra surāmaƀadra*2:65:125*

sāmpun manĕmbah aduluṙ sira karwa muṅgaḥ,ṅkānèṅ umaḥ pawaraṅan paḍa haṙṣacitta,méraŋ-Iraŋ hana giraŋ nira yan pasaṇḍiŋ,tan yogya yan wuwusa wèḥ paturū nira ṅkā*2:66:126*

luṅhā-ŋ kulĕm rahinakāla wijil hyaṅ aṙkka,mamwit ta saŋ daśaraŧomulihéry-ayođyā,lāwan Anak nira ta rāǥawa lakṣmaṇāmtaḥ,sītā tumūt saparicāra parĕŋ Umaṅkat*2:67:127*

lāwan Amātya ƀaṭamantri kabèḥ manuṅgaŋ,luṅhā sirāta liwat iŋ wanadéśa rāmya,kāwit hana pwa maṅawit wiku rodrarūpa,pañjaŋnyawak nira satal mamikul ta laṅkap*2:68:128*

wok bris kumis nira piśaṅga jaṭā nirāwyaŋ,saŋ rāmaƀaṙggawa ṅaran Ira tan hanoli,saṅkèp sĕnadđa Umasö ta mapatrayudđa,mojaṙ nirādara wuwus nira tan hana twaŋ*2:69:129*

Ꜽ rāmadéwa Aku rāma ṅaranku riŋ rāt,yan śakti ko papagakĕn n-aku yan prawīra,ko mātya dèṅku Aŧawā Aku mātya dému,wĕṇṭaŋ larasku yadiyan tuhu śaktimānta*2:70:130*

nā liŋ niraŋ paraśurāma mapatrayudđa,sītā gĕlāna kumĕtĕṙ ta manon apūṙwwa,mojaṙ ta saŋ daśaratāsi manĕmba-nĕmbaḥ,saṅka ry-asiḥ nira maputra lawan mamantu*2:71:131*

hé jāmadagni kita śakti gahan rikèŋ rāt,kwèḥ śaktimānta ratu śīṙṇna pĕjaḥ ya dènta,mahyun ta mapraṅa puwiḥ kalawan si rāma,tan yogya dènta ya raray tuwi hīnaśakti*2:72:132*

nā liŋ narāđipa maminta kasiḥ manantwa,tan parĕṅö paraśurāma sirāƀimāna,saṅkā ri daṙppa nira tan panahā-nahā wwaŋ,tā śakti liŋ nira wanèḥ sira kéwalātaḥ*2:73:133*

laṅkap nirātiśaya dibya magöŋ Apañjaŋ,mwaŋ hrū pawèḥ ri sira saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma,yapwan wĕnaŋ mayat i-ko Alahāku dému,ƀaktyāku liŋ nira mahā mamarīkṣa śakti*2:74:134*

saŋ rāmadéwa sira śūra suđīra maṅsö,taṅgap tikaŋ laras agöŋ maduluṙ tat aṅgwan,śīǥrāṙ watĕk ya kawĕnaŋ tumihaŋ tikaŋ hrū,saŋ jāmadagni mawĕnĕs humĕnĕŋ kapūhan*2:75:135*

saŋ rāmaƀāṙggawa Apanta tujuṅku liŋta,yapwan gulūnta panahĕn yadiyan hatinta,tan dadya nisꝑala Iké kita matya dèṅku,yapwan palaṇḍuṅa manĕmbaha ƀaktya sojar*2:76:136*

méraŋ siraŋ paraśurāma gĕlāna képwan,trĕṣṇā sirèŋ hurip asiḥ wĕkasan ta mojar,swaṙggāṅku dibya I-ruhuṙ paṅahā hyaṅ indra,yékāt panaḥ hilaṅakĕn mara tak para ṅkā*2:77:137*

nā liŋ niraŋ paraśurāma nĕhĕṙ ta luṅhā,méraŋ tumona muꝁa saŋ nrĕpapūtra rāma,mahyā Ikaŋ bala kabèḥnya humuŋ paḍātri,saŋ mꜽtilī sira sahaṙṣa mariṙ makiṅkiŋ*2:78:138*

{mālinī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
Aŧa ri sĕḍĕṅ ikā saŋ ƀāṙggawālaḥ ya luṅhā,daśaraŧa sira haṙṣān kolakĕn pūtra rāma,krama lumaku Umaṅkat tuṅgaṅan kapwa maṅrap,satĕka nira sinuŋsuŋ dé nikaŋ wwaŋ ry-ayođyā#

#trĕtīyas saṙggaḥ#
<pṛŧiwītala>:3
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
^3/1/140.
ḍatĕŋ pwa maharāja saŋ daśaraŧa ry-ayođyāmpura,Inastuti ta saŋ naréndrasuta rāma dé niŋ sarāt,Apan Ilaṅakĕn musuḥ nira mahāṙṣi riŋ Āśrama,lawan paraśurāma śakti tuwi sor ataḥ dé nira*3:1:139*

tatan hana wanèh anuŋ pinuji dè nikaŋ wwaŋ kabèḥ,naréndrasuta rāmadéwa sira śakti tātan kalèn,Amātya ƀaṭamantri tuṣṭa magiraŋ paḍāṅastuti,sirékana Iniṣṭi ratwa nikanaŋ Ayođyāpura*3:2:140*

samaṅkana naréndra saŋ daśaraŧāsi haṙṣāgiraŋ,si rāma juga ratwa tan si ƀarata pwa nā liŋ nira,praśāsta karĕṅö parampara Ujaṙ naréndrāpagĕḥ,samāpta winaraḥ tikaŋ bala kabéḥ ry-ujaṙ saŋ praƀu*3:3:141*

Anéka saji saṅgrahékaṅ aƀiṣéka yomèḥ tĕkā,sinaṅgraha sapādapāṭa maṇimuꝁya siṅhāsana,lawan kanaka kumƀa tīṙŧa ya Isinya sāmpun mawit,ginomaya Ikaŋ saƀā sinawuran ta ganđākṣata*3:4:142*

suganđa kumukus ṅ-asöp ya tinatā kabèḥ tūt sisī,kukusnya mawĕlun-wĕlun gugula đūpa ganđotkaca,sĕkaṙ suraƀi cāmpakāsana suganđa lumrā marūm,lawan đwaja patāka komala kĕlabnya dé niŋ Aṅin*3:5:143*

sĕḍĕŋ nira kināṙyya ratwaṅaƀiṣéka yomèḥ tĕkā,gĕlāna sira saŋ naréndraǥariṇī siraŋ kékayī,Anak nira Ataḥ siraŋ ƀarata ratwa kahyun Ira,Apan pasamayan sĕḍĕŋ nira sinoma-somaḥ pwa wèḥ*3:6:144*

nda tan hana Anak nirāpara-paran maré saŋ kaki,siraŋ ƀarata taṙ wĕruḥ ry-aṅĕn-aṅĕn Iraŋ kékayī,sirāta juga moǥa kimburu tumon siraŋ rāǥawa,Alaḥ pracaya riŋ Ujaṙ samaya niŋ sumomaḥ sira*3:7:145*

masö sira ri saŋ narāđipa mahā mamiǥnāna don,pininta nira saŋ naréndrasuta rāma muṅgèṅ alas,Anak nira Ataḥ ya ratwa kaharĕp niraŋ kékayī,gĕlāna ta naréndra saŋ daśaraŧāśa képwan sira*3:8:146*

sawèt nikana satya saŋ praƀu kinon ṅ-anak miṅgata,kadi pwa ya Ilaŋ Asiḥ nira hiḍĕp nikaŋ wwaŋ kabéḥ,gĕlāna maṅaraŋ Alaḥ salahasātimohāṅĕsaḥ,mahöm ta sahananya kapwa Umasö ri saŋ rāǥawa*3:9:147*

Ah-o lalu lalis naréndra tamatan panoliḥ guṇa,lawan ƀarata duṣṭa hāḥ lalu gĕlĕḥ niraŋ kékayī,nahan ya ta wuwusnya wĕḥ ri harĕpan Iraŋ rāǥawa,tumūta Umarèṅ alas kira-kiranya tan kantuna*3:10:148*

suđīra ta siraŋ nrĕpātmaja wawaŋ ta mojaṙ sira,lakiṅku sahananta haywa malarāk parékaŋ Alas,Apan Ikana Ājña saŋ praƀu Anugrahéki-n tĕka,prayojana nikaŋ Anak gumawayaŋ pakon iŋ bapa*3:11:149*

Apan sira mamĕtwakĕn sira mawèḥ wruhèŋ loṙ kidul,siréka maṅiṅū rumakṣa rikanaŋ Anak riŋ ƀaya,Agöŋ paṅupakāra saŋ praƀu mataŋnya tag laṅǥana,lĕhöŋ mati misan-misan saka rikaŋ wihaŋ riŋ bapa*3:12:150*

tuliḥ ta sahananta haywa ta saśoka dé ni ṅhulun,Ariṅku ya siwinta saŋ ƀarata ratwa tan saṅśaya,Apan naku Ikāŋ ratuṇ ḍatu Ariṅku tātaṙ kalèn,lawan sira naréndra taṅguhana haywa śoka-ŋ hati*3:13:151*

nahan Ikana liŋ nira krama madĕg ta luṅhā sira,lawan Ari nirāta lakṣmaṇa tumūt siraŋ mꜽtilī,sumantri mapatiḥ sirāṅatĕrakĕn parékaŋ Alas,lawan sahana saŋ sumāđya sira ratwa yāsiḥ tumūt*3:14:152*

ḍatĕŋ sira rikaŋ Alas ri tamasā mahārāmya ya,lalu-ŋ diwasa maŋhinĕp sira rikaŋ Alas ƀīṣaṇa,rinākṣa nira tékanaŋ bala kabèḥ pijĕṙ yāturū,waṅuṇ ḍahina śīǥra miṅgat aṅĕnĕs ta saŋ rāǥawa*3:15:153*

siraŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇāmilu lawan siraŋ mꜽŧilī,tatan hana wĕruḥ sĕḍĕŋ niran umiṅgat aŋlĕs hilaŋ,gĕlāna Ikanaŋ balān pawuṅu lèn sumantryāṅaraŋ,Apan kahilaṅan taman wruh i-wĕkas niraŋ rāǥawa*3:16:154*

humuŋ ya manaṅis rikaŋ Alas alaḥ masāmbat masū,tatan wruh i-pamètananya ri siraŋ hilaŋ tan katon,maluy ta ya kabèḥ muliḥ tĕka rikèṅ ayođyāpura,manaḥnya juga tan muliḥ milu tumūt risaŋ rāǥawa*3:17:155*

lawan saṅ apatiḥ sumantri marahup sirèŋ lwaḥ magöŋ,linālana niraŋ manaḥ makin agöŋ ta kiṅkiŋ nira,muliḥ ta sira tūt hawan r-aṅĕn-aṅĕn ta saŋ rāǥawa,ḍatĕŋ sira rikaŋ Ayođyapura śūnya taŋ rāt hiḍĕp*3:18:156*

masuk sira rikaŋ kaḍatwan umasö ri saŋ ƀūpati,mulat pwa naranāŧa saŋ daśaraŧāṅaraŋ mūṙcꞓita,Apan mulat i-saŋ sumantri juga taṙ parowaŋ sira,tĕñuḥ hati nirāpasaḥ r-aṅĕn-aṅĕn larā niŋ Anak*3:19:157*

Inastuti sirèŋ daṅū pinuji đīra tātaṙ lĕgö,sahiṣṇu humĕnĕŋ kumölakĕn ikaŋ larāgöŋ tĕmĕn,mĕné ri papasaḥ nira pwa ya sahiṣṇu tātan hana,gupé kapalupuy hiḍĕp nira hilaŋ kađīran nira*3:20:158*

sĕkul tar aharĕp Asiŋ sarumakĕt tuwīn āryakĕn,mariṙ pawĕḍihan malit Inalapan tikaŋ ƀūṣaṇa,mahās mabayaṅan manaḥ nira n-akūŋ kinuṅkuŋ juga,nahan laku marèŋ taman sira lumālanékaŋ manaḥ*3:21:159*

makin pwa ya makūṅ ikaŋ hati gĕlāna monĕŋ Ataḥ,naréndra baribin manaḥ nira tumon taman rāmya ya,waliŋ nira paṅoṣađān lumipuraŋ Unĕŋ riŋ Anak,muliḥ sira sakèŋ taman malara kaṣṭa puḥ mūṙcꞓita*3:22:160*

hanan kĕlu rikaŋ tilām tuwi malit malĕmbut matīs,Awak nira linépanèŋ sulur usĕṙ lawan caṇḍana,nda tan paraṣa tan panīsi mapanas kabèḥ yan hiḍĕp,ri tībra nikanaŋ Unĕŋ dadi muliḥ sirèŋ swaṙgga wèḥ*3:23:161*

mawū mawalikan n-anākĕbi niraŋ naréndrānaṅis,gĕluŋ linuputan Apusnya Umuré sawèt niŋ lara,maṇik kanaka ƀūṣaṇādi sĕsĕran tibā riŋ lĕmaḥ,Apan maguliṅan gĕlāna makuśā masāmbat masū*3:24:162*

Amātya ƀaṭamantri kapwa ta masö mahöm-höm kabèḥ,siraŋ ƀarata śīǥra yaṙ laku muliḥ Inundaŋ ḍatĕŋ,tinon ira tikaŋ kaḍatwan asamun ya tistis kabèḥ,kadi pwa lĕburékanaŋ lĕbuh apan tayāŋ dwal mĕtu*3:25:163*

sagadgada manaḥ niraṙ laku masuk riṅ aƀyantara,Umuŋ sahana saŋ kapaṅguh anaṅis sumuṅsuŋ sira,matakwan amĕpĕṙ siré kalara saŋ naréndrāṙ pĕjaḥ,satorasi siraŋ Ibū marahakĕn siré saŋ Anak*3:26:164*

huwus nira wĕruḥ ri hétu nira saŋ naréndrāṙ pĕjaḥ,saroṣa magĕlĕŋ sirèṅ ibu masö ta mojaṙ sira,lukan kita harébu niṙǥrĕṇa hatinta duṣṭāgĕlĕḥ,wĕnaŋ kita rumudđa kāṙyya naranāŧa tātaṙ hĕnĕŋ*3:27:165*

Apa k-ꝑala ri saŋ tigāṙ para rikaŋ Alas duṙggama,kitat hana rikaŋ Ayođya pira göṅa nīnakta wèḥ,kunaŋ kami kabèh umilwa mati dènta wèt niŋ lara,Ah-o saꝑala dènta māmbĕk umatīŋ sarāt taṙ masiḥ*3:28:166*

ṅhulun niki kinonta ratwa Aparan guṇā niŋ ratu,yadin pamuharā wirođa Umalākĕnaŋ rāt kabèḥ,lawan n-aku winèḥta sora Ađamā sakèŋ lakṣmaṇa,tumūt ya drĕḋaƀakti tār alaṅ-alaŋ ri saŋ rāǥawa*3:29:167*

nahan nikana liŋ nirāṅuman-uman ri saŋ kékayī,tataṙ gĕrĕmĕ ratwa đīra sira satya ƀaktīŋ kaka,nirantara humīs ta luḥ nira gĕlāna wèt niŋ lara,wawaŋ sira kataṅguhan maṅĕn-aṅĕn pĕjaḥ saŋ praƀu*3:30:168*

sinantwa sira dé nikaŋ bala kabèḥ lawan saŋ Ibu,Ilaŋ lara nirālilaŋ hati maho maluy niṙmmala,Apan prakrĕti jāti niŋ dadi kabèḥ matuŋtuŋ pati,ya tékan inaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn Ira hilaŋ ta kiṅkiŋ nira*3:31:169*

kinon ira ta saŋ balāđika tumunwa saŋ ƀūpati,maśoca ta mawèḥ tilĕm sira rikaŋ tilĕm niŋ wulan,samāpta maharèp ta saŋ ƀarata mèta saŋ rāǥawa,ri satya nira ƀakti riŋ kaka tirun nikaŋ rāt kabèḥ*3:32:170*

liman kuda lawan raŧa pramuꝁa niŋ balānuŋ tumūt,sĕnadđa dumuluṙ siraŋ ƀarata śīǥra luṅhā sira,tĕka pwa sira riŋ Alas gaja raŧāśwa kapwānusup,mahās sira rikaŋ Alas Umulisāk ri saŋ rāǥawa*3:33:171*

ri piṅgir ikanaŋ nadī ri tamasérikā duṙggama,Alas gahana gahwarāgraha guhānya gamƀīra ya,lawan kali juraŋ trĕbis biṣama ƀīṣaṇālwāṅawit,siraŋ ƀarata tātakut nira Alaḥ Umèt saŋ kaka*3:34:172*

taman katĕmu saŋ pinèt lumaku saŋ mamèt taṙ maṅèl,tĕmu-ŋ lwah atiniṙmmalātiśaya dibya gaṅgā gahan,maṇik sꝑaṭika candrakāṇṭa ya paḍanya śudđāputiḥ,kadi pwa ya manaḥ niraŋ ƀarata satya ƀaktīŋ kaka*3:35:173*

muwaḥ ta manusup rikān katĕmu tékanaŋ lwaḥ magöŋ,pratīta yamunā ṅaranya makiris hilīnyāhĕniŋ,I soṙ hana ta saṅgamanya kalawan ta gaṅgāputiḥ,kadi pwa ya ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu kalawan ƀaṭāréśwara*3:36:174*

muwaḥ ta manusup hana pwa patapan pinaṅguḥ nira,suƀikṣa ya manoharāśrama niraŋ ƀaradwāja ya,sĕḍĕŋ tiba-tibāṅlaluŋ diwasa kāla soré n-tĕka,mahāṙṣi saha śisya gorawa masö manuŋsuŋ sira*3:37:175*

Anéka panamuy mahāṙṣi mĕtu saṅka riŋ yoga ya,Amoǥa manurun manojña kayu pārijātādƀuta,Asiŋ sakaharĕp saménaka pawèḥ niraŋ paṇḍita,Aho saꝑala niŋ tapātiśaya sarwakāmaprada*3:38:176*

Anākĕbi riṅ indraloka manurun lawan Apsarī,ya téka makurĕn-kurĕn ri sira saŋ tamuy kādƀuta,mabaṅsi maṅiduŋ makinnara malāwu wīṇāṅigĕl,jĕnĕk ta sira saŋ tamuy dadi tĕhĕṙ maṅantyaṅhinĕp*3:39:177*

waṅuṇ ḍahina śīǥra yaṙ laku muwaḥ Umèt saŋ kaka,lawan bala ḍatĕŋ sirèŋ talaga dibya mandākinī,kaŧañcana hana pwa nagna wanawāsa paṅguḥ nira,siromarahakĕn pradéśa kahanan niraŋ rāǥawa*3:40:178*

pawitra hana citrakūṭagiri duṙggamāwān magöŋ,manohara ya rāmya yéka kahanan niraŋ rāǥawa,sahaṙṣa winaraḥ ta saŋ ƀarata śīǥra maṅkat sira,lawan bala kabèḥ manèk sira rikaŋ gunuŋ duṙggama*3:41:179*

Umèḥ nira tĕkā sasaṅśaya mulat ta saŋ lakṣmaṇa,waliŋ nira musuḥ ḍatĕŋ r-adĕgakĕn ta laṅkap nira,sĕnadđa pinasuk niraŋ kawaca yatna đīrāṅadĕg,Alis nira ya cāla mārĕṅu lalāṭa kumrūkĕna*3:42:180*

tinon ira ya taṙ pasañjata taya-ŋ galaḥ tāpapan,tuhun kuda liman raŧādulu-duluṙ ya makwèḥ juga*3:43:181*
makin ta maparö wĕruḥ siran inaryakĕn taŋ laras,masö sira ri saŋ kakāwara-waraḥ ri saŋ rāǥawa*3:44:182*

siraŋ ƀarata śīǥra yaṙ tĕka masö manambaḥ sira,lawan bala nirāwaraḥ ta sira yaṙ pĕjaḥ saŋ praƀu,saśoka manaṅis humuŋ sira kabèḥ sawèt niŋ lara,Anantara mariṙ makiṅkiṅ arahup ta madyus kabèḥ*3:45:183*

naréndrasuta rāma sāmpun arahup ta mojaṙ sira,Ariṅku ƀaratāt Uliḥ hara rikaŋ Ayođyāpura,Ujaṙ haji Ikā dumèh aku marèṅ alas tan kalèn,kitékana gumantya ratwa ya mataŋnya tat saṅśayā*3:46:184*

lawan kita magöŋ guṇanta gaṇitan tatan hĕntya ya,prawīra wihikan kitèṅ aji lawan kalap niŋ naya,mataŋnya kita yogya ratwa saꝑalān siwin rākṣakā,guṇanta Aparan guṇanya yadi tan guṇā niŋ ratu*3:47:185*

kunĕŋ yan alĕmĕḥ pi ratwa ri hanaṅku muṅgwiŋ Alas,Ujaṙku pituhunta kéwala kitāta ƀaktyākaka,Awās ya mulihāta liṅku kita haywa śoka-ŋ hati,hanā ta juga rākṣakā kita rikaŋ kaḍatwan Ari*3:48:186*

nahan ya ta wuwus nirātiśaya đīra dibyaŋ manaḥ,wĕnaŋ nira rumākṣa saŋ bapa rikā kasatyan Ira,samaṅkana siraŋ kinon muliha ratwa tātan lĕgö,siraŋ ƀarata ƀakti riŋ kaka wawaŋ ta mojaṙ sira*3:49:187*

pirā Inaka ni ṅhulun hana rikaŋ kaḍatwan kunĕŋ,sĕḍĕŋta humiḍĕp Ikaŋ lara hanèṅ alas kāsyasiḥ,lawan kita ta yogya ratwa tuwi rākṣakā niŋ jagat,Apan matuha śaktimānta guṇamānta śūrèŋ raṇa*3:50:188*

nya taŋ kuda liman lawan kanaka ratna yogya praƀu,ndya yuktyan ikihĕn ṅhulun kumawaśākĕnékā kabèḥ,Amātya ƀaṭamantri yogya karikā sumiwya ṅhulun,mataŋnya mulihāta ménaka kitāta ƀūpālaka*3:51:189*

lawan ṅhulun atīta niṙguṇa-guṇanta gaṅgopama,diwākara gunuŋ paḍanta himawān lawan sāgara,ṅhulun pwa pinujinta śakti guṇamānta tātan tuhu,Asamƀawa wuwusta maŋduhuṅakĕn mahā maŋlaré*3:52:190*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
nahan ikana wuwus saŋ kékayīputra sāđu,dadi sumahur ikā saŋ rāmaƀadrāsi maswī,muliha Ata kitāntĕn ṅkā ry-ayođyā tamolaḥ,yadin alĕmĕha séwan pādukaṅkwīki ratwa*3:53:191*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
– ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :15:
ndan kita pi saraƀāran rākṣaŋ sakala jagat,kṣatriyawinaya yékā rākṣan katuturakĕn,
{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
– ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :14:
śāsaṇa ya gĕgĕn taŋ śāstra d-wulati lanā,sojariṅ aji tūtĕn yékā mawa kasukan*3:54:192*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
– ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :14:
– ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :15:
dèwa kuśala śālā mwaŋ đaṙmma ya pahayun,mās ya ta pahawrĕdđin byāyā riŋ hayu kĕkĕsĕn,ƀukti sakaharĕptād wèhi-ŋ bala kasukan,đaṙmma kalawan aṙŧa mwaŋ kāmāta ṅaran ikā*3:55:193*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
– ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :15:
śīla rahayu rākṣan rāga dwéśa hilaṅakĕn,kimburu ya ta hīlan śūnyāmbĕkta lawan awak,nyā-ŋ winaya gĕgön āsiŋ solaḥ kinalulutan,mwaŋ Aƀimana sampat Antĕnku praƀu maṅaliḥ*3:56:194*

wruḥ pwa kita rikāṅdé prajñā dibya ṅaran ikā,riŋ raṇamuꝁa sāra mwaŋ wākśūra ya guṇitan,tyāga kita mapuṇyā riŋ brahmāṅśa muniwara,nāgata gawayĕntāt rākṣāŋ rāt ya pahapagĕḥ*3:57:195*

{rucira}
⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
krĕtajñatā haran ikanaŋ wruh iŋ guṇa,mulat rikaŋ bala manĕkĕt manon ulaḥ,Asiŋ lĕwiḥ linĕwihakĕn rikaŋ hayu,Ikaŋ masoṙ kinila-kilèŋ sasamƀawa*3:58:196*

mahāt-manon guṇagaṇa dibya riŋ praƀu,tumon ikaŋ hala-hayu yatna tan hĕnĕŋ,rumĕŋ­wakĕn lara nikanaŋ prajā kabèḥ,Apan Ikaŋ Uƀaga lanā ri saŋ praƀu*3:59:197*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :8:
Utsāhāta larapana,kāṙyyāsiŋ pahapagĕhĕn,sampay tan gawayakĕna,riŋ satwāđama ya tuwi*3:60:198*

śaktī siṅha katatakut,riŋ wīrāsama winuwus,yatnānyān pamati-mati,yékānuŋ satiru-tirun*3:61:199*

göŋ hĕṅkāra ya ta hilan,nindā tan gawayakĕna,tañ janmāmuhara wĕrö,yékā praśraya sumuka*3:62:200*

{pawitrā}
– – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :9:
nyā-ŋ mukyāntĕn kanĕkĕtakĕn,haywāsampay riṅ asih-asiḥ,dibyaŋ śāstrān linagi-lagin,yāwat mèwĕḥ ya pinituhun*3:63:201*

saṅkā niŋ wruḥ Aji ginĕgö,nītijñācāra kapuhara,paṇḍyācāṙyya dwija pahayun,göṅĕntātaḥ Ikanaṅ asiḥ*3:64:202*

krođāmbĕk yélagakĕn ika,doṣākwèḥ duṙbbala winuwus,mwaŋ wadwānuŋ rahayu milag,mitrādoḥ taŋ musuh aparĕk*3:65:203*

śāntāsiḥ nitya tuhagaṇan,haywāpĕs riŋ kinatakutan,wadwā doṣanya palĕ-palĕḥ,tan wruḥ riŋ twaŋ ya guragaḍa*3:66:204*

kadyaṅgā niŋ wĕḍus upaman,ƀītātwaŋ riŋ kayu maṅadĕg,yapwan suṇḍé wijah umanèk,Īꞓā tan saṅśaya malayū*3:67:205*

doṣāgöŋ wwaŋ jĕnĕk aṅinum,māhā-ŋ cittālupa mawĕrö*3:68:206*
pāruṣyèŋ wwaŋ prakaṭa wĕgig,rāhasyāsiŋ winuni mĕtu*3:69:207*

haywādwa-dwāmuhara hala,duṙƀāgāwās ta ya Inupĕt,mwaŋ wadwāsiŋ kuṭila katon,tan wiśwāsāna ta Ikahĕn*3:70:208*

nindā riŋ wwaŋ ya ta manapis,tan saktā riŋ wiṣaya dahat,dyūtāsiŋ duṙyyasana kunĕŋ,yékānuŋ tan gawayakĕna*3:71:209*

{pṛŧiwītala}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
nihan ta gawayanta nitya maṅĕmit prajā maṇḍala,wihāra pahayunta paṙhyaṅan umaḥ ƀaṭārāmĕrĕn,hawan patani pañcuran talaga sétu tambak taman,pĕkĕn wwatan asiŋ sakahyuna nikaŋ prajā yad-gawé*3:72:210*

limanta raŧa tuṅgaṅan lagi-lagin śraman sañjata,mawèha kita kaṙmma piṇḍa rĕṣiƀojanāṅkĕn salèk,Ikaŋ kuśala hosakĕnta ya kabèḥ pamūjā gĕṅĕn,ya tonĕn ikanaŋ sarāt kita janānurāgérikā*3:73:211*

wulatta rikanaŋ manéwita kabèḥ watĕk séwaka,guṇanya kalawan Asiḥnya matuhan Ikā tiṅhali,suśīla saguṇātiƀakti yadi tan sujanmā tuwi,sayogya pahayun Ikā ṅuni-ṅunin sujanmālapĕn*3:74:212*

tatan wawaṅ awèha riŋ suka parīkṣanĕntériya,lumakwakĕna ṅ-ajña yan dadi rikā ta yan wèhana,guṇanya mapagĕḥ manaḥ nika sumiwya saŋ ƀūpati,kitékana kināsihan suƀaga dibya ratnopama*3:75:213*

samaṅkana Ikaŋ manéwita yadin saloƀāsulit,hanomarahakĕn ya tan rahayu lāgi saṅkĕŋ hala,Iṅötakĕna cāra yékana paṅawruhèŋ duṙjjana,Asiŋ lagi katon bĕnĕṙnya ya ta gopitan saŋ praƀu*3:76:214*

Awās ya hala wigrahanta Ika yan Ulaḥnyān salaḥ,hilāṅakĕna yan sadoṣa wuwusĕn wiwékan tĕmĕn,samaṅkana yadin r-ahat dĕmakananta wèhĕn suka,ya tékana wĕnaŋ Anugraha lawan wĕnaŋ wigraha*3:77:215*

ƀaṭāra rawi yopamanta manasèŋ sarāt taṙ maṅèl,samaṅkana ta saŋ praƀūmilaṅakĕn Ikaŋ duṙjjana,śaśaṅka magawé Asiḥ sira janānurāgèŋ sarāt,Awās ta kita maṅkanāri yat ahāta riŋ pun-punan*3:78:216*

gunuŋ ya ta paḍanta ƀūpati Ikaŋ prajāṅkĕn ḍukut,patūti guṇa-doṣa niŋ Ulah ikā mataŋnyān suka,Ikaŋ prawara pora waṙgga wanatulya yāṅkĕn Alas,kitékana ta siṅha rākṣaka dumèḥnya śoƀān katon*3:79:217*

{śiꝁariṇī}
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
Ikaŋ ŧāni prītīnuƀaya guṇa niŋ ƀūpati lanā,ya saṅkanyā-ŋ ƀogān hana pakĕna niŋ rājya ya tuwi,Asiŋ sénāluḥnyékana ta tuluṅĕn haywa humĕnĕŋ,lima lwiṙ niŋ sākṣāt ƀaya tĕka rikaŋ pora ya paḍĕm*3:80:218*

kinonkon saŋ swāmīkana ta Umarèŋ wanwa mapanas,maliŋ makwèḥ lumrāṅhala-hala lawan drohaka wanèḥ,kapātnyékā saŋ wallaƀa ya winilaŋ duṣṭa tan alaḥ,lima mwaŋ loƀé saŋ narapati nahannyaŋ ƀaya magöŋ*3:81:219*

mataŋnyāntĕn tiṅhal sahana ni watĕk niŋ bala dĕlön,Ikaŋ prajña wruḥ riŋ naya winaya śīlanya rahayu,tan alwāmwaŋ yatnān drĕḋa maniwi tan loƀa samatā,nahan pratyakṣantèŋ hala-hayu taman dadya manasar*3:82:220*

sunītī priḥ tāntĕn gagapi hati göṅĕn guṇagaṇan,musuḥ topāyan toḥ pisani panas iŋ pāśa pahasat,Iké śatruntad-don sahana pakĕna mwaŋ kira-kira,tatan wèhĕntātāƀawaha gĕsĕṅiŋ drohaka raraḥ*3:83:221*

Ikaŋ mèṅĕt wruḥnyèŋ maniwi mulat iŋ ƀakti ya gawé,prayatna wruḥ riŋ dé tan alĕmĕha riŋ krĕtya rahayu,wĕrö niŋ cittāgöŋ ya ta hilaṅakĕn riŋ hati lagé,swaƀāwèŋ janmékaŋ mada kaluṣa tātaḥ ya manaput*3:84:222*

kaśaktin mwaŋ prajñā kuśala ya ta ƀoganya tamalaḥ,surūpā tatwajñèṅ aji ya sapujintékana kabèḥ,kitāntĕn saṅkĕp riŋ guṇagaṇa Ikaŋ ƀakti sudrĕḋa,hilantékaŋ Ambĕk manaya-naya mattāmiṣa puji*3:85:223*

nahan dé saŋ nāŧākĕmita Irikaŋ ƀūmi suƀaga,parāṙŧāsiḥ yāgöŋ saka lara nikaŋ rāt winulatan,tumiṅhal yātāsiŋ sawuwus ikanāŋ śāsana tinūt,tĕpĕt māsiḥ taṙ wruḥ kutila milag iŋ bañcana dumèḥ*3:86:224*

{śiꝁariṇī}
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
nahan tojaṙ saŋ rāma manĕkĕt iṅ antĕn mapagĕha,sahaṙṣāmbĕk saŋ ƀārata ta rumĕṅö śabda karuṇa,manĕmbaḥ māmwīt saŋ ƀarata ri siraŋ rāmawijaya,lawan wadwākwèḥ mwaŋ sahana-hana niŋ ƀrĕtya mamuhun*3:87:225*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
Aŧa lumaku muliḥ saŋ kékayīputra luṅhā,tinawanakĕn irékaŋ pādukātyanta dibya,ya ta siniwi sinĕmbaḥ dé nikaŋ wwaŋ ry-ayođyā,ƀarata sira tamolaḥ ƀakti maŋ­rākṣa rājya*3:88:226*

#catuṙŧas saṙggaḥ#
<mālaƀāriṇi>
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
^4/1/227.
ndat atīta sirāṙ hanèŋ kaḍatwan,sira saŋ rāma hanèṅ alas tamolaḥ,rikanaŋ giri citrakūṭa r-uṅgu,kalawan lakṣmaṇa jānakī susatya*4:1:227*

hana tāśrama saŋ mahāṙṣi Atri,ya tikānuŋ pinaran niraŋ tigaŋ wwaŋ,Atigorawa saŋ mahāṙṣi maṅliŋ,karuṇékaŋ śaraṇāgatātidibya*4:2:228*

tamataṙ malawas sirāṙ hana ṅka,hana tālas karĕṅö pratīta riŋ lwā,Atiƀīṣaṇa daṇḍakā ṅaranya,ya paran saŋ raǥuputra rāmadéwa*4:3:229*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
Umahas sira tā hanaŋ katākut,kalawan saŋ Ari lèn priyā nira,hana rākṣasa rodra yéka maṅsö,Umahā mātyana donya tan kalèn*4:4:230*

{mālaƀāriṇi}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
si wirāđa ṅaranya tan panoli,I ruhuṙ n-uṅgu sukunya wèḥ sumuṅsaŋ,Atirodra taṅanya paŋlakunya,Atakut mrĕtyu tumon ya rodrarūpa*4:5:231*

Umulat ta naréndraputra kāliḥ,sira tātaṙ matakut masö tumandaŋ,Awamāna Ikaŋ wirāđa mūṙkꝁa,tumahā saŋ nrĕpaputra hīnaśakti*4:6:232*

Umasö ta maṅaŋ tutuknya malwa,kadi raṇḍö ta sukunya ƀinna yāgöŋ,maluṅid kadi gañjiran kukunya,ya ta paŋduknya ri saŋ naréndraputra*4:7:233*

Umulat sira karwa śīǥra maṅsö,sumikĕp karwa matuṅgalan sukunya,sinĕbit wadi dé nirāṙ dudut ya,mati tātan pabiṣān śiwak Awaknya*4:8:234*

ri pĕjaḥ nikanaŋ wirāđa mūṙkꝁa,Umahas saŋ nrĕpaputra niṙƀayātaḥ,tĕmu ṅ-āśrama dibya śoba rāmya,patapan saŋ śaraƀaṅga yoga sidđi*4:9:235*

sira saŋ rĕṣi sidđa dibya yogī,wihikan riŋ paramāṙŧa tatwa sūkṣma,paripakwa samāđi niṣkalĕṅka,dadi mamwit ta siromarèŋ kamokṣan*4:10:236*

kita rāma ṅaranta rājaputra,kami mamwīta marérikaŋ kamokṣan,lalu ƀāgya tĕmĕn kitāt para ṅké,kita nārāyaṇa maṅgalaṅku dibya*4:11:237*

hana tāśrama saŋ sutīkṣṇa yogī,yatikānuŋ wĕgilĕnta tat makūṅa,maparö ya taman madoḥ saka ṅké,rĕṣi yogī śaraṇānta saŋ sutīkṣṇa*4:12:238*

Iti nā ta wuwus niraŋ tapaswī,dadi tāyoga sirāsamāđi sidđi,magawé sira bahniđāraṇèka,magĕsöŋ śīṙṇna Awak nirātma pāsaḥ*4:13:239*

Aŧa mokṣa siraŋ mahāṙṣi sidđi,kawĕkas saŋ raǥuputra rāmadéwa,Umuwaḥ manusup sirèṅ alas göŋ,tĕmu tékāśrama saŋ sutīkṣṇa yogī*4:14:240*

saꝑalān winĕgil siraŋ sutīkṣṇa,karuṇā riŋ wanawāsakāciŧī ya,malawas ta naréndraputra rāma,rikanāṅ āśrama wètnyasiḥ mahāṙṣi*4:15:241*

{prabođitā}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :10:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
Umahas ta sirèŋ tapowana,tinamuy dé nira saŋ mahāmuni,ꝑalamūla pawĕḥ niraŋ rĕṣi,yatikāhāra nirāṙ hanèṅ alas*4:16:242*

I sĕḍĕŋ nikanaŋ wĕṅin tĕka,maturū saŋ nrĕpaputra riŋ Alas,kalaśā nira ron ikaŋ kayu,Umahā mabrata đīra taṙ lĕgö*4:17:243*

rahinanya mahās sirèṅ alas,mrĕga yā téka gawé nirāburu,mamatīka kĕnas rikèṅ alas,ya pamūjā nira nityakāla ya*4:18:244*

wiku paṇḍita wédapāraga,Umahas māmĕṅ-amĕŋ riṅ āśrama,rasikā tinamuy ya dé nira,pinakāhāra saśéṣa saŋ tamuy*4:19:245*

wiku rūpa nirāṙ hanèṅ alas,paḍa santoṣa rikaŋ kulit kayu,kayu yéka kadaŋ nirādasiḥ,ya paṅöban nira kāla niŋ panas*4:20:246*

sira tāpasawéṣa yan katon,ndan ikaŋ Āyuđa yéka tan kasaḥ,Aƀayā nira saŋ mahāṙṣi don,brata saŋ wīra rumākṣa saŋ wiku*4:21:247*

patapan ri samīpa niŋ gunuŋ,paḍa kapwénahasan ta dé nira,kinĕmit ya rinākṣa riŋ ƀaya,suka ménak ta pahoma saŋ rĕṣi*4:22:248*

salawas nirar uṅgu riŋ Alas,tamatan lèn inaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn Ira,suka duḥka niraŋ mahāmuni,ya cinittā winiwéka riŋ hati*4:23:249*

saꝑalāṙ wĕka saŋ raǥūttama,Ikanaŋ citta parāṙŧa kéwala,tar upékṣa laranyawak nira,prihataḥ kāṙyya niraŋ mahāmuni*4:24:250*

kramakāla Umèḥ kulĕm tĕkā,rikanāṅ āśrama sānđyawéla ya,tamataṙ malupèŋ bratājapa,kadi saŋ tāpa susatya sātwika*4:25:251*

rahinanya Atīta taŋ kulĕm,sakatambé Umuwaḥ sirājapa,tamataṙ kalupan hĕlĕm-hĕlĕm,matutuṙ tèŋ brata đīra niścala*4:26:252*

hana śūṙppaṇaꝁā ta rākṣasī,ya tikā cāra niraŋ daśānana,Umahas ya rikaŋ Alas kabèḥ,tĕka riŋ daṇḍaka kānanāśrama*4:27:253*

tinĕmunya ta saŋ nrĕpātmaja,riṅ alas kāwit amèt sĕkaṙ sira,kalawan janakātmajādulur,sira taṙ kāntun asiŋ paran tumūt*4:28:254*

dadi mūṙ ya tumon sirādulur,Ikanaŋ śūṙppaṇakā ta kéraṅan,manusup ya rikaŋ Alas wanèḥ,tĕmu saŋ lakṣmaṇa tāṅalap sĕkar*4:29:255*

kĕna kāma sarāga yan wulat,magawé ƀāwa mahiñji yan laku,paripūṙṇna Awaknya riŋ hayu,wulan iŋ puṙṇnamakāla tulya ya*4:30:256*

{mālaƀāriṇi}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
maḍĕmit sapĕgĕg tĕṅaḥnya māmbĕt,mamanis lèn pamatanya rāmya molĕm,malurus ta pupūnya lén wĕtisnya,jarijinyānuji laṇḍak ujwalābāŋ*4:31:257*

jaǥananya magöŋ susunya buntĕr,maputiḥ huntwalaris Iruŋnya śoƀā,sĕsĕranya maṇik manojña saśrī,masĕkaṙ rāmya marumpukan masumpiŋ*4:32:258*

mamanis ta wulatnya lèn guyunya,Ikana lwiṙnya makin sarāga mahyun,ri sawèt ni hiyunya tā Iraŋnya,ri siraŋ lakṣmaṇa yan masö ta mojar*4:33:259*

kaka lakṣmaṇa hé sumitraputra,Aku mūṙcꞓā kĕna kāma dènta tībra,Asihanta kunĕŋ taman pahīṅan,hulunantāku baśā kité tuwuḥku*4:34:260*

salawas ni huripku tan kasāha,ri kitāsiŋ saparanta tan madoha,sapakonta riké ṅhulun kadadya,ri sĕḍĕṅtāt anumāna riŋ kĕnèŋ hyun*4:35:261*

Iti nā ta wuwusnya tā Iraŋnya,sinaput dé ni panaḥ ƀaṭāra kāma,sumahuṙ ta siraŋ sinoma-somaḥ,sira saŋ lakṣmaṇa gadgadā ta dénya*4:36:262*

Aparan kita dibyarūpa mojar,ry-apa saṅkanta Amānuṣākrĕtinta,tamatat matakut rikèṅ alas göŋ,tak anon ṅwaŋ tuwi lèn anuŋ tĕka ṅké*4:37:263*

lalu dibya hayunta kādƀutāku,Apa jātinta yan apsarī ta kūnĕŋ,paricāra winèḥ ya kāntunèka,kita kanyāhayu towi tuṅga-tuṅgal*4:38:264*

{prabođitā}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :10:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
nya dumèh aku saṅśayā tĕmĕn,kita mojaṙ ry-aku tan kĕnèṅ iraŋ,kadi mèdi wuwusta maŋlaré,kita déwākrĕti mānuṣa ṅhulun*4:39:265*

yuwatī kita kanyakā kunĕŋ,Aŧawātaḥ palakunta diṇḍaré,ya mataŋnya taman kĕnèṅ iraŋ,ta wuwus torasi ri ṅhulun Ari*4:40:266*

kalawan n-aku tak sayogya wèḥ,ri kakaṅku t-para yogya māsiha,sira rāma ṅaran nirèŋ jagat,Anumānèŋ kĕna rāga mūṙcꞓita*4:41:267*

guṇamānta sĕḍĕŋta yowana,sira saŋ rāma ta māsihé kita,wihikan maṅiriŋ Anākĕbi,sira tāmolya ri kahyunanta wèḥ*4:42:268*

Amanis pamata-n-nirālaris,paṅawak sahya lawan muꝁābuṅaḥ,tuwi bāhu nirāwiḍaŋ katon,paṅalaḥ śatru gawénya riŋ raṇa*4:43:269*

hana kadga nirātitīkṣṇa ya,tan adoḥ yadyapi yan tĕkāŋ musuḥ,tinahā Ikanaŋ raṇān tĕkā,ya karākṣā nira don ikaŋ tĕwĕk*4:44:270*

wwara tāyuđa lèn laras magöŋ,taya tāŋ wwaŋ Umĕnaŋ mayat tikā,paṅalaḥ nira riŋ musuḥ kabèḥ,Ikanaŋ rākṣasa mūṙkꝁa sāhasa*4:45:271*

sumukū patapan mahāmuni,hana miǥnékana yajña saŋ rĕṣi,rĕṣiśatru ya mélik iŋ wiku,ya pinatyan n-ira tan paśéṣa ya*4:46:272*

suka saŋ rĕṣi niṙƀayĕŋ Alas,ri kadibyan niraṅ āṙyya rāǥawa,ya mataŋnya sayogya yat siwin,kita ƀāgyan yadiyat paré sira*4:47:273*

wara lakṣmaṇa nā ta liŋ nira,Ikanaŋ śūṙppaṇaꝁā gĕlāna ya,rumĕṅö guṇa saŋ raǥūttama,dadi maṅsö ya sahaṙṣa yan tĕka*4:48:274*

satĕkanya wuwusnya tan kalèn,sira saŋ rāma wawaŋ sirāsahur,Ari dibya hayunta komala,lalu hémanta ya tan kataṅgapa*4:49:275*

nya sirāri Ariṅku taṙ madoḥ,sira sītā karĕṅö rikèŋ sarāt,tamatak maṅaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn wanèḥ,rasikā tuṅgal ataḥ kurĕnkwari*4:50:276*

nya kunĕŋ wuwusaṅkwi yogya ya,Ikanāriṅku si lakṣmaṇāt para,kurĕnanya kitāri māsiha,kita kanyā ta surūpa komala*4:51:277*

raǥuputra nahan wuwus nira,Ikanaŋ śūṙppaṇaꝁā maluy ta ya,I siraŋ taruṇāṙyya lakṣmaṇa,Alah ahyun kĕna kāmabāṇa ya*4:52:278*

Umasö ta-taman kĕnèṅ iraŋ,sumĕḍĕk kéraṅ-iraŋ Ulaḥnya wèḥ,tan ulaḥ nikanaŋ Anākĕbi,pinakolaḥnya ya nīca kaśmala*4:53:279*

Umulat maṅiṅöt-iṅötakĕn,sira saŋ lakṣmaṇa kādƀutaŋ manaḥ,kala mūṙkꝁa Iké ta rākṣasī,ya ta sandéha sirāṙ sikĕp ta ya*4:54:280*

tinĕwöṙ nira nāsikā niké,Ikanéruŋnya huwus pĕgat hilaŋ,Umĕsat ya mibĕṙ marèŋ laṅit,mĕtu jātinya ya rākṣasīn katon*4:55:281*

Aku śūṙppaṇaꝁāku rākṣasī,kita tan wruḥ ry-aku mūḋa kāsyasiḥ,jaga yatna huripta rākṣa ya,biṣamāt-mātya tĕkā kakaṅku ya*4:56:282*

ꝁara dūṣaṇa rakṣasottama,rikanaŋ śākti paḍanya tan hana,Aniwāṙyya ya wīra riŋ raṇa,kita kāliḥ Ulihanya yan tĕkā*4:57:283*

ri huwus ni wuwusnya maṅgĕmĕr,malayū śūṙppaṇaꝁānaṅis ta ya,winĕgilnya kakanya śīǥra ya,triśiraḥ mwaŋ kara lèn si dūṣaṇa*4:58:284*

kaka hé triśiraḥ tuluŋ ṅhulun,lalu tad wruḥ ri laraṅku mohita,tamatan paṅaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn kita,Ikanaŋ śatru ya sāhasé ṅhulun*4:59:285*

wwara rāma ṅaranya tāpasa,hana tārinya ṅaranya lakṣmaṇa,wikuƀāwa katon mahāṙdđika,gumĕgö ṅ-āyuđa duṣṭacitta ya*4:60:286*

pariƀūta wĕnaŋ ya sāhasa,tumĕwöṙ téka Iruṅku niṙǥrĕṇa,tuwi tan hana doṣa ni ṅhulun,Ikanaŋ lakṣmaṇa yomahāwĕgig*4:61:287*

yadiyat hĕnĕṅāta riŋ musuḥ,tat asĕṅhit hana sāhasé ṅhulun,Apa dona ni jīwitaṅku wèḥ,Apa tak péruṅ iraṅku tan sipi*4:62:288*

praƀu rāwaṇa nāŧa ni ṅhulun,tuwi makwèḥ ta kakaṅku rākṣasa,tamataṙ matakut Ikaŋ musuḥ,ya masampé ry-aku tan pakāraṇa*4:63:289*

Aparan ta guṇaṅku yak hanā,lĕhĕṅaŋ mātya kunĕŋ misan-misan,yadiyat hĕnĕṅāta riŋ musuḥ,tat asĕṅhit hana sāhasé ṅhulun*4:64:290*

ya mataŋnya yadin hanāsihanta,Ikanaŋ rāǥawa lakṣmaṇolihanta,Aku niśśaraṇā kitāśrayaṅkwa,yan agöŋ śakti nikaŋ musuḥ prihĕnta*4:65:291*

Apa tan pasahāya tuṅga-tuṅgal,ꝑalamūlāśana yāmaṅan gĕgāṅan,daluwaŋ wĕḍihanya rūkṣa duḥka,Ikanaŋ sakṣaṇa yālahāta dènta*4:66:292*

kala śūṙppaṇaꝁā nahan Ujaṙnya,triśiraḥ krođa ya maṅgĕtĕm masĕṅhit,kara dūṣaṇa lèn sarodra matta,manĕpak bāhu masiṅhanāda mojar*4:67:293*

Ari śaṙppaṇaꝁā tamat saśoka,kami kāliḥ ta makolihékanaŋ wwaŋ,takarin naraƀakṣakāmaṅan wwaŋ,taya doṣanya tuwi n-pĕjaḥ ya dèṅku*4:68:294*

ri huwusnya masiṅhanāda maṅkat,kalawan rākṣasa ƀrĕtya kapwa saṅkĕp,tĕka yèŋ patapan parĕŋ ya mahyā,paḍa maṅsö sumahab lawan balanya*4:69:295*

mapapan makatap-katap ya saṅkĕp,matilañjaŋ majajaṙ kabèḥ mapañjaŋ,magalaḥ magalak malād ilatnya,malipuŋ puŋ juga riŋ wĕgig g-umaṅkat*4:70:296*

saḍatĕŋnya kabèḥ maṅĕmbuli,sira saŋ rāǥawa lakṣmaṇomasö,pinanaḥ nira tan paśéṣa ya,hibĕkan waṅkay ikaŋ tĕgal kabèḥ*4:71:297*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :10:

hana ƀinna śiwak Awak nikā,hana timpaŋ pinanaḥ pupūnya timpal,tahulan ni hulunya ya rĕmuk,hana mānaŋ-manaṅan hilaŋ taṅanya*4:72:298*

kumĕtĕṙ sawanèḥ hanālayu,hana méraŋ Umaluy pwa yékaṅāmūk,ri muꝁanya mabāŋ mulĕk m~tu rāḥ,gumaluṅgaŋ ri gulūnya rodra taŋ hrū*4:73:299*

{puṣpitāgra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:

bala makabalasaḥ wanèḥ kabuñcaŋ,dadi mapuliḥ triśiraḥ masö masĕṅhit,saraƀasa magalak Ulā paḍanya,garuḍa paḍā nira saŋ naréndraputra*4:74:300*

Inarah-arah ikā gulūnya riŋ hrū,hana warayaŋ dadalī jugāṅlayaŋ ya,suniśita maputiḥ tĕlas malaṇḍĕp,ya mĕgatakĕn ri gulūnya rāḥnya muñcar*4:75:301*

hulu makabarubuḥ tibā kabèḥnya,kadi ta ya pāṙśwa nikaŋ gunuŋ rubuḥ rūg,tat ujara ta-takut niraŋ tapārĕs,tuwi bala rākṣasa tan wĕnaŋ mulat ya*4:76:302*

#pañcamas saṙggaḥ#
<rajanī>:5
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
^5/1/303.
Aŧa ri pĕjaḥ nikaŋ triśira śīǥra hulūnya tibā,dadi ta masö masĕṅhit ikanaŋ ꝁara dūṣaṇa lèn,saha bala maŋlayaŋ kadi ta méǥa katon ahirĕŋ,karatala kadga cakra winawanya ya tulya kilat*5:1:303*

hana mamanaḥ wanèḥ kadi ta bajra panaḥnya biṣa,tali ni panaḥnya rodra kumupak kaharan gĕlapa,raǥusuta bāyubajra ya paḍā ni panaḥ nira bāp,ya ta kumĕnékanaŋ kala tibā sahananya pĕjaḥ*5:2:304*

ri pati nikaŋ musuḥ si ꝁara dūṣaṇa lèn triśiraḥ,makin asĕkĕl gĕlāna ta si śūṙppanakā manaṅis,dadi malayū tĕkènajarakĕn ta kakanya pĕjaḥ,ri sira ta saŋ daśānana masö ya mahā manĕsĕl*5:3:305*

praƀu kita rāwaṇātiśaya śakti jayèŋ ƀuwana,praṇata musuḥta ƀakti matakut sahananya kabèḥ,surapati saŋ hyaṅ indra tuwi ƀakti sira praṇata,kaŧam api duṙnaya pwa kita hīna tamat panulus*5:4:306*

hana kari cārakanta ya kinon mahasèŋ prĕŧiwī,sumusupanaŋ Alas biṣama śatru hanā matapa,ya tika tahānta haywa humĕnĕŋ pwa kitèŋ biṣama,ya Ika kaduṙṇnayanta Amĕṅāmni balanta pĕjaḥ*5:5:307*

si kara si dūṣaṇa triśira sūra suđīra pĕjaḥ,lumaku kinon matuṅgwa rikanaŋ giri ḍaṇḍaka ya,mati kapisan taman pabisa dé nika saŋ matapa,prakaśita rāma lakṣmaṇa matī ya taman pamalĕs*5:6:308*

sahana-hananta mātya kita dénya si dāśarati,ya ta walĕsĕnta toḥ kira-kiran pĕjahanya huwus,saꝑala Ikā kasĕṅhitakĕnéka pĕjaḥnya kabèḥ,Apan anipis pagĕṙta yadiyan mahurip biṣama*5:7:309*

kita mamaṅan magoṣṭi maṅinum saha ƀrĕtya wijaḥ,wiṣaya kasakta tat Aṅĕn-aṅĕn ṅ-awasāna pijĕr,kita wĕgig iŋ musuḥ daṅu-daṅū magĕlöm aṅawit,hana pariƀūta śatru tamatan pamalĕs pwa mĕné*5:8:310*

rikanaṅ alas ri ḍaṇḍaka siraŋ tapa taṙ matakut,pratidina homayajña ginawé nira kapwa lanā,tuwi taya rākṣasāṅipik-ipik rikanaŋ patapan,raǥusuta rāma lakṣmaṇa Ataḥ katakutnya kabèḥ*5:9:311*

rasika ta saŋ raǥūttama-taman pasahāya tuwi,Inatus-atus ta rowaṅ ikanaŋ ꝁara dūṣaṇa bāp,punar api tan hanāmyati matap mati yāguliṅan,Ikana panaḥ niraŋ raǥusutādƀuta mrĕtyu juga*5:10:312*

dađi ǥrĕta māṅsa matsya pinaṅan ꝑala dibya raṣa,surawara déwatā ya pinaṅan ya warĕg ya mĕné,Ikana balanta rākṣasa humöt ya kabèḥ malapā,Alah atakut ri saŋ prawara rāǥawa lakṣmaṇa ya*5:11:313*

ya tika dumèḥ kitāmriha mabudđya ya laṇḍĕpana,wiṣaya ya tāryakĕn maran agöŋ ta hayunta lanā,Atiśaya cañcalékanaṅ inak kṣaṇa matra hilaŋ,ya ta kĕmitĕn prihĕnta gawayĕnta ṅ-upāya huwus*5:12:314*

wwara ta ya ǥāra saŋ raǥusutottama riŋ rahayu,Awak akilākiris mrĕdu ya komala konĕṅ unĕŋ,swara nira haṅsanāda mamanis juga yan karĕṅö,ya ta Alapĕnta liṅku saꝑalān kawawéri kita*5:13:315*

Ataha-tahan matanta Apa tapwan anoṇ ḍahayu,Ikana Iruŋta tan saꝑala yan tan ikārĕkana,tuwi taliṅanta niṙ-guṇa ya tan paṅujaṙnya rĕṅön,suka paripūṙṇna riŋ hayu Asiŋ kahanan rasikā*5:14:316*

sari-sari niŋ rasātiśaya sāri nikaŋ wiṣaya,yan ika jugānakĕbya tat aṅipya wanèha ta ya,Asiṅ umulat riyāhyuna manaḥnya sumomaha ya,triƀuwanarājya yéka palakunya wĕlīna ta ya*5:15:317*

hari-dayitā śacī tuwi taman pamaḍāna hayu,girisuta rohiṇī rati Apūṙwwa taman pamaḍé,hayu rasikā kabèḥ rahayu liŋ niṅ apuṅguṅ ikā,Anakĕbi saŋ raǥūttama jugāhayu liṅku putus*5:16:318*

ya Ikana liŋ nikaŋ Ađama śūṙppanakān pawuwus,ri sira ta saŋ daśānana wawaŋ sumahuṙ ta sira,Ari kita haywa cāla hrĕdayanta tamat Alara,takarin iké si rāwaṇa ṅaranya jayèŋ ƀuwana*5:17:319*

syapa karikā tinonta kinaƀaktyan iṅ indra kunĕŋ,kuliśa ta śīṙṇna bajra ri ḍaḍaṅku taman paṅani,hana ta liman hyaṅ indra sinikĕpku taman paṅapa,ḍukut upamanya tan paguṇa dèṅku tinimpalakĕn*5:18:320*

nda taṅa-taṅā praƀāwa ni si rāwaṇa tan papaḍa,satata mara-ŋ wulan Umĕtu pūṙṇnama taṙ wiluma,mamawa wuṅa n-tahun sahana niŋ hyaṅ alaḥ matakut,sa Isi nikaŋ surālaya Anéka kahĕnti kabèḥ*5:19:321*

Ikana wuwusta hāsya mata kéraṅ-iraŋ dahatĕn,yak atukarāpraṅa mwaṅ ikaṅaŋ tapa dāśaraŧī,tuwi ya manūṣya hīnabala tan hana śakti riya,saka riyasiḥku tag wihaṅ asiŋ sapakonta rari*5:20:322*

Aŧa ri huwus nirominaki citta si śūṙppaṇakā,lumaku sirāhawan gagana śīǥra manojawana,pratita si candrahāsa ya tĕwĕk nira tan kapasaḥ,satĕka nirèŋ samudra sumĕpĕṙ ta sirèŋ pasisi*5:21:323*

mara-marahaŋ marīca ya ta don ira yan sĕpĕra,satĕka nirāṙ waraḥ ta si marīca ri karya nira,dadi sumahuṙ satorasi mataṅguh alaḥ matakut,ya huwus alaḥ pwa ṅūni pinanaḥ riṅ aṅin ya katūb*5:22:324*

praƀu kita hé daśānana nanā kita yat malagā,lawan ika saŋ raǥuprawara rāma ya śakti tĕmĕn,Ikana si candrahāsa ya tĕwĕkta taman paṅapa,mataṅ ika haywa māra Irikaŋ tapa dāśaraŧi*5:23:325*

hana sira jāmadagni wiku śakti matī ratu bāp,saṅ umĕjahīkaṅ aṙjjuna sahasraƀujèŋ palagan,syapa karĕṅö Anuŋ malahakĕn sira tan hana lèn,raǥusuta kéwalāta winuwus sira śakti jaya*5:24:326*

nya ta ya si tāṭakākya bali māti tĕkap rasikā,Aŧa ri sĕḍĕŋ mayajña sira saŋ rĕṣi kampalayu,kapati gupuy ṅhulun kapalupuy pinanaḥ riṅ aṅin,praƀu ta turuŋ tamad wruh i-gĕlis nira yan pamanaḥ*5:25:327*

Atiśaya riŋ đanuṙđara raǥūttama taṙ papaḍa,taku-takutĕn nikaŋ Asura rākṣasa taṙ papuliḥ,samĕna nikaṅwaṅal mati cĕṅĕlnya pĕgat pinanaḥ,si ꝁara si dūṣaṇa triśira śīṙṇna suđīra pĕjaḥ*5:26:328*

Umilu sirèŋ swayambara ri yajña niraŋ janaka,hana ta laras Umuṅgu ri tĕṅaḥ nikanaŋ pasaƀān,sahana niraŋ ratu pwa ya mayat ya taman kawĕnaŋ,kaŧam api saŋ raǥūttama mayat ya tikĕl wĕkasan*5:27:329*

kita suka kéwalāwĕrĕ-wĕrö mamaṅan maṅinum,saha bala matta māṅsaka surā Ininumta lanā,Amija-mijaḥ sĕkaṙ jĕnu suganđa jĕnĕk riṅ inak,ndya ta gamananta tat Alaha riŋ raṇa dé rasikā*5:28:330*

nahan ujar iŋ marīca ya mataṅguh akon maluya,muji guṇa saŋ raǥūttama ri śakti nirātiśaya,mĕdi-mĕdi saŋ daśānana ya donya Alaḥ matakut,dadi magĕlĕŋ ta saŋ daśamuꝁāsi wawaŋ sumahur*5:29:331*

guragaḍa ko marīca hatinīca wimūḋa cĕmĕr,Ikana Ujaṙ-mu jañjan ujar iŋ maṅajap juga ya,Umalahakĕn siraŋ paraśurāma sirékin alaḥ,Apan atuhā kĕlut sira si rāma sĕḍĕŋ taruṇa*5:30:332*

Ikana si tāṭakā pinĕjahanya taman sapujin,Anakĕbi tan pasāra tuwi tan pasabāya ta ya,ya ta pinanaḥ ni rāǥawa ya niṙǥrĕṇa tan paguṇa,yadiyan ikā pujinta lalu hātmu yu đik laku mūr*5:31:333*

tuwi pinanaḥ ni rāǥawa ta ko Atikaṣṭa dahat,wĕdi-wĕdi hīna nīca rumaras ta manaḥmu kawĕs,Ikana panaḥnya manda taman ādrĕs aṅinya malon,saka ri takutmu mamrih alayū juga tan Inapa*5:32:334*

hana ta Ujaṙmu lèn umuji śakti ni dāśaraŧi,Anikĕlakĕn laras Apan awūk malawas kinĕkĕs,ya pinaṅan iŋ bubuk gili-gilig ya dumèḥnya nana,Ikaṅ umayat ya tambayan ataḥ lalu hīna dahat*5:33:335*

pati nikanaŋ kara triśira tan ya dumèḥ ya pujin,Apan akĕlé pramāda ya dumèḥnya kabèḥ pĕjaha,yan agalakāṅlagāna ri si rāǥawa ǥoratara,niyata pĕjaḥ ni rāǥawa rikaŋ kṣaṇa taṙ paṅapa*5:34:336*

ndya ta ya pujimwa śakti ni si rāǥawa koŋ Ađama,druhaka jugāharĕp maliha budđimu ƀaktya riya,mataṅ ika kompujīriya guṇaṅku tamaṙ puji ya,jaga-jaga mātya ko druhaka cittamu taṇ ḍahayu*5:35:337*

Aŧa ri huwus nirāṅuman-uman maṅunus ta tĕwĕk,kumĕtĕr ikā kumis nira humīs hariṅĕt niṅ awak,kadi tinĕpak kabāṅan ikanaŋ muꝁa ƀīṣaṇa ya,tudiṅi tikaŋ marīca ya manĕmbah aminta hurip*5:36:338*

ṅhulun ikihĕn patik praṇata ƀakti taman druhaka,tuhu-tuhu ƀakti riŋ praƀu Asiŋ sapakona riya,Ikana kunaŋ dumèḥ ṅhulun ataṅguha đaṙmma tinūt,prakrĕti nikaŋ manéwaka mataṅguha donya hitā*5:37:339*

yadiyapi yat pituhwa hayu niŋ naya tan wihaṅĕn,sarahayu sèṣṭi saŋ praƀu ya tūtĕna dadyakĕna,nahan ikanaŋ Upāya yadiyan kĕna yat pituhun,tĕmahana ni ṅhulun kidaṅ arambuta mās kanaka*5:38:340*

Ikana si rāma lakṣmaṇa ya dohakĕnaṅkwa huwus,ri wuri nikā sakèṣṭi nira nāŧa taman warahĕn,nahan ujariŋ marīca wĕkasan maduluṙ lumaku,tĕka ya rikaŋ Alas matĕmahan ta kidaŋ kanaka*5:39:341*

marakatawaṙṇna rāmya makiris ta gigiṙnya katon,Ikana wulunyawaknya malĕṅis ya kabèḥ mas abāŋ,tĕka ya masö ri saŋ janakarājasutā ya mariŋ,kadi giniraŋ-giraŋ hati nirādƀuta dénya jĕnĕk*5:40:342*

Iniṅĕt-iṅĕt nirāhayu kulitnya kĕmul-kĕmula,Apan alĕṅis katon kanaka rambut alĕmbut alit,hati nira tībra dé nira harĕp ri hayunya katon,dadi ta makon makoliha rikaŋ mrĕga ratnamaya*5:41:343*

raǥusuta taṙ wihaŋ juga Asiŋ sapakon i-sira,Ari nira lakṣmaṇā ta kawĕkas makĕmit patapan,lumaku siromusī ya sinikĕp nira tan kawĕnaŋ,Apan agĕlis lumumpat analimpĕtakĕn mawilĕt*5:42:344*

kadi ya mariŋ mahā ya sakarĕŋ maṅadĕg maparö,wahu tinalandaṅan ya sinikĕp nira śīǥra mĕsat,Apan alĕyö wulunya malĕṅis linĕṅan juga ya,kamaga taṅan nirān kaluputan malayū ya muwaḥ*5:43:345*

dadi ta madoḥ Uliḥ nira manūti taman kawĕnaŋ,tuwi maṅidīdi yāmarimisin maṅadĕg sakarĕŋ,hati nira héwa dénya tamatan kawĕnaŋ sinikĕp,r-ayat ikanaŋ laras r-arah-araḥ ya rikaŋ warayaŋ*5:44:346*

kadi hinarit higānya mĕtu rāḥnya Ususnya mulū,wĕkasi huripnya yékana pawūnya mamañcana ya,janakasutā gĕlāna rumĕṅö ri taṅisnya mawās,kadi ta ya śabda saŋ prawara rāma maminta tuluŋ*5:45:347*

dadi manaṅis siraŋ janakarājasutā ta mawū,laku ta Ariṅku lakṣmaṇa tuluŋ pwa kakanta tasön,kita marikénuhuḥ nira makon umarātuluṅa,lalu tan asiḥ ta riŋ kaka tasö pwa tarākṣa sira*5:46:348*

ya Ikana liŋ niraŋ janakarājasutāṙ panaṅis,saka ri Asiḥ niréki panahā nikanaŋ hrĕdaya,dadi sumahuṙ ta saŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇa tan kagĕmĕr,pracaya ri śakti saŋ kaka rikaŋ raṇa taṙ malaha*5:47:349*

kita raǥuwīraǥāra kaḍasiḥ ni kakaṅku kita,Aŧawa naréndra saŋ janakarāja bapanta sira,lalu ta ya dènta hīna kagĕmö rumĕṅö manaṅis,sira karikānaṅis syapa wĕruḥta kunaŋ ya hadé*5:48:350*

syapa kari śakti riŋ ƀuwana liŋta Anuŋ wĕnaṅa,lumawana saŋ naréndrasuta rāǥawa riŋ palagan,sira juga śaktimānta wihikan ta riṅ astra kabèḥ,ndya ta ya kasaṅśayān pĕjaha paṇḍuk ikaŋ hariṇa*5:49:351*

syapa wĕka saŋ raǥūttama Anuŋ rinĕṅönta daṅū,Alah atakut ya mātya mamalakwa ta rakwa tuluŋ,sahana nikaŋ watĕk raǥu kabèḥ tak anon alayū,mati ya mamūk taman mawĕdi yan hana śatru biṣa*5:50:352*

Aŧawa Ikaŋ kidaŋ kadi mahā maharĕp pĕjaha,rasa ri Ulaḥnya kādƀuta tumon sira tan matakut,Atisaꝑalāstra saŋ raǥusuta pwa ya donya pĕjaḥ,maturun apuy hiḍĕpnya ri panaḥ nira bahnimaya*5:51:353*

syapa karikā tan adƀuta tumon raǥuputra haraḥ,jaya rikanaŋ musuḥ sira taman papaḍĕŋ ƀuwana,mataṅ ika haywa śoka kita dé nikanaŋ manaṅis,muliha kakanta rāǥawa makolih ikaŋ hariṇa*5:52:354*

Ikanaṅ awū taman sira Ikā kala rākṣasa ya,kira-kira bañcanékana ya don i-Uninya mahā,taṅis ikanaŋ kidaŋ Ikana liṅku huwus pinanaḥ,Umaḍa-maḍékanā swara niraŋ raǥusiṅha juga*5:53:355*

Aŧa ri huwus niraŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇa yaṙ pawuwus,janakasutā tataṙ pamituhu pwa Amoǥa wihaŋ,Ikanaṅ asiḥ takut ya maṅawéśa rikaŋ hrĕdaya,dadi sumahuṙ mrĕṣodita wuwus nira taṇ ḍahayu*5:54:356*

Ari kita saŋ sumitratanayāpa kalīṅan ikā,wahu-wahu dènta māmbĕk alĕmöḥ ri pakonku mĕné,Atiśaya ƀakti riŋ daṅu-daṅū kita sātya kaka,punar api duṙbbala pwa sira hīna tamat patuluŋ*5:55:357*

wruh aku ri don i-budđimu kaṭuṅka tamaṇ ḍahayu,druhaka ri saŋ raǥūttama manaḥmu harĕp wipaŧa,Atiśaya duṙjjanāđama dahat raǥuwaṅśa kariḥ,wĕnaṅ aƀimāna riŋ kaka Ah-o Atikaśmala ya*5:56:358*

Ikana Aṅĕn-n-aṅĕnmu ri siraŋ raǥupūtra nihan,mati sira dé nikaŋ mrĕga sadénya saƀāgya tĕmĕn,sumiliha tāku riŋ janakarājasutāku baśā,syapa śaraṇānya tan hana wanèh aku liŋmu nihan*5:57:359*

Ađama wimūḋa lakṣmaṇa waliŋmu manaḥku kalā,wĕnaṅa makāmbĕka-ŋ hala matāku mahālwana wèḥ,Aku tak aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn laki wanèḥ sira tuṅgal ataḥ,makahulunāku tan hana wanèḥ raǥuputra juga*5:58:360*

yan alalisāŋ ƀaṭāra pĕjahāta siraŋ siniwi,raǥusuta sora riŋ samara paṇḍuk ikaŋ hariṇa,pĕgatakĕnaṅkwa tékana guluṅkwa turūn apuya,tumutura tāku riŋ priya tamāg wĕgilāta ri ko*5:59:361*

ya Ikana liŋ niraŋ janakarājasutā magĕlĕŋ,maṅuman-uman Amoǥa wulaṅun maharĕp mahalā,hala ni manaḥ nirāta juga tan tinahān mahalā,saka ri wirođa niŋ hati mataŋnya halān tinahā*5:60:362*

daśaraŧaputra lakṣmaṇa gĕlāna ta mépu sira,Atiśaya dibya tékana wuwus nira yan karĕṅö,naya nira yukti tékana lalu pwa ya tan kahiḍĕp,ya ta lumaré manaḥ nira wawaŋ sumahuṙ ta sira*5:61:363*

ṅhulun ikihĕn sinaṅśaya kalā druhakāk makaka,Ikana manaḥku śudđa juga satya taman kalana,sahana baṭāra sākṣya ni hatiṅku siromulata,naraka tĕmuṅkwa duḥka hiḍĕpĕṅkwa yadin druhakā*5:62:364*

janakasutā samaṅkana kitāt mawuwus mahala,kadi maṅajap sumaṅguh aku mahyuna wèḥ ri kita,saka ri wuwusta taṇ ḍahayu duḥka tĕmunta magöŋ,tawanĕn ikāŋ musuḥ kita mĕné ri wuriṅku haraḥ*5:63:365*

nahan ika liŋ nirāṙ panapaŧé dadi śīǥra sira,laku tumutūr i-saŋ kaka tumūta manūta kidaŋ,ri wuri niromadĕg janakarājasutā wĕkasan,lumaku mamèt sĕkaṙ sira ri saṇḍiṅ ikaŋ patapan*5:64:366*

Aŧa ri sĕḍĕŋ nirāmupu sĕkaṙ manusup riṅ alas,tĕka ta siraŋ daśānana mahāṙdđika rūpa nira,wiku śuci śudđa śꜽwa sira sātwika śānta katon,hulu malĕṅis ginuntiṅ aratā hana kuñcir alit*5:65:367*

Atiśaya śudđa huntu maputiḥ sꝑaṭikopama ya,tuwi magaṇitrikuṇḍala waluḥ ya sinaṇḍaṅ ira,lituhayu waṙṇna lāka daluwaŋ nira rāmya mabāŋ,lumaku manasya yéka dalihan Ira tan katĕṅĕr*5:66:368*

majapa maṅunyakĕn ta sira mantra tĕhĕṙ lumaku,mrĕdu mamanis wulat nira marūm atisomya katon,Ikana karākṣasān ira kadi pwa ya tan hana wèḥ,tama ta macaṅkramé tĕpi niṅ āśrama rāmya kabèḥ*5:67:369*

tinĕmu nirā ta saŋ janakarājasutā riṅ alas,sira juga tuṅga-tuṅgal anusup tamataṙ matakut,dadi ta masö siraŋ daśamuꝁātisahaṙṣa sira,makin aparö sagorawa sirān pawuwus wĕkasan*5:68:370*

Apa kita dibya rūpa manusup maṅalap ta sĕkar,Atiśaya tā paḍanta rikanaŋ hayu pūṙṇna tĕmĕn,hayu nikanaŋ wulan tuwi taman pamaḍéri kita,Apan awĕnĕs ya riŋ rahina hīna tamaṙ pasĕnö*5:69:371*

kusuma saroja riŋ talaga kapwa sĕḍĕŋ sumĕkar,rahayu suganđa waṙṇna ya mabaŋ maputiḥ sawanèḥ,tuwi tamatan paḍékana hayunya masoṙ juga ya,Apan umaluy kucup ya rikanaŋ wĕṅi taṇ ḍahayu*5:70:372*

Iki kahananta ƀīṣaṇa Amānuṣagamya sukĕt,tan awĕdi riŋ Ulā biṣama lèn aliman magalak,syapa śaraṇānta liṅku yadiyan hana moŋ maṅawit,Ikana hayunta héman ari yogya kahātakĕna*5:71:373*

kita mrĕdu komalātiśaya konĕṅ unĕŋ ri hati,kadi ta ƀinūsaṇan Ikaṅ alas ri hananta riya,saṅapa ṅarān irāta sira saŋ siniwinta kunĕŋ,Atiśaya göŋ ni đaṙmma rasikān pamawéri kita*5:72:374*

Aku ta pariƀramanta paradéśa rikaŋ ƀuwana,tuwi tak anon anuŋ paḍa-paḍānta surūpa tĕmĕn,kita juga hīṅa niŋ hayu ya liṅku tanora wanèḥ,saꝑala Iké huripku ri huwusku wĕruḥ ri kita*5:73:375*

Ikana hayunta yāk iṅĕt-inĕt ya kadi pwa sĕkar,huwus inisĕp nikaŋ ƀramara téka sarinya rurū,hana ta hayunya mātra kawĕkas ya paḍanta katon,ya ta panĕṅĕṙkwawās ya sira saŋ siniwīnta hana*5:74:376*

Ikana ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu tuwi marya sirāṙ pahiyun,I sira ta saŋ priyā nira masoṙ sira dènta tĕmĕn,Aŧawa ƀaṭāra kāma sira kāmuꝁa liṅku pijĕr,ri sira ta saŋ ratiḥ nira taman pamaḍéri kita*5:75:377*

sahana nikaŋ Anākĕbi tuwin yadiyan wulata,niyata ya kādƀuté kita manaḥnya kapūhan ataḥ,ṅuni-ṅuni tékanaŋ taruṇa yan wruha mahyuna ya,pira warĕganya riŋ wiṣaya matta ƀaṭāra tuwi*5:76:378*

hana ta daridra duḥkita tuwin mari yan pahiyun,yan apa ya tāsihériya sumaṇḍiṅa yèŋ śayana,maṅayam-ayam mahās mabayaṅan hati saŋ wiṣayī,kita yatikāmrĕtosađa niraŋ kĕna kāmaśara*5:77:379*

wĕka-wĕka sāṅapéki sira saŋ siniwinta kunĕŋ,lalu wihikan Irān hana kitèŋ patapān asukĕt,saka ri takut nirān hana wanèha tumona kita,yatika dumèḥ sirānusup umuṅgu rikaŋ patapan*5:78:380*

daśamuꝁa nā ta liŋ nira sahaṙṣa sirāṙ pawuwus,janakasutā sagadgada manaḥ nira yan pinuji,hati rumaras puhun wulu niromuririŋ matakut,praṇata sirāṙ paśabda mawaraḥ ta ri saŋ siniwi*5:79:381*

wwara sira rāma dāśaraŧi śakti tamaṙ papaḍé,sira rasiké Anuŋ makahulun ṅhulun āṙyyaguṇa,Atiśaya ƀakti riŋ bapa siromituhu-ŋ sapakon,sahana niraŋ tapaswi sira rākṣaka riŋ patapan*5:80:382*

sahana nikā musuḥ nira mahāṙṣi pinatyan ira,sira ta sumorakĕn paraśu rāma rikaŋ palagan,sira kumĕmit mahāṙṣi yan ahoma mayajña lanā,mara ta sirèṅ alas saka ri ƀakti nirāṙ mabapa*5:81:383*

śatĕka nirèṅ alas hana ta rākṣasa sāhasika,ya ta lumagé sirāṙ tĕka parĕŋ maṅabèhi masö,saha bala śaktimānta sahananya pĕjaḥ pinanaḥ,ri tĕpi niṅ āśramāt taṅa-taṅā hana waṅkay atap*5:82:384*

sira karĕṅö đanuṙđara rikaŋ ƀuwanāṇḍa kabèḥ,magada-gadāna dadya tamatan hana koli nira,kadi pinusus tikaŋ musuh asiŋ Umasö kapisan,kita kadi molya mĕṅgĕp amĕpöri siraŋ siniwi*5:83:385*

Ikana mataŋnya tan katĕmu dènta nihan ya rĕṅön,wwara ya kidaŋ hĕmas ya Inusī nira kādƀuta ya,Ari nira lakṣmaṇéka kawĕkas-wĕkasan tumutur,saka ri pakonku yékana dumèḥ nira taṙ wihaṅa*5:84:386*

Aŧa ri huwus niraŋ janakarājasutāṙ pawaraḥ,makin umasö siraŋ daśamuꝁāṙ pawuwus ta muwaḥ,wruh aku rikā si rāǥawa ṅaranya taman paguṇa,Apa ta dumèḥ kitāhyun iriyā ri kaniṣṭa dahat*5:85:387*

Ađama masoṙ ya saṅka ri Arinya kabèḥ wihikan,ya matuha yogya ratwa ya kinon pwa marékiṅ alas,mamati-matīka rākṣasa Asiŋ mara riŋ patapan,ndya ta ya kawismayanta ri si rāǥawa hīnaguṇa*5:86:388*

ndak ajar-ajaṙ kitāri Ikanaŋ ratu śakti tĕmĕn,hana ri parākramanya ya dumèḥnya manĕmwa suka,sahana nikaŋ jagattraya taman hana moli riya,ya ta Ikahĕn si rāwaṇa ṅaranya yatéki ḍatĕŋ*5:87:389*

Aku ta jayèŋ surālaya manuṣya carācara lèn,Ikana ƀaṭāra wꜽśrawaṇa sāmpun alaḥ sinukū,yama ya maminta jīwita Alaḥ matakut pĕjaha,surapati saŋ hyaṅ indra ya ta ƀakti kabèḥ praṇata*5:88:390*

kadi ta karĕm rikaŋ tasik ikaŋ suraloka kabèḥ,paḍa mawĕnĕs kagöman asamun sahananya maruk,hana nikanaŋ praƀāwa ni si rāwaṇa tulya riwut,ya ta katakut nikaŋ sura dumèḥnya masor arusak*5:89:391*

#saṭ saṙggaḥ#
<waṅśasŧa>:6
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
^6/1/392.
Ikā kaḍatwanku samīpa niŋ tasik,gahan ri lĕṅkā kadi kānti niŋ wulan,I ratnapārāyaṇa nāma tan kalèn,ri dényan akwèḥ maṇiratna yojwala*6:1:392*

ya tékanānuŋ kawaśākĕnanta ya,mamuktya lāwan Aku haywa saṅśaya,Asiŋ sakahyunta hanā ta yériya,kawīt ta kĕmbaŋ haḍaṅĕn saménaka*6:2:393*

sayogya sampat Ika liṅku kāsiha,ṅhulun sĕḍĕŋ yowana śaktimānta ya,Awakta saśrī yuwatī sĕḍĕŋ hayu,si rāma tātaṙ paguṇāri tāryakĕn*6:3:394*

paṅan-n-inum saṅgama yéka ƀuktinĕn,ṅhulun hulun tulya manĕmbahé kita,tadĕg ri lĕṅkā nda huwus ta liṅkwari,Awakta yékā hyasi wèhĕn adyana*6:4:395*

Ujaṙ niraŋ rāwaṇa yaṙ panomaha,sitā tan aṅgā humĕnĕŋ taman sahuṙ
daśāsya sakrođa masö sirāṅgyakĕn,sitā pinuṇḍut nira śīǥra maŋlayaŋ*6:5:396*

gĕlāna dèwī janakātmajānaṅis,masū masāmbat karĕṅö rikaŋ laṅit,kidaŋ manuk riŋ patapan paḍomĕnéŋ,kagömanānon riṅ ulaḥ samaṅkana*6:6:397*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
Ꜽ rāma hé rāǥawa niṙǥrĕṇanta wèḥ,lukan kĕtékā tan asiḥ ta ri ṅhulun,Asiŋ pakon taṙ dadi laṅǥanā Ataḥ,waliṅku siḥ té ry-aku haḥ lalis kariḥ*6:7:398*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
lanā marīntoṣa kitāṅiriŋ manaḥ,widagda riŋ citta mariŋ Anākĕbi,Asiŋ sakahyunku dinadyakĕnta ya,ṅhulun n-atékīnuguṅan kināsihan*6:8:399*

samaṅkanāriṅku si lakṣmaṇottama,Ah-o mahāprajña rikaŋ nayèṅgita,Ujaṙ jugākās kadi śabda niŋ wihaŋ,hatinta māsiḥ takarin tĕmĕn-tĕmĕn*6:9:400*

kṣamākĕnôjaṙkwi kitāri lakṣmaṇa,Ayogya tātan parĕṅönta yāhala,swaƀāwa niŋ strī juga niṙwiwéka ya,kalotakĕn haywa kitāgĕlĕŋ ry-aku*6:10:401*

kakanta saŋ rāma lukan lalis nira,parintuṣāsiḥ sapakonku taṙ wihaŋ,kitāt wihaŋ ṅūni sakèṅ asiḥ kariḥ,ṅhulun Ataḥ pātaka nīca kaśmala*6:11:402*

piré kađīrān ira saŋ mahāṙdđika,rĕṅö wuwus niŋ kala mūr ataḥ sira,mataŋnya yuktīka ta dènta taṙ salaḥ,saké kaḍuṣṭan ni wuwusku mūṙ kita*6:12:403*

Ikāpi saŋ sajjana yan winèh ujar,gĕlĕŋ nirèŋ wwaŋ sapĕtik tamaṙ lanā,tinon irékaŋ kala duḥka kāsyasiḥ,Amoǥa māsiḥ Umasö sirānuluŋ*6:13:404*

mataŋnya hé lakṣmaṇa sāđu sajjana,tasö tuluṅtāku gĕlāna duḥkita,Ikā wuwustānapaŧé lukan tuhu,nihan ṅhulun wèḥ tinawan nikaŋ musuḥ*6:14:405*

nahan pasāmbat janakātmajāṙ pawū,humuŋ sirāminta tuluŋ masāmbatan,jaṭāyu kāwit sira marĕṅö taṅis,mĕsat siraṙ ton sira saŋ daśānana*6:15:406*

daśānanātyanta rikaŋ kalāđama,musuḥ niraŋ tāpasa mūṙkꝁa sāhasa,wĕnaŋ masampay pariƀūta riŋ wiku,tasö huwus yan tuhu wīra riŋ raṇa*6:16:407*

Ikāpi saŋ rāǥawa māsih iŋ wiku,ya sātwikāsiḥ tuwi ƀakti riŋ bapa,wĕnaŋ pwa ko sāhasa đik kalāđama,lukan tan éraŋ lumarèŋ mahāṙdđika*6:17:408*

jaṭāyu yékī ta ƀaṭāra ƀāskara,Umatyanaŋ mūṙkꝁa kabèḥ tamomaya,patik-patik saŋ raguputra tékihĕn,rĕṇāku ṅūnin pakamitra saŋ bapa*6:18:409*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
nāhan liŋ nira saŋ jaṭāyu Umasö masyaŋ humuŋ syāpraṅa,kumlab téka hĕlaṙ nirādƀuta makas malwā malaṇḍĕp kabèḥ,śāṙddūlākrĕti siṅhatulya magalak śīǥrāmarĕk sāhasa,tuṇḍāǥāta patuk nirāyuđa nirālaṇḍĕp ya bajropama*6:19:410*

yékān sāhasa saŋ daśānana r-unus taŋ candrahāsākilat,haṙṣāmbĕk nira saŋ jaṭāyu maṅĕpö rodran panampyal muꝁa,munduṙ yatna siromilag Inayatan riŋ candrahāsomĕsat,Āścaṙyyèkana saŋ daśānana mulat tĕṅhā jaṭāywī ruhur*6:20:411*

Umyus téka hĕlaṙ nirāṙ papagakĕn saŋ rāwaṇāṙ tuṅkuli,sakrođāṙ pamatuk-patuknya kapĕtĕk māṙ bāhu saŋ rāwaṇa,muñcaṙ taŋ rudirār isĕp ta ya muwaḥ munduṙ mĕsat riŋ laṅit,maṅkin daṙppa sirāwĕrö minum ikā rāḥ-rāḥ niraŋ rāwaṇa*6:21:412*

képwan saŋ daśawaktra soṙ sira sukĕṙ suṅgwī siraŋ mꜽŧilī,sambé taŋ bala rākṣasāṅhabĕt ikaŋ Aśwomibĕṙ taŋ raŧa,yèkoṅgwan n-ira maŋlayaŋ kuda manogāmī masö maŋdĕmak,śīṙṇnāsāk rinĕmĕk rĕmuk kinĕpĕkan rĕmpak tibā taŋ raŧa*6:22:413*

saŋ sītā sira muṅgu riŋ raŧa tibā ūmrĕm sawèt niŋ takut,mūṙccā riŋ gaganāntarāla maṅĕliḥ mosaḥ gĕlānomĕhaḥ,miṅsoṙ śīǥra siraŋ jaṭāyu sumuyug sāmbut ta saŋ mꜽŧilī,mahyā taŋ daśadéśadéwata humuŋ kapwādƀutāṅastuti*6:23:414*

pahyā niŋ surasaṅǥadéwata lawan ganđaṙwwa kapwāmuji,héwa krođa siraŋ daśānana nanā maṅkĕp tikaŋ bāhu mār,lāwan rāḥnya nirantaromĕtu humīs ndā tan hiḍĕp yālara,maṅsö sāhasikāṅusī mabayaṅan méraŋ jaṭaywaṙ layū*6:24:415*

saŋ sītā pinĕkul nirāṙdđa kapati glānāsi mosaḥ sira,tan mādrĕs ta Ibĕṙ nirāṙdđa malimĕṙ mamriḥ Alaḥ kabwatan,yan taṙ sāmbuta saŋ naréndratanayā byaktān pĕjaḥ yan tibā,yékā hétu niraŋ jaṭāyu malimĕṙ tébĕṙ nirāṅkin malon*6:25:416*

mĕḥ prāptā ta siraŋ daśānana maṅèl maṅliḥ jaṭāyūmĕhāḥ,mosaḥ mosyan asiŋ paran Ira tinūt dé saŋ daśāsyèŋ laṅit,tan dwān tandaṅi saŋ jaṭāyu dumilaḥ taŋ candrahāsākilat,sĕmpal taŋ lahuyaŋ huyuŋ nira tibān pinraŋ niraŋ rāwaṇa*6:26:417*

{puṣpitāgra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
daśawadana wawaŋ siromĕkul saŋ,janakasutāṙ wiparīta tībra mūṙccā,hana ta raŧa wanèḥ masö manuŋsuŋ,pinakahawan Ira yaṙ Uliḥ ri lĕṅkā*6:27:418*

{mālinī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
satĕka nira ri lĕṅkā glāna kāmāturāhyun,hana ri hati nirāṅhiŋ mꜽŧilī ūṣađātaḥ,winaliṅ ira Umaṅgā jānakī rājaputrī,dadi ta sira Umaṅsö wèt nikaŋ rāga tībra*6:28:419*

sahana-hana nikaŋ wwil wīra yékā kinonkon,Umiṅĕtakĕna saŋ śrī rāmaƀadrāṙ makiṅkiŋ,Alah awĕdi ri dényan śīṙṇna taŋ rākṣasākwèḥ,daśawadana sirādwāhĕnti wadwā nirākraḥ*6:29:420*

ri laku nikana taŋ wwil cāra yāmratyawékṣa,dadi ta sira sumomaḥ jānakī ndā tan aṅga,tinudiṅan i-kiwān lèn taṙ winèḥ śabda ménak,daśamuꝁa sira mūṙkkātyanta maṅsö tan éraŋ*6:30:421*

pratidina sira mojaṙ ndan mahāsatya dèwi,raǥutanaya cinittā dé nikaŋ citta tan lèn,salahasa sira mosaḥ saŋ daśāsyāsi maswī,r-ujari bala nirāṙ kon jānakī rākṣa-rākṣan*6:31:422*

Aŧa ri hana niraŋ śrī jānakī ṅkā ri lĕṅkā,raǥutanaya sirékātyanta saṇḍéha Āśa,marahakĕna hilaŋ saŋ jānakī duṙnimitta,manuk umuni masambat lwiṙnya maṅsö manuŋsuŋ*6:32:423*

daśaraŧasuta tībra glāna maṅliḥ makiṅkiŋ,janakatanaya haḥ Āḥ ƀāgya tékin katĕmwa,mati pinaṅan ikaŋ moŋ mwaŋ tibā riŋ juraŋ lwaḥ,capala ta kunaṅ oṅsil haḥ lukan kāsyasiḥnya*6:33:424*

sĕḍĕṅ aṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn saŋ rāǥawa ƀrāntacitta,tĕka ta sira saṅ antĕn ndān ikaŋ wéṣa rūkṣa,makin alara sirāṙ ton wéṣa saŋ lakṣmaṇoruk,niyata pati nikā saŋ mꜽŧilī liŋ nirāśā*6:34:425*

dadi ta sira matakwan śīǥra mojaṙ saṅ antĕn,duga-duga sira mājaṙ satya ƀaktīŋ kakāsiḥ,raǥutanaya gĕlānān paŋ­rĕṅö wrötamātra,hati nira ya ta śiṙṇnān śūnya taŋ rāt hiḍĕpnya*6:35:426*

kadi ta hilaṅ umĕtwaŋ jīwa saṅké śarīra,mamana-mana sirāṅhèl dé ni kiṅkiŋ nirākwèḥ,Alah umaṅĕn-aṅĕn saŋ jānakī citta luṅhā,satata ri pipi yan hīs luḥ nirādrĕs tan ampĕt*6:36:427*

Ari janakasutā ndī déśa Uṅgwanta tājar,sahuri Aku gĕlānāsyaŋ-syaṅ aswī masāmbat,pijĕr amupu sĕkaṙ kwèḥ nā mataŋnyāt tan aṅsö,Aŧawa milu maṅajyāṅrĕṅwakĕn đaṙmmaśāstra*6:37:428*

syapa ta kunaṅ ikānuŋ takwanaṅkwé wĕkasta,wruha ta ri Amĕṅantānuŋ satorasya mojar,bapa ta-taṅisanaṅkwébuṅku yādoḥ taman wruḥ,suragaṇa humĕnĕŋ đik déwatā tan hanojar*6:38:429*

Atiśaya Aku yatnāmèt kitèŋ déśa mamriḥ,mara haku ri paturw-Antèŋ daṅū tat kapaṅguḥ,hana watu maratālwa ṅkāk paromèt kitātaḥ,sahana ni hawalantāku k-parāmèt kitāntĕn*6:39:430*

masuk aku riṅ alas göŋ lèn pamètanta kĕmbaŋ,katĕmu kusuma lumrā kīṙṇna laywan rurū kwèḥ,saka ri panas ikaŋ wé kapwa lūm yātirūkṣa,kadi saka ri laranyān tat hanākūŋ ya māśā*6:40:431*

kusuma saꝑala dibyāsiḥnya tībré kitāntĕn,Atiśaya kari kiṅkiŋnyāṙ kasaḥ dènta monĕŋ,Aku kalana ta kāsiḥ puṣpa tātan paḍé ya,taya kita tuwi dèwī tan pĕjaḥ dényunĕṅku*6:41:432*

Apa kita mamarīkṣā donta mĕṅgĕp Umiṅgat,prahasana ta kunaŋ don iŋ humöt guywa-guywan,wĕtu ta rari huwus hé tan wruh iŋ śoka monĕŋ,biṣama tiki huripkun tūta miṅgat pwa dènta*6:42:433*

Aku mulih umatīkaŋ rākṣasa krūrakaṙmma,Apa kita tat anuŋsuŋ kolakĕntāku dèwī,Aparan ikana dosaṅkwī kitaŋ toḥ pwa tājar,lalu kita lumaré ṅwaŋ ƀakti māsiḥ pwa nitya*6:43:434*

giri gahana gunuŋ ndin takwanaṅkwé wĕkasta,lalu talib i-gĕlĕṅtāmoǥa héwāntat aṅliŋ,hilaṅ ikana kađīrankwāpasaḥ sakya dènta,kadi dinudutakĕn mĕḥ mĕtwa jīwaṅku luṅhā*6:44:435*

Aku manaṅis aböḥ mèḥ mĕtwa rāḥ niŋ matābaŋ,satata Aku masāmbat tan katoliḥ pwa dènta,yan ahuwusana k-āsiḥ tāri maryāku monĕŋ,kita tamat awaraḥ riŋ karya luṅhā tat amwīt*6:45:436*

tuwi Ikana Arintā lakṣmaṇékāna tan wruḥ,wruha rikana gĕlĕṅtātyanta sūkṣmanya mèwĕḥ,hana kari magĕlĕŋ riŋ swāmi tātaṙ padoṣa,Atiśaya kita sađwācāra śīlanta liṅku*6:46:437*

Umara Aku maniñjo ṅkā ri pahyas-hyasanta,hana ta ya wulakan lèn pañcuran ṅkākwaniñjo,katĕmu ta pasiwontékīŋ daṅū ṅkā tamolaḥ,Aku malara kapūhan dénya tan ton hana ṅkā*6:47:438*

nahan ikana taṅis saŋ rāmabađrātimūṙcꞓā,kapati kadi tinunwan dé nikaŋ śokabahni,pawana sumirir alwan tisnya tātan ya tamba,biṣa miṣani ya maṅdé mohita ṅwaŋ ta dénya*6:48:439*

krama mawuṅu sirāṅliḥ pér ikaŋ luḥ ya mādrĕs,lumaku ta sira madyus tuṅga-tuṅgal sirākūŋ,Alara tuwi makiṅkiŋ tan hilaŋ déwa pūjā,prakrĕti juga pajātyan saŋ mahāsatwa satya*6:49:440*

tĕlas ajapa mamūjāṅaṙccanèŋ hyaŋ masanđyā,laku ta muwah umèt saŋ jānakī riŋ Alas göŋ,katĕmu ta palagan saŋ rāwaṇa mwaŋ jaṭāyu,hati nira sawitaṙkkān ton ikaŋ cihna niŋ praŋ*6:50:441*

Ari taruṇa sumitrāsūta taṅsö ya tonton,Ahalĕpan iki mapraŋ rākṣasa ṅké ta ṅūni,ruđira ya tumibābāŋ bāhu sĕmpal katimpal,kawaca raŧa nihan taŋ tuṅgaṅan kapwa śīṙṇna*6:51:442*

ndak iṅĕt-iṅĕt ikāntĕn yan mapékā ya mapraŋ,susupi Ikanaṅ ālas mèt ikaŋ rākṣasa ṅké,maluya Ika laraṅkun ton ikaŋ rāḥ ya lumra,Alĕmĕh aku humèt saŋ jānakī liŋ nirāśā*6:52:443*

manuk apa kunĕṅ apraŋ hāḥ lukan kadƀutanya,lahuyaṅ atiśayèŋ göŋ cihna nāhan katimpal,Apa pinarĕbutanyān tan patrĕṣṇèŋ huripnya,harĕpa kunĕṅ ikā saŋ jānakī donya tan lèn*6:53:444*

nahan ikana wuwus saŋ rāmaƀađrān paṅūha,jwalita kadi tinunwan twas nira krođa muntab,mata nira ya kabāṅan wĕtwakĕn taŋ kađīran,triƀuwana kadi śīṙṇnā dé nirālaḥ saroṣa*6:54:445*

kadi ta sira ƀaṭārâditya maṅkin satéja,makin apupul atambĕḥ wikramotsāha wrĕdđi,Awak apanas ahosaḥ dé nikaŋ krođabahni,raǥusuta kadi siṅhāsiṅhanādātidaṙppa*6:55:446*

syapa ta kunaṅ ikānaŋ wwil wĕnaŋ sāhasa ṅké,rumaƀasa sira saŋ śrī jānakī rājaputrī,Apa kariki si rāmāwĕdya riŋ śatru śakti,mataṅ ika Awamānātyanta nīcanya duṣṭa*6:56:447*

dinakara tuwi soṙ hyaŋ sūṙyya dèḥkwi praƀāwa,giriwaraśata śīṙṇnā sāgarāsāta dèṅku,sahana-hana nikaŋ rāt hĕntya tātan paśéṣa,Uragapati Ulāgöŋ ṅkā ri pātāla śīṙṇnā*6:57:448*

nuni-ṅuni Ikanaŋ wwil hĕntya tātan paśéṣa,đanapati tuwi duḥkā yakṣa ya syūha mātya,Aku ta maliha kālomatyanaŋ kālamrĕtyu,sakala ƀuwana cūṙṇnā ƀūmi dĕṅkun pusus ya*6:58:449*

surawara Awarāṅkwī ṅ-indra mandālpaśakti,gaganatala tan alwā dèṅku wèhĕṅkwahöta,maluya laya Ikaŋ rāt-rātri tulyanya śūnya,Asiṅ-asiṅa ta sāđyān dadya tan dadya madwā*6:59:450*

nahan ikana wuwus saŋ rāǥawāsiṅhanāda,tihaṅakĕn ikanaŋ hrū héwa sakrođa riŋ rāt,prarudita manaṅis saŋ lakṣmaṇāsiḥ manĕmbaḥ,muhutakĕn ikanaŋ rāt mātya tātan padoṣa*6:60:451*

raǥusuta kita miŧyātyanta momo wimoha,wipaŧa ta ya katrĕṣṇantèŋ jagad-gadgadāku,Apa kita kadi médan tan padon dènta māmbĕk,ṅhulun alara gĕlānān ton kitātaḥ salaḥ ton*6:61:452*

gĕlĕṅ i-hati ya tībrātyanta kāmāturāhyun,wwaṅ apa wihikana ṅwaŋ manda maŋdāni citta,takarin atiśayāglis budđi médan pramāda,đrĕti ya ta duluranyān rudđa taŋ rodrabahni*6:62:453*

Apa ta guṇagaṇā niŋ krođa yan tūtananta,ya mataṅ amuharopĕk duṙyyaśèŋ rāt ya pāpa,kalawan ikana taŋ rāt tan hanātaḥ sadoṣa,kita juga wiparīta glāna dé niŋ larāgöŋ*6:63:454*

{śloka}

nāhan taṅguḥ niraṅ antĕn,tuṣṭođāni siraŋ kaka,kapwānusup sirèṅ ālas,Adoḥ saṅka riṅ āśrama*6:64:455*

tatkālān panusup kāliḥ,n-ton jaṭāyu manuk magöŋ,tan byakta téka dé niŋ doḥ,katon kadi gunuŋ magöŋ*6:65:456*

yéki mātī siraŋ sītā,liŋ niraŋ rāma niścaya,r-aṅsö tandaṅi taŋ pakṣi,jaṭāyu mawuwus wawaŋ*6:66:457*

hé rāma hé raǥusuta,haywa sāhasa ri ṅhulun,jaṭāyu tāku tan kālèn,wruḥ tākun jānakīn pinèt*6:67:458*

nā liŋ niraŋ mahāpakṣi,manĕmbaḥ saŋ raǥūttama,siraŋ jaṭāyu kāruṇya,mitra kāsiḥ niraŋ bapa*6:68:459*

sira glāna kanin tībra,taŧāpi mahurip sira,Alaḥ humèṙ siraŋ rāma,saṅka ri drĕḋa niṅ asiḥ*6:69:460*

tĕka pwa sira saŋ rāma,mājaṙ ta sira riŋ musuḥ,huwus mājaṙ pĕjaḥ sira,sawèt niŋ tībra niŋ kanin*6:70:461*

sapĕjaḥ nira mūṙccāśā,saŋ rāma manaṅis sira,hé jaṭāyu mahādibya,wĕnaŋ đāraka riŋ hurip*6:71:462*

śaṅka ry-asiḥ ta mamitra,bapaṅku kalulut tĕmĕn,tumuluy tĕka riŋ putra,Ah-o dibyanta hé kaga*6:72:463*

sĕḍĕṅtāt mahurip ṅūni,bapaṅku mahurip hiḍĕp,ri pĕjaḥta kunĕŋ maṅké,mĕnyāk uwuh-uwuḥ tĕmĕn*6:73:464*

huwus saŋ rāma manaṅis,tunu waṅkay ikaŋ manuk,maśoca ta mawèḥ piṇḍa,muwaḥ luṅhā sirānusup*6:74:465*

hana rākṣasa kāścaṙyya,bāhunya madawī tĕmĕn,malapā mahārĕp māṅsā,ya pinaṅguḥ nirèṅ alas*6:75:466*

musuḥ niŋ satwa yèḥ daṅū,dīṙgǥabāhu ṅaran ikā,ya ta maṅsö sira krūra,r-unus taŋ kadga tīkṣṇa ya*6:76:467*

sāṅsönya rodra yāgalak,pinraŋ nira taṅanya ya,sāmpun pĕgat pwa bāhunya,tibā ta yérikaŋ lĕmaḥ*6:77:468*

maluy ta ya ri jātinya,déwatārūpa yan katon,lumrā téja nikāwaknya,kadi saŋ hyaŋ diwākara*6:78:469*

maprĕśna ya ri saŋ rāma,mamĕpör i-ṅaran ira,lāwan don iŋ masusupan,ya tinakwanakĕn ikā*6:79:470*

satorasi siraŋ rāma,mawaraḥ ri ṅaran n-ira,lawan don iŋ masusupan,sumiliḥ ta sirātakon*6:80:471*

Apa jātinta hé sāđu,kita déwakrĕtin katon,nihan ta pajara wanèḥ,yan kasidđā sadon mami*6:81:472*

yan kapaṅguha saŋ sitā,lawan yan alaha-ŋ musuḥ,nahan takwan iraŋ rāma,dadi mājar-ajaṙ ta ya*6:82:473*

ṅhulun ānak ƀaṭārī śrī,ndan durācāra ta ṅhulun,sĕḍĕŋ kwacaṅkramèŋ swaṙgga,Aṅlaṅkahi mahāmuni*6:83:474*

saṅké gĕlĕŋ niré ṅhulun,manāpa dadya rākṣasa,kitātah antaśāpāṅkwa,Apan putrāku dènta wèḥ*6:84:475*

kunaŋ donta kasidđā ya,saŋ dèwīnta kapaṅguha,tinawan saŋ daśamuꝁa,ri lĕṅkā kahanan nira*6:85:476*

nihan gunuŋ parananta,rĕṣyamūka ṅaran nikā,hana ta wré tĕmu ṅkāna,saŋ sugriwa ṅaran nira*6:86:477*

mahāṙdđika mahāśakti,ndan glāna ta ya duḥkita,ya tékānugrahānanta,kakanya ya ta patyani*6:87:478*

saŋ sugrīwa gĕlānonĕŋ,ri saŋ tārā priyā nira,Inalap dé ni saŋ bāli,bāli atyanta duṣṭa ya*6:88:479*

saŋ sugrīwa sĕḍĕŋ monĕŋ,kadi lĕmbu lanaŋ sira,tan winèḥ maswa rikanaŋ,lĕmbu mānak wahū mĕtu*6:89:480*

mataŋnya hé raǥūputra,paḍa duḥkanta yak hiḍĕp,yan mitrā-ŋ kapi sugrīwa,sahāyāntāt patī musuḥ*6:90:481*

Iké wuwusku tan madwā,satyawākya ṅhulun tĕmĕn,mitrānta-ŋ kapi sugrīwa,niyatālaḥ ni rāwaṇa*6:91:482*

sĕḍĕṅtāt masihériya,Awās ya ƀaktya rī kita,kita gurwa Ikā śisyā,kāṙyyanta towi dadya ya*6:92:483*

pira doha ni kāṙyyanta,katĕmu ta ya dé nikā,tuwi makwèḥ ta wadwānya,wré magöŋ śaktimānta ya*6:93:484*

mataŋnya mitrā sugrīwa,duḥkanya ya hilaṅakĕn,marapwan pamalss dlāha,kitātĕmwa lawan priyā*6:94:485*

nahan ujaṙ nikaŋ déwa,Ikaŋ rākṣasa pūṙwwaka,mĕsat ta yomibĕṙ luṅhā,saŋ rāma manusup muwaḥ*6:95:486*

tinon iraṅ alas rāmya,wwa-wwahan tamalaḥ matöb,hilaŋ lapā nirānton ya,tĕmu taŋ lwaḥ magöŋ suci*6:96:487*

madrĕs hilīnya mahĕniŋ,Umĕntas ta sirādulur,tĕmu ṅ-alas rāmya tĕmĕn,manon ta sira tāpasī*6:97:488*

śawarī téka jātinya,kulit kayu tapiḥ nikā,waṙṇnanyawaknya mahirĕŋ,kadi waṙṇna niṅ añjana*6:98:489*

rūpanya sāđu tañcāla,pragrĕhyapāda tulya ya,wītarāga ya đaṙmmèṣṫa,ꝑalāhāra lanā bratī*6:99:490*

sawulat nira saŋ rāma,hilaŋ tékāna ṅhèl nira,kadibyan iŋ brata magöŋ,mojaṙ ta sira kādƀuta*6:100:491*
