hé tāpasī mahāsāđu,lalu dibyanta mabrata,Aparan lwiṙ ni pūjānta,yat satyèṅ īśwarāṙccaṇa*6:101:492*

pitrĕpūjā kunaŋ nitya,lanāsanđyā kunaŋ kita,yat satya riŋ waca-wacan,lawan carita saŋ wiku*6:102:493*

prastāwa niŋ tapa magöŋ,kāma moha kunaŋ hilaŋ,đīra-bratātwaṅ aguru,nā prakāra nikaŋ tapa*6:103:494*

nā liŋ saŋ rāma maprĕṣṇa,Irikaŋ śawarī bratī,sādarojaṙ ta ya mawèḥ,mađupaṙkka lawan ꝑala*6:104:495*

Om sājña hé kitaŋ rāma,ṅhulun ta magawé tapa,Asiŋ sakawĕnaŋ dèṅku,kasatyanku hĕlĕm-hĕlĕm*6:105:496*

kunaŋ hétuṅku mabrata,maŋhanākĕn kasambégan,Utpatti ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu,luṅhā mara ri pātāla*6:106:497*

kĕna śāpa dé hyaŋ rudra,ri kāla niŋ liṅgodƀāwa,madātĕmahan warāha,makastrī dèwī pātāla*6:107:498*

mijil pwa sira hyaŋ wiṣṇu,makarūpa ta warāha,Umĕgil irikaŋ gunuŋ,Amaṅan hāraka mami*6:108:499*

tĕlasnya maṅkanomati,śawanya tinaḍaḥ mami,ya tikāṅdadyakĕn duḥka,Awak mami nīla waṙṇna*6:109:500*

tāsyasiḥ hé kitaŋ rāma,tusapi muꝁa ni ṅhulun,pūṙṇnā kitāntaśāpāṅkwa,tāryakĕn kléśa ni ṅhulun*6:110:501*

nā liŋ saŋ śawarī bratī,Inusap dé niraŋ rāma,paripūṙṇna siraŋ yogī,gumanti maṅanugrahé*6:111:502*

hé saŋ rāma mahādibya,wiṣṇu sakala yaṙ katon,wĕnaṅ umalapi kléśa,mataŋnya malĕsa ṅhulun*6:112:503*

wānarađipa sugrīwa,ya mitrānta mahāṙdđika,katĕmwa jānakī dénta,nā liŋnya dadi mokṣa ya*6:113:504*

{turagagati}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
rāma lakṣmaṇa muwaḥ sira manusup,riŋ Alas pratita kampa ya karĕṅö,kwèḥ kĕnas riya wisāta ya kasukan,mwaŋ mahāmuni hanèṅ alas anusup*6:114:505*

trĕpti saŋ raǥusutāṙ wulat iṅ alas,rāmya kapwa manĕḍĕŋ kusuma matap,n-ton ikaŋ talaga dibya ya manulus,padma yéka maputiḥ tamalah-alaḥ*6:115:506*

śokacitta sira dénya ta maṅaraŋ,mꜽŧilī sira lanā Inaṅĕn-aṅĕn,wĕtnyunĕŋ nira kunaŋ dadi manaṅis,glāna yaṙ wara-waraḥ ta Ari nira*6:116:507*

lakṣmaṇāri wulati-ŋ talaga maho,ƀūṣaṇanya Uni niŋ ƀramara humuŋ,kokilomuni malon ya salaki-bi,hāḥ mahā juga ya mèdi riṅ apasaḥ*6:117:508*

padma rāmya sumĕkaṙ paḍa manĕḍĕŋ,wintaṅ iŋ gagana soṙ ta hayu nikā,komalanya ya mawèḥ lara ri hati,śoka saŋ priyawiyoga mulati ya*6:118:509*

saŋ sĕḍĕŋ priyasamāgama kasukan,dé nikaŋ ƀramara haṅsa paḍa munī,rāmanīya ya manohara ya mrĕdu,kaṙṇnaśūla ya ri saŋ priyawiraha*6:119:510*

kīṙṇna taŋ kusuma nitya ya marurū,dé nikaŋ manuk i-pādapa masiwo,wwaŋ wimūḋa ta kunaŋ taman alara,mwaŋ ri saŋ tan aharĕp suka wirati*6:120:511*

ganđa niŋ sĕkar arūm mara riṅ iruŋ,mwaŋ manuknya lumaré taliṅa muni,rūpa niŋ kusuma yānakiti hati,hāḥ ṅ-anaṅga mamanaḥ mamarimisi*6:121:512*

mwaŋ Ikaŋ kayu kabèḥ paḍa mamanaḥ,ronya yāpĕs alaris ya taji tajĕm,pāŋnya yéka larasanya ya malurus,wruḥnya yan tuju hatiṅku kĕna rujit*6:122:513*

mandamāruta miriṙ ya maṅiriri,wāsitanya waṅi niŋ wana kusuma,citta yāpuy umurub tĕhĕr apanas,hāḥ lukan lara nikiŋ priyawiraha*6:123:514*

cāla ron ikana taŋ kayu tumayuŋ,yoṅgwaniŋ bun aputiḥ makatiritis,mutyahāra juga riŋ gaganatala,n-ton ikā drawa hatiṅku juga tĕñuḥ*6:124:515*

hāḥ kapan kunaṅ iké kahuwusana,mukti duḥka nikanaŋ priyawiraha,kālamrĕtyu malalis tan anumata,tan patīn aku huwus kasula-sula*6:125:516*

śabda niŋ ƀramara matta ya Apuya,yak rĕṅö ya mahuyaŋ hati mapanas,tulya paṙbwata sĕḍĕŋ matunu murub,tan hanāta śaraṇāṅkwa manuluṅa*6:126:517*

moǥa mohita hatiṅku ya wulaṅun,n-ton alas ya manĕḍĕŋ masĕkar arūm,pomahan niraṅ anaṅga juga katon,yak pramāda kasasaṙ ta kunĕṅ ari*6:127:518*

paŋ nikaŋ kayu tinūb niṅ aṅin alon,naṙttakī ya maṅigĕl kayu mamijaḥ,daṙppa taŋ ƀramara matta maṅiduṅi,wètnyunĕṅku baribin n-aku kabaran*6:128:519*

nā taṅis nira saṅ āṙyya raǥusuta,sanđi tībra maṅĕliḥ hati wipayoḥ,rĕṣyamūka giri ƀīṣaṇa masukĕt,nā paran nira saśoka masusupan*6:129:520*

{basantatilaka}
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :14:
tatkāla yaṙ tĕka rikaŋ giri rĕṣyamūka,sugrīwa śoka sira tībra maṅön akiṅkiŋ,saŋ rāmaƀadra śaraṇā wĕgilĕṅkwa tan lèn,nā liŋ nirān laku manāsaka śīǥra maṅkat*6:130:521*

tāmoli riŋ malaya paṙbwata duṙggamāwān,yékā paran nira lawan bala wānarākwèḥ,ƀaktinya mapraƀu dumèḥ ya kabèḥ tumūta,sugrīwa sāđu tuwi yogya siwin hiḍĕpnya*6:131:522*

sāmpun ḍatĕŋ dadi kinon ta siraŋ hanūmān,dūtomarā ri sira saŋ raǥuputra pètĕn,tātaṙ wihaŋ pawanaputra kinon lumakwa,yékan pĕsat nira rikaŋ gaganāntarāla*6:132:523*

riŋ rĕṣyamūka dunuṅĕn n-ira śīǥra mādrĕs,humyus mĕsĕs Aṅin-aṅin n-ira bāyubajra,śīṙṇnékanaŋ kayu katūb mananā kabèḥ rūg,sĕmpal papal kaparapal kapupuḥ pukaḥ puḥ*6:133:524*

praptomasuk sira rikaŋ giri rĕṣyamūka,mĕṅgĕp mahātma sira sidđa sakāma-kāma,n-ton téka saŋ raǥusutāsusupan ƀramanta,maṅsö ta saŋ pawanaputra wawaŋ ta mojar*6:134:525*

hé sāđu dibya kita đīra wĕnaŋ marā ṅké,Atyanta duṙggama nikiŋ giri rĕṣyamūka,saŋ hyaŋ mahéśwara tuwin malĕmĕḥ marā ṅké,ndyānuŋ prayojana Iké panusupta kāliḥ*6:135:526*

lwiṙ niŋ ƀayātiśaya rodra Anuŋ hana ṅké,muṅgwiŋ guhām hana ta rākṣasa lèn piśāca,lāwan paran kari hawanta sukĕt t-agamya,wwaŋ lén saké kita taman hana wèḥ mara ṅké*6:136:527*

kwèḥ siṅha sāhasa musuḥ niṅ asiŋ marā ṅké,krūrāṅawit ya mawiṅit muruṅūtikaŋ moŋ,maṅgā Umuṅgah irikaŋ giri duṙggamāwān,wuṅkal galintuṅ agaliŋ gumuliŋ Iṅambaḥ*6:137:528*

malwā malok pĕluk ikaŋ lwah aluṅka-luṅka,molĕk ya kolĕk akĕlĕm kumĕlĕm Umĕntas,tambiŋ katambiṅ iṅ adoḥ ya tĕbĕŋ kahambĕŋ,dé niŋ mahāgaja lanā mara daṙppa madyus*6:138:529*

makwèh anuŋ ƀaya nikaŋ giri ƀīṣaṇa nké,lāwan śilātala tĕlanya malā Ulānya,moŋ māṅsaƀakṣa kaharĕpnya humöŋ galaknya,tan wismayan paṅĕbusan mamisan wiṣanya*6:139:530*

nā liŋ niraŋ pawanaputra masö matakwan,mojaṙ ta saŋ raǥusutāṙ pawaraḥ rikaŋ don,Ꜽ Āṙyya don mami nihan ta rĕṅö tat aṅsö,mwaŋ hétu niŋ malarasan ya ta pājaraṅkwa*6:140:531*

kyātīŋ sarāt daśaraŧa praƀu sarwaƀoga,salwiṙ nikaŋ suka wiśéṣa hané sirākwèḥ,Akwèh anak nira Ariṅku ya dibyaśakti,Aṅhiŋ ṅhuluñ juga Anak nira mandaƀāgya*6:141:532*

saṅké pakon ira marā riṅ alas malaṅǥya,yékā nimitta mami yan panusup ya kāliḥ,luṅhā mĕgil kami riṅ āśrama saŋ sutīkṣṇa,ṅkā tā tamolah aṅĕmit patapan prayatna*6:142:533*

sītā priyāṅku rasikā ta duluṙkwi ṅūni,ndan duṣṭa rāwaṇa malap sira śīǥra luṅhā,sītā sirékana pinèt mami kām para ṅké,nā hétu niŋ masusupan n-umahas ƀramanta*6:143:534*

nojaṙ niraŋ raǥusutāṙ pawaraḥ rikaŋ don,mājaṙ-Ajaṙ ta sumiliḥ ta siraŋ hanūmān,Ꜽ rāǥawa ṅhulun iké ta kinon marā ṅké,sugrīwanāma kapirāja makon amèta*6:144:535*

prastāwa yéka huniṅan hana wānarāgöŋ,śaktinya taṙ papaḍa śūra ṅaranya bālī,Āditya soṙ ta sira dé nikanāŋ praƀāwa,krođāgalak ya pariƀūta riké tuhanku*6:145:536*

saṅké takut nira ri saŋ kapirāja bālī,miṅgat siromara rikaŋ malaya pradéśa,maprītya don ira makon ta siromarā ṅké,mahyun tamolaha sumiwya sukunta nāŧa*6:146:537*

mitrānta yogya sira liṅku Anugrahāna,Āpan mahābala mahāṙdđika sāđubudđi,tūtūta māsiha mituhwa Asiŋ pakonta,milwomatī daśamuꝁa pramuꝁā sirèŋ praŋ*6:147:538*

nāhan Ujaṙ nira ta saŋ Anilātmajaswī,tātaṙ wihaŋ daśaraŧātmaja śīǥra maṅkat,sāṅkat nirātiśaya haṙṣa ta saŋ hanūmān,saŋ rāmadéwa hiniḍĕp nira kalpawrĕkṣa*6:148:539*

praptèŋ gunuŋ malaya saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma,rĕŋrĕŋ paḍām nira panaḥ nira yéka méǥa,bālī diwākara samopaśamāmatī ya,sugrīwa yéka mapanas ya maṅöb ikaŋ hrū*6:149:540*

tatkāla yaṙ patĕmu kālih amoŋ sirāpuy,sākṣyā nirān praŧama tambayaniŋ pamitra,sāmpun nirāsamaya kapwa sahaṙṣa kāliḥ,māṅĕn-n-aṅĕn ta sira kapwa mamèt upāya*6:150:541*

saŋ rāmadéwa mulat iŋ bala wānarākwèḥ,swécꞓā yaŧāsuka Ulaḥnya sajāti moṅsil,polaḥnya hūŋnya gumuruḥ maturū rikaŋ pāŋ,yékā dumèḥ nira sukā magiraŋ tumon ya*6:151:542*

sāmpun tĕguḥ rika pamitra nirāta kāliḥ,mojaṙ ta saŋ prawara wānararāja mitra,hé rāǥawātiśaya śakti nikaŋ kapīndra,bālī taman hana paḍanya rikaŋ triloka*6:152:543*

tan saṅka riŋ pariƀawéki wuwusku nāŧa,dényāt samitra ya dumèḥ ṅhulun ājarātaḥ,kabwat t-ikān pinuji śakti nikā si bālī,byaktān pĕjaḥnya tuwi dé ni panaḥta śakti*6:153:544*

nyānuŋ dumèḥ nika manĕmwa wiśéṣa riŋ rāt,saṅkĕŋ Anugraha niraŋ muni ṅūni māsiḥ,maṅkin ya śakti wĕkasan n-aniwāṙyya wīṙyya,sūṙyyopamanya rikanaŋ musuh anđakāra*6:154:545*

glāna ṅhulun mawĕdi dénya tumon ya śakti,tātan maṅĕn-n-aṅĕn i-kāpĕjahanya ṅūni,maṅké ḍatĕŋ pwa kita nāŧa Amoǥaśakti,cittaṅku niśꞓaya Awās ya patinya dènta*6:155:546*

bālī ya lāgi mamatī manikĕp gajéndra,rĕmpak-rĕmuk satinĕpaknya gunuŋ pasèwu,śatru hyaṅ indra mahiṣāsura śīṙṇna dénya,ndan byakta yan pĕjaha dènta rikaŋ raṇāṅga*6:156:547*

nā liŋ niromara-maraḥ nrĕpaputra rāma,saṅké takut nira ri saŋ kaka śaktimānta,mahyun sirāwruha ri śakti saṅ āṙyya rāma,prajñā siraŋ raǥusutāṙ pamanaḥ ta-tal trus*6:157:548*

kwèḥnyātatā pitu katūb tumuluy Ikaŋ hrū,sugrīwa kādƀuta sahaṙṣa tumon ikaŋ tal,maṅkat siraṙ pakaduluṙ nrĕpaputra rāma,kiṣkiṇḍa yékana parāna lumakwa maṅdon*6:158:549*

sugrīwa yajña gawayĕn nira riŋ raṇāṅga,bālī kĕbo ya wunuhan kaharan pamūjā,saŋ Āṙyya rāǥawa siréka kinon mayajñā,tārā sirāƀyudaya ƀoga ꝑalanya ƀuktin*6:159:550*

{śiꝁariṇī}
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
saluṅhā saŋ rāmāṙ laku mara ri kiṣkiṇḋa wiwara,lawan saŋ sugrīwātiraƀasa sahāsaŋ kinasigan,katon taŋ lyaŋ malwām giriwara guhā ǥora madalĕm,kaḍatwan saŋ bālī pratiƀaya lawaŋnyādƀuta pĕtĕŋ*6:160:551*

siraŋ sugrīwāgyāsyaṅ i-kaka niromĕtwa malagā,humuŋ makrak krūra ƀrukuṭi-kuṭilāhyā sira ri hèŋ,Umaṅkat saŋ bālī mĕtu ta sira saṅkèŋ giri guhā,malĕs makrak pūṙṇnāŋ gaganatala digdéśa hibĕkan*6:161:552*

humuŋ hūmrĕŋ maṅsö ta sira kadi ta wyāǥra magalak,lawan saŋ sugrīwogratara kadi siṅhāṅrĕpa maṅaŋ,masö madwandwāprĕp magarut asahut kapwa manikĕp,manampyal maŋ­rĕṅgut paḍa ta sira gut-gūtĕn abutĕŋ*6:162:553*

rumukrūk taŋ rambut ginĕrĕmus umuṅgwiŋ palipisan,miṅis méṅas méṅā paḍa ta kapaluḥ lud maṅĕsĕsan,humis mamwas taŋ rāḥ drawa ya mapisan syuknya ri pipi,tibā riŋ bāhwalwā ri ḍaḍa kaharan kumkuma mabāŋ*6:163:554*

makin daṙppān pāprĕp ta maṅuwil iruŋ riŋ kuku makas,manimprut rodrādrĕs paḍa kasidĕkuŋ maŋdudut ikū,hanan pāmrĕp jaṅgut paḍa kapisahut huntwa maṅani,Anèkārūpékaŋ kira-kira ya kapwāṅutitakĕn*6:164:555*

saka kwèḥ saŋ yogī matapa tĕpi niŋ paṙbwata kabèḥ,manonton tan kāntun hyaṅ anak aduluṙ kapwa sabatĕk,mahās māmèt kĕmbaŋ mari ya sakarĕŋ kapwa ya milu,siraŋ monāmomo mari muna manonton paḍa humuŋ*6:165:556*

pijĕṙ saŋ rāmāṙ ton ta sira mataruŋ kapwa ta bĕtaḥ,tatan wruḥ riŋ bālī paḍa-paḍa ta sugrīwa juga ya,kalépyan saŋ rāmāṙ miṅĕt-iṅĕtakĕn maṅkin alupa,wuruŋ tékaŋ tāṅan tumihaṅ apatan wruḥ riṅ uliha*6:166:557*

siraŋ sugrīwāṅliḥ tuwi kalalah aṅhèṙ sira tĕkā,Awak rĕñcĕm tāmbis mati sira gĕlānāṙ pinipitan,dudut tékā tĕṇḍas nira tuwi tinuṇḍĕs hinapitan,Umunduṙ méraŋ kapwa malara siroruk mamuruṅut*6:167:558*

mulat saŋ rāma ṙ-ton ta sira tĕka rūkṣāṙdđa mawĕnĕs,masö śīǥrānĕmbaḥ ta ri suku niraŋ rāmawijaya,Ah-o swāmī miŧyāsamaya kita hāḥ madwa riṅ ujar,ndya hétunyāt tonton palaga mami tātan lĕkasi ya*6:168:559*

wawaŋ mojaṙ saŋ śrī raǥusuta ri saŋ wānarapati,nihan prastāwanyān kadi ta nirapékṣāku humĕnĕŋ,sĕḍĕŋ tāprĕp tonton kita sadrĕśa rūpanta ya paḍa,rikaŋ bālī tak wruḥ ri kita tuwi maṅkin tak atutur*6:169:560*

nahan prastāwanyāk kadi malupa riŋ mitrasamaya,kunĕŋ topāyāntāsawita kita roṇḍon tĕṅĕrana,huwus tācihnā toḥ palaga ta muwaḥ haywa mawĕdi,Ikaŋ bālī yātaḥ pĕjaha kita tan dadya pi kĕna*6:170:561*

nahan liŋ saŋ rāmāsawiti sira roṇḍon ta riṅ alas,maluy maṅsö taŋtaŋ kaka nira ta bālī mapuliha,tumandaŋ saŋ bālī maluy apĕluk amriḥ ta manikĕp,mamöṅpöŋ saŋ rāmāṙ tuju ta sira riŋ hrū kĕna pisan*6:171:562*

{Upajāti bajra}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
bālī tibā wānara wāṇḍawāwu,manaḥnya mènĕḥ manĕhĕṙ ta yomūr,manaṅhulun kapwa manaŋ wanèhan,đik rāma liŋ saŋ muni mona moni*6:172:563*

gĕlāna saŋ wānararāja bālī,trus tékana pyaḥ nira dé nikaŋ hrū,suđīra tāmbĕk nira śūra sāđu,r-uman-Uman saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma*6:173:564*

hāḥ rāma ḍuṙttāđama đik wimūḋa,wéśanta śāntātiśayèŋ kaṭuṅka,salwiṙ nikaŋ pāpa magöŋ tĕmunta,Apat panaḥ mapraṅ ataḥ nda tan lèn*6:174:565*

Ah-o durācāra taman pahīṅan,tātan sapékṣāta bapanta sāđu,doṣaṅku tātan hana wèḥ tinonta,Amoǥa caṇḍāla manaḥta mūṙkꝁa*6:175:566*

lukan kari wruḥ ri bapanta ṅūni,waliṅku tan saṅka ri ko gĕlöṅa,dumèḥ sirākona Umiṅgatādoḥ,saké kaduṣṭanta kunaŋ ya hétu*6:176:567*

jātiṅkwasānak matukāra towi,doṣaṅku sātus giri méru riŋ göṇ,trèṣṇékanojaṙ śiwakĕn pasèwun,tātan pĕgat sānak apan dagiṅku*6:177:568*

ya lèn akun sānaka dibya yāgöŋ,sākāśa lāwan prĕŧiwī ya siḥnya,yan krođamātrāṅdadi mrĕtyu yāwat,tan saṅśayañcrol mamatī yapan lèn*6:178:569*

yan đaṙmma niṅwaŋ ratu śūra sāđu,śudđāmatī śatru kalĕṅka niŋ rāt,kĕmbaŋ ƀaṭārī prĕŧiwī ya pūta,tatan salaḥ pakṣa kawrĕdđyan iŋ rāt*6:179:570*

yan kéwalaŋ paṇḍita tūtananta,đaṙmmottamāgurwa nikiŋ kaniṣṭa,tambī niṅ oruk matukaṙ masānak,pantĕs ya toṣāđa mamin salaḥ dé*6:180:571*

tĕkwan pwa pakṣanta kuraŋ wiwéka,suṅguḥ wiśéṣajña tuhun mapuṅguŋ,hétunku niṣprāya tĕkanta sāđu,suṅsaŋ paṅawruḥta ya hiṅsakaṙmma*6:181:572*

lāwan ndya donaṅku kariḥ pinatyan,yan māṅsa kahyunta kunĕŋ Iréku,tuhun watĕk pañcanakā ta ƀakṣan,ndā tan Iluŋ wré tinulak ya ƀakṣan*6:182:573*

lāwan parĕṅwanta daṅū suśīla,wĕnaŋ prajārākṣaka māsih iŋ rāt,yasanta ƀagnéka Apan patī wré,lukan tan éraŋta kari ry-arinta*6:183:574*

lāwan pajātyaṅkwatukaṙ masānak,hĕlĕm-hĕlĕm kapwa maluy Ikātūt,Iké si sugrīwa kināsihanta,wré nīca śīlanya taman sayogya*6:184:575*

bālī nahan liŋ nira mamrihojar,saŋ śrī raǥuwyāǥra malĕs ta mojar,Ꜽ wānarā mĕṅgĕp iké wruh iŋ rāt,Akuk panaḥ ko tak anĕmwa pāpa*6:185:576*

swajāti niŋ kṣatriya nā tinūtku,tan hiṅsa tékin pamatī kĕnas kwèḥ,sakwèḥ niraŋ kṣatriya ṅūni pūṙwwa,siréka tūtĕnkwi taman padoṣa*6:186:577*

lāwan kĕnas jāti nikin pinatyan,pinriḥ linañjak kinalān sinuṅgan,sakwèḥ nikaŋ satwa hanèṅ alas göŋ,suśīla duśśīla wĕnaŋ ya hiṅsan*6:187:578*

kunĕŋ yadin mānuṣa liŋta tan knas,tumūta solaḥ mami jāti nin wwaŋ,taŧāpi tan dadya manĕmwa pāpa,Apak panaḥ ṅwaŋ paradārabudđi*6:188:579*

śīlanta sāmpun karĕṅö pwa dèṅku,sugrīwa yèkā pinasāhakĕnta,tārā ya kāsiḥ rasikénalapta,lanā ninindā kita dé nikaŋ rāt*6:189:580*

nā liŋ niraŋ rāǥawa satyawākya,bālī ya méraŋ humĕnĕŋ katuhwan,katānĕhan maṅkin umaṇḍĕm aṅliḥ,mamriḥ sirānambah aminta matya*6:190:581*

Ꜽ rāǥawātyanta mahāṙdđikanta,matīkasiŋ duṣkrĕta duṣṭa riŋ rāt,kunaŋ ta đaṙmmanta taman pahīṅan,tan ilwa matyātah anakku dènta*6:191:582*

samaṅkanāriṅku tasö para ṅké,sugrīwa mamwīta kakanta matya,kunaŋ ta riŋ janma dĕlāha sowaḥ,đaṙmmā ƀaṭāré kita sānakātaḥ*6:192:583*

mwaŋ tuṅgalātaḥ kahananta kāliḥ,Anuŋ gunuŋ konĕṅ unĕŋ kayunya,ꝑalanya madyanya mađunya wrĕdđi,taṙ hĕntya yad ƀuktya ya riŋ dĕlāha*6:193:584*

Iké Ulaḥ kwāri salaḥ tĕmĕn ya,nda tan sadé yā makadéya-déya,Ukuṙ ƀaṭāréki tukaṙ kwasānak,tādé Apan déwa wiđīki maṅdé*6:194:585*

lāwan nikaŋ déwa Acintya śakti,tan wèḥ kitāntĕn parĕṅān pamuktya,nyā kuk ruhun maṅguhakĕn wiƀūti,paṅdé nikaŋ déwa Ataḥ ya tūti*6:195:586*

nā liŋ niré saŋ Ari wèhakĕn taŋ,kĕmbaŋ Ĕmās riŋ hulu luḥ kumĕmbĕŋ,sāmpun kasimpèn kawawé saṅ antĕn,mūṙcꞓéki nīꞓā ri hurip nirāsiḥ*6:196:587*

soliḥ nirèŋ swaṙgga sawaṙgga yāwrĕg,kadaŋ-kadaŋ yéka masö manambaḥ,sugrīwa tātaṙ lupa riŋ swagotra,sāsiḥ kaḍatwan paṅasiḥ nirāsiḥ*6:197:588*

saṅ aṅgadātaḥ yuwarāja téka,Utus niraŋ rāǥawa hétu niŋ siḥ,samaṅkanékaŋ kapi wanđuwaṙgga,winèḥ dĕmak kapwa yaŧā kramanya*6:198:589*

{mandākrānta}
– – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :17:
ménak tāmbĕk nira lawan ikaŋ wānarātyanta tuṣṭa,kapwā yāṅsö praṇata matatā yaṙ panĕmbaḥ kabèḥnya,mériŋ matwaŋ ta ya ri sira saŋ rāǥawā yaṙ panĕmbaḥ,maṅsö cuṇḍuk ta ri suku niraŋ rāma maṅkin sahaṙṣa*6:199:590*

hāḥ Āḥ nāŧātiśaya ya magöŋ siḥ ta tāman pahīṅan,!
tātaḥ magyā ta ri pamalĕsā ni ṅhulun dlāha sidđā,dényān rĕŋrĕŋ Iki tĕka huwus duṙbbalāŋ wānarātīs,riŋ lahrū ṅkān t-alapa sira saŋ mꜽŧilī śatru śīṙṇnā*6:200:591*

{dođakawrĕtta}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
nā ta wuwus nira saŋ kapirāja,minta kasiḥ ri narāđipa rāma,duṙbbala niŋ bala wānara hétu,saŋ raǥuputra Umom yanumoda*6:201:592*

{tanumađya}
– – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏓ = :6:
sāmpun samayātūt,rĕŋrĕŋ ya ta hèrĕn,sugrīwa manĕmbaḥ,mamwīta misātā*6:202:593*

{mattamayūra}
– – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
sāmpun mamwit śīǥra muliḥ saŋ kapirāja,lāwan wadwā wānara maṅkin ya sahaṙṣa,riŋ kiṣkiṇḍā mukti ta sīraŋ kapirāja*6:203:594*
prāptāŋ rĕŋrĕŋ daṙppa Ikaŋ matta mayūra*6:204:595*

#saptamas saṙggaḥ#
<ratodđata>:7
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
^7/1/594.
ndā tatīta sira saŋ kapipraƀu,ƀukti taŋ wiṣaya niṙƀayaŋ manaḥ,rāma lakṣmaṇa muwaḥ sirānusup,mālyawān gunuṅ agöŋ paran nira*7:1:596*

prāpta saŋ prawara rāǥawèŋ gunuŋ,śokacitta rumaras manaḥ nira,dé nikaŋ Aṅin alon miriṙ tĕka,ḍūta niŋ rĕtu mahāgawé Unĕŋ*7:2:597*

méǥa moǥa mapupul ya riŋ laṅit,ǥora ǥūṙṇnita gĕrĕḥ magĕnturan,tulya kĕṇḍaṅa niraŋ manoƀawa,yan rĕṅö ya rumaras manaḥ nira*7:3:598*

syuk nikaŋ hudan agöŋ nirantara,nā panaḥ nira ƀaṭāra manmaŧa,taṙ kanin tuwi siraŋ raǥūttama,ndan tĕñuḥ hati nirāṙ wulat riya*7:4:599*

Indracāpa ya tinon irèŋ laṅit,lwiṙ nikān kadi rajaḥ tamaḥ katon,yéka laṅkapa niraŋ manoƀawa,yaṙ panaḥ priyawiyoga muṙcꞓita*7:5:600*

nyéka kuntul umuliḥ saké sawaḥ,haṙṣa yādulu-duluṙ paḍāputiḥ,laywa-laywan ira manmaŧā juga,n-ton ikā ta kumĕtĕṙ manaḥ nira*7:6:601*

taṙ katon wĕtu ƀaṭāra ƀāskara,dé nikaŋ jaladawrĕnda riŋ laṅit,yéka budđi nira tīkṣṇa yāṅlimut,dé ni moha nira wèt nikaŋ Unĕŋ*7:7:602*

maṅkin onĕṅ asĕkĕl manaḥ nira,n-ton kilat ya lumarap nirantara,luḥ tibā kabarabas sakiŋ mata,đꜽṙyya niŋ hati tĕñuḥ jugānilī*7:8:603*

taṙ wĕnaŋ tumahĕnékanaŋ taṅis,kaṇṭa gadgada gulū nirāsĕkĕl,mꜽŧilī sira katon na ménaka,nā ta hétu nikanaŋ taṅis mĕtu*7:9:604*

hāḥ samīraṇa miriṙ ya loṙ kidul,rūmnya rāmya sakadamba wāsita,saŋ jitèndriya hanèṅ alas tuwi,byakta monĕṅ ikanāta dé nikā*7:10:605*

mopĕk ambĕk iṅ anon pĕtĕŋ pĕpĕt,Anđakāra tamatan pasiṅkaban,tulya pañjara ƀaṭāra manmaŧa,sūkṣma taṙ pagamĕlan katon tuwi*7:11:606*

nya-ŋ kunaŋ-kunaṅ anaṅgadīpa ya,taṙ paḍĕm paḍa-paḍān kĕḍap-kĕḍap,maŋ­raras-rarasakĕn manaḥ mibĕr,hāḥ manaḥku baribin tumon ikā*7:12:607*

lèn kilat marimisī matāhulap,glāna kagyat aku dénya yan larap,tan lanā pwa ya hilaḥ wawaŋ muwaḥ,hāḥ mahā juga ya médi maŋlaré*7:13:608*

śabda niŋ Apa kunaŋ Ikaŋ gĕlap,ndan tahāṅkw-iriya śabda niŋ laras,kāmadéwa Umanaḥ jagat kabèḥ,nya-ŋ gĕlap Uni nikā panaḥ nira*7:14:609*

byakta manmaŧa sirāmanaḥ jagat,ndan rinambutan ĕmās panaḥ nira,yéka nitya lumarap rikaŋ laṅit,hāḥ manoƀawa lukan tamaṙ maṅèl*7:15:610*

cātakāmuhara kūŋ jugān uni,haṙṣa yan syaṅi Ikā priyānya wèḥ,māṙmmadoḥ ya sakarĕŋ maluy masö,mèdi riŋ madanawédanātura*7:16:611*

nyaŋ-Aṅin ya winaliṅku Oṣađa,śītalātiśaya tīsnya riŋ Awak,ndān apuy juga hiḍĕpku taṙ pahi,śīṙṇna téki hrĕdayaṅku yāgĕsöŋ*7:17:612*

nyā-ŋ mayūra ya Umūra ménaka,moǥa moruk aku dénya yan Uni,wruḥnya yan priyawiyoga duḥkita,mohita ṅwaṅ umawaŋ Unĕŋ magöŋ*7:18:613*

nyā-ŋ hudan tan anumāna riŋ kasaḥ,médi riŋ kinawaśākĕn iŋ lulut,tan pararyan amĕwĕḥ nirantara,hāḥ warĕg Aku huwus rikaŋ lara*7:19:614*

saŋ mahāmuni hanèṅ alas kabèḥ,kölan iŋ daṅu-daṅū tatan lĕgö,wèt nikaŋ diwasa röŋrĕṅ aṅgĕgĕs,mohitā ta sira liṅku taṙ suka*7:20:615*

nyā-ŋ wihuŋ muni lawan manuk humuŋ,tulya mātyana Ikaŋ kĕnèṅ unĕŋ,moni taṙ pahuwusan rikaŋ kulĕm,hāḥ tan éraṅ aṅidīdi maŋlarè*7:21:616*

jānakī mapa kunaŋ laranta wèḥ,tan kasaḥ daṅu-daṅū saké ry-aku,hāḥ Ah-o lalu lalis nikaŋ wiđi,wèḥ kitāri mapasāha-sāhasa*7:22:617*

tībra tékana Unĕṅku tan sipi,duṙbbalālara mataṅku yan wulat,riŋ laṅit Aŧawa riŋ Alas tuwi,kapwa hètu nikanaŋ Unĕŋ kabèḥ*7:23:618*

riŋ kidaŋ katutur iŋ wulat marūm,riŋ liman katutur īŋ Ulaḥ wagĕd,riŋ wulan katutur iŋ muꝁābuṅaḥ,hāḥ hayunta maṅawéśa ri ṅhulun*7:24:619*

wway nikaŋ lwah adalĕm ya cañcala,ṙyyaknya tulya halisanta yañcala,rambutiŋ mrak aṅigĕl ya tākiris,byakta liṅku gĕluṅanta yākila*7:25:620*

haṅsa kapwa ya mibĕṙ ya tāṅalor,ṅkāna riŋ talaga mānasa n-para,wètnyunĕṅku harikā kunĕŋ muni,nā swaranta ri hiḍĕpku tan pahi*7:26:621*

komalāŋ malaya mārutomirir,déwadāru Inarasnya riŋ Alas,rūmnya sumrak umarèṅ iruŋ sumār,tulya ganđa ni pipinta yak hiḍĕp*7:27:622*

kāla niŋ rahina tan makūŋ dahat,kwèḥ tinonku riṅ alas ya lālana,kāla niŋ wĕṅi Ataḥ makūŋ tĕmĕn,taṙ tinonku ta paran nikaŋ manaḥ*7:28:623*

prāṙŧanaṅku wĕṅi yéka méṅgala,nityakāla rahinā kunĕŋ lanā,hāḥ lukan wita gĕlāna ni ṅhulun,yan kaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn ataḥ kitèŋ kulĕm*7:29:624*

O kataṅhi ṅ-alarāṅaraŋ makuŋ,prĕmm-Akĕn kasula tan pijĕṙ pwa wèḥ,tan hanāṅrasa sawèt nikaŋ huyaŋ,hāḥ wiyoga kadurus niroṣađa*7:30:625*

{prĕŧwītala}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
nahan ta ya taṅis nirān hana rikaŋ gunuŋ mālyawān,Ikaŋ wĕṅi tamaṙ kĕjĕp maṅĕn-aṅĕn priyā mꜽŧilī,nirantara sirānaṅis kapati tībra dé niŋ lara,Ah āḥ kadi ta sèwu waṙṣa Ikanaŋ Unĕŋ sakṣaṇa*7:31:626*

nda tātita Ikaŋ ǥanāgama tĕkāŋ śaratkāla wèḥ,wiśudđa malilaŋ laṅit kadi ta budđi saŋ paṇḍita,Ikaŋ jalaḍa tulya moha nira kapwa yāsāk hilaŋ,katon hana ta haṅsa śudđa kadi budđi satwāputiḥ*7:32:627*

mulat ta sira saŋ raǥūttama rikaŋ laṅit niṙmmala,tinon nira ƀaṭāra candra mawĕlū sĕḍĕŋ pūṙṇnama,kadi pwa muꝁa saŋ priyā janakarājaputrī n-hiḍĕp,wawaŋ sira kataṅguhan r-ujari téka saŋ lakṣmaṇa*7:33:628*

Ariṅku wulati-ŋ laṅit hana ta haṅsa haṙṣāṅlayaŋ,mamèt talaga haṙṣayan muni kabèḥnya konĕŋ Unĕŋ,Awās ya Iki lahru liṅku samayanta yèkin tĕka,Ah adwa tikanaŋ kapindra samayanya yā tan tuhu*7:34:629*

lawan wĕnaṅa yāparāđa n-alupā Ikaŋ wānara,Ikāna samayanya ṅūni lalu đūṙtta tātan tĕka,Alaḥ pijĕr amukti tan tĕṅa-tĕṅèn laṅit yālilaŋ,satéja hana tārakā tuwi lukan pwa tan ton ikā*7:35:630*

rikaŋ rahina taṙ wĕnaŋ mĕtu kunaŋ pijĕṙ yāturū,mataŋnya tar iṅöt-iṅĕt hayu nikaŋ sarojānĕḍĕŋ,pramāda maṅinak-Inak kapijĕran ya dé niŋ suka,Ah-o tan atakut ya milwa ri kakānya bālīn pĕjaḥ*7:36:631*

jĕnĕk lawan anak rabinya ya dumèḥnya mohā kunaŋ,Ariṅku laku tāt parériya Usönta haywāmtakut,Ikaŋ plawaga duṣṭa wèhi ta wuwus Anuŋ maŋlarè,Apan ya rumuhun tan atwaṅ i-kitān wĕnaŋ madwa ya*7:37:632*

parigraha jugéniwönya tan aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn mitra ya,magoṣṭi maṅinum warĕg mađu ya liṅku mattāwĕrö,ṅda tan wawa-rĕṅö ri hétu ni hayunya hāḥ moha ya,mataŋnya laku tāt parāt ujari yan mapāmbĕk nikā*7:38:633*

raǥūttama nahan ta liŋ nira madĕg ta saŋ lakṣmaṇa,widagđa wihikan sirāṅinaki citta saŋ rāǥawa,laras ya pinikul nirāṙ laku maréri kiṣkiṇḋaka,ḍatĕŋ sira rikaŋ guhā kabalasaḥ Ikaŋ wré mulat*7:39:634*

kapi prawara māruti praṇata yaṙ panuŋsuŋ masö,sagorawa sirāṙ pakon ta tumamā riṅ aƀyantara,masuk sira saṅ āṙyya lakṣmaṇa kapīndra śīǥrāṙ parĕk,manĕmbah umusap lĕbū ni suku saŋ sumitrātmaja*7:40:635*

ṅhulun n-iki patik pramāda maṅinak-k-inak tak para,kṣamākĕna tĕmĕn ṅhulun n-iki nihan katuhwan n-araḥ,Alaḥ pijĕr amukti ƀoga paṅasiḥ ta tékin kabèḥ,tĕkāŋ samaya lahru tak maṅĕn-aṅĕn sawèt niŋ jĕnĕk*7:41:636*

nihan ṅhulun akona wānara lumakwa tan saṅśayan,Ikaŋ wrayatagĕn kabèh umahasèŋ gunuŋ riŋ Alas,piraŋ sukĕta niŋ Alas susupananya kapwāmriha,Asiŋ sakahanan niraŋ janakarājaputrī n-parā*7:42:637*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
saŋ sugrīwa nahan ta liŋ nira ri saŋ somitra maṅkat sira,ṅ-kon tékaŋ bala wānarāmriha kabèḥ tātan hanā kāntuna,śīǥrāŋ wré Inatag ḍatĕŋ kakurutug maṅsö kabèḥ maŋ­rakĕt,saŋ somitra madĕg sirāṅdulurakĕn saŋ sugriwāgyā sira*7:43:638*

śīǥra prāpta ri mālyawān dadi masö cuṇḍuk siraŋ rāǥawa,saŋ sugrīwa huwus manĕmbah umarĕk taŋ wré kabèḥ maŋ­rĕpa,sāmpunyān praṇatān paluṅguh abukuḥ matwaŋ tumuṅkul kabèḥ,dényāṙ ton sira saŋ kapīśwara masö mojaṙ I-saŋ rāǥawa*7:44:639*

hé nāŧākṣama śīla ni ṅhulun apan tan yukti madwèṅ ujar,tan wruḥ riŋ samayān tĕkāṅinak-inak mĕṅgĕp krĕtajña ṅhulun,tan kiṅkiŋ Upakāra tan Aṅĕn-aṅĕn yātālupālaḥ jĕnĕk,jātī mūḋa minitra tan wruh iniwö tan ṅèḥ gumantyāṅiwö*7:45:640*

lāwan jāti nikaŋ wyamoha tumĕmu-ŋ ƀogāwĕrö yālupa,tan wruḥ riŋ maṅanugrahé ya mahiwaŋ saktèṅ inak kéwala,ndan lotatya naréndra ri ṅhulun apan mūḍātimūḍāđama,saṅké pèt naranāŧa hétu ni tutuṙ niŋ mūḋa yékin tĕka*7:46:641*

nā liŋ saŋ kapirāja tuṣṭa sira saŋ rāmā-ṅrĕṅö Akṣama,n-ton taŋ wré maśilāsĕsĕk ya hibĕkan tékaŋ gunuŋ mālyawān,byakta-ŋ rāwaṇa śīṙṇna dé nika kabèh āpan mahāśakti ya,nā liŋ saŋ raǥuputra trĕpti mulat iŋ wré wīra sāmpun tĕka*7:47:642*

tatkālān pasamūha taŋ kapibalomaṅsö ta saŋ māruti,mwaŋ nīlāṅgada jāmbawān gĕnĕp anuŋ katwaŋ nikaŋ wānara,wīrotsāha catus samudra juga riŋ wīrātigamƀīra ya,yékānuŋ winaraḥ niraŋ kapipatī sugrīwa mojaṙ sira*7:48:643*

Ꜽ nīlāṅgada jāmbawān laku ta tūt dūtā ri saŋ māruti,yan byaktā hana saŋ naréndra ǥariṇī sītā ri lĕṅkāpurī,nāhan dona nihan hawanta maṅidul saṅkérikaŋ mālyawān,t-ambaḥ taŋ giri pāṙśwa toḥ laku muwaḥ ton taŋ tasik loṙ kidul*7:49:644*

sāmpunyān haliwat rikaŋ jalađi ton tékaŋ suwélācala,yapwan prāpta tĕkāṅhinĕp jaga-jagā yatnā magantyāturū,Akwèḥ rākṣasa sāhasèŋ wĕṅi mahās yékān kayatnākĕna,mwaŋ saŋ śrī janakātmajā t-iṅĕt-iṅĕt riŋ rājya lĕṅkāpura*7:50:645*

tātan wāk prakaṭā yadin tĕmu mahādèwī siraŋ mꜽŧilī,yatnātaḥ susup iŋ pakuwwan atitip tiñjon wulat loṙ kidul,yapwan kāwit anon anak-k-ĕbi makūŋ monĕŋ tuwī yānaṅis,tāṅsö takwani lèn yadin hana sĕḍĕŋ mojaṙ-Ujaṙ rĕṅwakĕn*7:51:646*

nā liŋ saŋ prawagāđirāja sumiliḥ mojaṙ ta saŋ rāǥawa,Ꜽ saŋ māruti yatna-yatna ta kité lĕṅkāpurāmriḥ-mriha,simsimkwīki wawanta wèhakĕna yat paṅguḥ siraŋ mꜽtilī,donanya pracayā niré kita kinonkon dūta saṅké ry-aku*7:52:647*

nā liŋ saŋ nrĕpa rāǥawa krama madĕg luṅhā ta saŋ māruti,mwaŋ nīlāṅgada jāmbawān hana pataŋ koṭīkanaŋ wré tumūt,lumpatnyèŋ gaganāntarāla kumĕlab rambutnya mawyaŋ kabèḥ,tulyāditya sakoṭi tīkṣṇa mapanas śaktinya téjopama*7:53:648*

luṅhā-ŋ dūta madĕg ta saŋ śatabali wré śakti śīǥrāṅalor,ṅkānèŋ paśꞓimadéśa yéka pinaran dé saŋ susénāṙ laku,wétan déśa paran niraŋ winata wèt niŋ gyā lumumpat kabèḥ,lāwan wré śata koṭi saṅꝁya ya tumūt śāṙddūlawikrīḍita*7:54:649*

{twaritagati}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = :10:
Aŧa lumaku-ŋ wrayasasaran,saka ri pakon raǥutanaya,tucapa tikaŋ watĕk aṅidul,makajuru saŋ pawanasuta*7:55:650*

krama tĕka taŋ kapibala riŋ,giriwara winđya ya maruhur,mrĕgapati siṅha ya matakut,makabalasaḥ twaritagati*7:56:651*

śikara nikaŋ giri biṣama,wwara kali luṅka hana juraŋ,lwah adalĕm adƀuta ya trĕbis,haliwatan iŋ prawagabala*7:57:652*

paḍa ya humuŋ rikanaṅ alas,makakarasāk ya masusupan,hariwara siṅha kapĕlĕṅĕn,kapatuli kapwa ya malayū*7:58:653*

saka ri sukĕt nikanaṅ alas,tuwi giri windya ya maruhur,kapi ya maṅèl paḍa ya mĕhāḥ,dinakara tīkṣṇa mamanasi*7:59:654*

kapibala duṙbbala malapā,maṅĕlih alaḥ warĕg anusup,saka ri lapānya mari humuŋ,kadi ta-tasik sŧiti ta tĕḍuḥ*7:60:655*

hana ta śilātala maratā,kayu-kayu höbnya ya marĕñĕb,kapi maruhun-ruhunan aṅöb,paḍa maguliŋ-guliṅan aṅĕl*7:61:656*

hana ta manuk madulu-dulur,mĕtu saka riŋ giriwiwara,kapibala kadbuta ya mulat,paḍa maṅadĕg maṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt*7:62:657*

dadi ya manon wiwara guhā,Ikana lawaŋnya katatakut,wigata ƀaya-ŋ prawagabala,tama ta maṅöb makakurutug*7:63:658*

satama nikaŋ kapi ri dalĕm,hana ta Umaḥ đawala putiḥ,Atiśaya ƀāswara sumĕnö,ya ta tinĕmunya paḍa masö*7:64:659*

Anĕmu ta yānakĕbi rarā,rahayu sulakṣaṇa manulus,kadi ta wulañ juga gumawaŋ,ya ta kumĕmit Ikanaṅ umaḥ*7:65:660*

gumuyu masö ya tan atakut,tĕka ya mawèḥ ꝑala matasak,wwayatiśayĕŋ mahĕniṅ atīs,ya ta panamuynya śuci marūm*7:66:661*

dadi ya tumakwani Ikanaŋ,prawaga huwusnya ya tinamuy,suka paripūṙṇna paḍa warĕg,duga-duga yan pawara-waraḥ*7:67:662*

wwara sira rāǥawa karĕṅö,sira makadūta kami kabèḥ,lumaku kinon lumawada saŋ,janakasutā sira tinawan*7:68:663*

kami ta tumakwanakĕn i-saŋ,gumawayikaŋ giriwiwara,syapa Umaṅun nikanaṅ umaḥ,ya tikana pājara ri kami*7:69:664*

lawan ika saŋ dumadi kita,syapa paṅaran nira karĕṅö,kita ta rarāhayu saꝑala,saṅapa ṅaranta warahakĕn*7:70:665*

{tanumađya}
– – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏓ = :6:
nā liŋ nikanaŋ wré,mītrĕṣṇa kabèḥnya,mojaṙ tikanaŋ strī,kanyā tanumađyā*7:71:666*

{tiḍak dikĕtahui}

wwara sira dānawarāja,ṅaran ira saŋ wiśwakaṙmma tamoli,sira umaṅun nikanaṅ umaḥ,Ikaŋ guhā ṅké sira sumuk ya*7:72:667*

sāmpun swaṙggasŧāna sira,prastāwa binajra dé ƀaṭāréndra,saṅkā ya taṙ pahīṅan,Umariṣṭākĕn nikaŋ prĕŧiwī*7:73:668*

Aku Iki dānawakanyā,ṅaranku karĕṅö swayĕmpraƀā nāma,dānawarāja bapaṅku,praśāstébuṅku mérusāwaṙṇni*7:74:669*

yapwat mahyun śīǥra tĕkā,ri lĕṅka mĕné-ŋ gĕlĕk méṅgal,ndak wĕtwakĕn kita kabèḥ,ndan tukupi matanta haywa mulat*7:75:670*

{Indrabajra}
– – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
nā liŋ nikaŋ dānawarājakanyā,Ūmañcana-ŋ wānara donya tan lén,Āpaṇ ḍĕṅö wré ya marā ri lĕṅkā,Iṙṣyā tikāmbĕk nika moǥa héwa*7:76:671*

swāƀāwa niŋ dānawa rākṣasātūt,sāmitra jātinya Ulaḥnya tuṅggal,nāhan ta hétunya dumèḥ ya mélik,miǥnèkanaŋ wré magawé ta māyā*7:77:672*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
samaṅkanaŋ wré tamataṙ wihaŋ kabèḥ,siraŋ hanūmān tuwi moǥa mohita,wijaḥ kabèḥ mrĕm matukup-tukup mata,tatan hanātaḥ tumahā ya bañcana*7:78:673*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
sawèt ni ṅèlnyān panusup saranta ya,magyān tĕkā yéka dumèḥnya maṅga ya,sĕḍĕŋnyan ūmrĕm kinĕnan ta yĕŋ mayā,taṙ ton ry-awaknyan mĕtu saṅka riŋ guhā*7:79:674*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
tinonya tāwaknya ri hèŋ nikaŋ guhām,wimoha tan wruḥ wulaṅun hilaŋ tutur,salèk rikaŋ sakṣaṇa mātra yaṙ hiḍĕp,dumèḥnya māyā nikanaŋ swayĕmpraƀā*7:80:675*

saṅ aṅgada glāna sirāṅaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn,taman tĕmuŋ budđi hilaŋ hiḍĕp nira,saśoka māśā humĕnĕŋ saniścaya,hanékanāmbĕk nira mātya riŋ Alas*7:81:676*

samaṅkanātaḥ kapiwīra jāmbawān,tumon siraŋ Aṅgada śoka mānasa,manaḥ niropĕk wulaṅun hilaŋ tutur,tumūta mātyāku nahan ta liŋ nira*7:82:677*

siraŋ hanūmĕn milu śokamānasa,tumon siraŋ wānarawrĕdđa jambawān,ndya dona niŋ jīwita niṙguṇān hanā,Umilwa mātyāku nahan ta liŋ nira*7:83:678*

satūt niraŋ wānarawīra māruti,tumūt ikaŋ wré sahananya duḥkita,sawismrĕti ṅkā paḍa tan hanaŋ tutur,pinatyakĕn yéka Awaknya riŋ gunuŋ*7:84:679*

sĕḍĕŋ nikaŋ wānara śoka kāsyasiḥ,hanéka sampāti ṅaranya ƀīṣaṇa,manuk magöŋ saŋ garuḍopamā nika,ya tomasö riŋ bala wānarāṅaraŋ*7:85:680*

ndatan parambut malĕṅis Awak nikā,patuknya tīkṣṇogra makas ta yāluṅid,mulat Ikaŋ wānara kapwa yātakut,makin makiṅkiŋ sahananya duḥkita*7:86:681*

Ah-o mahākaśmala duṙyyaśāđama,tuhun ṅaran dūta lukan pwa tan tuhu,sawèt ni māyā nikanaŋ swayĕmpraƀā,tatan wruh iŋ déśa parāna loṙ kidul*7:87:682*

lukan kariḥ dibya kitāri jāṭayu,huwus krĕtāṙŧāṅupakāra mitrakā,siromaraḥ saŋ raǥuputra rāǥawa,sĕḍĕŋ kapaṅguḥ rikanaŋ Alas magöŋ*7:88:683*

kami pwa yātyanta krĕtaǥna duṙnaya,taman walés saŋ raǥuputra rāǥawa,Apā guṇaṅkū mahurip ya tan padon,mataŋnya tāṅhiŋ pĕjahāta ménaka*7:89:684*

kuyaŋ manuk rodra kagéndra tulya ya,magöŋ malaṇḍĕp ta patuknya ƀīṣaṇa,masö tumandaŋ kadi mrĕtyu yak hiḍĕp,saƀāgya yan mātya ta liṅku dé nikā*7:90:685*

Iké śarīranta ya wèhakĕn huwus,rikaŋ manuk glāna wiƀukti yālapā,sawètnyan aṅliḥ malimöṙ ta yan laku,lukan pwa nohan ya tumĕmwakĕn kita*7:91:686*

nahan Ujaṙ niŋ bala wānarālara,nasö ta mojaṙ Ikanaŋ manuk magöŋ,ndya donta hé wānarawīra kottama,rikèŋ gunuŋ winđya Atīta duṙggama*7:92:687*

Aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn towi tamaṙ tĕkériya,lawan ruhuṙnyātiśayèŋ sukĕt tĕmĕn,kitāt para ṅké Aparan prayojana,mataŋnya tāśā sahananta duḥkita*7:93:688*

lawan sinaṅguḥ ta Awakta duṙyyasa,jaṭāyu yékām pinujinta sajjana,Ariṅku kāsiḥku Ikā taman kalèn,praśāsta sampāti ṅaranku riŋ jagat*7:94:689*

patatri sampāti nahan ta liŋ nikā,wawaŋ ta mojaṙ bala wānarāwaraḥ,kamīkihĕn dūta niraŋ raǥūttama,marā ri lĕṅkā ya pakon iré kami*7:95:690*

priyā niraŋ rāǥawa dèwi jānakī,siréka pètĕn mami yaṙ hanāhurip,nda tan kasidđéki pakon iré kami,mataŋnya kāmbuḥ kami śokamānasa*7:96:691*

salèk tikaŋ kāla hiḍĕp mamīrikā,huwus Atīta-ŋ samayālawas dahat,tatan tĕmu-ŋ donnya ta hétu niŋ Iraŋ,mataŋnya taṅsö ta patuk paṅan kami*7:97:692*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
nā liŋ nikaŋ wré paḍa mātya don ikā,sampāti māsiḥ Umuwaḥ siromajar,Ah-o lukan kāsih-asiḥ ta mohita,Amoǥa māśā wulaṅun kuraŋ tutur*7:98:693*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
pinatyakĕntéka Awakta duṙyyaśa,ndya dona niŋ mātya tatan pakāraṇa,Adĕg tat amriḥ sahananta cāraka,katĕmwa dontāt aṅidul Aŧomuwaḥ*7:99:694*

{Upastiŧa}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
yapwan panon rājya Umaḥ hĕmas kabèḥ,Umuṅgwi puñcak nikanaŋ gunuŋ magöŋ,ya téka lĕṅkā kahanan niṅ apsarī,tatan pahi mwaŋ himawān ikaŋ hayu*7:100:695*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
lĕwiḥ sakèŋ swaṙgga hayunya kādƀuta,tahaṅkwi lĕṅkā sari niŋ jagat kabèḥ,ƀaṭāra đātā gumawéya tan kalèn,Uliḥ nirāmriḥ ya dumèḥ ya Ujwala*7:101:696*

praśāsta saŋ wꜽśrawaṇā đanèśwara,sira praƀu ṅkāna ta ṅūni pūṙwwaka,sawèt nirāsoṙ sinukū ni rāwaṇa,mataŋnyan uṅgwiŋ Alakāwatī dumèḥ*7:102:697*

Ikāpi saŋ rāwaṇa yadyapiñ jayā,baśèŋ jagat tan hana tan huwus Alaḥ,Awās ya-yan mātya ya dènta riŋ raṇa,Apan mahāśakti kabèḥ mahābala*7:103:698*

mataŋnya tātan malarā t-adĕg huwus,pakon iraŋ rāǥawa yéka dadyakĕn,katĕmwa saŋ śrī janakātmajān pinèt,hané kaḍatwan nika saŋ daśānana*7:104:699*

taman mrĕṣāwāda wuwusku satya ya,prayojanantāt laku dūta dadya ya,Awās ya tuṣṭā nira saŋ raǥūttama,sawèt ni pamriḥta Umèt priyā nira*7:105:700*

kagéndra sampāti nahan ta liŋ nira,tumaṅguhi-ŋ wānara kapwa yātutur,madĕg ta luṅhā sahananya haṙṣaja,tĕkèŋ gunuŋ ꝁyāti mahéndra paṙbwata*7:106:701*

tĕkanya riŋ pāṙśwa kidul sahaṙṣa ya,maṅan nikaŋ wwa-wwahan īŋ Alas matöp,sakèŋ gunuŋ n-ton ikanaŋ tasik kidul,laṅit jugèŋ lwā Atiǥora ǥūṙṇnita*7:107:702*

Ikaŋ tasik ṙyyaknya humuŋ nirantara,lanā tumampuḥ suku niŋ gunuŋ makas,kadi pwa sakrođa ya héwa riŋ gunuŋ,ri dénya tan ton hayu niŋ pradéśa lor*7:108:703*

lawan nikā lwiṙnya kadi pwa yāwĕrö,sadaṙppa dé niŋ maṇiratna taṙ malaḥ,Anéka tolaḥnyan alaḥ wimohita,swaƀāwa niŋ śrī ya nimitta riŋ wĕrö*7:109:704*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
Aṅinya mādrĕs ya lanomiriṙ matīs,kadi pwa yośwāsa nikaŋ samudra ya,Ahos ikāmbĕknyan alaḥ warĕg dahat,minum Ikaŋ lwaḥ humilī nirantara*7:110:705*

{kusumawicitra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
jĕnĕk ikanaŋ wānara Umulat riŋ,jalađi humuŋ ṙyyaknya paḍa manĕmpuḥ,dadi tumurun wānara sahananya,ri tĕpi nikaŋ sāgara ta ya pāran*7:111:706*

tĕka ya mararyan paḍa ta manonton,makara Uraŋ riŋ karaṅ akaramkam,hana ta Iwak wré paḍa ya lumumpat,gumuyu kĕkĕl wānarabala dénya*7:112:707*

{pṛŧiwītala}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
sĕḍĕn pijĕr ikaŋ kapiprawara yan panonton iwak,saṅ aṅgada makon umaṅkata madĕg ta saŋ māruti,Apan pawanaputra muꝁya nikanaŋ kinon cārakā,madĕg ta sira mĕḥ lumakwa kawĕkas tikaŋ wré kabèḥ*7:113:708*

#Aṣṭamas saṙggaḥ#
<drutawilambita>:8
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
^8/1/707.
Aŧa mĕsat ta siraŋ pawanātmaja,gagana yéka hawan nira maŋlayaŋ,garuḍa sūṙyya ṅ-aṅin tamataṙ paḍé,laku nirādƀuta śīǥra manojawa*8:1:709*

kadi dĕwākara tékana yaṙ katon,wulu nirojwala téjamayān katon,tuwi malit madawā kadi cāmara,kapilawaṙṇna Apūṙwwa ri ƀāswara*8:2:710*

pinahagöŋ nira téka Awak nira,katatakut kadi paṙbwata maŋlayaŋ,Umĕlĕtuk sira śīǥra Umiṇḍuhur,grahagaṇāṙkka wulan ya katuṅkulan*8:3:711*

jalađi đꜽṙyya guṇanya tataṙ paḍé,Ikana đꜽṙyya niraŋ pawanātmaja,Aṅin-aṅin nira ǥora ya ǥūṙṇnita,pralaya bāyu paḍanya riwut magöŋ*8:4:712*

hana ta sāhasa ƀīṣaṇa rākṣasī,pratita rodra ṅaranya si ḍākinī,Atiwiśāla tutuknya mĕṅā maṅaŋ,ya humĕlö sira śīǥra tĕkĕŋ wĕtĕŋ*8:5:713*

pawanaputra widagđa sirāṅduduk,sĕbitakĕn ta wĕtĕŋnya mĕsat sira,dadi maṅohan ikaŋ kala rākṣasī,katatakut kadi śabda niṅ ampuhan*8:6:714*

Aŧa pĕjaḥnya tibā ta ya riŋ tasik,wuhaya lèn hyu masö marĕbut dagiŋ,hana timiṅgila kapwa warĕg kabèḥ,saka ri göŋ nikanaŋ jaḍa dākinī*8:7:715*

{prahaṙṣiṇī}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
sāmpun māti dadi sahaṙṣa saŋ hanūmān,n-ton taŋ paṙbwata ri tĕṅaḥ nikaŋ samudra,riŋ ménākagiri ṅaranya duṙggamāwān,Aṅhiŋ yādƀuta kumĕlab gunuŋ Apūṙwwa*8:8:716*

saŋ hyaŋ māruta makamitra ya pratīta,tāmoli n-pawanasakā ya bāyumitra,wruḥ yan bāyutanaya saŋ marutpraṣūta,mojaṙ swāgata masayut sagorawāṅliŋ*8:9:717*

hé bāywātmaja sĕpĕr i-ṅhulun ta raryan,haywāgyā hana panamuyku jambu ḍuṙyyan,poḥ maṅgis kacapi limo limus kapuṇḍuŋ,mwaŋ laṅsĕb duhĕt amanis paṅan sakahyun*8:10:718*

riŋ pāṙśwā ta turu-turū yaŧāsukā ṅké,tonton taŋ manuk amijaḥ rikèṅ alasku,yan magyā sakarĕṅa wèḥ kitat pararyan,wruḥ tākun kita ta kinon lumakwa dūta*8:11:719*

Atyantékana ta giraṅku dènta putra,dibyāsiḥ wĕnaṅ amalĕs ƀaṭāra rāma,sakwèḥ saŋ wiku hana riŋ gunuŋ masāđya,kāṙyyantékana Inaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn kasidđā*8:12:720*

ta ṅhèṙ-hèṙ pwa ta sakarĕŋ lukan swagāta,mitra hyaŋ pawana matāku tan hanoli,saŋ hyaŋ wé tuwi mapanas ta ṅöb pwa ta ṅké,yan sāmpun marĕn apanas lumakwa śīǥra*8:13:721*

nyaŋ kumbaŋ ya rĕṅĕ-rĕṅönta daṙppa moni,kĕmbaŋ niŋ Asana sĕḍéŋ manojña tonton,tontonĕn n-aku kalalaḥ pwa dènta ṅūni,ƀāgyaṅkun tĕka kita bāyuputra tan lèn*8:14:722*

nā liŋ niŋ gunuṅ asayut ri saŋ hanūmān,wèt niŋ gyā nira sumahuṙ wawaŋ ta mojar,hé ménāka giri huwus ta haywa képwan,prĕgyākun samaya baṭâra rāma magyā*8:15:723*

tāmolin kita ta samīraṇā ta mitra,ndā magyā wruha ri si rāwaṇāku maṅké,māpa pwékana muꝁa niŋ Inaṅluh iŋ rāt,śaktinyékana papagĕ-ṅkwa yan prawīra*8:16:724*

lĕṅkā yékana raƀasā-ṅkwa tan paśéṣā,sakwèḥnyā-ŋ suraripu rākṣasolihĕṅkwa,swasŧā niŋ ƀuwana ya sāđya déṅku tan lèn,nā liŋ saŋ pawanasutomibĕṙ ta luṅhā*8:17:725*

{bramitākṣara}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
hana rākṣasī katĕmu dé nira lén,wikaṭākṣinī ya ta ṅaranya gahan,suka yan pacaṅkrama rikaŋ jalađi,manikĕp Iwak ya pinaṅanya lanā*8:18:726*

Umulat pwa yèŋ gagana yéka mĕsat,Inusī ta saŋ pawanaputra wawaŋ,sinikĕpnya śīǥra hinĕlönya sira,kadi tuhwa śakti ya wĕnaŋ raƀasa*8:19:727*

ri gulūnya hīṅan ira yaṙ kahĕlö,pahagöŋ Awak nira Umaṅkak akas,wikaṭakṣinī kahalĕlön mĕlĕlö,Umulū matanya ya maṅèl umĕlĕd*8:20:728*

tinuhuk nirèŋ naka gulūnya ḍuhak,dinugaŋ rĕmĕk rahu-rahunya śiwak,sinahut nirékana guruŋ-guruṅa,nya pĕgat mĕsat sira muwaḥ ya mibĕr*8:21:729*

haliwat nirèŋ jalađi śīǥra ḍatĕŋ,rikanaŋ suwélagiri ǥoratara,hana rodra rākṣasa ya māmĕṅ-amöŋ,pinapag nirādƀuta kumöl ta sira*8:22:730*

Atiyatna saŋ pawanaputra huwus,saśaśā ta göŋ nira rikaŋ rahina,ri tutuṙ niré sapawĕkas nira saŋ,raǥuputra ṅūni mawuwus ri sira*8:23:731*

maṅidul muwaḥ manĕmu dūṙgga tĕmĕn,kali luṅka yākuliliṅan kumalūŋ,Ikanaŋ gunuŋ pinakaduṙgga nikaŋ,nagarātƀutātiśaya kātara ya*8:24:732*

haliwat nirèŋ kali kulĕm ya huwus,daśadéśa kapwa ya pĕtĕŋ ya kabèḥ,rikanaŋ kulĕm pasuki taŋ nagara,tĕmu taŋ pakuwwan atitip ya matap*8:25:733*

rikanaŋ hawan manĕmu rākṣasa lèn,ƀaṭa wīra mantri maduluṙ ya kabèḥ,masuluḥ lumakwa makĕmit ri dalĕm,Atakut katona sira yatna kumöl*8:26:734*

tĕpi niŋ hawan hana ta mojar-ujar,jaga yatna saŋ pawanaputra masö,rinasan nirékana Ujaṙnya dudū,guṇa saŋ daśāsya pinujinya kabèḥ*8:27:735*

hana tāṅinum paḍa wijaḥ maṅigĕl,hana maṅgupit hana mabaṅsi wanèḥ,masiwo humuŋ hana wijaḥ masĕkar,suraloka tulya nikanaŋ nagara*8:28:736*

wwara śāla yékana wiśāla tĕmĕn,yatikā paran nira masuk ta sira,wiku rākṣasékana Isinya kabèḥ,mamasaŋ-masaŋ Aji sirĕp sisulap*8:29:737*

Aji bajrakāya pinasaŋnya wanèḥ,Aƀiśāra mona hana tāji tiḍĕm,makupik makuṇḍah aṅadĕg mrĕgigiḥ,Atirodra yoga saƀayāṅikikan*8:30:738*

sanĕnĕḥ nikaŋ maṅaji śāstra wĕgig,macĕṅil wahil matĕmahan matukar,tamataṙ wiwéka rasa niŋ winuwus,swaṅ awū mawākya manĕhĕṙ mamisuḥ*8:31:739*

hana lèn sagulma ya watĕk mapĕkĕn,naramāṅsa yéka pinaṅanya lanā,Ininumnya rāḥ wija-wijaḥ mawĕrö,patukaṙ-tukaṙnya Inucapnya kabèḥ*8:32:740*

hana téka rākṣasa bĕtaḥ maṅinum,Amaṅan tasak-mĕtah asiŋ sahanā,manĕwĕṙ pupū ya manisig ya dagiŋ,Amĕcĕl-mĕcĕl hana kulub-kuluban*8:33:741*

Ininumnya rodra sakawaḥ ya magöŋ,Ibĕkan wuduk kinĕla lèn ruđira,Ininum hĕlèd pisan ikaŋ sakawaḥ,mawĕrö kabèḥ ya paḍa wāk prakaṭa*8:34:742*

hana ta prawīra sabatĕk maṅinum,tan adoḥ tĕwĕknya Inunusnya kabèḥ,Atidaṙppa sāmpun aṅinum ya madĕg,Amutĕṙ krĕtāla hana ḍaṇḍa gadā*8:35:743*

wwara lèn wimāna ya hawanya mibĕr,suka yan pacaṅkrama rikaŋ gagana,hana tāhawan raŧa liman turaga,rikanaŋ kulĕm suka ya māmĕṅ-amĕŋ*8:36:744*

sawanèḥ krĕtāṙŧa ya huwus manukū,jayaśatru kapwa ya muliḥ manawan,Amaṅan magoṣṭi sahananya wijaḥ,masĕkaṙ karaŋ bali sawit majĕnu*8:37:745*

wwara kāminī ya mamarīkṣa mahā,humĕnĕŋ pwa mĕṅgĕp agĕlĕŋ ya malök,tinawanya māstawa tamaṙ paṅinum,taruṇātidaṙppa ya manantwa maṅol*8:38:746*

Umulat ta saŋ pawanaputra rikaŋ,masiwo sarāga ya sĕḍĕŋ paḍa siḥ,kalaran sirāṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn matutur,ri larā niraŋ raǥusutāṙ papasaḥ*8:39:747*

karuṇā manaḥ nira saśoka tĕmĕn,mari yaṙ wulat riṅ aṅinum masiwo,mari maŋ­rĕṅö kiduṅ alaḥ malara,humilī ta luḥ nira-nirantara ya*8:40:748*

kramakāla mèḥ ta ya pisan tabĕha,pratipāda krĕṣṇa ya rikaŋ diwasa,malayū-ŋ pĕtĕŋ mĕtu ƀaṭāra wulan,kadi dꜽtya yaṙ wĕtu ƀaṭāra hari*8:41:749*

Atiśīǥra maṅkin aruhuṙ ta sira,rikanaŋ gunuŋ Udaya r-uṅgu katon,maharĕp tumona hayu niŋ nagara,ya mataŋnyan uṅgu rikanaŋ Udaya*8:42:750*

Umulat ta saŋ pawanaputra rikaŋ,daśadéśa niŋ nagara kapwa katon,hana ta prasāda maruhuṙ ya magöŋ,ya tinon ira sꝑaṭika-ratna-maya*8:43:751*

hana satwa śāśa kanakāṙ pinahat,gaja sihha moŋ mrĕga warāha warak,hana lèn alas ya ta pahatnya wanèḥ,Ikanaŋ prasāda kadi paṙbwata ya*8:44:752*

maṇi candrakānta ya nataṙnya maṇik,hana ratna ƀāswara hĕninya malit,wĕtu niŋ wulan dadi humīs ya matīs,rikanaŋ nataṙ drawa maho mahĕniŋ*8:45:753*

sꝑaṭika prasāda kadi mandara ya,Ikanaŋ nataṙ kadi tasik susu ya,maṇi mutya yékana kadi pwa wĕrĕḥ,wway aho matīs ya Amrĕtanya mĕtu*8:46:754*

hana tambak ujwala pinik ya kabèḥ,sapuluḥ tumāp kadi Alun ṙyyak agöŋ,paḍahi prasāda ri dalĕm tinabĕḥ,ya ta śabda niŋ jalađi kapwa humuŋ*8:47:755*

ri yawā nikā hana ta yāwaraṇa,tamalaḥ prasāda marĕṇik maḍĕmit,Inukiṙ ya kapwa ta maṇik mahirĕŋ,kaharan karaŋ kumuliliŋ ri tĕpi*8:48:756*

Ikana prasāda I-yawānya kabèḥ,paḍa kapwa mèsi kanaka pratimā,kadi déwa dānawa parĕŋ Umasö,malapékanaŋ Amrĕta yékana don*8:49:757*

paḍa kapwa sāyuđa Ikaŋ pratimā,magadā maśūla malaras malipuŋ,matĕwĕk macakra hana bajra wanèḥ,kadi tāpraṅārĕbuta yèŋ Amrĕta*8:50:758*

hana lén suwuk lawaṅ ikaŋ pratima,maṇi candrakānta pinahat mahalĕp,mawĕlū matanya dumĕlö malĕlö,kadi rāhwamilwa marĕbut Amrĕta*8:51:759*

wiṣa kālakūṭa ya kunaŋ malayū,Ikanaŋ suwuk lawaṅ atā matakut,ri baṭāra śaṅkara ri pāpahara,hana riŋ prasāda ri dalĕm satata*8:52:760*

ri yawā niṅ āwaraṇa rāmya katon,hana kalpawrĕkṣa matatā marĕnöb,suka hétwamĕtwakĕn asiŋ sakarĕp,kadi pārijāta Ulihiŋ mamutĕr*8:53:761*

I samīpa niŋ kanaka kalpataru,hana maṇḍapādbuta ya ratnamaya,pitiganya maṙkata maṇik makiris,gawayan ƀaṭāra ya Isinya kabèḥ*8:54:762*

wwara mutyahāgra hana téka payuŋ,hana tuṅgaṅan gaja raŧāpratima,maṇiratna sāri-sari niŋ jalađi,pinutĕṙ huwus mĕtu katon asinaŋ*8:55:763*

hana téki déwagrĕha ratnamaya,matatā mahojwala kabèḥ sumĕnö,ya tikā wimāna nira saŋ mamutĕr,kawĕkas ri hĕŋ hawana niŋ mibĕra,
wwara téki tambak i-yawā maruhur,rajatāputiḥ kumuliliŋ ri tĕpi,kadi nāga bāsuki mararyan aṅèl,ri huwus nikaŋ jalađi yan pinutĕr*8:56:764*

sumĕnö maṇik pawal abāŋ lumarap,ya ta gopuranya kadi cūla lumön,ri lawaŋnya rākṣasa mapaṇṭa kĕmit,ya tikā sihuŋnya masalit maluṅid*8:57:765*

{śālinī}
– – – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
nāhan lwiṙ niŋ paṙhyaṅan ṅkā ri lĕṅkā,saśrī téjanyojwalāƀrā praƀānya,maṅkin māwān hyaŋ wulan maṅkin āwā,maṅkin saśrī paṙhyaṅan srīnya kasraŋ*8:58:766*

déwī sītā byakta liṅkun hana ṅkā,liŋ niŋ cittānaṙkka yākon lumakwa,yékān lumpat saŋ hanūmān tĕka ṅka,ton taŋ wadwā rākṣasāṅrākṣa tan kraḥ*8:59:767*

momo niŋ wwil yéka wīnāni-wāni,yatnā tuṅgw-Iṅkaŋ catuṙ dwāra n-uṅgu,kapwāṅraṅkak caŋ-ciṅ añcaŋ kacaṅkag,moṅsil mèṅsĕl pāwakanyākral-akral*8:60:768*

mawyaŋ mèkĕl woknya mākrĕp kumisnya*8:61:769*
wakṣa bris-bris rodra malwā ḍaḍanya,siṅhākāra krūra lūṅid sihuŋnya,byaktān matwaŋ mrĕtyu yaṙ ton muꝁanya*8:62:770*

yaṙ ton taŋ wwil yéka liṅsiṙ nirāṅdoḥ,dū niŋ tambak ṅkan panèk yatna śīǥra,mamriḥ tātaḥ mèt mahādèwi sītā,tātaṙ paṅguḥ mꜽŧilī śīǥra luṅhā*8:63:771*

n-ton taŋ kāmī wwil sĕḍĕŋ yowanākwèḥ,monĕŋ yaṙ ton téja saŋ hyaŋ śaśāṅka,maṅdon dwa-dwal riŋ rarā ṅkān parāwrĕg,kapwāsyaŋ-syaŋ kāminī wwaŋnya mosyan*8:64:772*

sāmpunyā ṅèl kapwa maṇḍĕk maluṅguḥ,maṅsö dwa-dwal saŋ rarānori pāna,sīđu mwaŋ brĕm māstawa drākṣa kiñca,daṙppa-ŋ kāmī yānaḍaḥ pūṙṇna dénya*8:65:773*

lyan taŋ swécꞓāpāna mahniŋ suganđa,muṅgwiŋ pintwan tulya caṙmmiñ jugāho,cāyā saŋ hyaŋ candramī byakta ya ṅkā,lwiṙnyaŋ kāmī tulya rāhu n-minum ya*8:66:774*

lāwan kāmī bwat harĕp ri priyānya,yékāsaṇḍiŋ taṙ madoḥ nityakāla,Aṅhiŋ krīḍā yéka ménak ta liŋnya,maŋlaṅga twak taṙ pawĕḥ mèdi yāglis*8:67:775*

Akwèḥ taŋ wwil ǥora yānuŋ kapaṅguḥ,katwaŋ saŋ hyaŋ Indra tan swaŋ galaknya,ndā tan kagyat saŋ hanūmān tumon ya,soma-somaḥ kapwa tèkān tiniñjo*8:68:776*

ndā taṙ wruḥ wwil saŋ hanūmān paniñjo,Āpan māyārūpa mĕṅgĕp sirān wil,hāḥ mūḍékiŋ mūṙkꝁa tan wruḥ pramāda,swaŋ-swaŋ caṅkak đūṙtta nā liŋ nirèŋ twas*8:69:777*

maṅké n-luṅhā yaṙ pĕsat riŋ kaḍatwan,n-ton taŋ ratnāpèni lāwan n-umaḥ mās,yèkoṅgwan saŋ rāwaṇāmukti ƀoga,salwiṙ niŋ strī Apsarī mālinī kwèḥ*8:70:778*

hyaŋ śrī saśrī soṙ ya kasraŋ ta dénya,śrĕṅgārārūm komalolĕm wulatnya,wruḥ riŋ krīḍā riŋ Ulaḥ haṅsalīlā,riŋ Indrāṇī śāstra sāmpun paṅajyan*8:71:779*

tātan kéwran hyaŋ Anaṅgāṙ hana ṅka,moliḥ taŋ hrū mwaŋ laras tan lĕsū ya,strī yāgantī yomanaḥ taŋ manaḥ syuḥ,cakṣunyādrĕs nā panaḥnyātitīkṣṇa*8:72:780*

sāmpun tonton apsarī tan masowé,wwantĕn téjojwāla maƀrā ya lumrā,maṅkin méṅān ton wimānojwalāƀrā,kaꝁyātiŋ rāt puṣpakānāma tan lèn*8:73:781*

tulyanyé göŋ niŋ gunuŋ mandarādri,yapwan riŋ drĕs yan mibĕṙ cittagāmi,yan riŋ téjā sūṙyya sèwūpamanya,yan riŋ krūrā-ŋ rāhu sākṣāt muꝁanya*8:74:782*

ṅkānāṙ tonton saŋ daśāsya prasupta,tulyātĕṅgö nidra tan paŋ­rĕṅö rāt,lāwan cèṭī cèṭṭa riŋ krīḍa tan kraḥ,māmbö rūm niŋ kasturī bāhu sumrak*8:75:783*

lwiṙnyèŋ gātra byakta kꜽlāśa riŋ göŋ,tĕṇḍas makwèḥ yéka puñcak nirocꞓa,lāwan bāhu rwaŋ puluḥ yéka mālyus,yāṅkĕn raṇḍö yālĕsĕs mwaŋ kĕpuḥ poḥ*8:76:784*

mawyaŋ mèkĕl taŋ kumīs aṙdđa mākrĕp,nityān polaḥ dé niṅ uśwāsa mādrĕs,tulyālas niŋ méru kolāhalolaḥ,wètnyān séḍuŋ ǥūṙṇnitādrĕs pracaṇḍa*8:77:785*

Āśꞓaṙyyāmbĕk saŋ hanūmān tumon ya,Aṙdđāsowé wèt nirān kādƀutātaḥ,maŋ­ruṅkuk riŋ pañcaraṅkaŋ rumaṅkaŋ,raṅcānāmbĕk yaṙ paluṅguḥ wisāta*8:78:786*

sakwèḥ niŋ strī kapwa nidrā kabèḥnya,tan saŋ dèwī téki liŋ saŋ hanūmān,yan saŋ sītā byakta liṅku n-pataṅhya,Āpan monĕŋ rāǥawātaḥ cinitta*8:79:787*

Āśā tāmbĕk saŋ hanūmān wimoha,tan ton dèwī mꜽŧilī riŋ kaḍatwan,Aṅhiŋ tékin samƀawār uṅgwa liṅku,nāhan liŋ saŋ bāyuputrān makiṅkiŋ*8:80:788*

tapwan ton saŋ mꜽŧilī yéka lumpat,saŋ mārutyākāśagāmī maluy wré,makwèḥ taŋ wwil yākĕmit kapwa nidrā,tātaṙ moṅsil đīra tātan patī ya*8:81:789*

saŋ sītātaḥ kwan Iṅ āmbĕk tatan lèn,ndi ṅgwan dèwī ṅké kunaŋ liŋ nirāmèt,hāḥ wyaṙŧékin ṅèlku tātaṙ padon ya,tātan paṅgiḥ mꜽŧilī ṅèlku wrĕdđi*8:82:790*

tuṣṭā saŋ śrī rāma yaṙ tĕmwa dèṅku,mwaŋ trĕpti śrī jānakī nā wanèhan,tan sidđékā dèṅku tapwan kapaṅguḥ,dūtāpékin hīna tan sidđakāṙyya*8:83:791*

nyā-ŋ wwil nidrāwās ya mātyéki dèṅku,yak tampyal yāpīla tékā pipinya,ndan wyaṙŧékāpan ya tan muꝁya niŋ don,Aṅhiŋ dèwī muꝁya tapwan kapaṅguḥ*8:84:792*

nā liŋ saŋ bāywātmaja glāna ṅ-āmbĕk,dolārūḍa-ŋ citta kĕpwan ta mawruḥ,riŋ digdéśa ṅkā wulat ton aśoka,kĕmbaŋnyājrābaŋ ya waṙṇnanya śoƀā*8:85:793*

kaṙṇnaḥ wétan saṅka riŋ rājya lĕṅkā,Udyānārūm kwèḥ sĕkaṙnyātimalwā,dényān makwèḥ pwaŋ Aśokānĕḍĕŋ ṅkā,nā hétunyān riŋ Aśokā ṅaranya*8:86:794*

lāwan ṅwaŋ tātan kĕnĕŋ śoka r-uṅgu,muktī kĕmbaŋ kālahan nityakāla,rĕŋrĕŋ lahrū kāla tātaṙ makiṅkiŋ,prastāwanyān riŋ Aśokā ṅaranya*8:87:795*

lāwan saŋ hyaŋ candramāwwat haji ṅkā,saṅka ry-ājñā saŋ daśasyāđirāja*8:88:796*
tātan paṅlwaŋ taṙ tilĕm pūṙṇnamātaḥ,riŋ Udyāna ṅka ṅ-amāwāsyakāla*8:89:797*

ṅkā toṅgwanyā ṅ-apsarī mālyakaṙmmā,tā kolinyèŋ puṣpaganđaprawanđa,kapwa wruḥ yĕbŋ śāstra niŋ ganđayukti,ṅkānèŋ cĕṭṭātyanta riŋ wruḥ maganđa*8:90:798*

Akwèḥ rārā rākṣasī rākṣaka ṅka,ndan māyātaḥ rūpa-rūpanya mārūm,kèn-kènyāṅkĕn taŋ pakĕnnāryakĕnya,dodotnyālit sūtra lèn luṅsir aƀrā*8:91:799*

dèwī sītā ṅkā tamolaḥ tinuṅgu,Ékākyaṅhiŋ kāsyasiḥ yaṙ kinuṅkuŋ,mènĕḥ monĕŋ mona māśā saśoka,Aṅhiŋ wwil kwèḥ taṙ parowaŋ sira wwaŋ*8:92:800*

{punaṙmmada}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
ya Ikā paran saṅ anilātmajāṙ pamèt,maṅikis sirāṙ tĕka manèk rikaŋ kayu,ri takut nirān kawurugāŋ manuk pijĕr,maturū ri pāŋ nikaṅ aśoka pādapa*8:93:801*

kramakāla mèḥ rahina yaṙ pituŋ tabĕḥ,Umiriṙ ṅ-aṅin pracalitékanaŋ kayu,Aṅatag mawuṅwa juga yāṅgugaḥ sĕkar,dadi jāgra taŋ kusuma māri yākucup*8:94:802*

matakut ta saŋ pawanaputra riŋ Aṅin,tumahā pawuṅwa nikanaŋ manuk kabèḥ,humĕnĕŋ sirāmrih aṅuḍampĕl iŋ kayu,cala pāŋnya tulya ya maṅulyat aṅlilir*8:95:803*

maṇi candrakānta tamalaḥ rikaŋ taman,kĕna raśmi ya drawa humīs nirantara,kadi luḥnya yaṙ wulat i-dèwi jānakī,manaṅis rikaŋ wĕṅi tamaṙ kĕnĕŋ turū*8:96:804*

Ikanaŋ sĕkaṙ ya rinurū rikaŋ Aṅin,manaṅis jugān paguliṅan rikaŋ lĕmaḥ,tumibāṅhĕbun kabarabas ya luḥ nikā,malarāṙ wulat ri sira dèwi jānakī*8:97:805*

Aŧa mĕḥ wwaluŋ tabĕh ajāgra taŋ manuk,mrĕdu komala swara manoharān uni,kadi śabda niŋ kayu ya kāsihan mulat,Umahā tumaṅguhana saŋ kĕnèŋ lara*8:98:806*

janakātmajā ta rumĕṅö manuk humuŋ,tuwi suswarān uni manojña yaṙ hiḍĕp,mahĕbaŋ-hĕbaŋ hati nirāgiraŋ manaḥ,Umaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn prawara rāǥawān mara*8:99:807*

pawanātmajātiśaya haṙṣajāṅrĕṅö,Uni niŋ manuk śuƀanimitta liŋ nira,saꝑaléki ṅèlku wĕkasanta yaṙ hiḍĕp,niyatān katĕmwa sira dèwi jānakī*8:100:808*

tinabĕḥ tikaŋ bahiri riŋ taman wawaŋ,kataraṅgulādƀuta ta saŋ marutsuta,hana dūta yékana tĕkā mĕné ṙ-hiḍĕp,kadi maṅkanèn uni makin ta yānitir*8:101:809*

wahu mèh umĕtwa ta ƀaṭāra ƀāskara,makucĕm wulan kadi wulat nikaŋ laṅit,kalaran manon alara rūkṣa kāsyasiḥ,milu téki duḥka mawĕnĕs tikaŋ śaśī*8:102:810*

nayawit widagđa sira saŋ marutsuta,maḍĕmit sawut sira sawèt nikaŋ naya,tumulaṙ-tulaṙ sira lumumpat iŋ kayu,kumĕtĕṙ-kĕtĕṙ tika wugat-wugat nira*8:103:811*

Umulat sirèŋ lĕmah anon ta yānaṅis,wwaṅ akūŋ sĕḍĕŋ malara tībra kāsyasiḥ,kadi rūpa niŋ priyawijāya duḥkita,A-ha dèwi liŋ nira saniśꞓayèŋ manaḥ*8:104:812*

maṅiṅĕt-Iṅĕt maṅujiwat sirāṙ wulat,mĕtu kawrayan nira tumuṅkul aṅjĕṅok,masĕkĕl tikā hati nirāṙ wulat masiḥ,lara niŋ kasaḥ priyawiyoga liŋ nira*8:105:813*

makurū ṅ-awak raga-ragékanaŋ Igā,kuruṅañ jugāraṅ anipis yayénaṅit,Ikanaŋ manaḥ kadi manuk jugéniṅu,kinuruŋ kinuṅkuṅ aṅaraŋ makin makuŋ*8:106:814*

gĕluṅan masāk ya makusut kĕnèŋ lĕbu,magĕlöh apan maguliṅan rikaŋ lĕmaḥ,sumaput pwa yé muꝁa nirākilāputiḥ,kadi candra pūṙṇnama kĕnèŋ lamad-lamad*8:107:815*

hana saṅgrahé sira Umaḥ hĕmās tuwi,tar ahūrakĕn ya gumuliŋ sirèŋ lĕmaḥ,kadi duḥka saŋ raǥusutāṙ hanèṅ alas,hiḍĕpĕṅkwa liŋ nira mataŋnya taṙ lĕgö*8:108:816*

baribin manaḥ niran inambulan nikaŋ,kala rākṣasī tan anumāna riŋ kasaḥ,maṅidīdi mèdi ri siraŋ kĕnĕŋ Unĕŋ,Awijaḥ mamid maṅujiwat Alaḥ puji*8:109:817*

Umulat sirékanaṅ agupyan aṅdĕlö,mawisik-wisik mrisakiti-ŋ wiyoga wèḥ,I lukān iké tan anumāna duṙjjana,ya ta liŋ nirojar-ujar iŋ dalĕm hati*8:110:818*

maṅisĕk-k-isĕk sira sĕsök tikaŋ hati,Ibĕkan Unĕŋ Ika manaḥ nirāsĕkĕl,Ikanaŋ taṅis juga lanā hané sira,kadi gaṙbƀa wālaka raré wahū mĕtu*8:111:819*

nda tatīta saŋ malara kaṣṭa duḥkita,daśadéśa māwa ya mawās huwus katon,ƀuwanāntarāla malilaŋ hilaŋ pĕtĕŋ,hati saŋ wiyoga winĕgilnya yan pasuk*8:112:820*

sira saŋ daśānana gĕlāna taŋ manaḥ,Inusī nikaŋ wiṣaya lèn unĕŋ lanā,dadi śīǥra yaṙ laku marèŋ taman muwaḥ,maluyāmujuk-mujukanéki don ira*8:113:821*

saḍatĕŋ nirār ujar i-dèwi jānakī,Ari mꜽŧilī lalu lalista ri ṅhulun,narakāku tāri yadiyan mrĕṣodita,kita tāri kéwala gumantuṅ iŋ mata*8:114:822*

janakātmajātiśaya maṅkin aṅlaré,sa Ulaḥta tan malalisāta liṅkwari,nya laraṅku dènta kalalaḥ lĕhöŋ pĕjaḥ,kaśulāpa tan hana Asiḥ ta ri ṅhulun*8:115:823*

sira saŋ daśānana nahan ta liŋ nira,mawuwus gĕlāna sira kāma mohita,maṇiratna ƀūṣaṇa Asiŋ saménaka,ya pawèḥ nirāmujuki maṅgiraŋ-giraŋ*8:116:824*

janakātmajātiśaya satya riŋ priya,Ikanaŋ manaḥ sŧiti taman parĕŋ wanèḥ,kadi paṙbwaténugah-ugaḥ nikaŋ Aṅin,kṣaṇamātra tañcala manaḥ nirāpagĕḥ*8:117:825*

Umuwaḥ manantwa sira saŋ daśānana,humĕnĕŋ Ataḥ janakarājaputrikā,dadi héwa citta nira saŋ daśānana,ndan ikaŋ gĕlĕŋ ya ta ginūḍa tan katon*8:118:826*

janakātmajāpa ta guṇā ni ko-t hĕnĕŋ,tar ikā dumèh aku Umarya mojara,Apa tan salaḥ Iki Ulaḥku liṅkwari,prakrĕtiṅku rākṣasa tinūtku tan kalèn*8:119:827*

kalawan n-anuŋ matakutèṅ ulaḥ salaḥ,Ikanaŋ tĕbĕŋ-tĕbĕṅ inaknya māđyama,kami kām huwus warĕg amukti riŋ jagat,mari yan prayatna riṅ ulaḥ salaḥ kĕna*8:120:828*

ya mataŋnya tañ jalani haywa tālara,tamataṙ pahīṅan ikanaŋ Aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn,Apa saṅśayéry-aku jayèŋ jagat kabèḥ,tuwi ƀaktya tāku ri kitāri Adyana*8:121:829*

nyaṅ umaḥ maṇik kita sinaṅgrahérikā,ta turū yaŧāsuka lawan ṅhulun Ari,lalu tan matīs maguliṅan kitèŋ lĕmaḥ,ri ḍaḍaṅku t-uṅgu ta turū saménaka*8:122:830*

ri hatiṅku t-uṅgu ta kunĕŋ misan-misan,mara tan madoḥ ry-aku Asiŋ parankwari,Aŧawī hatinta kahanan hanā ṅhulun,mara tan madoḥ ri kita nitya hé priyā*8:123:831*

pituhun pwa tāri sawuwusku yukti ya,Apa tan wanèḥ kita siwinku kāsiha,kalawan huripta saꝑalān paréry-aku,raǥuputra kiṅkiṅĕn apā guṇā nikā*8:124:832*

yadiyan hanoliha susun pamö hĕnī,ya Ikā manĕmwa hayu dé ni rāǥawa,ya mataŋnya haywa ta wihaŋ ry-ujaṙkwari,Aku kéwalékana siwinta rākṣakā*8:125:833*

yadiyan kĕnéka pasiwinta ri ṅhulun,kita ratwa niŋ triƀuwanāta dèṅkwari,Ikanaŋ taṅis Apa guṇanya târyakĕn,Aku toṣađā lumipura-ŋ putĕk hati*8:126:834*

nya balaṅku rākṣasa baśā kitériya,sapininta yékana pawèha ni ṅhulun,yadiyan hyaṅ indra kaharĕpta séwakā,Atiwāhya ménak ari yan ya kahyuna*8:127:835*

Iti nā wuwus nira ta saŋ daśānana,janakātmajātiśaya đīra niśꞓaya,raǥuputra kéwala hané manaḥ nira,sumahuṙ sa niṣṭura Ujaṙ nirāpĕḍĕs*8:128:836*

kala đik daśānana si rāwaṇāđama,jaḍa ḍūṙtta moha ya piśāca kaśmala,yadiyan paḍāna sira saŋ raǥūttama,Apa ko malap ry-aku sĕḍĕŋnya tan hana*8:129:837*

yadiyan prawīra kamu wāni riŋ raṇa,ndya mataŋnya taṙ papagakĕn sirèṅ alas,syapa śūra maŋ­raƀasa yan taya-ŋ musuḥ,ya ta hīna śakti tĕṅĕranmu duṙjjana*8:130:838*

tĕṅĕranyu yan wĕdi-wĕdī raṇāṅgaṇa,paradāra kéwala manaḥmu taṙ wanèḥ,rinĕṅöṅku dé nikana saŋ jayèŋ musuḥ,Ikanaŋ tawan ya ta winèḥ yaŧāsuka*8:131:839*

Apa paŋ­rĕṅömu I-siraŋ raǥūttama,takarin sirékana đanuṙđarèŋ jagat,puruṣottamāṅśa sira déwamānuṣa,niyatāta ko pĕjaha dé nirèŋ raṇa*8:132:840*

yadiyan palaywa masĕnötanèŋ tasik,mahiranđra duṙgga giri gahwarā kunĕŋ,gawayanta sūkṣma ta Awak-mwatīndriya,luputāta dūran ika dé nirèŋ raṇa*8:133:841*

Aŧawā yadin wĕgila riŋ praƀūttama,ratu śaktimānta ya ta liŋmu Āśrayan,tuwi tan panĕmwa śaraṇā nrĕpodđata,mapaga praƀāwa nira saŋ raǥūttama*8:134:842*

paraméśwarātiśaya śakti riŋ jagat,tuwi dadya saŋ raǥusutomapag sira,kimuta-ŋ surāsura manuṣya rākṣasa,panahĕn pisan niyata yan pĕjaḥ kabèḥ*8:135:843*

lalu kasyasiḥmu lumawan sirātukar,laku tām panĕmbah i-narāṙyya rāǥawa,sira śūra taṙ papaḍa riŋ parakrama,yadi taṙ panĕmbaha Awās ta ko pĕjaḥ*8:136:844*

Iti nā sahuṙ nira ta dèwi jānakī,wĕkasan madĕg ta sira saŋ daśānana,maṅunus tĕwĕk tudiṅi dèwi jānakī,mĕlĕlö wulat nira mahāṅgĕmĕṙ-gĕmĕr*8:137:845*

janakātmajā taṅa-taṅāparan n-iké,kadi mrĕtyu muṅgu ri taṅanku ƀīṣaṇa,sabarin ya tan pamatihé si rāwaṇa,niyatān tibānya ri gulūnyu sāhasa*8:138:846*

ri huwus nirāṅgĕmĕr ahos ikaŋ hati,Umuliḥ marèŋ nagara kéraṅan sira,hana rākṣasī paḍa-paḍā tigaŋ Atus,ya kinon irāṅgĕmĕra śīǥra yaṙ tĕka*8:139:847*

paḍa kapwa sāhasa parĕŋ maṅĕmbuli,mawuwus mamātyana kabèḥnya maṅgĕmĕr,janakātmajātiśaya niṙƀayā-ŋ manaḥ,humĕnĕŋ suniśꞓala tumon ya sāhasa*8:140:848*

hana rākṣasī Atiśayèŋ mahāṙdđika,saꝑalān anak nira ta saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,trijaṭā ṅaranya ya Amoǥa kāsihan,ya rumākṣa dèwi janakātmajèŋ taman*8:141:849*

tudiṅīkanaŋ Ađama rākṣasī kabèḥ,Apa donmu koŋ kala kabèḥmu duṙjjana,sira tan padoṣa mapasaḥ lawan priya,sira patyanamwa lalu đūṙtta niṙǥrĕṇa*8:142:850*

tuwi satya taṙ papaḍa riŋ patibrata,saꝑalān siwin huluna tāku dé nira,yadiyan sahāsa ta manaḥ-mwamātyana,niyatāku mātya rumuhun sakè sira*8:143:851*

trijaṭā nahan ya ta wuwusnya niṣṭura,rikanaŋ maṅĕmbuli muliḥ ya kéraṅan,kawĕkas ta saŋ janakarājaputrikā,trijaṭā ya téka tan adoḥ saké sira*8:144:852*

ya ta sāđu dibya winaraḥ nirèŋ lara,kalawan Unĕŋ nira ri saŋ raǥūttama,mwaṅ asiḥ nirèŋ priya ya téka pājarĕn,ya winaṙṇnanā nira samantarānaṅis*8:145:853*

trijaṭāri haywa Upahāsa ri ṅhulun,ndak ajaṙ kité lara ni tībra duḥkita,hrĕdayaṅku śīṙṇna ya dinagđa riŋ Unĕŋ,sinarik nikaŋ wiđiwaśāku kāsyasiḥ*8:146:854*

kita kanyakāri tamatan wruh iŋ lara,Aku mānasān mapa manaḥta ri ṅhulun,saꝑalātisāđu wĕka niŋ mahāṙdđika,ya mataŋnya kājar ari tan hanā ṅ-iraŋ*8:147:855*

nya ta-takwa-takwana kitāri tā-rĕṅö,tat-anon rikaŋ ƀuwana tībra duḥkita,Umaḍāna téki kalaraṅku tan sipi,sinaranta riŋ wiđi huripku saṅsara*8:148:856*

nya tiké hiḍĕpku rika tan hanā juga,kadi pāpakaṙmma ni Awakku mandadi,A-ha mandaƀāgya mapasaḥ sĕḍĕŋ masiḥ,Aparanta ménaka Iké Awakkwari*8:149:857*

ndya kunĕŋ kaŧā carita pūṙwwakāla ya,Irikaŋ purāṇa Aji parwa kāṇḍa lèn,mapasaḥ gĕlāna rasa mātya tambayan,wĕkasan mapaṅguh aduluṙ lawan sĕnĕŋ*8:150:858*

ya tikā saménaka rĕṅönku lālanan,maluyākwapaṅguha ƀaṭāra māsiha,mahurip kariḥ sira kunèŋ paḍāṅunĕŋ,yadiyan pĕjaḥ nrĕpati hāḥ ndya mājara*8:151:859*

syapa déwa māsiha tĕkāwaraḥ kunĕŋ,ndya siraŋ mahāṙṣi rikanaŋ tapowana,lalu nisꝑalāŋ parahitèŋ jagat kabèḥ,tuwi déwatā wimuꝁa đik tamaṙ wulat*8:152:860*

Atitībra riŋ lara wimoha bāp aku,satinonkwasiŋ sarinĕṅöṅku yāṅlaré,tuwi baṅsi kinnara ya kaṙṇnaśūla ya,lara niŋ wiyoga kadurus niroṣađa*8:153:861*

nya ta ya-ŋ paṅan Inum anékawaṙṇna ya,kadi tāmaṅan wiṣa pasuknya riŋ gulū,Ikanaŋ kulĕm kĕlu rikaŋ palaṅka lèn,kadi pañjarékana hiḍĕpkwalaḥ makūŋ*8:154:862*

baribin manaḥku mulat iŋ sĕkaṙ marūm,suka tāpuluŋ jĕnu suganđa Utkata,paḍa maŋlaréki sahananya niṙguṇa,magawé prapañca ya mawèh unĕŋ magöŋ*8:155:863*

kapanānta nora ta kunĕŋ Ikèṅ unĕŋ,mananā manaḥku manasaṙ manāŋ lanā,manaranta saŋ madana mèdi maŋlaré,mamanaḥ sirāmanasi maŋ­ruraḥ hati*8:156:864*

hati niŋ wiyoga juga tībra yāgĕsĕŋ,dadi kaṣṭa dé ni śara saŋ manoƀawa,pariƀūta đuṙtta kadi ƀūta yan tamé,hrĕdayātutuṙ katutupan rajaḥ tamaḥ*8:157:865*

tamataṙ wruh īŋ Asih atīta niṙǥrĕṇa,sira śatru niŋ ƀuwana sūkṣma tan katon,kusumāyuđā nira tajĕm ya soṙ taji,ya panaḥ nirāŋ jaya-jayèŋ jagattraya*8:158:866*

mapa déwa manmaŧa kitāŧa mānuṣa,mara yan wruh iŋ lara marān kĕnĕŋ Unĕŋ,kadurus kitéki malarāku dènta wèḥ,pinanaḥ nda tan mati winèḥta monĕṅa*8:159:867*

pĕpĕk-opĕk-āpĕga manaḥku riŋ Umaḥ,tumurun matāku maturū hanèŋ lĕmaḥ,trijaṭā tumūt ry-aku lumālana-ŋ manaḥ,Anumāna riŋ priyawiyoga duḥkita*8:160:868*

pinipisnya taŋ sulur atīs lawan Usör,paṅasaḥnya caṇḍana Atīta śītala,siniramnya tékana Awakku toṣađā,tuwi tan suka pwaku makin Aliṅsaṅĕn*8:161:869*

Ikanaŋ Aśoka suƀagèŋ jagat kabèḥ,Atiśoƀa saśri ya hayunya riŋ maṅöb,ri sawèt ni tībra ni laraṅku tan suka,lara śoka téki hiniḍĕpku tan wanèḥ*8:162:870*

marurū sĕkaṙ nikaṅ aśoka śīṙṇna ya,tuwi pādapanya manĕḍĕŋ manohara,tinulup nikaŋ Anila cāla yomirir,kadi māsih iŋ kapanasan kĕnèṅ unĕŋ*8:163:871*

hana nāgapuṣpa paripūṙṇna riŋ halĕp,matatā manojña manĕḍèŋ rikaŋ natar,ri wĕruḥnya yaṙ wiraha duḥkitālara,puya kapwa yāsĕkar awèh unĕŋ magöŋ*8:164:872*

tan akūŋ manaḥkwi kusumāti Utkaṭa,magawé raras hati kucupnya komala,mrĕdu pallawanya ya mawèḥ lulut masiḥ,humilī ta luḥku maṅadĕg wulat riya*8:165:873*

tamatan tulaṙ haṅĕn-aṅĕnku kāsrĕpan,mulat iŋ śilātala I-soṙnya yālilaŋ,katutuṙ pwa tāmĕṅ-amĕṅ iŋ tapowana,kalawan priyottama naréndra rāǥawa*8:166:874*

maṅĕsaḥ tamolah aku moha mūṙcꞓita,balisaḥ masārabali mātya tan mati,tamataṙ kĕjĕp mataha-tāha taṙ padon,Apa tan tumon priya manaḥku duṙyyaśa*8:167:875*

nya ta lèn mawèh unĕṅ atīta maŋlaré,winarāwa naṣṭa maṅuyūyu riŋ kulĕm,kiniduŋnya taŋ priyawiyoga suswara,rumarab ta luḥku rumĕṅö ya kāsrĕpan*8:168:876*

Ah-a mandamāruta miriṙ ya śītala,marurū Ikaŋ kusuma dénya riŋ lĕmaḥ,mapupul ta ganđa nikanaŋ sĕkaṙ kabèḥ,tumĕñuḥ hatiṅku ya sumāṙ marèṅ iruŋ*8:169:877*

tamataṙ hanékana hiḍĕpku sakṣaṇa,wiparīta taṙ wĕnaṅ aśabda mohita,kumĕtĕṙ ta sanđi nikanaŋ Awak kabèḥ,Ikanaŋ hurip kadi ta līna tan hana*8:170:878*

Umiriṙ tikaŋ Aṅin atīs mawoṙ hrĕbuk,mapanas hiḍĕpku riya mimbuhiŋ Unĕŋ,kumĕlab hatiṅku rumĕṅö gĕrĕḥ malon,tumibā hudan kadi ya mèdi lot humuŋ*8:171:879*

{turagagati}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
riŋ śilātala rikāku tĕka maṅö,swāmi nitya ya lanā maṅaway-away,toḥ ndya tā ya hana tamba k-aṅĕn-aṅĕn,tā kadaŋ taṅisi tāwaku n-agati*8:172:880*

syuk nikaŋ jawĕh awèh unĕṅ amatī,hrū nikaŋ madana sūkṣma ya maṅani,rāḥ nikaŋ hati humīs mĕtu ri mata,mandamāruta miriṙ kadi matuluŋ*8:173:881*

hyaŋ Aṅin kita ta māsiha śaraṇā,sanmatèŋ kasiharĕp sĕḍĕṅ apasaḥ,saŋ raǥūttama riṅ āśrama warahĕn,yak hanèŋ kalana rākṣasa tinawan*8:174:882*

ƀakti niŋ Unĕṅ akūŋnya ta tĕkakĕn,mwaŋ laraṅku mapasaḥ Asama-sama,moǥa mātya yak adoḥ saka ri sira,nā ta pājara ri saŋ priyawiraha*8:175:883*

monĕṅ āmbĕk i-siraŋ ratu janaka,ƀakti ni ṅhulun agöŋ ya tĕkakĕna,liṅku yaṙ wiraha duḥkita tinawan,nā ta pājara rikā ta laku huwus*8:176:884*

haḥ bapaṅku Umapā ta lara nira,tībra māsih iṅ anak sira maharis,ḍū ndya tolahan ikin priyawiraha,yak hanèŋ kalana rākṣasa tinawan*8:177:885*

{mālinī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
krama lumaku ta kāliḥ riŋ prasāda ṙ-pamūjā,mapunagi ta ri saŋ hyaŋ prāṙŧanākèn naréndra,ri hurip a-nira lāwan ménakékaŋ paluṅguḥ,ya Ikana ta sināđyā tan kalèn dé nirāsiḥ*8:178:886*

{punaṙmmada}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
Anilātmajātiśaya haṙṣa yaṙ wulat,tumurun sakèŋ kayu ḍatĕŋ sirèŋ lĕmaḥ,ri harĕp nirāṙ wruha ta dèwi jānakī,maṅuliḥ-Uliḥ macaritā makin masö*8:179:887*

papasaḥ niraŋ raǥusuténucap nira,kalawan Unĕŋ nira Ināryakĕn wanèḥ,panaṅis nirèṅ alas umèt priyā nira,ya winaṙṇnanā nira ta saŋ marutsuta*8:180:888*

Umulat pwa dèwi janakātmajé sira,dadi saṅśayékana manaḥ nirāṙ wulat,wrayapéki mĕṅgĕp aṅuliḥ-huliḥ masö,si daśānanéki juga liṅkwamañcana*8:181:889*

ri lĕmĕḥnya kawruhana yan si rāwaṇa,ginawénya tékana Awaknya wānara,caritanya bañcana waliṅku tan tuhu,ri harèpnya yan syaṅana marya rākṣasa*8:182:890*

hana paŋ­rĕṅöṅku tuwi wrĕttamātra ya,pawaraḥ nikaŋ pinakacāra rākṣasa,wwara rakwa wānara kinon marā ry-aku,ndan asamƀawa-ŋ prawaga yan ya cārakā*8:183:891*

nya wanèḥ dumèh aku ya saṅśayérikā,Ikanaŋ nimitta sakatambay adƀuta,Uni niŋ manuk paḍa ya komala swara,ndan ikāpi rakwa śuƀadūta wākta ya*8:184:892*

ndya kunĕŋ Anuŋ mutusana-ŋ sinaṅśaya,Ikanā ri daṇḍaka Atīta riŋ madoḥ,mahĕlĕt tasik gunuṅ alas juraŋ trĕbis,priya rāǥawa ndya ta gamā nirān wruha*8:185:893*

I sĕḍĕŋkwi ṅūni Inalap ni rāwaṇa,tĕmu taŋ gunuŋ lwah adalĕm lawan n-alas,paḍa kapwa ƀīṣaṇa kabèh amānuṣa,Aliwat ta riŋ tasik asiŋ wiśāla ya*8:186:894*

rwa jugékanā wĕnaṅ alintaṅèn tasik,hyaṅ aṅin lawan garuḍa lèna tan hana,ndya ta hétu niŋ wray umarā tĕkéry-aku,ya mataŋnya bañcana ni rāwaṇékihĕn*8:187:895*

Iti nā ta saṅśaya niré dalĕm hati,mawiwéka wèt nira gĕlĕm binañcana,Umasö ta saŋ pinakadūta māruti,praṇatāṙ panĕmbah aśilāwaraḥ sira*8:188:896*

jaya dèwi haywa kita saṅśayèŋ manaḥ,pawanātmaja ṅhulun iké kinon marā,nrĕpaputra rāma makacāraké ṅhulun,lumawad hurip nrĕpasutā nahan ya don*8:189:897*

kahanān naréndra nrĕpaputra rāǥawa,rikanaŋ gunuŋ pratitanāma mālyawān,giri winđya yékana kidul nikāparö,wwara rĕṣyamūkagiri loṙnya tan madoḥ*8:190:898*

wahu mèḥ pitu-ŋ tabĕha ṅūni riŋ kulĕm,Umahas ṅhulun tĕka masuk rikaŋ taman,ri sĕḍĕŋ nikaŋ daśamuꝁāṅunus tĕwĕk,maharĕp ṅhulun pwa lumagé ya mapraṅa*8:191:899*

wahu mèh umaṅswa maṅaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn ṅhulun,ri Iwĕḥ nikaŋ wwaṅ amĕnaŋ rikaŋ raṇa,Ikanaŋ pakon ƀiṣama yan kasiđđa ya,ya dumèḥ ṅhulun wuruṅ umaṅswa maŋlagā*8:192:900*

{Āṙyyā}

wwara mitra rāka dèwī,saŋ sugrīwa ṅaran nira,ratu niŋ wré śakti tĕmĕn,sira kumon ṅhulun dūtā*8:193:901*

Umahas ṅhulun anusup,ri kaḍatwan umèt dèwī,mamriḥ ta ṅhulun maniñjo,nda tan paṅguḥ rikaŋ rajya*8:194:902*

makwèḥ tāpsarī kapaṅguḥ,sĕḍĕŋ rarā ta manojña,lawan rākṣasa makĕmit,wiparīta kabèḥ nidrā*8:195:903*

naranāŧa raǥusuta,glānākiṅkiŋ maṅĕn dèwī,wèt niṅ unĕŋ sirākurū,mataŋnyākon ṅhulun dūtā*8:196:904*

Inaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn nirākūŋ,ri tan pāṙꞓaya riŋ dūta,nya ta simsim nirāṙ pawèḥ,niré ṅhuluñ cihnā donya*8:197:905*

tuwi rāntĕn dèwi makūŋ,saŋ lakṣmaṇa śoka sira,magyā ta sirān parā ṅké,mātyanaŋ rāwaṇān mūṙkꝁa*8:198:906*

bala wānara Umaḍaŋ,mahöm makoliha-ŋ śatru,ya mataŋnyan dèwi t-aṅhèr,haywa gyā rākṣan huripta*8:199:907*

matakut ta ṅhulun ṅūni,sĕḍĕŋ ta mojar iŋ mūṙkꝁa,yukti puwiḥ biṣa tĕmĕn,lĕpas riŋ rākṣasa duṣṭa*8:200:908*

niyata-ŋ rāwaṇa pĕjaḥ,dé śrī rāma riŋ palagan,prāṇanya panahuranya,doṣanyan mālap ri dèwī*8:201:909*

mawĕkasa mahādèwī,ri sira saŋ raǥusuta,pĕpöṅĕn taya nikanaŋ,makĕmit ya huwus luṅhā*8:202:910*

kunaŋ sira rāka dèwī,kawĕkas rikaŋ mālyawān,sātus tahun ikanaŋ wé,sowé-sowé wèt nirāgyā*8:203:911*

nā liŋ nira saŋ hanūmān,dèwī sītā sirāśꞓaṙyya,rumĕṅö pawarah i-saŋ,marutsuta haṙṣacitta*8:204:912*

hé pawanātmaja t-aṅsö,tuṣṭāmbĕkwi dènta dūta,cūḍāmaṇiṅku ya téki,wĕhakĕna ri saŋ rāma*8:205:913*

lawan ta rékaṅku wanèḥ,cihnaṅku malara monĕŋ,ya ta wawan iki dènta,sinūṅakĕn i-saŋ rāma*8:206:914*

mwaŋ taṅguhi sira nihan,maṅanāturw-a haywākūŋ,taya soka ṅwaŋ maṅaraŋ,ṅhulun huwus wruḥ ri donya*8:207:915*

nahan tojaṙ mahādèwī,tan sandéha manaḥ nira,tumon simsim niraŋ rāma,ya dumèḥ sira niścaya*8:208:916*

marutsuta siromaṅsö,maṇik ya téka tinaṅgap,maṅañjali sirānĕmbaḥ,madĕg ta sira śīǥra ya*8:209:917*

manaḥ nira sahaṙṣātaḥ,huwus tumĕmu ri dèwī,wisāta maṅĕn-aṅĕn,ta sira ri sakamantyan*8:210:918*

nihan pinuji niŋ dūta,Ikaŋ tumĕmwa ri donya,Amètayasā yaśanya,Anuŋ taṅ adƀuta cihnā*8:211:919*

huwus ta yāku Umaṅguḥ,ri siraŋ janakaputrī,nda tan hana ya wanèhan,Anuṅ ayasā yaśaṅkwa*8:212:920*

Aśokawana ya téki,taman atiśaya riŋ lwā,ya téki raƀasanaṅkwa,kayunya ya ta śīṙṇnanĕn*8:213:921*

yadiyan hana masĕṅhit,ya tékana laganaṅkwa,pĕjaḥ pwa Ika ya dèṅku,yaśaṅku tuwi ya wrĕdđya*8:214:922*

{drutawilambita}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
Aŧa huwus nira māṅĕn-aṅĕn madĕg,raƀasa taŋ kayu rāmya rikaŋ taman,syapa ta rākṣasa wānya masö huwus,papagakĕnta si māruti liŋ nira*8:215:923*

{Aśwalalita}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :23:
pracalita puṣpa niŋ kayu rurū sarinya ya mĕlĕk kadi pwa ya kukus,kalawan ikaŋ palāśa tumibā sĕkaṙnya ya mabaŋ Akĕn hudan apuy,Ibĕkan ikaŋ lĕmaḥ kadi dilaḥnya riŋ pralayakāla ƀīṣaṇa katon,ruru kĕna lèn kidaŋ masasaran kadi pwa matakut manon hudan apuy*8:216:924*

#nawamas saṙggaḥ#
<kusumawicitra>:9
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
^9/1/921.
Aŧa ri sĕḍĕŋnyāñcalita nanā rūg,kayu nikaṅ udyānawana ya śīṙṇna,makaparapal pāŋnya ya paḍa sĕmpal,manuk umibĕṙ ǥūṙṇnita paḍa kagyat*9:1:925*

Ikaṅ akĕmit kādƀuta sahananya,dadi malayū riŋ nagara paranya,tĕka ya nikaŋ rājya paḍa manĕmbaḥ,ri suku niraŋ rāwaṇa dadi mojar*9:2:926*

tumaḍaha sojaṙ suraripunāŧa,wwara ya mahāwānara Awamāna,rumabaśa ṅ-udyānawana nanī rūg,Awu tĕmahanya-ŋ kusumawicitra*9:3:927*

Ikana daṅū déwata tuwi matwaŋ,kimuta Ikaŋ mānuṣa paḍa ƀakti,tatan ujarĕn wré Ađama ya tiṙyyak,kim api mĕné wānara ya tan atwaŋ*9:4:928*

dinakara tīkṣṇāmanasi tĕṅaḥ ṅ wé,kadi tan atis ṅ-ātiśaya ya tīkṣṇa,tĕka ri taman nāŧa tan apanas ya,dumadak atis twaŋnya ya makadéya*9:5:929*

hana ta haṅiŋ séḍuṅ atiśayèŋ drĕs,kayu kahawā dénya paḍa rĕbaḥ rūg,tĕka ya riṅ udyāna mari ya mādrĕs,Alah atakut komala ta gatinya*9:6:930*

wulan awĕlū pūṙṇnama ya hana ṅkā,rikaṅ amawāsyā tuwi ta ya māwā,satata tan aṅluḥ maṅurugi téja,sumuluhi ṅ-udyānawana gawénya*9:7:931*

kaŧam api maṅké lalu wiparīta,wrayađama jātinya tuwitan atwaŋ,niyata taman ƀūpati ya ta śīṙṇna,dadi ta wamānāt hĕnĕṅakĕna-ŋ wré*9:8:932*

Aŧa ri huwus niŋ makĕmit anĕmbaḥ,daśamuꝁa sakrođa sira kabāṅan,dadi Inatag rākṣasabala maṅswa,mĕjahana saŋ mārutasuta donya*9:9:933*

paḍa ya madĕg sātus-iwu sĕnadđa,paraśu lipuŋ ꝁaḍga ya winawanya,palu-palu laṅkap watu lawan umban,ya winawa niŋ wīra parĕṅ umaṅkat*9:10:934*

tĕka ya riṅ udyāna paḍa ya magyā,kadi ta gĕrĕḥ ǥūṙṇnita ya gumĕntĕr,pawanasuta krođa wadana hūmrĕŋ,jalada si sambaṙttaka juga moni*9:11:935*

saha bala taŋ rākṣasa kaharan lwaḥ,tĕka gumuruḥ ǥora kadi sĕḍĕŋ wāḥ,pawanasutāṅkĕn jalađi suđīra,pratidina taŋ wāḥ tĕka riya tan sök*9:12:936*

babahaniṅ udyānawana ya māwān,hana katimaŋ gĕŋnya satakuraŋ twas,dadi Umanèk saŋ Anilasuta ṅkā,humarĕpakĕn rākṣasabala māṅsö*9:13:937*

paḍa ya tumaṇḍĕm hana ta humaṇḍĕm,hana maṅarug rodra paḍa tumĕṅhā,wugari hilaŋ yéka makahalintaŋ,hana mamanaḥ lèn manuligi maṇḍuk*9:14:938*

Ikana kabèḥ tan hana maṅani ṅkā,makapalĕyö hrū wugari kawaṅsul,Arug apupug kapwa kapĕluk āpĕs,wulu nira tuṅgal tuwi taya siṅsal*9:15:939*

hana ta kayū candana madawāgöŋ,paḍa ya sakol göŋnya malurus atwas,ya ta ḍinawut saŋ prawaga hanūmān,pamalu nirèŋ wwil mati ya kariṅkĕl*9:16:940*

hana sumirat rāḥnya lawan utĕknya,makakĕrĕpĕk kapwa rĕmĕk igānya,kaguliṅ ikaŋ wwil pinalu gulūnya,maṅutahakĕn rāḥ mati kagulimpaŋ*9:17:941*

hana sipi-simpiṙ saꝑala mamūka,prihawak aṅiṅkis lumaku rumuṅkuŋ,Ikanaṅ umaṇḍĕm paḍa ya kahaṇḍĕm,pinalu pisan sūh ikana pupūnya*9:18:942*

hana kabubat bĕntis ika wĕtĕŋnya,paḍa ya tĕḍas rodra mĕtu Ususnya,Ikaṅ alaras yālara kapaliṇḍĕs,pinalu larasnyān kapalu wĕhaŋnya*9:19:943*

hana ta wanèḥ wwil wĕdi-wĕdi hīna,ya ta Inusī san pawanasutādrĕs,kĕna walakaŋnyān pinalu karaṅkaŋ,mawuṅu rumĕṅkĕŋ lumaku rumuṅkuŋ*9:20:944*

hana ta luput śīǥra ta ya lumumpat,lumaku muliḥ tan hana ya manoliḥ,kadi ta kidaŋ siṅha ya ta musī ya,makabalasaḥ duṙbbala paḍa mosaḥ*9:21:945*

hana ta wanèḥ rākṣasabala wīra,ya ta mapuliḥ śīǥra tĕka sĕnadđa,gaja raŧa lāwan kuda ya dalanya,Atiraƀasāṅĕmbuli tĕka maṅduk*9:22:946*

makin agalak saŋ pawanasutāṅhrĕŋ,jumĕṅat ikékū nira madawāgöŋ,Umaṅun umuṙ~gaŋ wulu nira maṅkak,maluy umanèk riŋ katimaṅ anumpak*9:23:947*

maṅamah-amaḥ rākṣasa ya tumĕṅhā,watu sakĕbo göŋ ni pamugarinya,ḍaḍa nira saŋ māruti kĕna paṇḍĕm,makakĕrĕtĕg ndām tan alara dénya*9:24:948*

tĕḍuni tikaŋ wwil maraŧa kagöman,pinalu nirèŋ ḍaṇḍa mati kariṅkĕl,makabalasaḥ sāraŧi ya lumumpat,Umĕgil awaknyān pati ni tuhanya*9:25:949*

hana ta wanèḥ wwil makuda tumandaŋ,mapulih asĕṅhit mamawa krĕtāla,salahasa méḥ mamraṅa ya ginĕgwan,mati kapisan tan pabiṣa tinampyal*9:26:950*

{toṭaka}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
hana lén aliman ya dalanya masö,binulusnya luput sira śīǥra mĕsat,matakut ya tumon sira sāhasika,tumĕḍun ya sakèṅ aliman malayū*9:27:951*

pinupuḥ nira kumƀa nikaŋ Aliman,sumirat ta Utĕknya matanya mulū*9:28:952*
pinupak nira téka gaḍiŋnya tikèl,kadi siṅha sirādƀuta rodra dahat*9:29:953*

bala rākṣasa śūra padāti masö,sumiliḥ mapuliḥ malĕmöḥ suruda,laju hīna nikaŋ malayū Umuliḥ,ya ta liŋnya maṅĕmbuli kapwa mamūk*9:30:954*

{citrālaya}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
mamĕkul ya sadaṙppa hana ta manĕwĕk,pinĕrĕp tinĕkĕk siniku ya dinĕdĕl,binubat riṅ ikū kumĕbu-kĕbu tibā,mati tan hana mamyati matitih atap*9:31:955*

hana śéṣa nikaŋ mati ya ta malayū,sipi tan kapisan siniku juga pisan,tinukupnya hatinya makĕsĕl ahĕnĕk,mananaŋ manaṅis tĕka mawara-waraḥ*9:32:956*

A-ha nāŧa nanā sahana-hana mami,tuwi sāyuđa sāśwaraŧagaja kabèḥ,paḍa śakti daṅū tuwi taya mamalĕs,wray apéki kunĕŋ saraƀasa ya biṣa*9:33:957*

Aŧa sāmpun anĕmbah ikanaṅ alayū,makin udđata saŋ daśamuꝁa mabutĕŋ,bala mantri kinon ira mapulihana,tamataṙ pamihaŋ lumaku saha bala*9:34:958*

jayaśatru daṅū lagi maṅalahakĕn,tahu riŋ raṇa sāyuđa Asama-sama,hana konta kalā ya ta winawa nikā,tĕka matri humuŋ prakaṭa kadi gĕlap*9:35:959*

makuwal paṅawaknya mabukĕt abikal,kadi paṙbwata ƀīṣaṇa kagiri-giri,kadi méǥa kumisnya mahirĕṅ asukĕt,masalit ta sihuŋnya kadi ta ya kilat*9:36:960*

masĕluk pamatanya dumilah awĕlū,kadi sūṙyya sahasra kiraṇa kumĕñar,mapanas kadi bahni ya malatu-latu,makusut ta halisnya kadi ta ya kukus*9:37:961*

muririŋ mararöm surawara Umulat,pawanātmaja đīratara tan atakut,kadi siṅha manon gaja sĕḍĕṅ agalak,tamataṙ kagĕmĕṙ sira makin umasö*9:38:962*

lumĕkas ya maṅĕmbuli tĕka sumahab,maṅalā ya maṅonta hana manuriga,manuhuk ya mañakra hana ya mamalu,paḍa sāhasikākira-kira-r-ahata*9:39:963*

Anilātmaja niṙƀaya pinarĕbutan,pinutĕṙ nira taŋ palu-palu ya satal,Umasö manalandaṅi sira mamalu,marĕmuk ya Asiŋ kĕna mati kapisan*9:40:964*

hana mèḥ mati yādƀuta ya katatakut,paḍa kapwa maṅohan awurahan awū,kadi paṙbwata ƀīṣaṇa juga ya rubuḥ,Ibĕkan prĕŧiwī gaganatala pĕpĕt*9:41:965*

ri pĕjaḥnya kabèḥ śawa ya maguliṅan,sagunuŋ juga göŋnya paḍa ta ya kanin,Umilī mĕtu rāḥnya ri muꝁa ya mabāŋ,kadi đātu sakèŋ giriwiwara mulĕk*9:42:966*

{citraraśmi}
– – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :19:
sāmpun śīṙṇnā rākṣasabala maṅadĕg saŋ hanūmān sadaṙppa,riŋ Udyāna ṅkān ya mara rumaƀasā-ŋ pārijātātiśoƀa,māwān pāŋnyāgöŋ kadi ta ya himawān méru mās witnya téja,kwèḥ pāŋnyomĕṇḍuḥ paḍa ya satakuraŋ pāŋ ni pāŋnyān samèŋ göŋ*9:43:967*

gantiŋ kuŋkuŋ nopura kanaka kilatbāhu lèn brahmasūtra,simsim mwaŋ cūḍāmaṇi ya ta pinakawwaḥnya néka prakāra,lunsiṙ déwāṅga pracalita ya mabāŋ lèñ jamaŋ ronya kumlab,mwaŋ mutyāhārojwalita ya mamilĕt pāŋnya yékā pralĕmba*9:44:968*

saśrī taŋ wwad-wad kanaka ya mamilĕd pāŋ nikaŋ pārijāta,salwiṙ niŋ kĕmbaŋ ya ta pinakasĕkaṙnyéka māmbö sumāṙ mrik,tuñjuŋ tañjuŋ cāmpaka suraƀi puḍak mandarāśoka mĕṇḍur,nĕp punnāga mwaŋ kurawa Asana lèn dālima śrīgaḍiŋ poḥ*9:45:969*

yékānuŋ śīṙṇnān rinaƀasa mananā dé niraŋ bāyuputra,sĕmpal pāŋnyāgöŋ ya ta makabarubuḥ puḥ gumĕntĕṙ tibānya,liṇḍū taŋ lĕṅkā kadi ya lĕbura lūd ǥūṙṇnita-ŋ rākṣasāwū,cihnanyān ƀraṣṭā sahana-hana nikaŋ rākṣasa krūrakaṙmma*9:46:970*

tatkālanyan śīṙṇna kayu-kayu riṅ udyāna dé saŋ hanūmān,maṅkat ta sy-akṣa prakaśita ya Anak saŋ daśāsyāđirāja,śūrèŋ praŋ wīrātiśaya ya ta mahāśaktimāntāđikāra,gaṇḍéwanyāgöŋ ya ta winawa nikā mwaŋ panaḥnyāstra tīkṣṇa*9:47:971*

ry-aṅkatnyān ton taŋ kayu-kayu mananā rūg rĕbaḥ pāŋnya sĕmpal,wĕṇṭaŋ laṅkapnyān tujun ata sira saŋ mārutīṅ aṙdđacandra,tātan madwékām lagi ta ya mapisan yaṙ kĕnāŋ śatru dénya,tātaṙ pawyat saŋ bayusuta kĕna ta pyaḥ nirā ṅkān tĕka syuḥ*9:48:972*

krođékāmbĕk saŋ pawanasuta sira krūra maṅsö tumandaŋ,sāmbut tékaŋ pāŋ ya ta pamalu nirèŋ rākṣasa sy-akṣa śīǥra,rĕñcĕm bāhunyān pinalu ya kapisan mūṙcꞓitāmriḥ lumumpat,moruk méraŋ mūṙ mari ta ya sakarĕŋ riŋ raŧa ṅkān pararyan*9:49:973*

ménak pwékāmbĕknya mari ya mahuyaŋ śīǥra gumrit raŧanya,sāmbut tékaŋ hrū Umaluya ta manaḥ saŋ hanūmān riṅ astra,mākrĕp ta hrūnyān kadi ta ya hinatĕp lwiṙ niṅ ākāśa dénya,kĕmbaŋ tulyanyān tĕka ri ḍaḍa nirĕŋ māruti syuḥ wiśīṙṇna*9:50:974*

maṅkin sakrođān kapalupuy ikanaŋ hrū tĕkap saŋ hanūmān,maṅsö sy-akṣa ṅkān muwah amanahi riŋ Astra saṅhārarāja,tātandwan tandaŋ saṅ anilasuta yaṙ duk tikaŋ sy-akṣa riŋ paŋ,sĕmpal bāhunyān kĕna mati kapisan rāḥnya muñcaṙ ya mūṙcca*9:51:975*

{ƀujaṅgaprayāta}
⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
huwusnyān pĕjaḥ sy-akṣa dé saŋ hanūmān,lumumpat sirè sāgara ṅkān parādyus,ri dényān maṅèl wèt ni sowé nirāpraŋ,mataŋnyāṙ parèŋ sāgarān maṇḍi moǥa*9:52:976*

huwus trĕpti madyus mĕsat śīǥra luṅhā,maluy riŋ taman rūgakĕn pārijāta,kayuḥ pāŋnya sĕmpal rurū ronya lumrā,lawan wwaḥnya kégū kaböbĕl tibā bāp*9:53:977*

sĕkaṙ niŋ Aśokākusut sāk sarinya,rujit śīṙṇna tātan paśèṣa-ŋ palāśa,lawan nāgapuṣpāpĕpĕs pāŋnya māpés,pukaḥ puḥ Ikaŋ poḥ papal ron i-pāŋnya*9:54:978*

gaḍuŋ soṇḍuṅ-uṇḍuŋ Umĕṇḍuŋ katuṇḍuŋ,karūgan kapuṇḍuŋ Umĕṇḍuḥ ya kāṇḍĕḥ,maḍĕmpĕl maḍām wwaḥnya soṇḍuḥ ya koṇḍuḥ,kasaṇḍuŋ sĕḍĕŋ saŋ hanūmān lumumpat*9:55:979*

nanā tékanaŋnyū kĕna-ŋ naṅka dénya,cacal caṇḍanāpan kĕné wit nikaŋnyū,Anak niŋ manuk glāna monĕŋ ya moni,manuŋsuŋ Inaŋnyan Umaṅsö manambĕr*9:56:980*

{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:11: = :39:
wuru-wuru kawurug rikaŋ wrĕkṣa mawwaḥ wwara wwawwa yāwū lawan wūt mawūŋ jīwa-jīwāwĕdi wwawwa yāwok umūṙ mwaŋ lutuŋ,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:11: = :39:
kaḍawa wuru kutut katūt yān tumūt riŋ Atat yātatā yātakut n-ton ikaŋ lomaśa mriḥ mibĕṙ mwaŋ mayūrāduluṙ syuŋ swarī,
{daṇḍaka}
