Umulat umututuŋ lutuŋ tuṅga-tuṅgal manuŋtuŋ ri tuŋtuŋ nikaŋ gintuṅantaṙ paṅan wwaḥnya kéṅin-n-iṅin,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:9: = :33:
ƀramara mara mariŋ rikaŋ kaṙṇnikārārurū rūg karūgan paḍāntĕn sarinyéniriṙ dé nikaŋ mārutā*9:57:981*

{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:24: = :78:
saƀaya masasaran śaśanyān saśokānusup ṅkā ri soṙ niŋ saruṇyārĕṇĕb ronya mākrĕp sukĕt witnya śūnyomasuk taŋ śaśa ṅkāṅikiṙ mīs awaknyomahā yāṅrĕpāṅhèṙ hana pwéki kañcil kumuñcaŋ lumumpat mĕsat taŋ śaśān śīǥra kagyat kabèḥnyālayū,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:23: = :75:
camara-mararakan parĕŋ yālayū līla yālon lumonlon lakunyābalĕm miṅgut-iṅgut liman glāna Abwat maṅaṇḍuŋ wĕtĕŋnyān palaṇḍuŋ Ikātan wĕnaŋ yan maṅèl kāpwa mĕṅgaḥ Umaṅguḥ gulūnyā ṅĕliḥ lolya molaḥ Ilatnyāmalāṅèl mĕhāḥ,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:23: = :75:
saraƀa-saraƀasan mĕsat śīǥra luṅhā milu-ŋ tiṅgiliŋ tan Ilu-ŋ tan lĕgö niścayāpan subadđāṅrasuk riŋ sukĕt héwa riŋ laṇḍak amriḥ makuṇḍaŋ priyā maŋ­rĕpātaḥ ri soṙ niŋ puḍak döḥ Ah-o hīna yā liŋ nikaŋ tiṅgiliŋ siḥ nikaŋ tīṅaluŋ,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:24: = :78:
pati susu-susup iŋ sukĕt rūmnya rūkṣāpasaḥ kāsyasiḥ satwa sakwèḥnyanuṅgwiŋ taman maṅkana wwa-wwahan kapwa héman-manisnyénigū saŋ hanūmān babaryan tibā riŋ lĕmaḥ kapwa kāmbaḥ humis duḥnyaduḥkānaṅis lwiṙnya yāpan salaḥ lwiṙ rĕmĕk yārĕmuk*9:58:982*

{ƀujaṅgaprayāta}
⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
huwus saŋ hanūnān rumūg pārijāta,mararyan sirèŋ hèŋ niṅ udyāna kulwan,humèṙhèr ikaŋ rākṣasānuŋ masĕṅhit,hanāmbĕk nikā saŋ daśāsyāṅlagāna*9:59:983*

yadin rāwaṇāsĕṅhitātaḥ marā ṅké,lagānaṅkwa tĕṇḍasnya yékolihaṅkwa,ya pawwat-wwataṅkwè siraŋ rāma tuṣṭā,lawan dèwi sītā ya sāhaṙṣa dèṅku*9:60:984*

nahan liŋ nirāṅĕn-Aṅĕn tan masowé,tĕkā rājaputréndrajit ꝁyāti riŋ rāt,Anak saŋ daśasyottamèŋ śaktimānta,praśāstèŋ jagat śūra saŋ méǥanāda*9:61:985*

yatékā masĕṅhit pĕjaḥ sy-akṣa ṅūni,pratijñānya saŋ bāyuputrolihanya,tatan madwa maṅsö lawan n-āyuđanya,titaḥ téka wadwānya wīnāni-wāni*9:62:986*

raŧanyādƀutāgöŋ ya malwā ya mādrĕs,lawan tuṅgaṅan saṅkĕpan yéka mīṙ ya,panaḥ tīkṣṇa tan kraḥ Umuṅgwī raŧanya,lawan rākṣasāŋ-rakṣa yékā panĕṇḍas*9:63:987*

tĕkanyèŋ taman ǥūṙṇnitāṅin-Aṅinya,makin śīṙṇna ṅ-udyāna kégū sĕkaṙnya,mulat saŋ hanūmān umaṅsö manuŋsuŋ,sinambé niraŋ Indrajit śīǥra mojar*9:64:988*

Asö ko durācāra sakwèḥmu duṣṭa,papag tékihĕn dūta saŋ rāmadéwa,sakakwèḥmwi lĕṅkā wiśīṙṇnā ta dèṅku,ya tan ƀaktya ri śrī mahārāja rāma*9:65:989*

nahan liŋ niraŋ mārutī méǥanāda,Umaṇḍĕm ya lāwan balanyātirodra,parĕŋ yomanaḥ saŋ hanūmān sadaṙppa,n-arāraḥ sirèŋ hrūnya nārācaƀalla*9:66:990*

malaṇḍĕp Ikā hrūnya mākrĕp tibānya,nda tan pamyatī saŋ hanūmān tĕka syuḥ,kadīkaŋ hudan riŋ gunuŋ kwèḥ watunya,wiśīṙṇnāpasaḥ yaṙ tibā tan paśéṣa*9:67:991*

saka kwèḥ ni wadwā niraŋ méǥanāda,mahāǥora rūpānđakārātidaṙppa,Umaṅsö pwa yāṅĕmbuli ƀraṣṭaśīṙṇna,hanūmān sirāditya sākṣāt musus ya*9:68:992*

makin daṙppa saŋ mārutī ṙ-pāṅalāpā,ya paṅduk nirè rākṣasāsiŋ Umaṅsö,gĕlāna-ŋ balān ton sirānékarūpa,kapūhan kabèḥnyādƀutānon sirākwèḥ*9:69:993*

hanānuṅga-nuṅgal hanāsèwu saṅꝁya,Inaṅsö lumumpat riṅ ākāśa r-uṅgu,tumūt maŋlayaŋ rākṣasātyanta śīǥra,maluy riŋ lĕmaḥ saŋ hanūmān umiṅsor*9:70:994*

parĕŋ yan tĕḍun tūtakĕn saŋ hanūmān,tĕkanyèŋ lĕmaḥ kapwa maṅsö tumandaŋ,muwaḥ saŋ hanūmān mĕsat sèp ikaŋ wwil,tumĕṅhā kabèḥnyā ṅĕsaḥ kapwa képwan*9:71:995*

makin tībra yānliḥ pwa ya glāna mosaḥ,siraŋ mārutī pöṅakĕn téka ṅèlnya,n-alap pāŋ nikaŋ pārijāṭāta tuṅgal,pupuḥ tékanaŋ mūṙkꝁa sakwèḥnya śīṙṇna*9:72:996*

pĕjaḥ pwékanaŋ rākṣasānuŋ surākṣa,masö ṅ-indrajit śīǥra gumrit raŧanya,panaḥ téka saŋ mārutī ṅ-astra tīkṣṇa,tataṙ pāṅapātaḥ panaḥnyāṙ pupug ya*9:73:997*

masö tuṅgaṅan tulya yā siṅha maṅhrik,parĕŋ yāṅdĕmak saŋ hanūmān lumumpat,tuhuk pyaḥ nikaŋ tuṅgaṅan riŋ nakāgra,mĕtu-ŋ rāḥ sakéruŋnya jīwanya luṅhā*9:74:998*

pĕjaḥnyékanāśꞓaṙyya saŋ méǥanāda,Apan riŋ daṅū tan hanātaḥ matī ya,Asiŋ lwīra niŋ śatru śīṙṇnā ta dénya,lukan yān pĕjaḥ dé niraŋ bāyuputra*9:75:999*

gumantīkanaŋ tuṅgaṅan dibya śakti,Umīṙ taŋ raŧāgöŋ ya sāmpun dinānan,sĕsök rākṣasānuŋ surākṣanya sèwu,huwus muṅgu maṅsö paḍānuŋ sĕnadđa*9:76:1000*

dinānan Ikaŋ rākṣasānuŋ prawīra,Asiŋ tan surud riŋ musuḥ śūra sāra,ya muṅgwī harĕp niŋ raŧānuŋ panĕṇḍas,ṅaranyāhalĕp śākaṭabyūhanāma*9:77:1001*

huwus tékanaŋ rākṣasābyūha saṅkĕp,paḍātuṅgalan kadga gaṇḍéwa konta,tumandaŋ kabèḥnyāmanaḥ saŋ hanūmān,sĕsök hrūnya yātip laṅit wuntu dénya*9:78:1002*

Ikā tèŋ daṅū tan hanānuŋ mapag ya,hyaṅ indrātakut dé nikā hrūnya tīkṣṇa,Apan yāwat aŋ wwaŋ kĕnī dénya śīṙṇna,pĕjaḥ tan paśéṣā Ikaŋ śatru dénya*9:79:1003*

Ikaŋ bwat nikā tan hanānuŋ mapag ya,nda tan paŋlaré yan tĕké saŋ hanūmān,tuhun trus pupū saŋ marutputra dénya,nda tār ambili hrū tamolaḥ tumaṅgö*9:80:1004*

pajātyan nikā saŋ mahāśūra riŋ praŋ,tan aṅgĕḥ ta yāmbĕk nirān tan pacihnā,mataŋnyān hĕnĕŋ saŋ hanūmān suđīra,tumaṅgö panaḥ riŋ pupū taṙ watĕk ya*9:81:1005*

mulat t-indrajit Aṙdđa sakrođa yaṙ ton,kađīran niraŋ bāyuputrèŋ raṇāṅga,winĕṇṭaŋnya laṅkapnya Ākāra pūṙṇna,panaḥ saŋ hanūmān rikaŋ nāgapāśa*9:82:1006*

Ulā lwiṙ nikā hrūnya sākṣāt ya māwān,satal göŋnya lāwan dawānyāpraméya,mapañjaŋ sihuŋnyāmsalit yātirodra,miṅis krūra huntunya bajropamanya*9:83:1007*

ya tékomilĕt bāhu saŋ bāyuputra,Apit taŋ Igā dé nikaŋ nāgapāśa,pupū yāpisit kapwa kāpus tĕkèn tūr,tibā saŋ hanūmān kĕnèŋ nāgapāśa*9:84:1008*

nda tan saṅka riŋ hīna śakti n-kapāśa,Awās yékanaŋ pāśa śīṙṇnā yar ahyun,Upāyā nirāṙ tona saŋ rāwaṇèkā,mataŋnyān hĕnĕŋ riŋ ƀujaṅgaprayāta*9:85:1009*

{suwadanā}
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :20:
tat kāla n-kāpusan saŋ pawanasuta humuŋ taŋ rākṣasabala,lāwan saŋ méǥanādāṅamah-amah umahöm mahyā saha bala,kapwomaṅsö sĕsök sāhasa maṅĕsĕs-ĕsĕs māmrĕp ya mamalu,taṙ pawyat saŋ hanūmān kadi wĕsi pinupuḥ riŋ mudgara timaḥ*9:86:1010*

mojaṙ saŋ méǥanādé harĕp ira hagahĕn dé saŋ daśamuꝁa,Ꜽ haywātā sadényān ahuripa takariḥ tan dadya luputa,toḥ priḥ puṇḍut kabèhi d-wawa ta ri harĕpan śrī rākṣasapati,tontonĕn dé niraŋ ƀūpati biśa nikanaŋ pāśāsama-sama*9:87:1011*

nā liŋ san méǥanādār ujari sahana niŋ wadwā nira kabèḥ,māri n-pāmrĕp ya śīǥrénusuṅ-usuṅ ika saŋ bāywātmaja wawaŋ,hāḥ wré duṣṭāṭiđūṙŧāđama pĕjahi huwus tunwīka ta mĕné,ndaḥ krĕt tĕṅgĕknya rāḥnyéninum aŧa ca pupuḥ tĕṇḍasnya rĕmukĕn*9:88:1012*

đūṙttèkī dūta niŋ rāǥawa mamati-matī donyā ṅalah-alaḥ,mĕṅgĕp śāntān tinonton iniṅĕt-iṅĕtakĕn caṇḍāla ya wĕgig,niṙ dosa-ŋ rākṣasātaḥ tuwi yatika pĕjaḥ dényāsiṅ umasö,ndya-ŋ đaṙmma ndya-ŋ kawikwan riya mamati-matī đik tan tuhu wiku*9:89:1013*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}
– – ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :9:
nā liŋ nikanaŋ mūṙkꝁa kabèḥ,mahyā ya riṅ ākāśa humuŋ,luṅhī ya muliḥ śīǥra ḍatĕŋ,winwatnya ta saŋ bāyusuta*9:90:1014*

hé nāŧa ya téki-ŋ mahala,mraṣṭākĕn ikaŋ kalpataru,śīṙṇna-ŋ kayu rūg dénya rĕbaḥ,sèsī nikaṅ udyānawana*9:91:1015*

tat kāla sĕḍèŋnyā winaraḥ,saŋ rāwaṇa sakrođa sira,wré duṣṭa durācāra pati,nā liŋ nira wètnyāṙ magĕlĕŋ*9:92:1016*

{halamuꝁī}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :9:
saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa sira mulat,n-ton marutsuta Inapusan,kāsihan ta sira karuṇa,yatna śīǥra sira mawuwus*9:93:1017*

ƀūmināŧa daśawadana,sojariŋ Aji ya pituhun,dūta tan dadi pinĕjahan,yadyapin ya wĕgiga tuwi*9:94:1018*

#daśśamas saṙggaḥ#
<tiḍak ḍikĕtahui>:10
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = :8:
^10/1/1014.
Iti nā liŋ nira mojar,Irikaŋ śāsana yukti,sira saŋ rāwaṇa mūṙkꝁa,sumahuṙ maṅkin asĕṅhit*10:1:1019*

ndya mataŋnyān luputéki,pĕjahātaḥ ya Awās ya,Apan atyanta wĕgignya,numanākĕn tanĕmaṅku*10:2:1020*

nya wanèḥ doṣa nikaŋ wré,Umatī rākṣasa ƀrĕtya,bala mantrī tuwi śīṙṇnā,yadi tan patyana liŋta*10:3:1021*

niyata-ŋ rājya wiśīrṅnā,raƀasānyéka kabèḥnya,ya mataŋnyān pĕjahātaḥ,Ikanāsiŋ Awamāna*10:4:1022*

Ikanaŋ wwaŋ kawamāna,humĕnĕŋ yan hana śatru,niyata śrīnya Umiṅgat,matakut riŋ pariƀūta*10:5:1023*

kalawan ndya-ŋ wwaṅ asampay,salawaskuñ jayaśatru,praṇata-ŋ rāt sahananya,Ikanaŋ hyaŋ tuwi ƀakti*10:6:1024*

ya mataŋnyān pĕjahéki,Ikanaŋ wré ya masampè,numanākĕn tanĕmaṅku,sĕḍĕṅ awwaḥ ya rinūgnya*10:7:1025*

satĕka ṅkā ri tamanku,mararĕm kapwa kumöl ya,Ikanaŋ wé tĕka yātīs,haṅinādrĕs tĕka manda*10:8:1026*

Apa sādyanta riki-ŋ wré,kita trĕṣṇā ri huripnya,tuwi tiṙyyak mapacāra,Umĕnaŋ sāhasika ṅké*10:9:1027*

{campakamālā}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏓ = :10:
nā ta wuwus saŋ rāwaṇa maswī,mātyana saŋ bāywātmaja tan lèn,śīǥra malĕs saŋ māruti mojar,mĕṅgĕp anantwāmbĕk nira hūmrĕŋ*10:10:1028*

rākṣasanāŧa wyaṙŧa gĕlĕŋta,tan hana yuktinyān tĕka riŋ wré,dūta ya Ékākī kĕna pāśa,tan pĕjahātaḥ wānara dènta*10:11:1029*

jāti nikā saŋ dibya jayèŋ praŋ,lajjita méraŋ riŋ Apalīṅa,tan dadi sakrođèṅ ađamātaḥ,solaha niŋ satwénanumāna*10:12:1030*

lāwan ikā saŋ rāǥawa śāđu,nitya rumākṣèŋ rāt sira dibya,taṙ wijigī riŋ śatru tar élik,ndan kita mūṙkꝁāmoǥa masĕṅhit*10:13:1031*

strī kalawan mās ratna wiśéṣa,lāƀa niṅ apraŋ yañ jayaśatru,yapwan ikā sāđyām tat anĕmwa,wèt ni kaduḥkan saŋ raǥuputra*10:14:1032*

rāǥawa sugrīwā ta wanèhan,yat pakamitrātaḥ sira kāliḥ,byakta sukā-ŋ rāt wrĕdđya hayunta,haywa ta sandéha-ŋ hati śānta*10:15:1033*

tulya tasik saŋ rāma kapīndra,śakti nirāgöŋ yékana ratna,yapwat amitra byakta hayunta,hyaŋ himawān māwak kita sampat*10:16:1034*

kāma ya sāđyan lāƀa kaniṣṭa,Aṙŧa ya sāđyan mađyama lāƀa,mitra ya sāđyan Uttama lāƀa,yéka mataŋnyān yogya samitrā*10:17:1035*

ꝁyāti sirè rāt lakṣmaṇa sāđu,śūra sirāntĕn saŋ raǥuputra,ƀakti sirojaṙ Iŋ kaka satya,tan wihaṅātaḥ milwa samitrā*10:18:1036*

maṅkana tékaŋ wānarawīra,śakti ya ƀaktī saŋ kapirāja,nāparicārāsiŋ sapakona,taṙ wilumāsiŋ kāṙyya kasidđa*10:19:1037*

kwèḥ pwa Ikā lāƀā niṅ amitra,haywa ta sakrođa-ŋ hati śānta,sĕmbahakĕn dèwī nira sītā,saŋ raǥuputrāwās sira haṙṣā*10:20:1038*

đaṙmma lawan Aṙŧottama kāma,nya-ŋ tiga yékāwās ya tĕmunta,sĕṣṭi niṅ āmbĕk byakta katĕmwa,yat praṇatāpī saŋ raǥuputra*10:21:1039*

yogya Ataḥ saŋ rāǥawa nāŧā,taṙ papaḍèŋ rāt riŋ jayaśatru,hrū nira tuṅgal mrĕtyu paḍanya,yaṙ pralayākĕn śatrwaniwāṙyya*10:22:1040*

tāṭaka bālī yojanabāhu,dūṣaṇa lèn mārīca wirāđa,yéka pĕjaḥ dé saŋ raǥuputra,kabwatakĕn yan śakti kabèḥnya*10:23:1041*

tātan ikā hétwanta masĕṅhit,yadyapin akwèḥ rākṣasa śīṙṇna,Āpan ikā wadwānta ya duṣṭa,mātyana saŋ rāmékana donya*10:24:1042*

yukti tĕmĕn dé saŋ raǥuputra,Aṙ pralayākĕn rākṣasa mūṙkꝁa,mūlya Awak niṅwaŋ ya rinākṣa,yéka panāđyān đaṙmma wiśèṣa*10:25:1043*

nā ta wuwus saŋ mārutaputra,rāwaṇa maṅkin krođa kabāṅan,krođa niṅ āṅin bajra paḍanya,ǥūṙṇnita molaḥ taŋ mukapadma*10:26:1044*

hāḥ Ađamékiŋ wānara duṣṭa,mūḋa mapuṅguŋ tan tuhu dūta,tan pati mojaṙ tan pati molaḥ,donya ya donyātaḥ ya ta dūta*10:27:1045*

ko pwa ya mĕṅgĕp dūta hiḍĕpmu,rākṣasa tan kraḥ śīṙṇna ya dému,tan panĕpĕṙ kon rūg tanĕmaṅku,śāsana niŋ dūta ndi tinūtmu*10:28:1046*

ko pwa mujī śaktinya si rāma,swaŋ puji tan wruḥ riŋ sapujinmwa,taṙ papaḍèn pāpéka si rāma,bwat pĕjahi-ŋ tan yogya ya hiṅsan*10:29:1047*

wruḥ kari ko riŋ yojanabāhu,duṙbbala paṅguḥ yékana timpaŋ,yéka pĕjaḥ dé niŋ raǥuputra,pātaka ko đik niṙǥrĕṇa duṣṭa*10:30:1048*

tāṭaka tātan yogya ya mātya,strī tuwi lāwan tan pasahāya,ya pwa pinatyan dé ni si rāma,hāḥ kala tan wriŋ wlas Apalīṅa*10:31:1049*

ratna maṇik strī lāƀa niṅ apraŋ,yèkana pājaṙmwiryaku ṅūni,tātan ikā don saŋ Aƀimāna,kīṙtti yaśātaḥ don ira tan lèn*10:32:1050*

jāti nikā saŋ göŋ Aƀimāna,đīra tan aṅgā yaṙ kapaḍāna,ƀaktya nikaŋ lèn yékana pinriḥ,yan pwa tan aṅgā ƀaktya pinatyan*10:33:1051*

nā ta sināđyā saŋ tuhu wīra,śrī ya ta tūtūtanya sināđyā,Āpan ikā bwat cañcala méṅā,yāta mataŋnyān tan ya sināđyā*10:34:1052*

hāḥ lalu tan wruḥ riŋ paramāṙŧa,Anđya mataŋnyān kādƀuta dému,jāti wĕgig taŋ rākṣasa wīra,đaṙmma nikin hīnāparadāra*10:35:1053*

rāma lawan sugrīwa ya mitran,yéka Ujaṙmun mūḋa mapuṅguŋ,yogya kari-ŋ wwil wwaŋ wrayamitra,tan patut iŋ śīlanya Ulaḥnya*10:36:1054*

wīra wirāđānuŋ mati dénya,tan pĕjahékākīnya ya tuṅgal,rāǥawa đūṙŧātyanta tan éraŋ,lakṣmaṇa yékānuŋ tumuluŋ ya*10:37:1055*

lāwan ikaŋ mārīca kaniṣṭa,tan sapujimwīkaŋ mĕjahīkām,kātara yan ton śatru ya méṅas,tulya kĕnas yan ton ikanaŋ moŋ*10:38:1056*

nūni sĕḍĕŋ kwākon ya lumakwa,mamrih anĕmbaḥ wèt ni takutnya,twaŋnya kunĕŋ ry-ājñaṅku n-alaṅǥya,yéka dumèḥnyāmriḥ-mriha wānya*10:39:1057*

wānara bālī śakti ya liŋmu,Andya mataŋnyān trus pinanaḥ pwa,yan tuhu śakti syūha Ikaŋ hrū,yéka mataŋnyān hīna si bāli*10:40:1058*

maṅkana tékī pāpa si rāma,mūṙkꝁa matīkaŋ bāli si bālī,ndan sĕḍĕṅ apraŋ lāwan arinya,hā haha ho hāḥ hīna si rāma*10:41:1059*

{ƀujagaśiśrĕta}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – ⏓ = :9:
daśawadana huwus mojar,jwalita hati nirān krođa,pawanasuta malĕs mojar,hati nira matĕguḥ đīra*10:42:1060*

Apa kita mupawādāku,raƀasa kayu riṅ udyāna,makira-kira maraŋ dūta,maṅaṅĕn-aṅĕna mopāya*10:43:1061*

Aku Ikana kinon dūta,lumawada hana saŋ sītā,ndan alĕmĕh aku maŋ­rakwa,wruha ri sira Ataḥ byakta*10:44:1062*

nahan ikana ya don kwaṅrug,kayu sahana riṅ udyāna,tat agĕlĕṅa tatat krođa,Apa ta halĕpakĕn molaḥ*10:45:1063*

Aku mĕjahikana sy-akṣa,kalawan ikana wadwānta,saha bala ya pĕjaḥ dèṅku,kira-kira ya tikā tan lèn*10:46:1064*

kalawan ika kabèḥ mūṙkꝁa,sahana-hana ni wadwānta,pĕjahana ya kayogyanya,saraƀasa numanākĕn rāt*10:47:1065*

Aŧawa ya ta kunĕŋ donku,mĕjahi sahana niŋ mūṙkꝁa,prakrĕti juga Ikaŋ māna,ri hati nikana saŋ đīra*10:48:1066*

kita tuwi mawaraḥ ṅūni,yaśa juga ya ta doniŋ praŋ,tan ahala ta kariḥ donku,mĕjahi sahana niŋ mūṙkꝁa*10:49:1067*

kita tuwi magawè śīla,prakrĕti juga tinūtanta,Ikaṅ ađama karākṣasyan,ya pinakalarapan dènta*10:50:1068*

swaṅ awara-warah iŋ đaṙmma,takari naya nikaŋ jāti,bali kari tahu riŋ śāstra,guragaḍa juga mĕṅgĕp wruḥ*10:51:1069*

ndya ta ya paramađaṙmmanta,prakrĕti ya kawĕkas ṅūni,satata kita rumākṣāŋ rāt,ya ta tuhu-tuhu rākṣasyan*10:52:1070*

saṅ atapa hana riŋ śūnya,sira tika tuwi rākṣanta,yadi tuhu-tuhu rākṣasyan,tan ikanaṅ amati-ŋ rāt pwa*10:53:1071*

Aḍah ađama dahat mūṙkꝁa,kaliku kita ri janmanta,tuhagaṇa magawè pāpa,ri hala-hayu ni jātinta*10:54:1072*

Aku mujari kitāmitrā,kalawan ikana saŋ rāma,tat amituhu Alaḥ mūḋa,tuhu-tuhu tahu riŋ pāpa*10:55:1073*

byasana lawan ikaŋ śīla,ya mapa salaha nā liŋta,tuhun ikana Apan mūṙkꝁa,tamat aṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn đaṙmma*10:56:1074*

lawan ika si wirāđākya,saṅ atapa ya winiǥnanya,ya pinĕjahan iraŋ rāma,ri hati nira pi tan krođa*10:57:1075*

saꝑala sira siwin liṅku,hati nira muditī riŋ rāt,saṅ atapa pinaritrānan,sꝑaṭika paḍa nikaŋ citta*10:58:1076*

kalawan ika si mārīca,yan apa salaha dé niŋ hrū,tuwi ya dadi kidaŋ māya,masasaran alayū méṅas*10:59:1077*

punar api kapisan dé saŋ,raǥusuta Umanaḥ pyaḥnya,syapa ta ratu wanèḥ śaktya,nuṅ amanaha kidaŋ māya*10:60:1078*

kita Umupĕt ikaŋ bālī,Apa kita malupān śakti,hana mara ya huwus mūṙcca,Inapitan ikanaŋ bālī*10:61:1079*

ndak acarita rĕṅöntéki,praŧama sĕḍĕṅ ikaŋ bālī,majapa ya rikanaŋ sanđyā,pijĕr umaṅĕn-aṅĕn saŋ hyaŋ*10:62:1080*

kaŧam api hana téki wwaŋ,kadi Ayuyu taṅanyākwèḥ,maṅawara ya mahā mèdi,ri sira saṅ ajapāmūjā*10:63:1081*

tĕka mamĕlĕg ikaŋ duṣṭa,mamarimisi ri saŋ sāđu,kadi tuhu ya mahāśaktya,guragaḍa juga yāsampay*10:64:1082*

sĕḍĕṅ amĕlĕg ikaŋ duṣṭa,dadi ya Inapitan mosaḥ,sagila mati Alaḥ mopĕk,syapa ta kunĕṅ ikaŋ tan wruḥ*10:65:1083*

{kāmadattā}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
daśamuꝁa ya mataŋnya śāntacittā,tat atukara lawan ƀaṭāra rāma,marat anĕmu wiƀūti yāpraméya,yat atukara kita pralāya lĕṅkā*10:66:1084*

raǥusuta ya nahan siwinta nāŧā,janakasuta ta tulya déwatānta,waluyakĕna ri saŋ naréndra rāma,kanaka maṇi wawan saha praṇamya*10:67:1085*

pawanasuta nahan wuwus nirojar,Atiśaya sira niṙƀayĕŋ swacitta,maruti ya mapĕḍĕs waliŋ nirālon,ri harĕp i-balamantri rākṣasākwèḥ*10:68:1086*

daśamuꝁa magalak madĕg sirāglis,tudiṅi ta pawanātmajé kiwātaḥ,ƀrukuṭi-kuṭila ƀīṣaṇā muꝁābaŋ,kadi dumilah ikā wulat nirācrĕŋ*10:69:1087*

wrayapa naraka đik luluynya mojar,kadi maṅajap-ajap wuwusnya jañjan,Apusi pahatĕguḥ Ikūnya tunwi,prisakiti ta hatinya wĕḥ sarantmè*10:70:1088*

{madahaṙṣa}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏓ = :18:
daśawadana huwus nirojaṙ madĕg tèkanaŋ rākṣasa,hana Alalaṅ akiŋ pamuṅkusnya rīkū niraŋ māruti,Apusi ta daluwaŋ lawan bwat kĕliŋ kusyara mwaŋ jamaŋ,Asiṅ-asiṅ anipis dilaḥnyāhaṅan ndan bĕbĕdnyāpagĕḥ*10:71:1089*

krama huwus inapus pwa ya dyus ta riŋ tꜽla lāwan miñak,tĕka ṅ-amawa suluḥ Umaṅsö sĕsök sāhasāṅĕmbuli,paḍa tan anumanān panunwī murub tékanékū nira,kagiri-giri dilaḥnya tèjanya maƀrā sinaŋ loṙ kidul*10:72:1090*

#Ĕkādaśamas saṙggaḥ#
<daṇḍaka>
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:29: = :93:
^11/1/1086.
Aŧa sĕḍĕṅ umurub Ikū saŋ hanūmān Umaṅkak tikāwak nirāgöŋ gunuŋ méru tulyānanāŋ nāgapāśāpasaḥ sāk pasātus tatas śīṙṇna rampuŋ pĕgat dénikā bāhu saŋ bāyuputromĕsat śīǥra Ākāśagāmī miriṙ taŋ Aṅin ǥora yāǥūṙṇnitādrĕs riwutpāta humyus musus yomĕlĕk taŋ lĕbu,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:28: = :90:
kadi ta Inububan ya maṅkin murub tékanékū nirāpan katūb dé nikaŋ bāyubajré sĕḍĕŋnyār ibĕṙ tulya saŋ hyaŋ lĕmaḥ maŋlayaŋ mwaŋ Apuy ꝁyāti kālāgni rodrāṙ dunuŋ taŋ Umaḥ ṅkā riṅ antaḥ purāpūṙwwa rūpanya saśrī saśoƀā yatékān tinunwan nirānéka waṙṇnanya nānāwiđa*11:1:1091*
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:29: = :93:
paḍa makaparupuḥ ṅ-apuy yan dilaḥ riŋ Umaḥ kapwa rĕmpak rĕmukmaṅkana-ŋ maṇḍapāpan parĕŋ yan katunwan sakanyomakin wrĕdđitékaŋ Apuy Ujwalālola kumlab dilaḥnyā laṅit niṙƀayātaḥ manaḥ saŋ hanūmān mulat kādƀutékaŋ watĕk rākṣasé soṙ kasoran kaśūran kawīran kađīran tuwi,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:29: = :93:
pa ḍa ta ya mututuŋ tutuknyān kagöman kapūhan tumĕŋ­hāmtakut n-tonkaḍatwan katunwan kutug taŋ Apuy loṙ kidul kālamrĕtyūpamanyomaladtan dilaḥ tulya télatnya molaḥ mĕlĕk taŋ kukus Aṙdđa mawyaŋ-wyaṅèkĕl-l-ikĕl yéka rambut ni tĕṇḍasnya rodrān katon kātara-ŋ rākṣasā ǥūṙṇni-tāwū humuŋ*11:2:1092*

{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:29: = :93:
tripura-pura murub tinunwan ƀaṭāréśwarānuŋ paḍanyān tĕñuḥ taŋ Umaḥ mās ya masyūḥ masāk kaŋ sakāgöŋ maṇik bajra bajropamanyān makas kāsyasiḥ tékanaŋ Apsarī riŋ purāpūṙwwa yaṙ ton apuy kapwatékāgupuy kwèḥ kapöyĕḥ gĕyuḥ yan kayuḥ kèn i-cèṭinya maṅluḥ Umaṅguḥ huyaŋ yāṅĕliḥ,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:30: = :96:
talaga-talaga riŋ kaḍatwan winatwan ya dé niŋ maṇik candrakānté daṅū ndan mĕné śuṣka yāsāt ya kèsĕp sĕkaṙ niŋ Aśokāṅasut yan kasūban panasrūkṣa sakwèḥnya yākiŋ makiṅkiŋ manuknyānaṅis moni kolāhalāwū walācakrawākā gĕlāna-ŋ pĕluŋ haṅsa māśā saśokāswarāsū Ikaŋ sārasa*11:3:1093*
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:27: = :87:
bala makabalasaḥ Ikaŋ rākṣasosaḥ mĕsat ṅkā riṅ ākāśa yāpan katunwan pakuwwanya tātan paśéṣāgĕsĕŋ śīṙṇna Éman liman ṅkā riṅ ālāna yāglāna dé niŋ Apuy maṅkana-ŋ tuṅgaṅan tuṅga-tuṅgal ya tātan hanānuŋ manuṅgaŋ riyāmriḥ lumumpat luput riŋ Apuy yāṅliput,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:26: = :84:
jalak ajar-ajaran bayan syuŋ puyuḥ kwèḥ pĕjaḥ muṅgu rin pañjaré pañcaraṅkaŋ hĕmas tan katoliḥ Alaḥ mriḥ Awaknyèkanaŋ rākṣasī śīǥra luṅhā hah-āh-āh-ah-āḥ liŋnya kapwāmĕhāḥ yāṅuhuḥ mohitān ton ikaŋ rākṣasomèḥ tibā riŋ Apuy moǥa momo Umèḥ mātya ya*11:4:1094*

{sragđara}
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :21:
nā lwiṙ niŋ rājya lĕṅkā matunu ya mananāŋ nāgapuṣpé nataṙnya,mandārāśoka punnāga ya raƀasa gĕsĕŋ ronya kĕmbaŋnya pāŋnya,tañjuŋ poh ambawaŋnyū maja kadi pinusus jambu wulwan katunwan,dūṙyyan maṅguṣṭa puṙyyan panasa kapanasan nāśa sakwèḥnya śīṙṇna*11:5:1095*

ƀraṣṭāŋ lĕṅkā ya sāmpun matunu dadi mĕsat saŋ hanūmān lumumpat,riŋ Udyānèṅ aśokāṙ waluy umara ri saŋ mꜽŧilī prāpta śīǥra,n-ton dèwī glāna monĕŋ maṅisĕk-isĕk asāk taŋ gĕluŋ nitya moré,śoké soṙ niŋ Aśokākĕlu ta ya kalasā ṙ-kölakĕn duḥka kāla*11:6:1096*

maṅsö saŋ bāyuputra praṇata ri suku saŋ jānakī śīǥra mojar,hé dèwīnya ṅhulun māruti tuhu-tuhu yan dūta saŋ rāmaƀadra,tātā rakwān kinonkon raǥutanaya Apan n-ton ikaŋ cihna makwèḥ,ndaḥ mamwīta ṅhulun mājar-ajara ri mahārāja rāmāƀirāma*11:7:1097*

nā liŋ saŋ bāyuputra krama lumaku muliḥ sāmpun amwit Anĕmbaḥ,riŋ Ākāśā-ṙ mĕsat maŋlayaṅ atiśaya riŋ kādƀutātyanta riŋ göŋ,gamƀīra krūrarūpogratara kadi gĕrĕḥ riŋ laṅit ǥora gĕntĕr,humyus taŋ bāyubajrèŋ gaganatala pĕpĕt déwatā kapwa kagyat*11:8:1098*

molaḥ wwꜽ niŋ tasik ǥūṙṇnitatara gumuruḥ dényaṅin saŋ hanūmān,kagyat sèsī nikaŋ sāgara kadi ginugaḥ nāga kolāhalāwū,luṅhā taŋ bāyu mādrĕs kayu-kayu ya katūb kampitékaŋ mahéndra,sakwèḥ niŋ wānarāṅhèṙ kaburu kabarasat saṅśayé śatru śakti*11:9:1099*

mèḥ prāptā saŋ hanūmān pracalita Ikanaŋ ṙyyak magöŋ kapwa mombak,kontal tĕmpuḥ ta pāŋ niŋ kayu ri tĕpi rurū rāmya kĕmbaŋnya saśrī,lumrā riŋ ƀūtalātap mrĕdu kadi ta tilām komalārūmnya māṙ mrik,daṙppékaŋ kinnarācumbana tĕka maguliŋ riŋ sĕkaṙ ṅkān tĕkāṅliḥ*11:10:1100*

tat kālanyan tĕka ṅkā ri kawĕkasan ikaŋ wānarāṅhèṙ kabèḥnya,maṅsö saŋ jāmbawān aṅgada milu ta siraŋ nīla haṙṣān panuŋsuŋ,lāwan sakwèḥ nikaŋ wré niyata sira huwus sidđakāṙyyéki liŋnya,tapwan mojaṙ sira ndān guyu nira mamanis nā paṅawruḥ nikaŋ wray*11:11:1101*

sakwèḥ niŋ wré ya kapwomulat aṅiṅĕt-iṅĕt cihna saŋ bāyuputra,n-ton taŋ taṅgwan tumaṅgö ri pupu nira nahan cihna niŋ sāmpun apraŋ,ṅkāśꞓaṙyyāmbĕk nikaŋ wré mututuṅ aṅujiwat n-ton ikaŋ cihna makwèḥ,hāḥ saŋ śūrātiđīrèŋ lara sira Umahāƀūṣaṇékaŋ śarīra*11:12:1102*

wèt niŋ göŋ paṙbwatāwān paḍa nira kaharan tambiṅékaŋ ḍaḍālwā,rambut mākrĕp mapañjaŋ ya ta kaharan alas nā-ŋ śiraḥ yéka puñcak,mwaŋ taṅgwan yèkanolā kanin ira ya guhā đātutulyékanaŋ rāḥ,nā liŋ niŋ wré sahaṙṣāmuji-muji ya wijaḥ kapwa mojaṙ magupyan*11:13:1103*

wètnyān haṙṣékanaŋ wānarabala kaharan paṙśwa niŋ mèru sākṣāt,molaḥ mawyaŋ wulunyān kadi kanakalatāñcāla dé niŋ samīra,nétranyékān kĕḍap lwiṙ sꝑaṭika kadi maṇik candrakāntātikānta,saṅké tuṣṭinya yan ton pawanasuta humīs luḥnya yékāmrĕtanya*11:14:1104*

sāmpun maṅsö tikaŋ wré dadi mawara-waraḥ saŋ marutputra mojar,dèwī sītā kapaṅguḥ hana sira mahurip ṅkā ri lĕṅkā tamolaḥ,nāhan liŋ saŋ hanūmān makin agiraṅ ikaŋ wré ṇ-ḍĕṅö wrĕtta dèwī,haṙṣanyāgöŋ ya wrĕdđī hati ya kadi tasik yaṙ wĕtu-ŋ pūṙṇna candra*11:15:1105*

{mālaƀāriṇi}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
krama kāla muliḥ ta saŋ hanūmān,kalawan wānarawīra śīǥra luṅha,tĕka riŋ giri winđya kapwa haṙṣa,mamaṅan wwa-wwahan īŋ Alas wisāta*11:16:1106*

sira saŋ pawanātmajāta sūṙyya,Ikanojaṙ nira tulya téja sākṣāt,Atitībra Unĕŋ ƀaṭāra rāma,ya tikā ǥora pĕtĕŋ wiśīṙṇna dénya*11:17:1107*

Aŧa śīǥra ḍatĕŋ ta saŋ hanūmān,rikanaŋ paṙbwata mālyawān ya māwān,tĕmu saŋ nrĕpaputra rāmadéwa,kalawan lakṣmaṇa lèn kapīndrarāja*11:18:1108*

makulit kayu kapwa śānta wéṣa,majaṭāđāra kulit liman sinaṇḍaŋ,śuci sātwika satya riŋ samāđi,narayāṇāṅśa siréka wiṣṇu sākṣāt*11:19:1109*

Umasö ta siraŋ marutprasūta,ri sira śrī naranāŧa rāmadéwa,paripūṙṇna sirāt apūṙṇnacandra,saha cūḍāmaṇi cihna yéka winwat*11:20:1110*

Umulat pwa naréndraputra rāma,Ikanaŋ ratna maṇik surat duluṙnya,kadi jīwa niraŋ priyā hiḍĕp ya,lumipuṙ kūŋ nira māri śokacitta*11:21:1111*

Anilātmaja dūta sāđu dibya,sira cintāmaṇi mĕtwakĕn sakahyun,raǥuputra nahan ta liŋ nirojar,muji saŋ māruti māri yaṙ makiṅkiŋ*11:22:1112*

Atituṣṭa ƀaṭāra rāma yaṙ ton,Ikanaŋ réka surat naréndraputrī,Inalap ya Inuṅkaban ya saśrī,waca taŋ réka tulis mawèḥ prahaṙṣa*11:23:1113*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
sĕmbaḥ ni ṅhulun āṙyyaputra ya tĕké pādadwayanta praƀu,nyékiŋ réka wacān uninyaya Iko cihnanyunĕŋ ni ṅhulun,mwaŋ cūḍāmaṇi tulya ni ṅhulun iké maṅsö sumĕmbaḥ kita,nyā-ŋ simsim pakirim naréndra ya Ikā spaṙśanta tékāk hiḍĕp*11:24:1114*

yak ton yāta makuŋ manaḥku maṅaraŋ ƀrāntāpa tak ton kita,hāḥ śrī ƀūpati rāmadéwa huniṅantékī taṅis ni ṅhulun,mwaŋ ƀaktiṅku magöŋ taman hana wanèh iṣṭiṅku tan lèn kita,Aṅhiŋ saŋ praƀu nitya kéwala siwinkwé saptajanmāntara*11:25:1115*

ṅūnī tan karĕṅö huripta kalawan wrĕttanta tātan hana,Aṅhīŋ mātya taman wanèh aṅĕn-aṅĕn niṣkāṙyya tākun hana,nāhan saŋ hyaṅ apuy gunuŋ tasik asiŋ māṙggā nikaŋ jīwita,hīṅanyān patulaŋ manaḥku malilaŋ nistrĕṣṇa wèt niŋ lara*11:26:1116*

sakwèḥ niŋ marasèŋ daṅū ya rinasan tātan hanékāŋ-rasé,kĕmbaŋ bāp hana riŋ taman-taman ikā tāmbānyunĕŋ ni ṅhulun,sakwèḥ niŋ karĕṅö manohara lawan sakwèḥ nikaŋ srak marūm,yékān wyaṙŧa hananya niṙguṇa kabèḥ wway tan pasuk riŋ gulū*11:27:1117*

lāwan haywa naréndra mālara dahat wöhĕn wiśudđāŋ manaḥ,sāmpun tāku wĕruḥ rikèŋ lara magöŋ niṣkāṙyya tātan padon,sugyan dudwa kunĕŋ Ikéṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn tan dadya dé saŋ praƀu,nāhan hétu niké mataŋnya kawaraḥ swasŧā jayā ƀūpati*11:28:1118*

lāwan haywa kataṅguhan kita rikī ta lwiṙta ṅūniṇ ḍaray,kālantād winaraŋ naréndra mahulun kāliḥ sukāmbĕk nira,salwiṙ niŋ Upaƀoga yogya ya pawèḥ tātan kuraŋ riŋ suka,riŋ krīđā wihikan kité sawinuwus riŋ kāmaśāstrottama*11:29:1119*

riŋ Indrāṇi lawan śacī tama tuwin tātan mapuṅguŋ kita,ri pratyéka niké rasanya ya kabèḥ sāmpun kita wruḥ rikā,nāhan tèki dumèḥ manaḥku kalaran śīṙṇnātĕñuḥ taŋ hati,Āpan tan hana lèn paḍanta rikanaŋ jñānādi lāwan guṇa*11:30:1120*

ndan prāptā ta naréndra haywa masuwé pöŋpöŋ hurip ni ṅhulun,yékiŋ rāwaṇa mūṙkꝁa tan Aṅĕn-aṅĕn đaṙmmā wĕrö-yālupa,haywopĕk maṅaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn baṣama tan sidđā sakāṙyyā haji,pöŋpöŋ śakti nikaŋ prawīra kapi sakwèḥnyādƀutèŋ papraṅan*11:31:1121*

yadyan prāpta naréndra ri ṅhulun apā tékīn anuŋ paṅguhĕn,kasyāsiḥku hanèŋ musuḥ kapilaṅö hétunya tag wruḥ huwus,ṅhiŋ kiṅkiŋ pasajiṅku tan hana wanèḥ kāliḥ putĕk niŋ hati,lāwan luḥ juga timtimĕn nahan iké cihnānyunĕŋ ni ṅhulun*11:32:1122*

tāmbĕḥ niŋ lumaré ṅhulun hulun asiŋ saṅkā nikĕŋ wédanā,hétunyān mapasaḥ pakonku ginawé saṅké ry-asiḥ té ṅhulun,yapwan paṅguha saŋ naréndra Umuwaḥ tan maṅkanātaḥ maluy,solaḥ niŋ kahulun ṅhulun juga hulun yékā gĕgönkun hulun*11:33:1123*

sāsiŋ sajña naréndra yéka pituhun sojaṙta tak laṅǥana,nāhan prāṙŧana ni ṅhulun taya wanèḥ saṅkā ri göŋ niŋ rĕṇa,yapwan tan wulati ṅhulun Apa kunĕŋ līṅaṅkwa tag wruḥ huwus,nī hétunya tĕkā naréndra huwusĕn saṅkā ry-unĕŋ ni ṅhulun*11:34:1124*

nāhan toni nikaŋ tulis dadi gupuy saŋ rāmaƀadrāmaca,saṅké tībra nikaŋ lulut Unĕṅ asiḥ luḥ nityakāla n-tibā,saṅké drĕs nikaṅ aśrupāta humilī taṙ wruḥ tibānyèŋ tulis,kagyat n-ton ya lĕbuṙ taman wruh i-wĕkas niŋ réka śokāŋ manaḥ*11:35:1125*

Ꜽ saŋ māruti toḥ tuluŋ Aku tasö saŋ lakṣmaṇāri ṙ wulat,ndaḥ tontonta Ikèŋ tulis hana lĕbuṙ makwèḥ surud tan katon,hāḥ tag wruḥ Aparan Uninya ta kunĕŋ saṅké laranyāk hiḍĕp,đū ndyātaḥ karikā kunĕŋ hamĕṅaniŋ rékān susuk riŋ hati*11:36:1126*

nāhan liŋ naranāŧa yāwara-waraḥ mājaṙ ta saŋ māruti,sājñā śrī nrĕpati nda haywa kalaran wèḥ taŋ manaḥ ménaka,Āpan sāmpun ikā Ujaṙ nira kumon ƀūpālakātaḥ tĕkā,Aṅhiŋ déya lumakwa ƀūpati huwus nāhan ta tāmbā nikā*11:37:1127*

lāwan saŋ praƀu haywa képwan irikā ndyānuŋ dayā ƀūpati,Āpan sāmpun awās naréndraǥariṇī ƀyaktāhurip niśꞓaya,Aṅhiŋ maṅkata saŋ praƀū marawaśèŋ sārājya lĕṅkāpura,liŋ saŋ lakṣmaṇa taṙ wihaŋ nrĕpati yan tiṅhal ri saŋ māruti*11:38:1128*

{mālaƀāriṇi}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
I tĕlas nikanaŋ tulis wināca,Inalap dé nira taŋ maṇik liniṅliŋ,Inaras ri pipī nirātihaṙṣa,pamawā nāŋ lara kūŋ lulut hiḍĕp ya*11:39:1129*

ri huwus nikanaŋ maṇik tinonton,kinudaŋ dé nira saŋ naréndraputra,dadi mājar-ajaṙ ta saŋ hanūmān,ri siraŋ rāma kapīndra lakṣmaṇātaḥ*11:40:1130*

naranāŧa Ikā musuḥta siṅhā,pinakālasnya Ikaŋ purī ri lĕṅkā,dayitā janakātmajā hana ṅkā,sira tāpuy sakunaŋ-kunaŋ ya tālöŋ*11:41:1131*

raǥuputra kitāta bāyubājrā,Umara ṅkāna dumamwanīkanaŋ wā,dumilaḥ pwa ṅ-apuy makin ya wrĕdđi,niyata-ŋ siṅha gĕsĕŋ lawan Alasnya*11:42:1132*

byasananya lanā Umañcana-ŋ rāt,sira saŋ wꜽśrawaṇénadĕḥnya miṅgat,gawayan nira mās kinoṭi-koṭi,ya Ikānuŋ Inalapnya tan paśéṣa*11:43:1133*

surasaṅǥa lanā nanā ta dénya,tamatan wruḥ riṅ iraŋ hilaŋ panonya,mawĕrö wiparīta dé nikaŋ śrī,Ika saŋ sajjanamāṙgga tan tinūtnya*11:44:1134*

tuwi rākṣasajanma duṣṭacitta,tinĕmunyékaṅ inak makin ya daṙppa,Ikanaŋ Upadéśa sèp ya ri ṙyya,ya mataŋnyān pĕjahāta dé naréndra*11:45:1135*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
lāwan sira śrī janakātmajā makūŋ,rantĕn mahārāja wiyoga duḥkita,naréndra tātaḥ hinaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn Ira,lanānaṅis rin rahinèŋ kulĕm sira*11:46:1136*

gĕlāna maṅliḥ mawĕnĕs sirākurū,wulan rikaŋ krĕṣṇa paḍā nirèŋ kṣaya,kunĕŋ kasoṙ niŋ śaśiwimba dé nira,Ikā kalĕṅkanya ya jāti tan hilaŋ*11:47:1137*

sirāṙ hana ṅkā kadi padma riŋ latĕk,Apan nikoṅgwan nira mūṙkꝁa tan maya,Ikā kasatyan nira śudđa niṙmmala,lanā hanèŋ citta ya kéśarā nira*11:48:1138*

nahan ta liŋ saŋ pawanātmajāwaraḥ,sahaṙṣa tāmbĕk nira saŋ raǥūttama,kadīnĕnö riŋ Amrĕtékanaŋ hati,ṇ-ḍĕṅö wuwus saŋ kapiwīra māruti*11:49:1139*

sĕḍĕŋnya tapwan tĕka saŋ marutsuta,makiŋ kasātan mapanas manaḥ nira,tĕka pwa saŋ māruti māri yāpanas,kadi pwa yāwyāđi mamaṅgih oṣađa*11:50:1140*

mulat siré saŋ taruṇāṙyya lakṣmaṇa,Ikaŋ Aƀiprāya makon umaṅkata,kapīndra sugrīwa wĕruḥ riṅ iṅgita,r-atag Ikaŋ wré sahananya maṅkata*11:51:1141*

madĕg ta saŋ rāǥawa mèḥ lumampaha,madan tikaŋ wré maṅusuŋ-Usuŋ masö,parĕŋ Umaṅkat Umibèṙ ta yān laku,marĕp kidul prāpta sirèŋ mahéndra ya*11:52:1142*

{Upajāti bajra}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
gunuŋ magöŋ mèru paḍanya saśrī,samīpa niŋ sāgara n-uṅgu sāra,saké takutnyaṙ kĕbĕkékanaŋ rāt,mataŋnya wèḥ tambakakĕn Awaknya*11:53:1143*

Ikaŋ tasik jāti wiśudđa yāhniŋ,saḍā tikaŋ wāḥ tĕka ri ṙyya tan lyab,na lwiṙnyan ahyun rikanaŋ kađīran,mataŋnyan uṅgwī tĕpi niŋ samudra*11:54:1144*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
dudug ri soṙ witnya tĕkèŋ rasātala,mahocꞓa puñcaknya tĕkèŋ ƀuwaḥ pada,kadi pwa mahyun ḍumĕpāŋ jagattraya,mataŋnya miṅsoṙ salayā Umiṇḍuhur*11:55:1145*

kanyā muḍā tulya nikaŋ naƀastala,kĕṇḍitnya naŋ wintaṅ akĕn maṇik tinū,ya téka kahyun Ikanaŋ gunuŋ kunĕŋ,mataŋnya māwān dumudug tĕkèŋ laṅit*11:56:1146*

kayunya nānāwiđa kapwa yānĕḍĕŋ,matöb ya mĕṇḍuḥ tumĕluŋ tĕkèŋ lĕmaḥ,Anéka ta wwaḥnya hanan tasak maḍam,kadī ta pawwat Ikanaŋ gunuŋ mawit*11:57:1147*

lawan sĕkaṙnyojwala yānĕdĕŋ kabèḥ,rurū ya lumrā rikanaŋ lĕmaḥ marūm,kadi pwa mahyas humaḍaŋ ya saṅgrahā,ḍatĕŋ nira śrī nrĕpaputra rāǥawa*11:58:1148*

kadi pwa kéndran nikanaŋ mahéndra ya,ri dényan akwèḥ kayu kalpawrĕkṣa ya,lawan maṇik yéka śilātalānya ya,dudū-ŋ manuk kinnara jīwa-jīwa ya*11:59:1149*

tĕka pwa saŋ śrī raǥuputra riŋ gunuŋ,mulat sirèŋ pāṙśwa saśoƀa rāmya ya,jĕnĕk sirāṙ ton talagāhatuṙ sĕkar,sĕkaṙnya tuñjuŋ muꝁa saŋ priyāṙ hiḍĕp*11:60:1150*

samaṅkanékaŋ ƀramara ƀramanta ya,maśabda n-ambuŋ sari niŋ saroruha,kadi pwa saŋ śrī janakātmajāṅliṅa,manaḥ niraŋ rāma makin sahaṙṣa ya*11:61:1151*

huwus mararyan sira riŋ mahéndra ya,katon ikaŋ rāwaṇarājya lĕṅka ya,lawan nikaŋ wré Umulat kabèḥ nikā,siraŋ hanūmān tumudūhakĕn riya*11:62:1152*

{swādamālinī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
Aŧa ri huwusnya katon pura lĕṅkā,dadi tumurun sira riŋ giripāṙśwa,kalawan ikaŋ bala wānarawīra,ri tĕpi nikaŋ jalađi n-tĕka śīǥra*11:63:1153*

satĕka niréŋ tĕpi kapwa sahaṙṣa,mulat irikaŋ ṙyyak agöŋ giritulya,paḍa gumuruḥ ya maśabda gaƀīra,kadi ta ya māstuti saŋ raǥuputra*11:64:1154*

wĕrĕh aputiḥ ya nirantara lumrā,kadi ta ya puṣpa pamūṙṣita niŋ ṙyyak,Alah agiraŋ ya tumon nrĕpaputra,milaṅakĕnéka kalĕṅka nikaŋ rāt*11:65:1155*

hana ta karaŋ ya katon i-dalĕm wwꜽ,bahuwiđa ratna maṇik ya Isinya,Atiśaya ƀāswara mutya ya tan kraḥ,kadi ta ya pawwata niŋ jalađi n-ton*11:66:1156*

hana ta maṇik mahaṅan ya kumambaŋ,paḍa ya mabāŋ maṇibajra satèja,jwalita lumöŋ kĕna riŋ rawiraśmi,kadi guyu niŋ jalađi n-tĕka maṅliŋ*11:67:1157*

hana ta gunuŋ ri tĕṅaḥ nikanaŋ wwꜽ,pinakawatunya maṇik śaśikānta,wuhaya Ulā ya Umuṅgwi guhānya,kadi kumĕmit Ikanaŋ maṇiratna*11:68:1158*

hyu pĕñu kakap kadiwas hana baṅlus,himi-himi tan papasaḥ saparanya,kadi ta ya mèdi siraŋ raǥuputra,hati nira moǥa kataṅguhan onĕŋ*11:69:1159*

satata mara ṅ ṙyyak agöŋ ya tumĕmpuḥ,karaṅ aruhuṙ kakĕbĕk ta ya dénya,kadi Anumoda ya téka kakīṅan,dinakara raśmi dumèḥ ya kasātan*11:70:1160*

jalađi kadi pwa gunuŋ himawān ta,sahana nikaŋ ṙyyak agöŋ śikaranya,tuwi paḍa kapwa niđāna nikaŋ śrī,paḍa ta mawidruma kapwa manāga*11:71:1161*

Ikana hayunya lĕwiḥ ya samaṅkā,ri hayu nikaŋ suraloka kasoran,surapada candra dumèḥ ya satéja,jalađi taman pawulan ya sakānti*11:72:1162*

kulagiri nāga sadiggaja ƀūmi,tuwi ya đināraṇa dé niṅ udan wān,pralaya warāha masoṙ ta ya dénya,śaraṇa nikaŋ prĕŧiwī ta ya ṅūni*11:73:1163*

hana ta ya paṙbwata muṅgwi tĕpinya,paḍa ta ruhuṙnya kaliḥ ya sumaṇḍiŋ,sama-sama göŋnya wĕlunya ya sampat,kadi susu niŋ prĕŧiwī juga buntĕr*11:74:1164*

ri sĕla-sĕlānya hawan nikanaŋ wwꜽ,kadi ta saput ni susunya kaluṅsur,tĕka Ikanaŋ ṙyyak agöŋ ya tumĕmpuḥ,kadi ta maṅumbana daṙppa sakāma*11:75:1165*

I tĕka niraŋ raǥuputra mararyan,kadi ta-tasik sira śudđa Alaṅǥya,guṇa nira kādƀuta yékana ratna,tuwi śuciśīla suđīra gaƀīra*11:76:1166*

hana maḍĕmit salĕṅĕn nikanaŋ ṙyyak,hana ya magöŋ kadi parwata māwān,pasili-siliḥ nikanaŋ suka-duḥka,winarahakĕnya kadi pwa mataṅguḥ*11:77:1167*

ndan ika manaḥ nira tan mari monĕŋ,makin aṅalaḥ dayitā ya paranya,madana Ah-o wihikan n-umanaḥ ṅwaŋ,priyawirahālara mūṙcꞓita dénya*11:78:1168*

kusuma panaḥ nira komala yāpĕs,tuwi taya tan paṅanī hati sūkṣma,kaŧam api kāmaturan hati saŋ śrī,raǥusuta moǥa tĕñuḥ Alah onĕŋ*11:79:1169*

pawana miriṙ ya malon tuwi mātis,pinaka Apuy nira saŋ hyaṅ anaṅga,Atiśaya kādbuta dénya manunwi,hati nira saŋ wirahālara dénya*11:80:1170*

Aŧa sumurup ta ƀaṭāra wiwaśwān,wĕṅi ya huwus daśadéśa pĕtĕŋ ya,Ikana Unĕŋ nira maṅkin atambĕḥ,Umilu pĕtĕŋ ta manaḥ nira dénya*11:81:1171*

taya ta winođana niŋ hati mopĕk,kadi ta pinañjara citta nirākūŋ,Inaṅĕn-aṅĕn n-ira riŋ wĕṅi tan lèn,janakasutā sira nītya cinitta*11:82:1172*

mĕtu ta ƀaṭāra śaśāṅka satéja,riṅ udaya paṙbwata ƀāswara rāmya,kadi Anumoda tumon sira mopĕk,suluh ikanaŋ daśadéśa ya māwā*11:83:1173*

Aŧa wa parāṙŧa kunĕŋ sira riŋ rāt,kalĕbur ikaŋ pĕtĕṅ aṙdđa gĕlāna,ya ta watĕkĕn nira wèhĕn anona,prakrĕti saṅ āṙyya parāṙŧa rikèŋ rāt*11:84:1174*

kusuma parĕŋ sumĕkaṙ ya saśoƀa,lawan ikanaŋ daśadéśa ya saśrī,kadi taruṇī huwus ahyas anuŋsuŋ,ri tĕka nikaŋ siniwinya manambaŋ*11:85:1175*

dadi mapasaḥ malayū-ŋ pĕtĕṅ amriḥ,sumusup i-soṙ nikanaŋ kayu māṙ~ṇĕb,ri sĕla-sĕlā nikanaŋ watu n-uṅgu,kadi matakut ri ƀaṭāra śaśāṅka*11:86:1176*

Aŧa Umulat sira saŋ raǥuputra,Umiṅĕt-iṅĕt rikanaŋ śaśiwimba,kadi wulaṅun sira moǥa wimoha, 
r-ujari ta saŋ Ari lakṣmaṇa śīǥra*11:87:1177*

Aparan ikāri tinonku satéja,ya kunaṅ ikāyuđa saŋ hyaṅ anaṅga,kadi warayaŋ maputiḥ ya malaṇḍĕp,priyawirahātura muṙcꞓita dénya*11:88:1178*

Aŧawa kilat lumarap ta kunaŋ ya,Ikana manaḥku Apūṙwwa tumon ya,gagana ya māwa taman hana méǥa,kaŧam api nitya kilatnya tinonku*11:89:1179*

{prahaṙṣiṇī}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
nā liŋ saŋ raǥutanayān wimoha citta,tātaṙ niśꞓaya rikanaŋ śaśāṅkawimba,wèt niŋ kāmaśara mawèḥ wiyoga ri ṅwaŋ,moǥékaŋ hati wulaṅun kadi pwa médan*11:90:1180*

glānosaḥ hati balisaḥ manaḥ nironĕŋ,taṙ nidrā tuwin ikanaŋ kulĕm mataṅhi,maŋ­ruṅkuk sira ta masamparan saśoka,sītātaḥ satata taman kalèñ cinitta*11:91:1181*

tat kālān madanaśarān wiƀūta monĕŋ,dé saŋ hyaŋ wulan agawé larèŋ wiyoga,prajñā saŋ Ari taruṇāṙyya lakṣmaṇojar,gamƀīra swara nira yaṙ masö mataṅguḥ*11:92:1182*

hé wīrottama raǥuputra haywa monĕŋ,tan yuktīka śaraṇa niŋ jagat pramāda,Āpan tan hana hinarĕp-harèp wanèhan,prastāwan hilaṅan ikā kalĕṅka niŋ rāt*11:93:1183*

mwāŋ sāmpun pinuji nikaŋ jagat suđīra,yan piṇḍā Inuyut-uyūtakĕnta yèŋ rāt,wruḥ pwa-ŋ rāt rika saguṇanta đīrajāti,byaktékaŋ salahasa dènta yat saśoka*11:94:1184*

tan saṅkèŋ guragaḍa ta ṅhulun mataṅguḥ,lāwan tan hana kakuraŋta riŋ wiwéka,solaḥ tāṅĕn-aṅĕn ataḥ ya pūṙwwakanya,tan yogyāt wara-warahĕn n-apan huwus wruḥ*11:95:1185*

kabwatnyan nipuṇa rikaŋ wiwéka yukti,ndan mĕṅgĕp ṅhulun awaraḥ kitèŋ kalīṅa,trĕṣṇāsiḥ ya juga makon mataṅguhātaḥ,hétunyāk pawara-waraḥ tatan sakèŋ wruḥ*11:96:1186*

{mattā}
– – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏓ = :10:
nā liŋ saŋ lakṣmaṇa maṅuđāni,tuṣṭāmbĕk saŋ nrĕpasuta rāma,māriṙ monĕŋ dadi sira nidrā,roṇḍon anwam ya ta pinakolĕs*11:97:1187*

sakwèḥ niŋ wānarabala jāgra,yatnātuṅgū pinakasurākṣa,saŋ sugrīwāmĕdĕli sumaṇḍiŋ,maṅkin nidrā raǥusuta tuṣṭa*11:98:1188*

#dwādaśamas saṙggaḥ#
<jalađaramālā>:12
– – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏓ = :12:
^12/1/1182.
sāmpun luṅhā-ŋ wĕṅi sumurup hyaŋ candra,mèḥ mĕtwa-ŋ wé dadi sumĕkaṙ taŋ tuñjuŋ,mārin saśrī kumuda kucup rūkṣālūm,tan lèn yaṙ ton hayu nikanaŋ padmārūm*12:1:1189*

lāwan wintaŋ milu sumurup sakwèḥnya,saŋ hyaŋ candrékana dinuluṙnyā ṅulwan,wadwā mīsiḥ milu saparan saŋ swāmī,nā tulyanyān milu sumurup riŋ candra*12:2:1190*

ṅkāné lĕṅkā mawuṅu ta sakwèḥ niŋ strī,moré molĕm salah aṅĕliḥ makrīḍā,saŋ hyaŋ candrāwĕdi malayū mūṙ méraŋ,saṅkā yan soṙ hayu nira dé nīkaŋ strī*12:3:1191*

mèḥ prāptā pwa-ŋ rahina sadaṙppa-ŋ kāmī,kapwāmĕṅpöŋ wĕṅi ya wijaḥ yātaṅhi,masnéhācumbana ya sĕḍĕŋ göŋ rāga,saktèŋ krīḍātiśaya bĕtaḥ saṅgāma*12:4:1192*

glānékaŋ strī guragaḍa mĕṅgĕp mélik,ṅūni n-sinyaŋ Umalĕk umuṅkuṙ héwa,saṅkā yan mĕḥ rahina Umaṅsö yāṅol,tātan méraŋ mawĕdi ya sèpèŋ kāla*12:5:1193*

ndā tan Aṅgā-ŋ taruṇa kinol tan paṅliŋ,héwāmbĕknyān salahasa ṅūni n-pasyaŋ,Āśā taŋ strī maṅisĕk-isĕk yomuṅkur,kāmī māsiḥ dadi humarĕp haṙṣāṅol*12:6:1194*

tat kālanyan patĕmu maluy kapwāṅliŋ,wèt niŋ haṙṣāƀinawa rasāmbĕknyāhyun,tuṣṭāmuktī rasa suka niŋ makrīḍā,sāt kārā mūṙcꞓita muririŋ rambutnya*12:7:1195*

tātan polaḥ paḍa kumĕtĕṙ sanđinya,Ūmrĕk māmrĕk susu ya makas kapwāmhrit*12:8:1196*
tan wruḥ riŋ rāt paḍa wiparītān mūṙcꞓā,Uśwāsādrĕs drawa hariṅĕtnyèŋ bāhu*12:9:1197*

sāmpun mūṙcꞓān pawuṅu ya mosaḥ maṅliḥ,képwan yāpèt rasa suka niŋ makrīḍā,tātan byaktān rinasa-rasan riŋ citta,Atyantālit hana riṅ awak tan pāwak*12:10:1198*

saŋ hyaŋ kāmātiśaya dahat kaśꞓaṙyyan,lumrā riŋ rāt baśa sira rin trꜽlokya,māyārūpādƀuta gumawé hyun ni-ṅwaŋ,ndā tan pāwak hana ri manaḥ niŋ kāmī*12:11:1199*

yan wruḥ ri lwiṙ nikanaṅ inak riŋ mūṙcꞓā,yan yékānuŋ parama sumuktèŋ yoga,yékā lwiṙ niŋ mati ta kunaŋ liŋ niŋ rāt,hāḥ hyāŋ kāmāsama-sama riŋ duṙgrāhya*12:12:1200*

nāhan liŋnyān uđani ta mārin mūṙcꞓā,maṅkin daṙppè surata sukākol-kolan,pīnrĕk-māmrĕk maṅarĕki wèt niŋ haṙṣa,ndā tan puṙṇnāhĕla-hĕla taḥ riŋ dwadwal*12:13:1201*

lāwan kanyā wahu winaraŋ tat kāla,yéka glānāwĕdi rumaras cittanya,méraŋ yan ton muꝁa nikana swāminya,dé niŋ pañjut sawĕṅi lanā téjanya*12:14:1202*

sinyaŋ muṅgwiŋ śayana tan aṅgā yāṅdoḥ,wètnyān méraŋ kĕtĕ-kĕtĕgĕn tan pojar,magyā tékaŋ wara taruṇāṅdon taŋ strī,maŋ­riŋriŋ yāmujuki maṅol yāṅaṙ~ki*12:15:1203*

sāmpun yāṅol dinudutakĕnya-ŋ kanyā,wètnyān magyā baśa lumukaṙ kèn-kènya,glāna-ŋ kanyā kinayuhakĕn saŋ swāmī,mamriḥ munduṙ manulak umuṅkuṙ héwa*12:16:1204*

haṙṣa-ŋ kāmī tuwi tinulak bāhunya,kahyunyātaḥ tuwi sa Ulaḥ niŋ kanyā,maṅkin yāmriḥ maṅayuhakĕn wètnyāsiḥ,glāna-ŋ strī tan tahu pinĕkul yāṅgaṙ~mus*12:17:1205*

sāmpunyāṙ wruḥ ri pakĕna nīkāŋ swāmī,moǥāmbĕknyān kĕna riṅ asiḥ lāwan hyun,ndām tan kāya n-wahu-wahu tan daṙppātaḥ,Āpan méraŋ taku-takut iŋ saṅgāma*12:18:1206*

tapwan trĕpta-ŋ taruṇa maluy yānantwa,ndan maṅsö taŋ wara taruṇī tan paṅliŋ,tan wruḥ ri ṅhèl titihi pupūnya-ŋ kanyā,pūṙwwāmbĕknyan wahu-wahu maṅkin dāǥa*12:19:1207*

mĕṅgĕp mélik Anakĕbi maṅkin mundur,śabdanyéṅas maṅilagakĕn rāmyārūm,lāwan lwiṙnyān umulat alök maṅdé hyun,jātī kanyā kadi ta ya tuhwā méṅā*12:20:1208*

wruḥ pwa-ŋ kāmī parama widagđèŋ krīḍā,cèṭṭèŋ céṣṭāmuhara sarāgèŋ kanyā,tāmolī cumbananaꝁa mūṙcꞓākalpa,salwiṙ niŋ strī madanawilāsāƀyāsa*12:21:1209*

{swāgata}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
mĕḥ wwaluŋ tabĕba riŋ sakatambay,téja saŋ hyaṅ aruṇojwala maƀrā,ṅkāna riŋ Udaya-paṙbwata saśrī,tulya rāga nikanaŋ warakāmī*12:22:1210*

na-ŋ naƀastala kadi pwa ya kĕmbaŋ,rukṣa yan taya ƀaṭāra śaśaṅka,sūṙyya raśmi kadi mitra mataṅguḥ,māwa taŋ gagana māri makiṅkiŋ*12:23:1211*

kanyakā mrĕdu manojña surūpa,bwat hajinya maṅiduŋ saha wīṇā,somya suswara sarāga kiduŋnya,sāwadāna tuwi maṅgalagīta*12:24:1212*

jāgra taŋ taruṇa kapwa ya kagyat,sakṣaṇa-ŋ wĕṅi hiḍĕpnya ya mèṅgal,Āpa taṙ warĕg asaṅga sĕḍĕŋ hyun,daṙppa riŋ wiṣaya ƀoga sarāga*12:25:1213*

candratulya nikanaŋ taruṇāṅol,nī taṅanya malurus ya satèja,candrakanta paḍa niŋ warakanyā,yan kinol drawa humis hariṅĕtnya*12:26:1214*

mwaŋ hanéki taruṇāṙdđa sutrĕṣṇa,riŋ turū ya ta turuŋ kaharĕpnya,wètnya māwa Ikanaŋ daśadéśa,glāna yan Aruṇa siḥ sakatambé*12:27:1215*

tan wĕnaŋ ya marihāra manaḥnya,tātan éraṅ umaluy ta ya muṅgaḥ,mĕṅgĕp orĕm umasö ya sumaṇḍiŋ,taŋ hanénaka gawénya wanèhan*12:28:1216*

Aṅganā huwus asaṅgama yāṅliḥ,sāk apus ni gĕluṅanya ya moré,rāmya komala muꝁanya ya somya,maṅkanékana wulatnya ya molĕm*12:29:1217*

mwaŋ hanéki taruṇī mapadohan,taṙ pahī lawan ikaŋ sapaturwan,jagra riŋ wĕhi nahan ta paḍanya,ndan dudū pi ta dumèḥ ya mataṅhya*12:30:1218*

strī sahaṙṣa masiwo ya sĕḍĕŋ hyun,taṙ warĕg Arĕki saŋ siniwinya,yan turun dadi kĕkĕl taruṇī lèŋ,n-toñ cĕlĕknya rumakĕt ri hiruŋnya*12:31:1219*

kāminī ya marahup ta ya mahyas,jāti somya mamanis pamatanya,hinyasañ cinĕlĕkan pwa ya dénya,toḥ guṇanya Upakāra jugāhyas*12:32:1220*

nitya tékana tutuknya suganđa,tan bināsita tuwi n-satata mrik,ndaḥ wijaḥ mamukawāsa gawénya,mépu méñjuh awajik-wajikan ya*12:33:1221*

maṅkana-ŋ taruṇa kapwa ya mahyas,rāmya waṙṇna wĕḍihanya suganđa,ƀāswarékana muꝁanya satéja,cihna niŋ wahu huwus rumahasya*12:34:1222*

kapwa yājĕnu manohara sumrak,mwaŋ priyanya makawit ta manisnya,sāmpun ahyas asinaŋ ya makĕmbaŋ,hyaŋ manoƀawa-ratiḥ juga sākṣāt*12:35:1223*

strī mulat ri ḍaḍa niŋ wara kāmī,n-ton wurinya ginarut priya ṅūni,saṅśayān gĕlĕṅanāta tumuṅkul,ndan hatinya rumaras ya sarāga*12:36:1224*

maṅkana-ŋ taruṇa Aṙdđa ya méraŋ,n-ton wurinya manahut pipi māṙ mrik,tuṣṭacitta muririŋ ya sahaṙṣa,sāṙjjawā-n śiwa-siwo dayitānya*12:37:1225*

hé priyèryaku gĕlāna wimūṙcꞓā,n-ton hayunta ri sĕḍĕŋta ya mahyas,sāmpun ahyas acĕlĕk pwa kitāntĕn,syūh atiṅku mananān pinanaḥta*12:38:1226*

nā halista malaris ya larasta,mwaŋ matanta taji tulya tajĕm ya,lèn hiḍĕpta mahalĕp hĕlaranya, 
nā cĕlĕkta ya Upas Upamanya*12:39:1227*

komalālĕṅis alit gĕluṅanta,śūlatulya lumaréki hatiṅku,nā susunta mawĕlū ya ta cakrā,citta cañcala tuwin kĕna dénya*12:40:1228*

nāgapāśa taliṅanta ya liṅku,ƀūṣaṇanya cuni yéka culanya,nityakāla sumirat ya sĕnönya,nā wiṣanya kapisan syaku dénya*12:41:1229*

lèn tĕṅaḥta maḍĕmit tuwi māmbĕt,kādƀutākwari tumon ya majambĕt,yak wulat riya manaḥku katūtūt,tucꞓa moǥa gigirĕn milu maṅliḥ*12:42:1230*

{mattamayūra}
– – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
mwaŋ lambaytārī ya sumambé hrĕdayaṅku,téjanyābāŋ bajra saśoƀādƀuta maƀrā,lwiṙnyān kātĕn widruma muṅgwiŋ mukapadma,huntuntāntĕn tan pacalā yéka sarinya*12:43:1231*

rāmyéruṅtātyanta larisnyāri ri piṅgir,sandéhākun pöla sĕḍĕṅtāri maṅaṙ~ki,ṅūnintāmbuŋ nā jĕnu muṅgwīri ḍaḍaṅku,mamriḥ munduṙ tāku satrĕṣṇā ri larisnya*12:44:1232*

bāhuntālyut loƀa hatiṅku g-wulatī ya,mahyun kolĕn lwiṙnya ri yan ton ya majambĕt,yapwat taṅgé yan wilĕta ṅké ri gulūṅku,byaktān riŋ tūtā saparantāku katalyan*12:45:1233*

nāhan tojaṙ saŋ taruṅāṅliŋ taruṇīnya,jañjan méñjuḥ jāti nikaŋ wwaŋ wahu wanwa,mārin méraŋ maṅkin umāsö ya sumaṇḍiŋ,wèt niŋ hyunyān ton ikana strīnya ya mahyas*12:46:1234*

{malinī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
Aŧa huwus arahup taŋ kāminī sāmpun ahyas,kadi talaga ya malwā lwiṙ nikaŋ rajya lĕṅkā,sahana ni muꝁa niŋ strī yéka tuñjuŋ paḍanya,mata calita ya mādrĕs tulya kumbaŋ maṅambuŋ*12:47:1235*

kadi gagana nataṙ niŋ rājya sāmpun sinapwan,mahirĕṅ alĕṅis alwā yāratālit hĕnīnya,kadi sinawurakĕn taŋ puṣpa wintaŋ paḍanya,ƀuwana niraṅ anaṅga ṅgānya wètnyān manojña*12:48:1236*

maśila sahana niŋ wwil wallaƀé saŋ daśāsya,paḍa ta drĕḋa suƀakti swāmi cittajña đīra,tan ulad-alid ulaḥnyāséwakāmriḥ manaṅkil,Uminakana Ulaḥ saŋ swāmi yolaḥnya tan lèn*12:49:1237*

sapaśila nikanaŋ wwil kapwa tékā mapaṅkat,matutur i-paśilanyātyanta tūtūt riṅ ājñā,praṇata matakut atwaŋ tan hanāṅambah-ambaḥ,dumunuṅ i-paśilanyānuŋ yaŧāsamƀawātaḥ*12:50:1238*

sari-sari ni guṇanyāséwakāṅhiŋ ya kahyun,sama-sama wihikan riŋ nīti cĕṭṭèŋ wiwéka,paḍa-paḍa juga yèḥ wruḥ śāstra tan sèp ya sāmpun,saminakana Ulaḥ saŋ swāmi yékā Ulaḥnya*12:51:1239*

Atiśaya ya widagđé solahiŋ ƀrĕtya kāsiḥ,saꝑala tiru-tirun riŋ satya maswāmi māsiḥ,Ikana pinakacālanyān watĕk rākṣasātaḥ,satata ya numanākĕn rāt kabèḥ tā pakāsiḥ*12:52:1240*

guragaḍa paḍa baṅkak loƀa riŋ lāƀa damƀa,muha-muha ya wimohān mohitāmañcanāŋ rāt,humaruhara Ikèŋ wwaŋ yan parèŋ đaṙmmamāṙgga,śaṭa kuṭila kaṭuṅka bwat kĕṭul kaṣṭa duṣṭa*12:53:1241*

Anuṅ amuhara duḥkèŋ wwaŋ wanèḥ nā Ulaḥnya,bahaṅ asahaṅ atiṅgaṙ kapwa sāhitya caṅkak,patakuraṅan asiṅsĕt yan pisit siṅha sākṣāt,mawila-wila mawiṅkal woknya mawyaŋ kumisnya*12:54:1242*

krama lumaku manaṅkil saŋ mahāmantri muꝁya,Anuṅ atuha patiḥ ṅkā saŋ prahasta praśāsta,Atiśaya sira đīrāꝁyāti riŋ śūra wīra,naya winaya widagđé tiṅkahiŋ rājanīti*12:55:1243*

salaku nira manaṅkil ƀrĕtya waṙggāduluṙ kwèḥ,paḍa ya lituhayu wruḥ riŋ Ulaḥ rāja yogya,masiga ya wihikan riŋ Iṅgitākāra céṣṭā,sahana ni guṇa niŋ wwaŋ ƀrĕtya tātan mapuṅguŋ*12:56:1244*

saṅ apaṅalih apaṅkat sèwu saṅꝁyā panĕṇḍas,paḍa-paḍa saṅ anaṇḍaŋ maŋ­rakĕt koṭi piṇḍa,kalalu ya ta pamuntat tan wiwékan wilaŋnya,makakurutug atuṇḍuŋ tūt hawan wāḥ paḍanya*12:57:1245*

wataṅan atiśayèŋ lwā yéka kāṅkĕn samudra,gupura ya paripūṙṇnāpūṙwwa yèkā karaŋnya,sahana niraṅ anaṅkil ṅkā ri hèŋ yan pararyan,kadi ta ya kalibiŋ lwaḥ yan paṅāmbĕg katambak*12:58:1246*

ƀaṭa saha bala kapwāsaṅgrahānéka pawwat,Inawitakĕn i-hèŋ niŋ gopurāpūṙwwa riŋ kwèḥ,tatan ujarĕn ikānuŋ kādƀuta-ŋ wwaŋ tumon ya,Ikaṅ aƀinawa riŋ rāt yéka pawwatnya makraḥ*12:59:1247*

liman atiśaya daṙppa krūra tan swaŋ galaknya,kagiri-giri Asiŋ wwaŋ maswa śīṙṇnāta dénya,tuwi ta pinakapawwat dé nikaŋ wīra śakti,Asama-sama ya sāmpun paṇḍitèŋ hastiśikṣā*12:60:1248*

hana ta ya wihikan riŋ Aśwaśikṣā wiśéṣa,ry-aji niṅ ahawaśākĕn tuṅgaṅan wus widagđa,hana ta kadi panaḥ drĕs niŋ manaḥ drĕsnya maṅrap,ya ta Inawitakĕnnyottuṅga niŋ tuṅgaṅan kwèḥ*12:61:1249*

Aŧawa hana ta wīrāśꞓaṙyya pawwatnya rodra,wwara ta warak ulāgöŋ siṅha barwaŋ lawan moŋ,saka sapuluh iniṇḍit dénya tan pañjaré ya,kadi ta ya kura pawwat lwiṙ nikaŋ siṅha dénya*12:62:1250*

hana mulih umahas riŋ swaṙgga maŋ­rudđa kéndran,Asiṅ isi ni taman hyaŋ Indra yékénalapnya,ya ta tĕka paḍa moliḥ wwa-wwahan pawwatanya,kadi Amrĕta rasanyāmānuṣātyanta paŧya*12:63:1251*

hana ta wahu tĕkāwwat puṣpa niŋ pārijāṭa,kalawan ikana ronyānuŋ sĕḍĕŋ komalānwam,ya tikana Inalapnya glāna saŋ hyaŋ kahĕntyan,paḍa mawĕdi kumöl kul tulya tātan hanolaḥ*12:64:1252*

{madahaṙṣa}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏓ = :18:
Aŧa huwus umawit pwa pawwat nikaŋ wīra maṅhèṙ kabèḥ,Umĕtu ta sira saŋ daśāsyāśilèŋ ratna siṅhāsana,kanaka maya maṇik ta kĕmbaŋ nirānéka taŋ ƀūṣaṇa,tuwi sira mahirĕŋ kadi pwékanaŋ kālaméǥākilat*12:65:1253*

sawĕtu nira rikaŋ saƀā śīǥra monīkanaŋ kāhala,dadi tumama siraŋ patiḥ wrĕdđa lāwan ta sénāpati,satĕka nira parĕŋ masö gorawātwaŋ tumuṅkul kabèḥ,maśila ri harĕpan niraŋ rāwaṇé pöhaniŋ maṇḍapa*12:66:1254*

#trayodaśamas saṙggaḥ#
<rucira>:13
⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
^13/1/1247.
tĕlas masö sahana niraŋ patiḥ kabèḥ,siraŋ wiƀīṣaṇa juga tapwa yaṇ ḍatĕŋ,pijĕṙ maṅaṙcꞓana ri ƀaṭāra śaṅkara,maṅĕn-n-aṅĕn Inaka nikaŋ jagat kabèḥ*13:1:1255*

manaḥ nira sŧiti masamāđi tañcala,wulat marūm mrĕdu mamanis manohara,kalĕṅka niŋ hati ya hilaŋ Ikaŋ tamaḥ,taman katon ikana karākṣasan nira*13:2:1256*

huwus maṅaṙcꞓana saha citta niṙmmala,Umèḥ lumakwa ta sira taṙ salaḥ dunuŋ,masö sirèṅ ibu katĕkā manaṅkila,hĕlĕm-hĕlĕm tar alupa ƀakti riŋ Ibu*13:3:1257*

swadaṙmma niŋ Anak inaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn nira,kasajjanan ya juga lanā Inaṙjjana,nahan dumèḥ sira satatān panĕmbaha,tirūn ikaŋ parajana ƀakti riŋ Ibu*13:4:1258*

mulat pwa saŋ Ibu dadi tuṣṭa taŋ manaḥ,tumon ṅ-anak praṇata Umèḥ manaṅkila,masö sirāṙ wuwusi ta saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,sukā nikaŋ ƀuwana ya donnyujaṙ nira*13:5:1259*

Anakku hé suƀaga wiƀīṣaṇād wulat,nda tag waraḥ kita ri kaduḥkan i-ṅhulun,manaḥku moǥa ya karuṇī ta yālara,tumon ikaŋ ƀuwana nanā sadālara*13:6:1260*

kakanta saŋ daśamuꝁa mūṙkꝁa mūḋa ya,Atīta niṙǥrĕṇa tamataṙ kĕnèṅ asiḥ,jagat kabèḥ malara gĕlāna dè nira,swaśakti yékana paṅayāya tan kalèn*13:7:1261*

Ikaŋ jagat kadi kĕna dé nikaŋ wiṣa,kakanta rāwaṇa wiṣatulya maŋlaré,kunĕŋ yatanyan upaśamā ta-taṅguhi,kitāmrĕtā humuripana-ŋ jagat kabèḥ*13:8:1262*

nya yogya taṅguha ri kakanta rāwaṇa,siraŋ raǥūttama juga liṅku sĕmbahĕn,priyā nirékana dulurĕn panĕmbaha,ya toṣađā gumawaya tuṣṭa niŋ jagat*13:9:1263*

daśānana mrisakiti déwatā kabèḥ,Ikaŋ hiḍĕp kadi wiṣa kālakūṭa ya,nda saŋ hyaṅ īśwara paḍa saŋ raǥūttama,Awās pĕjaḥ niyata kakanta dé nira*13:10:1264*

nihan dumèh ikana manaḥku niśꞓaya,I patya saŋ daśamuꝁa dé nirèŋ raṇa,nanā nikèŋ nagara wiśīṙṇna yātunu,nahan dumèḥnyaku pi saniśꞓayèŋ pati*13:11:1265*

nya taŋ taman satata kinatwaṅan daṅū,mĕné pwa ya pralaya kayunya kapwa rūg,luwan balāđika ƀaṭamantri rākṣasa,prawīra śakti tuwi daṅū pĕjaḥ kabèḥ*13:12:1266*

mataŋnya taṅguhi ka-kakanta duṙjjana,waraḥ ry-ulaḥ nikana saṅ āṙyya sajjana,yatanya taṙ wihaṅa kunaŋ t-upāya taḥ,prihĕn tĕmĕn wara-warahĕn riṅ āgama*13:13:1267*

nahan ta liŋ saṅ ibu makon mataṅguha,siraŋ wiƀīṣaṇa tamataṙ wihaŋ kinon*13:14:1268*
Apan manaḥ nira maharĕp mataṅguha,Ujaṙ niraŋ Ibu juga nī hinèṙ nira*13:15:1269*

majaṙ pwa saŋ Ibu magiraŋ Ikaŋ manaḥ,makin mawās ikana Aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn nira,ḍatĕŋ sirā tama ta manaṅkilé dalĕm,tĕlas tamĕŋ wataṅan apūṙwwa riŋ hayu*13:16:1270*

pasuk siraṙ wulati ta saŋ kakāśila,maluṅguh iŋ kanakapalaṅka yāpuya,Awak nirāhirĕṅ alĕṅis kukus juga,Ikaŋ wulat-latu-latu tulya cañcala*13:17:1271*

sakèṅ asiḥ sira tuwi yaṙ pawèḥ wulat,nda rūpajāti katatakut wulat nira,tatan pahī kalawan ikaŋ Ulā biṣa,Ulaḥ nirāmuhara takut nikaŋ mulat*13:18:1272*

Aŧomasö pwa sira ta saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,sagorawa praṇata manĕmbah iŋ kaka,madĕg ta sādara Umasö sirāśila,samīpa niŋ kanakapalaṅka tan madoḥ*13:19:1273*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
huwus maluṅguḥ pwa siraŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,rikaŋ saƀā sāƀinawojwalān katon,sahaṙṣa mojaṙ ta siraŋ daśānana,ri saŋ patiḥ kapwa patiḥ wuwus nira*13:20:1274*

sakwèḥta śaktīŋ raṇa śūra sāhasa,tan swaŋ masö riŋ samarāsamèŋ biṣa,praśāsta śūrātiśayèŋ jagat kabèḥ,Asiŋ musuḥ śīṙṇna ya dènta sakṣaṇa*13:21:1275*

tatan wĕlaŋ śudđa manaḥta yālawan,huwus kita wruḥ riṅ upāya niśꞓaya,wiśudđa riŋ nīti wiśéṣa budđimān,Asiŋ sināđyānta daṅū kasidđa ya*13:22:1276*

mĕné pwa yan ton ndya ta déya riŋ musuḥ,si rāma sāmpun tĕka riŋ mahéndra ya,Umèḥ ya maṅké ta Umĕntasaŋ tasik,lawan watĕk wré pwa balanya taṙ wanèḥ*13:23:1277*

ṅūnin patī wīra balanta rākṣasa,si tāṭakā mwaŋ si wirāđa dūṣaṇa,nahan pĕjaḥ dé ni si rāma riŋ Alas,nda tan masĕṅhit ri lĕmĕḥta riŋ tukar*13:24:1278*

bālī ya mitraṅku Awakku tulya ya,kāsiḥku māsiḥ ry-aku taṙ halaŋ-ṅ-alaŋ,pĕjaḥ pwa dé niŋ raǥuputra taṙ walĕs,kadi pwa tan śakti hiḍĕpku wèt hĕnĕŋ*13:25:1279*

lāwan nikaŋ sy-akṣa Anakku kāsyasiḥ,Upékṣakātaḥ kita ṅūni yaṙ pĕjaḥ,nya taŋ kaḍatwan tamatan paśéṣa ya,gĕsĕŋ kabèḥ ndan humĕnĕŋ Ataḥ kita*13:26:1280*

taṅèḥ pwa sampay ni si rāma yak hiḍĕp,rĕṅö ya maṅké ya Umèḥ ya mĕntasa,tajaṙ ta ya ndyékaṅ upāya riŋ tasik,yadin tĕkā ṅké naya yukti kiṅkiṅĕn*13:27:1281*

daśāsya nā liŋ nira mojar iŋ patiḥ,madĕg watĕk wīra masiṅhanāda ya,parĕŋ ta yāṅambul anambut āyuđa,mĕniŋ ta kadganya krĕtāla laṅǥala*13:28:1282*

hanāmutĕṙ ḍaṇḍa gadī sagadgada,wanèḥ manāmbut paraśunya lèn laras,madĕg ya makrak kadi siṅha ƀīṣaṇa,mintonakĕn gyānya makoliha-ŋ musuḥ*13:29:1283*

prahasta papraŋ pratitèŋ prawīra ya,nahan tuhanyān umĕniŋ rikaŋ saƀa,mahöm ya momo ya makoliha-ŋ musuḥ,humuŋ ya mojaṙ kadi moŋ sĕḍĕŋ galak*13:30:1284*

sojaṙ mahārāja tĕlas ta kabwatan,Apā guṇā niŋ wwaṅ ahöm tĕwas Iwö,musuḥ ta māpĕs kadi lumbu yak hiḍĕp,muṅuṙ-muṅuṙ duṙnaya lumbu tan pahi*13:31:1285*

hiḍĕp mahārāja mĕné balik dahat,ṅūnin sukū ṅ-indra tamāt haro-hara,tatan hanāhöm kamĕnānya mapraṅa,maṅké pwa yan mānuṣa-śatru yéniwö*13:32:1286*

lawan mahārāja kadi pwa tan wulat,suśakti niŋ rākṣasa wīra riŋ raṇa,nihan taṅ āditya yadin ya patyana,nda kam rĕmuk hyaŋ prĕŧiwī pasātusĕn*13:33:1287*

nya taŋ wulan yan ya kunaŋ ya patyana,hulunta tuṅgal wĕnaṅomaṅāna ya,yadin hĕlön yan gilutĕn Asiŋ Ataḥ,sakahyuna śrī wararāja dadya ya*13:34:1288*

Ikā pwa yan śatru si rāma lakṣmaṇa,lawan nikaŋ wānara mūḋa tan pira,kĕpĕl-kĕpĕl tulya nikā yadin tĕkā,tatan Iwö tan sapahömakĕn naya*13:35:1289*

kꜽlāśa kolāhala ṅūni yāhaṅan,sinaṅga dé saŋ praƀu riŋ taṅan kiwā,ƀaṭāra māhéśwara dampatī sira,Umuṅgwi puñcak nikanaŋ gunuŋ tuwi*13:36:1290*

haywénujaṙ tékana śakti saŋ praƀu,wadwāḍĕmit niŋ bala rākṣasojarĕn,nya-ŋ ƀūmi dadyākĕna dénya piṇḍaha,muṅgwé ruhuṙ swaṙgga I-soṙ nikaŋ lĕmaḥ*13:37:1291*

mwaŋ dūta niŋ rāǥawa wānarāđama,Ikān panunwī tuwi tan paśakti ya,kunaŋ dumèḥ rākṣasa sora dé nikā,pajātya niŋ śaktyagĕlĕm pramāda ya*13:38:1292*

mataŋnya tātan paguṇékanaŋ naya,yadin pahömākĕna tan hanāṅapa,Apan nikaŋ śakti daṅū huwus Alaḥ,salaḥ kiniṅkiŋ ta si rāma yan tĕkā*13:39:1293*

nahan Ujaṙ niŋ bala rākṣasèŋ saƀā,Alaḥ ṅ-ahĕṅkāra manaḥnya gaṙjjita,malĕs ta mojaṙ sira saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,sagorawātaṅguha don irā-n sahur*13:40:1294*

hé wīra sakwèḥta hulun ri saŋ praƀu,yuktīkanojaṙta kabèḥ tatan salaḥ,Apan kitékā hinarĕp-harĕp tĕmĕn,makoliha-ŋ śatru makabyaya-ŋ hurip*13:41:1295*

Iké mahārāja matakwan iŋ naya,lawālawānuŋ winiwéka saŋ praƀu,Upāya yātaḥ sahuranta ménaka,lukan pwa yan sambutakĕn taṅ āyuđa*13:42:1296*

doniŋ mahöm budđiwiwéka yénayu,tatan kaśūran paṅayāya riŋ naya,Asiŋ mahāprajña ri sojar īŋ Aji,nahan kinon mojara mājarèŋ naya*13:43:1297*

sakiṅkiṅĕn saŋ raǥuputra yaṙ tĕkā,Apan nikā dūta nirātiśakti ya,ṅūnin panunwi syapa rākṣasāṅlawan,ta śūra méraŋ ya kabèḥ tĕlas hilaŋ*13:44:1298*

walīṅa yā tan kĕna nāgapāśa ya,pramāda yékā dalihanta yan luput,huwus masiṅsĕt pwa Awaknya kāpusan,mataŋnya śaktinya dumèḥ ya sāhasa*13:45:1299*

Aṅhiŋ Ikaŋ pāśa marāyuđottama,tuŋtuŋ ni śaktinta Ikā taman kalèn,ya pwāpasaḥ sakṣaṇa śīṙṇna yan tatas,tātan pramādanta mataŋ nikān luput*13:46:1300*

yatnānta riŋ nīti t-anūt iṅ āgama,haywāwamānèŋ wihikan rikaŋ naya,Apan nikaŋ śakti kabèḥ nda tan lanā,Akwèh ahĕṅkāra manaḥnya sor ataḥ*13:47:1301*

tan swaŋ kata ṅwaŋ mamĕnaŋ rikaŋ raṇa,mwaŋ tan Asiŋ ṅwaŋ kahanan rikaŋ hayu,saŋ đīra sāmpun paripakwa riŋ naya,ṅkā yan lanāŋ wīṙyya lawan nikaŋ śri ya*13:48:1302*

lawan nihan hétu nikaŋ hayū lanā,widagđa ni-ṅwaŋ mawiwéka ṣadguṇa,guṇanya doṣanya nahan kinawruhan,tĕlas katon yan saꝑalāta yan tinūt*13:49:1303*

nya-ŋ sanđi lèn wigraha yānasāsana,lawan nika dwéṣa sahāya yāśrayan,nā-ŋ ṣadguṇānuŋ pakĕnā nikaŋ naya,kinawruhan saŋ maharĕp jayèŋ raṇa*13:50:1304*

janānurāgottamaƀūmi niŋ naya,sahāya niŋ ṣadguṇa hétu niŋ jaya,yapwan tayékaŋ Anurāga saŋ praƀu,wyaṙŧékanaŋ ṣadguṇa niṙguṇān hana*13:51:1305*

yadin masorèŋ bala kośa saŋ praƀu,Awās ya soréka musuḥ nirèŋ raṇa,Apan hanékaŋ Anurāga yāgĕlis,wĕnaŋ paṅākaṙṣaṇa kośa lèn bala*13:52:1306*

kāmādi ṣad waṙgga musuḥ tatan madoḥ,nahan dumèḥ taŋ Anurāga tan hana,mataŋnya ṣadwaṙgga kayatna saŋ praƀu,dinohakĕn tan hinanākĕn iŋ hati*13:53:1307*

ya tan baśèŋ śatru Anuŋ hanèŋ hawak,mwaŋ tan prayatnèṅ anurāga lèn naya,pirā ta kośā nira lèn balā nira,musuḥ tiké kāla nikaŋ raṇān tĕka*13:54:1308*

lawan nihan nitya kayatna saŋ praƀu,haywéka mapraŋ yadiyan taya ṅ ꝑala,yapwan panon lāƀa magöŋ kapaṅguha,tan dadya dadyāpi kĕnékanaŋ raṇa*13:55:1309*

tan kéwalāpraŋ kinanityakĕn nira,yadin pamitran tuwi yatna saŋ praƀu,Apan nikā tan niyatāꝑalā hayu,dadinya saṅkā nikanaŋ halān tĕkā*13:56:1310*

Ikā ta wèḥ kāla hinèrakĕn nira,lawan nikaŋ déśa wiśéṣaṇā pinèt,yapwan saṅ apraŋ swaṅ amitra saŋ praƀu,wyaṙŧāŋ prayā sakṣaṇa tan tĕmu ṅ ꝑala*13:57:1311*

mataŋnya dé saŋ maharĕp jayèŋ raṇa,Upāya yātaḥ winiwéka pūṙwwaka,salwiṙ nikaŋ nīti pananđya riŋ musuḥ,nyānuŋ Inālocita saŋ mamèt hayu*13:58:1312*

nahan ta dé saŋ wihikan rikaŋ naya,mataŋnya tan wrĕdđya Ikā musuḥ nira,mitranya pinriḥ nira mélikériya,yāwat ya mélik niyatān paré sira*13:59:1313*

tĕlas maliḥ pwékana mitra niŋ musuḥ,sinwāgatan dé nira riŋ saménaka,winèḥ sakahyunya mataŋnya tāsiha,waraḥ ta yèŋ śīla nikaŋ musuḥ nira*13:60:1314*

lawan ta sakwèḥ ni sawaṙgga niŋ musuḥ,ya ténupāyān papasāha mapraṅa,Apan sĕḍĕŋnyān patukaṙ taman patūt,jātinya mètāśraya tan salaḥ dunuŋ*13:61:1315*

tĕlasnya sāk waṙgga nikaŋ musuḥ nira,rikān paṅārĕmba maṅiṣṭi yāpraṅa,tataṙ wawaŋ wèḥ lumĕkas dumon musuḥ,Asiḥ ni rowaŋ nira yéniṅötakĕn*13:62:1316*

śaktinya ƀaktinya nahan kinawruhan,katon ya tan dadya Umantunèŋ raṇa,lawan tan aṅgā ya marī rikaŋ wanèḥ,nahan tinonton ri samūha niŋ bala*13:63:1317*

tĕlas nirāṙ wruḥ ri samūha niŋ bala,mwaŋ duṙgga Uṅgwan nira tan kasaṅśaya,saṅkĕp ta riŋ sañjata kośa wāhana,yan maṅkana byakta jayā nirèŋ raṇa,
yan duṙbbalā saŋ praƀu tan wĕnaŋ marā,lawan nikaŋ śatru ya tan wĕnaŋ tĕkā,yatnā sirèŋ rājya tamolahèŋ kuṭa,duṙgga prawīrāyuđa kośa saṅgrahan*13:64:1318*

yapwan nikaŋ śatru dumona saŋ praƀu,salwiṙ nikaŋ duṙgga ya tāśrayā nira,tambak gunuŋ wway madalĕm juraŋ rĕṇök,wwaŋ kwèḥ kunaŋ yékana duṙgga rakṣakā*13:65:1319*

mwaŋ yan mahāśakti kunaŋ musuḥ nira,makwèḥ ta mitranya balanya tan malaḥ,rikān pamètāśraya mitra māsiha,Anuŋ mahāśakti wĕnaŋ mawèḥ hayu*13:66:1320*

nahan ta dé saŋ tahu riŋ nayāhayu,dumèḥ sirāmaṅguha sidđa riŋ raṇa,kunaŋ ya pinriḥ Inupāya dé nira,janānurāgāta ya watwaniŋ naya*13:67:1321*

janānurāga pwa ya tan hané kita,sawaṙgga mitranta kabèḥ taman wulat,Umūṙ ya mārin para tan sagorawa,Alaḥ Umaṅluḥ ya manon ulaḥ salaḥ*13:68:1322*

ndya tékanānuŋ hinarĕp-harĕp tĕmĕn,mataŋnya tan sora rikaŋ raṇāṅgaṇa,Apan saka kwèḥ nikanaŋ tayé kita,ya tāpuluŋ muṅgu ri saŋ raǥūttama*13:69:1323*

taman pahīṅan sira yan maṅĕn-n-aṅĕn,Apan rikaŋ śakti lĕwiḥ tĕmĕn sira,Ikā si bālī bali śaktimānta ya,taŧāpi saŋ rāma matī ya taṙ maṅèl*13:70:1324*

kapīndra sugrīwa rinatwakĕn nira,Ikā ta mitranta tĕmĕn taman kalèn,magöŋ kaƀaktinya ri saŋ raǥūttama,hilaŋ sahāyanta hayunta ya kṣaya*13:71:1325*

Ikā pratāpanta magöŋ hilaŋ pwa wèḥ,Apan pĕjaḥ rākṣasa wīra tan malaḥ,śīṙṇna-ŋ taman sy-akṣa nahan huwus pĕjaḥ,ƀraṣṭātunu-ŋ rājya wiśīṙṇna yāgĕsĕŋ*13:72:1326*

mwaŋ tañ jayātaḥ rikanaŋ musuḥ madoḥ,Apat kalaḥ dé ni musuḥta yāparö,rāgādi yāgöŋ lagi maŋlagè kita,nda tan pamaŋ paŋ juga hīna taṙ walĕs*13:73:1327*

lawan sawaṙgganta kabèḥ wimūḋa ya,makāmbĕk-āmbĕknya paraŋ mukèṅ aji,taman wiwékèŋ naya wètnya wèn kala,tātan panon rāt aƀimāna kéwala*13:74:1328*

bālī ya mitranta Anuŋ huwus pĕjaḥ,sugrīwa yékā mahurip maliḥ pwa ya,musuḥta makwèḥ wihikan ta yèŋ naya,mataŋnya ƀaktīka ri saŋ raǥūttama*13:75:1329*

sirāta mitrānta taman sasamƀawa,Apan paḍa krođa paḍāṅhiḍĕp lara,sirālarāpan n-inalap priyā nira,kitālarān śīṙṇna balanta dé nira*13:76:1330*

pahuntu lāwan wĕsi yan paḍākasa,rikān paḍāpĕsnya tinon ta yātĕmu,nahan paḍantat paḍa paŋhiḍĕp lara,yadin samitrā kita karwa māsiha*13:77:1331*

Ikā gĕlĕŋ saŋ raǥuputra yāpuya,murub ya dé niŋ bala wānarāṅina,Ikopaśāmanta ya tāṅkĕna wwaya,dumèḥ gĕlèŋ marya murub rikaŋ hati*13:78:1332*

lawan sĕḍĕṅtāt malagā lawan sira,Agöŋ ta ƀāgyanta hiḍĕpku yat puliḥ,Apan mahāśakti widagđa riŋ naya,lĕwiḥ ta wèḥ riŋ Anurāga riŋ jagat*13:79:1333*

Apan lĕwihtèŋ bala kośa paŋhaḍa,makin kitānĕmbaha haywa maŋlawan,Apan yadin sora taman tĕmu ṅ ꝑala,kita pwa soṙ kośa balanta ya kṣaya*13:80:1334*

yapwan kita byakta jayā rikaŋ raṇa,mataŋnya haywāta maṅiṣṭi mapraṅa,Apan nikaŋ wwaŋ gumawè kasaṅśayan,sukanya miṅgat lara yāpuluŋ riya*13:81:1335*

nahan tinon saŋ praƀu yaṙ gawé-ŋ gawé,byayanya méman tuwi duṙyyaśériya,sukāwasānanya ꝑalanya Uttama,nahan ya pinriḥ ginawé niraŋ praƀu*13:82:1336*

kita pwa yāṅiṣṭi makāṙyya mapraṅa,kṣayanta makwèḥ tuwi lāƀa duṙllaƀa,lawan tĕmuntèṅ awasāna tan hana,mataŋnya yogyāt praṇatān panĕmbaha*13:83:1337*

Anakta mitranta balanta yan pĕjaḥ,praƀāwa saŋ rāma dumèḥnya tan kalèn,sugrīwa mitranta Umūṙ maraŋ sira,tan dadya tékan maluyomarè kita*13:84:1338*

nihan dumèḥ ya praṇatā manĕmbaha,kasajjanan yāta tinūt nda tan kalèn,swajāti saŋ sāđu tĕlas winèḥ hayu,lanāgawé pratyupakāra riŋ mawèḥ*13:85:1339*

lawan nikaŋ wānara wīra đīra ya,tataṙ hanātaḥ malihomarè kita,Agöŋ Asiḥnyé sira saŋ raǥūttama,mahöm kabèḥ mo dadahĕŋ raṇāṅgaṇa*13:86:1340*

maṇik lawan mās wĕḍihan malit kunaŋ,pawèha riŋ wānara tan parā ta ya,ta mūlya taŋ mūlya kabèḥ tĕkériya,ṅhiŋ wwa-wwahan yaṙ kaharĕpnya tan wanèḥ*13:87:1341*

yapwan nikaŋ Aṅgada liŋta ya prihĕn,pétĕn marā ṅké kirimĕnta mās maṇik,taŧāpi tan dadya Ataḥ marö kita,Apan mahāsāđu suđīra budđimān*13:88:1342*

mwaŋ tak manon śakti rikèŋ jagat kabèḥ,Anuŋ sayogyā śaraṇānta riŋ raṇa,haywā lĕwiḥ saṅka ri saŋ raǥūttama,paḍā nirātaḥ tuwi tat pamaṅguha*13:89:1343*

sakwèḥ niraŋ déwata yukti Āśrayan,ri ṅūni kānyānumanèŋ jagat kita,tapwan hanāsiḥ ta musuḥta taŋ sarāt,ndi tāt amèta-ŋ śaraṇānuṅ āsiha*13:90:1344*

yapwan ƀaṭāréśwara liŋta Āśrayan,taŧāpi tan māsiha riŋ wwaṅ udđata,Apan sukā saŋ śuƀaśīla don ira,tatan Asiŋ wwaŋ pwa kināsihan nira*13:91:1345*

Iké ri lĕṅkā Atiduṙgga-duṙggama,samudra gamƀīra gunuŋ pagĕṙ nira,kabwat nikān maṅkana tan ya paŋhaḍa,ta duṙgga dé saŋ Aƀimāna-mānasa*13:92:1346*

saṅkĕp kitèŋ sañjata kośa wāhana,wadwā niraŋ rāǥawa tan pasañjata,kabwat nikān tan hana ṅ-āyuđériya,saṅkĕp nikān maṅkana kapwa sāyuđa*13:93:1347*

Asiŋ mawit t-āyuđa yan tĕkèŋ raṇa,tahĕn magöŋ mwaŋ watu paṙbwatottama,yan tan hana-ŋ paṙbwata lèn śilātala,kukūnya huntunya paḍāyuđériya*13:94:1348*

tatan hanātaḥ gamananya duṙbbala,Aṅhiŋ balantékana liṅku duṙbbala,mataŋnya tan lèna lanākĕnā huwus,manĕmbahātaḥ ri ƀaṭāra rāǥawa*13:95:1349*

ṅhulun n-umĕṅgĕp humĕnĕŋ manaṅguhi,tatan sumaṅkā ri widagđa ni ṅhulun,trĕṣṇérikaŋ ƀoga taman warĕg suka,na hétu niŋ mūḋa wĕnaŋ manaṅguhi*13:96:1350*

nahan ya taṅguḥ nira saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,kumonakĕn saŋ raǥuputra sĕmbahĕn,sakrođa tāmbĕk nira saŋ daśānana,tataṙ sahuṙ héwa ri saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa*13:97:1351*

#catuṙ daśamas saṙggaḥ#
<basantatilaka>:14
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :14:
^14/1/1344.
tat kāla yaṙ kahĕnĕṅan ta siraŋ daśāsya,mojaṙ ta-taŋ kaki ṅaran nira saŋ sumāli,wruḥ riŋ wiwèka kaki riŋ Ibu budđimānta,saṅké ry-asiḥ nira sagorawa yaṙ pataṅguḥ*14:1:1352*

hé rāwaṇātiśaya yogya wuwusnyarinta,tat saṅśayan pituhu haywa wihaŋ hatinta,Āpan sĕḍĕŋ kita mituhwa lanā hayunta,yapwat wihaŋ niyata yan pralayā sa-lĕṅkā*14:2:1353*

nyānuŋ dumèh aku mituhwa Ujaṙnyarinta,saŋ rāmadéwa sira mānuṣa tuṅga-tuṅgal,laṅkap jugāyuđa nirèŋ raṇa taṙ wanèhan,kapwāpa yan kapalupuy pwa balanta ṅūni*14:3:1354*

wwāliṅku yan duga-dugāta taman pamāyā,mwaŋ tan wruhāpraṅa rikaŋ gaganāntarāla,tātan kabèhana ri saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma,wĕt niŋ suśakti nira hétu nikān wiśīṙṇna*14:4:1355*

ndan saṅśayaṅkwi rasikāpi Upāya niŋ hyaŋ,mwaŋ saŋ watĕk rĕṣi kabèḥ magawé Upāya,wwaŋ śaktimānta ginawé nira kāraṇī niŋ,lĕṅkāpura pralaya rākṣasa tan paśéṣā*14:5:1356*

mwaŋ dé ƀaṭāra magawé naya sūkṣma mèbwĕḥ,wwaŋ lwiṙnya wānara balanya Apūṙwwa riŋ rāt,yapwan lagāna rasikā yadiyan tĕkā ṅké,byaktān pĕjaḥ kita mataŋnya tanĕmbahītaḥ*14:6:1357*

Akwèh asamƀawa huwus rinĕṅö pwa ṅūni,tan yogya kāraṇa nikaŋ pati yomatīya,śatru hyaṅ indra karĕṅö ta si wrĕtra nāma,yékaŋ Apūṙwwa Umatī ya wĕrĕḥ nikaŋ wwꜽ*14:7:1358*

pinriḥ binajra tamataṙ kawĕnaŋ Akampya,sakwèḥ niṅ āyuđa tĕñuḥ tĕka ri ṙyya śīṙṇna,sinyaŋ ya madyusa ri mađya nikaŋ samudra,dé saŋ hyaṅ indra kapisan ya tinampĕkan wwꜽ*14:8:1359*

nā taŋ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ taya moli ri ṙyya,śaktinya tan papaḍa śīṙṇna Asiŋ musuḥnya,saṅké ry-anugraha ƀaṭāra dumèḥnya śakti,tan matya riŋ rahina riŋ wĕṅi liŋ ƀaṭāra*14:9:1360*

tan déwa dānawa Anuŋ wĕnaṅomatī ya,tan yakṣa rākṣasa piśāca manuṣya tīṙyyak,sakwèḥ niṅ āyuđa taman paṅapéka ri ṙyya,nā liŋ ƀaṭāra paraméśwara nugrahé ya*14:10:1361*

sāmpun winèḥ ta ya warātiśayéka riŋ rāt*14:11:1362*
daṙppāwĕrö ya wiparīta taman panoliḥ,tan déwa tan rĕṣi tĕlas karuhun tikaŋ wwaŋ,ƀraṣṭānanā sahana niŋ ƀuwanāṇḍa dénya*14:12:1363*

tapwan hanāta gamanānya tumoliha-ŋ rāt,glāna-ŋ watĕk rĕṣi lawan surasidđasaṅǥa,kapwāsamūha Umĕgil ri ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu,Āpan sirékana surākṣa rumākṣa riŋ rāt*14:13:1364*

māsiḥ ƀaṭāra winĕgil magawé ta māyā,wwaŋ lwiṙnyawak nira Ikaŋ muꝁa siṅharūpa,krūrékanaŋ kuku ya bajra paḍanya tīkṣṇa,māyā ƀaṭāra narasiṅha ṅaran nirèŋ rāt*14:14:1365*

kyātīŋ sarāt sira matī kala dꜽtya mūṙkꝁa,śīṙṇna-ŋ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ binĕlaḥ ḍaḍanya,Atyanta kasnya wĕsi tulya nikā Awaknya,ndā tan pasāra tinĕwĕk nira riŋ nakāgra*14:15:1366*

nāhan Asamƀawa Anuŋ rinĕṅö ya ṅūni,tan yogya kāraṇa nikaŋ pati yomatī ya,nāhan dumèh aku makona Ataḥ prayatnā,riŋ śatru yadyapin asora titiḥnya towi*14:16:1367*

lāwan hiḍĕpku kita Aṙdđa masoṙ titiḥta,Āpan pramāda rikanaŋ naya niṙwiwéka,Ékānta wigraha Anuŋ ginĕgö ya dènta,saḍgūṇa yogya ya gĕgön tuwi tad gĕgö ya*14:17:1368*

mwaŋ tat hiḍĕp guṇa nikaŋ Anurāga riŋ rāt,solaḥta sāhasa sasaṙ tan anūt i-yukti,saŋ Āṙyya sāđu sasiwin sira śatru dèŋta,maryāda saŋ sujana sajjana tad-gawé ya*14:18:1369*

nāhan kasoṙta ya mataŋnya manĕmbahātaḥ,sojaṙnyarinta pituhun Apatan salaḥ ya,Āpan ya hétu ni hayunta hiḍĕpku tan lén,ƀaktyanta kéwala ri saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma*14:19:1370*

nā liŋ niraŋ kaki-kakiṅkiṅan amrihojar,saṅkā ry-asiḥ nira mapinta kasiḥ mataṅguḥ,saŋ rāwaṇātiśaya māna manaḥ nirākas,tātaṙ lĕgö sapinatiḥ tuwi taṙ patiḥ ya*14:20:1371*

{turagagati}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
kāla saŋ kaki sĕḍĕŋ mawara-waraḥ,kumƀakaṙṇna sira jāgra ya rumĕṅö,dé nikaŋ Ujar-ujaṙ pasili-siliḥ,śīǥra yaṙ pawuṅu Aṙdđa warurutĕn*14:21:1372*

wruḥ siré naya nikaŋ Inulih-uliḥ,sāri-sāri niṅ ujaṙ Iniṅĕt-iṅĕt,budđipūṙwwaka huwus maṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn,yaṙ sahuṙ kadi gĕrĕḥ swara matĕrĕḥ*14:22:1373*

hé daśānana salaḥ naya winuwus,tā guṇanya Apa tan hana pituhun,wèt i-māna ni hatinta ya matĕguḥ,saŋ widagđa mawaraḥ sira sinalaḥ*14:23:1374*

saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa wicakṣaṇa riṅ aji,yukti tékana wuwus nira pituhun,ndan hatinta Aƀimāna juga wihaŋ,taṙ hiḍĕp rasa nikaŋ naya pawaraḥ*14:24:1375*

ƀāskarogra tuwi dadya sira matīs,hyaŋ śaśāṅka tuwi dadya mapanasa,ndan kitān winuwusan pi sakapisan,tan hanāta gamananta mamatiha*14:25:1376*

jāti niŋ praƀu puwiḥ hana ri kita,đīra tātan aharĕp wara-warahĕn,saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa wĕnaŋ sira mawaraḥ,wruḥ sirékana dumèḥ ya majar-ajar*14:26:1377*

đaṙmma niŋ prakrĕti séwaka tinañan,dé niraŋ praƀu rikaŋ naya winaya,wètnya siḥ nira ri saŋ siniwi kunĕŋ,donya tan hana wanèḥ hita satata*14:27:1378*

mwaŋ widagđa kita riŋ rahayu daṅū,yukti tékana Ujaṙ nira ri kita,ndā mĕné mari guṇajña kita wihaŋ,tan rĕsĕp rasa nikaŋ Ujar i-kita*14:28:1379*

saṅśayāmku ri Ulaḥta lagi salaḥ,krūra kéwala taman hana tinahā,ndān awās ya maꝑalā hala ri kita,tan dadīnalaṅ-alaŋ pati ya tĕkā*14:29:1380*

pāmbĕkanta karĕṅö lagi Inupĕt,sāhasèŋ sakaharĕp taya katakut,sakta riŋ paṅan inum jĕnĕk iṅ inak,grāmya-ƀoga ya manamtam iri tamaḥ*14:30:1381*

saprakāra niṅ ulaḥ kinatakutan,mwaŋ sarūpa nikanaŋ magaway ilik,yéka nitya ginawé tinuhagaṇa,byakta yan pamuharāŋ ꝑala mahala*14:31:1382*

wruḥ ṅhulun lara tĕkā ri kita huwus,ndā ta kantuna rikaŋ kṣaṇa ri kita,dꜽtya dānawa Asiŋ musuh umarā,nyā ṅhulun pĕjaha riŋ raṇa dadaha*14:32:1383*

tā kasaṅśaya huwus manĕmu suka,yajña puṇya tapa kapwa ya gawayĕn,tuṣṭi séṣṭi humaḍaŋ taya kakuraŋ,mātya riŋ raṇa nahan suka kawĕkas*14:33:1384*

haywa taŋ naya hinöm pinakagawé,Āpa tan tahu manīti daṅu-daṅu,śakti sāhasa lanā ya mapakĕna,maṅkanāta kita rin raǥutanaya*14:34:1385*

nā ta liŋ nira ri saŋ daśawadana,kumƀakaṙṇna maturū ta sira muwaḥ,saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa muwaḥ sira mawuwus,duṙnimitta ya tinon ira mahala*14:35:1386*

hé daśāsya niyata-ŋ pati ya tĕkā,kādƀutāṅ aśuƀacihna wahu-wahu,nya-ŋ lĕbū Umibĕk iŋ pura sumaput,tan pakāraṇa Amoǥa juga mĕlĕk*14:36:1387*

bāyubajra kadi bajra ya biṣama,ǥūṙṇnitèŋ nagara ǥora ya gumuruḥ,mwaŋ manuk muni humuŋ kadi manaṅis,lèn kidaŋ masasaran masuk i-Umaḥ*14:37:1388*

mwaŋ ƀaṭāra rawi rodra makalaṅan,kālamrĕtyu juga yan Iniṅĕt-iṅĕt,maṅkanékana sĕnö nira makuniŋ,tan sinaṅśaya Ikaŋ mahala daṅū*14:38:1389*

lèn hanāṙdđa maputiḥ makuliliṅan,ṅkā ri wimba nira ƀīṣaṇa ya mabāŋ,yan katon kadi ta siṅha wahu mĕtu,kéśarā nira sĕnö nika kumĕlab*14:39:1390*

mwaŋ wrĕhaspati katon rahina tuwi,néka handaru rurū juga tumibā,ƀūmi kampita tibānya ya kumĕtĕr,yan kĕtug kadi matag pralaya tĕkā*14:40:1391*

kwèḥ piśāca maṅigĕl kagiri-giri,matri ya prakaṭa sāhasa Umasö,krośa tātan atakut ri kita mĕné,cihna niŋ pati tĕkā ri kita huwus*14:41:1392*

lĕmbu lĕmbita susunya ya makĕḍik,yan pinöḥ mĕtu wiwaṙṇna ya mahaṅi,hyaŋ Apuy tuwi wikāra sira mĕné,tan dilaḥ tinahĕnan tamala-malaḥ*14:42:1393*

lèn kukus nikanaṅ āhuti mahalé,yan wĕlĕk matĕmahan sĕmut apupul,rambut īŋ Ulu wanèh umilu mĕlĕk,byakta yan pati ꝑalā nikana kabèḥ*14:43:1394*

śānti kāṅĕn-aṅĕnĕn paṅupaśamā,haywa tan wawarĕṅö lara humaḍaŋ,kwèḥ Ariṣṭa Atikaṣṭa katatakut,yapwa tan Upaśaman pati biṣama*14:44:1395*

haywa taŋ hati wihaŋ hita pituhun,mèwĕha-ŋ mawarahèŋ hayu ri kita,séwakātiśaya riŋ kaba-kaba ya,kéwalāṅuguṅ-uguŋ praƀu juga ya*14:45:1396*

tan hanoṣađa wanèḥ paṅupaśama,ṅhiŋ manĕmbaha ri saŋ raǥutanaya,mꜽŧilī sira wawan waluyakĕna,yéka śāntika sahasra paḍa nikā*14:46:1397*

tan kitékana kakiṅkiṅa pĕjaha,riŋ raṇāṅgaṇa Apan warĕg iṅ inak,saŋ krĕtāṙŧa paripūṙṇna krĕtayaśa,lāƀa liŋ nira rikaŋ mati malaga*14:47:1398*

saṅhulun kunaṅ anuŋ pinakahulun,tan warĕg suka sĕḍĕŋ maharĕp inak,yukti tékana hiḍĕpnya Anumanan,ƀaktya liŋnya ri siraŋ raǥutanaya*14:48:1399*

saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa huwus nira mawuwus,krođa saŋ daśamuꝁa jwalita murub,ƀīṣaṇékana wulat nira mawĕlū,kampitékana kumis nira kumĕdut*14:49:1400*

maṅkana-ŋ ƀru kuṭi lèn rahi marĕṅu,téja niŋ muꝁa mabāŋ kadi tinĕpak,Ambĕkan nira mahos hati mapanas,krūra tékana sahuṙ nira magalak*14:50:1401*

Ꜽ wiƀīṣaṇa milag pwa yu laku mūr,duṙnimitta sawuwusmu ya mahala,rāǥawāmĕnaṅa rāwaṇa Alaha,hāḥ m-asamƀawa dahat puliha tuwi*14:51:1402*

ron ikaŋ kayu makiŋ ya kumĕlĕma,riŋ tasik watu kumambaṅa maliha,wway manunwana Apuy mamaḍĕmana,yan kadi pwa ya rikā Aku n-alaha*14:52:1403*

hāḥ wiƀīṣṣaṇa bali pwa ya piwaras,ṅhiŋ mĕné wruh i-hatinyu ya kuṭila,drohakātiśaya duṣṭa ya ta kariḥ,ndan mĕné kawĕtu ṅūni ya winuni*14:53:1404*

riŋ daṅū hana musuḥ kinira-kira,tan pisan-pisana tan milu malaga,ndan waliṅku kawikuñ juga ginĕgö,tākariḥ druhakan īca kanaraka*14:54:1405*

mwaŋ dudū hati nikaŋ wiku Ađama,ƀoga-ƀuṅga kaharĕpnya taya wanèḥ,tan sakahyuna nikaŋ tahu riṅ aji,yapwa donmw-apilĕhĕŋ Umari wiku*14:55:1406*

rākṣasa prakrĕti śudđa ya wulana,nyaŋ wbihīṣaṇa ya wuṅkukana nikā,wanđuwaṙgga ya banantĕna maputiḥ,ka pwa tulya talutuḥ kala sumĕlat*14:56:1407*

wwaŋ Apa ṅwaṅ aharĕp huluna juga,kaśmalāṅiraṅ-iraŋ maniwi-niwi,ƀaktya riŋ musuh alaḥ maharĕp inak,đik lĕhèŋ mati manĕmwa kanaraka*14:57:1408*

hāḥ Aḍā pira harĕpmu n-ahuripa,hīna mahyun umarèŋ musuh ađama,byakta kon ahuripāmĕgil iriya,yan hĕnĕŋ wĕnaṅa téka mahuripa*==0=0=

kāla niŋ nagara śīṙṇna ya matunu,tuṣṭa cittamu sĕḍĕŋnya wahu murub,ko dumèh ađama wānara luputa,cihnamu druhaka nīca kala cĕmĕr*14:58:1409*

saŋ daśānana huwus maṅuman-uman,riŋ palaṅka tumurun ta sira madĕg,maṅkas-aṅkas umasö ta manudiṅi,maŋdĕdĕl muꝁa Ah-o karacapala*14:59:1410*

saŋ mahāṙdđika minaṅkana humĕnĕŋ,citta niścala wulat nira mamanis,budđi śudđa malilaŋ taman agĕlĕŋ,mwaŋ manaḥ nira kadi sꝑaṭika maṇik*14:60:1411*

jāti saŋ sujana yaṙ pinariƀawa,niṙwikāra sira đīra tar akumĕl,tulya sāgara Ikaŋ hati malilaŋ,taṙ kĕnèŋ gĕlĕ-gĕlĕḥ śuci satata*14:61:1412*

taṙ masora sira yaṙ pamalĕsana,mapraṅātĕhĕra towi tar alaha,ndān ikaŋ brata magöŋ ya ta ginĕgö,śāntikī kinĕkĕsan pinakamaṇik*14:62:1413*

wruḥ nirèŋ winaya sajjana carita,yéka nitya pamasĕḥ hati magĕlĕḥ,śānta satya sawuwus nira ya sadon,somya suswara sahuṙ nira wĕkasan*14:63:1414*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}

hé nāŧālapana-ŋ gĕlĕŋ pahalilaŋ wèhĕn wiśudđā-ŋ manaḥ,swasŧā saŋ praƀu haywa kéwala tumūt sojaṙ nikaŋ wwaŋ wanèḥ,tan swaŋ yan pamituhwa taṅguh apa tan moli pwa riŋ dé kabèḥ,séṣṭintékana tūtakĕn pahatĕguḥ budđinta tan piṇḍaha*14:64:1415*

lāwan ṅwaŋ kadi saṅhulun hana hulun mamriḥ ya mojaṙ hita,ndan budđinta ya kaṙṇnaśūla rumĕṅö mèwĕḥ kitān māpĕsa,yogyāyogya nikaŋ ṅ-ujaṙ tinahilan dé saŋ praƀu n-paŋ­rĕṅö,Āpan đaṙmmatulā ṅaran nikar alap budđi prasidđāhayu*14:65:1416*

lwiṙ ni-ṅwaŋ kadi saṅhulun salah ikā riŋ doṣa yan tan tinūt,kadyaṅgā nikanaŋ parāṙŧa manuluŋ wyādi n-pawèh oṣađi,tātan wꜽdya sadoṣa yan tan ininum tambanya paŧyāpahit,nāhan lwiṙ mami kam panaṅguhi Ataḥ tātan kĕnĕŋ duṙyyaśa*14:66:1417*

sakrođa pwa hatinta yan Inujaran tag wruḥ ri doniŋ wuwus,wĕt niŋ göŋ Aƀimāna saŋ praƀu Iké sojaṙ nikaŋ wwaŋ wanèḥ,ṅwaŋ tan patya marān manohara kunaŋ yānuŋ sinaṅguḥ kĕna,ndak tontona wasāna saŋ praƀu hĕlĕm mamwīta mūra ṅhulun,
saŋ hyaŋ śāstra mĕné katon tuhu nirāṙ ton ṅwaŋ prayatnā tuhan,wwaŋ wadwā nira mūṙkꝁa rakwa ya Ikān byaktān pamaṅguḥ hala,kadyaṅgā nikanaŋ wwaṅ āmĕṅ-amĕṅan moŋ mwaŋ Ulāgöŋ biṣa,yékān kāwit-awit pamaṅguha ṅ-inak duḥkanya yāgöŋ tĕmĕn*14:67:1418*

lāwan yan syapa tāhaṅan syapa salaḥ śīlanya liŋ saŋ praƀu,yan ṅwaŋ ƀrĕtya mataṅguh iŋ praƀu kunaŋ yānuŋ kĕnā riŋ salaḥ,yan saŋ ƀūpati niṙwiwéka capalèŋ wadwā kunaŋ yāhayu,sakwèḥ saŋ mapatiḥ sirékana Anuŋ prĕṣṇān apan wruḥ kabèḥ*14:68:1419*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
