nā liŋ niraŋ Āṙyya wiƀīṣaṇān sahur,sāmpun sirāmwīt krama śīǥra yaṙ wĕtu,madĕg ta rowaŋ nira ƀakti tan kasaḥ,tumūta sakwèḥ nira wèt nikaŋ Asiḥ*14:69:1420*

#pañcadaśamas saṙggaḥ#
<praharaṇakalika>:15
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :14:
^15/1/1413.
Aŧa lumaku siromaliha saha bala,raǥutanaya sirékana wĕgilĕn ira,gaganatala hawan nira mibĕr aṅalor,prawara giri mahéndra ya hinarĕpakĕn*15:1:1421*

tasik atiśaya ƀīṣaṇa hinaliwatan,tĕka ri tĕpi nikaŋ jalađi sira huwus,makaburĕṅaṅ ikaŋ wray umulat i-sira,paḍa majaga waliŋnya daśamuꝁa tĕka*15:2:1422*

pawanasuta sirékana wawaṅ umulat,maṅiṅĕt-iṅĕtakĕn sira dadi matutur,gumuyu sira manuŋsuṅ agiraṅ umasö,hana rĕṇa nira ṅūni ya kinatuturan*15:3:1423*

prakrĕti nira saṅ āṙyya satata matutur,ri guṇa nikana saŋ sujana maṅasihi,makĕḍika tuwi tan dadi ya kinalupan,ṅuni-ṅuni yan agöŋ hana ri hati sadā*15:4:1424*

wwara mara rĕṇa ṅūni ya hana ri sira,giri sadrĕśa hiḍĕp nira riya sagunuŋ,ya Ikana kaharĕp nira walĕsĕn ikā,brata nikana saṅ āṙyya mamalĕsa guṇa*15:5:1425*

pinalaku ṅ-asihéki sira mawaraha,Umajarakĕna ƀakti rasikana tĕka,pawanasuta kinon ta sira dadi masö,tĕka mawarah i-saŋ raǥusuta wijaya*15:6:1426*

prawaraguṇa wiƀīṣaṇa Ikana tĕka,huluna ri suku saŋ praƀu tan alaṅ-alaŋ,sahuripana mahāṙdđika tuwi guṇawān,nipuṇa riṅ aji śāstra wĕnaṅa śaraṇa*15:7:1427*

nahan ikana wuwus niraṅ anilasuta,Umajar-ajarakĕn guṇagaṇa rasikī,raǥusuta rumĕṅö guṇa nira ya magöŋ,kadi Inalap ikaŋ hati maṅanumata*15:8:1428*

prakrĕti nira guṇajña satata mapagĕḥ,maṅasihi śaraṇāgata saꝑala siwin,musuh amalaku jīwita tuwi hinurip,tuhu-tuhu puruṣottama Atikaruṇa*15:9:1429*

Api tuwi sira saŋ mamalaku śaraṇa,sari-sari nikanaŋ guṇa hana ri sira,saꝑala sira rinakṣa wĕnaṅa śarana,mamawa suka magöŋ Ikana gati nira*15:10:1430*

huwus inajarakĕn ta sira dadi masö,praṇata ri suku saŋ prawara raǥusuta,satama nira tĕḍuḥ jalađi mari humuŋ,marahakĕna panĕmwa nira suka magöŋ*15:11:1431*

Aŧa huwus apagĕḥ tikana gati nira,Inanumata sirān pamalaku śaraṇa,kadi ta tinitisan Amrĕta hati nira,mahawan anĕmu höb ya paḍa nira suka*15:12:1432*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
nda tatīta yaṙ hana siraŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,maṅaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn ta sira saŋ raǥūttama,Atimèpu riŋ hawana niŋ Umĕntasa,Ikanaŋ Upāya kadi tan kapaṅguha*15:13:1433*

Aputĕk manaḥ nira taman pasiṅkaban,manurun ta moha nira jāti niŋ dadi,Ikanaŋ tasik kadi ta wiǥna yak hiḍĕp,pratibanđa maŋhalaṅi tan pawèḥ hawan*15:14:1434*

tuhu śabda saŋ prawara wrĕdđa paṇḍita,Ikanaŋ Unĕŋ lawan asiḥ mawèh ilik,raǥuputra monĕṅ aṅaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn priyā,Agĕlĕŋ sirèŋ tasik apan ya wāđaka*15:15:1435*

tĕka niŋ gĕlèŋ ri hati moǥa yānaput,mapanas diwākara sahasra tulya ya,ginamĕl-gamĕl nira Iké laras nira,wĕkasan madĕg tihaṅakĕn panaḥ nira*15:16:1436*

paripūṙṇna dé nira mayat Ikaŋ laras,dumilaḥ ta tuŋtuṅ ikanaŋ panaḥ murub*15:17:1437*
Ikanaŋ samudra panahĕṅkwa liŋ nira,Alah épu tan tĕmu ṅ-upāya riŋ tasik*15:18:1438*

ri sĕḍĕŋ nirānihaṅakĕn laras nira,kumĕtĕṙ samudra prĕŧiwī prakampita,giripaṙśwa cāla kalawan rasātala,paḍa saṅśayèŋ pralaya kāla yaṙ tĕka*15:19:1439*

linĕpāsakĕn pwa Ikanaŋ panaḥ murub,kumisik tasik kapanasan Iwak kabèḥ,maṅĕliḥ timiṅgila gĕlāna duṙbbala,balisaḥ kabèḥ kaburu dé nikaŋ panas*15:20:1440*

wuhayāhuyāŋ-huyaṅan aṙdđa mātya ya,Umĕhāḥ mahosyan umahas mamèt atīs,wwara lumba-lumba ya malumba yālayū,hana mīna buntĕk amĕtĕk rikaŋ latĕk*15:21:1441*

Ikanaŋ Iwak tuli ya tan tulus tuli,Apa tan tuluy panas ikaŋ panaḥ riya,haha mīna baṅlus anulus prawīra ya,Umasö masāđya malĕsān turun Apuy*15:22:1442*

wwara lèn pĕsut kabarasat mĕsat kabèḥ,sakarĕŋ kariṅkĕl aṅĕnèŋ karaŋ magöŋ,malĕtuk Utĕknya sumirat sakèŋ tutuk,tĕpi niŋ karaŋ kadi rinĕṅga rāḥ mabāŋ*15:23:1443*

makarāduluṙ mararakan kaŧañcana,kawurug ri kāla ni pĕsat nikan pĕsut,kaparĕk parik ya kaparag rĕmĕk rĕmuk,makarādĕmit ya kapicil tĕbĕŋ cacal*15:24:1444*

hana lèn iwak liman agöŋ gunuŋ juga,ya kumumbu-kumbu matasak rikaŋ tasik,milu tékanaŋ Iwak anuŋ sĕḍĕŋ-sĕḍĕŋ,kapisan kabèḥ kapanasan wijaḥ pĕjaḥ*15:25:1445*

r-umahan nahan ya rumuhun ya hantu bāp,sakapatya kapwa kapatīkanaŋ kakap,kaḍiwas lawan kaḍawa sāŋ panas riya,balanak kadi pwa tinanĕk paḍātasak*15:26:1446*

kadi ténariŋ huraṅ akiŋ ya riŋ karaŋ,mahuyaŋ Ikaŋ bahi ḍuyuŋ paḍāhuyuŋ,pĕñu yātĕñuḥ juga sawèt nikaŋ panas,Ikanaŋ gĕtĕm mati ya śūra maṅgĕtĕm*15:27:1447*

wwara śukti tulya marasuk tiwas pwa wèḥ,mati mĕtwakĕn prawara mutyahāra ya,śata saṅꝁya śaṅka mati tan pasaṅku ya,wĕṅi paŋhiḍĕpnya tamatan wĕṅa-ŋ wiṅa*15:28:1448*

pralaya-ŋ layaṙ-layar awor uwuṙ-Uwur,mapuluŋ wiluŋluṅ umilu-ŋ juluŋ-juluŋ,kalawan Iwak kawan awoṙ giliŋ-giliŋ,matitip matip matap-atap ta yātitiḥ*15:29:1449*

Iwu lakṣa koṭi niyutāṙwudāṙwuda,ya Ikā sawaŋ-sawaṅ ikaŋ Iwak pĕjaḥ,mahaṅi-ŋ mahodađi hamöŋ ya loṙ kidul,kadi ganđa niŋ samaraƀūmi ƀīṣaṇa*15:30:1450*

tumuluy panaḥ nira tĕkĕŋ rasātala,maṅĕné ya nāga kapisan pĕgat pisan,makin ujwalādƀuta dilaḥnya cañcala,maṅilū ŋ-Ulā kapanasan gĕlāna ya*15:31:1451*

tuwi nāga bāsuki sukī nikaŋ lĕmaḥ,pinujin suđīra sira đārakèŋ jagat,ri sawèt ni tībra ni panas nikaŋ panaḥ,kumĕtĕṙ tatan tuhu suđīra đāraka*15:32:1452*

{suwadanā}
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :20:
tat kālān glāna kolāhala sahana nikaŋ nāgéndra malayū,kombak taŋ ṙyyak lumimbak jalaniđi kakĕbĕk ƀūḥ ƀāga gumiwaŋ,ǥorāgraḥ Agra niŋ paṙbwata kagiri-giri-ŋ méǥāgra gumuruḥ,riŋ digdéśāwilĕt taŋ kilat upama kilat niŋ kāla ya tĕka*15:33:1453*

maṅkin sāk sāgarāǥūṙṇnita kadi ginugaḥ gamƀīra gumuruḥ,dé niŋ nāgāpalaywan mĕtu matakut anon hrū rodra ya murub,kagyat kāṅgĕk ta saŋ hyaŋ baruṇa maśila riŋ siṅhāsana maṇik,méṅguŋ maṅguŋ paluṅguḥ nira hana ri tĕṅaḥ niŋ sāgarajala*15:34:1454*

sandéhāmbĕk nirāṙ ton haru-hara nikanaŋ nāgādƀuta kabèḥ,yaṙ saṅhārā Ikèŋ rāt ya tika tinaha riŋ twas citta kumĕtĕr,ton taŋ pātāla māwāƀinawa kadi hanā tā dibya manurun,dé niŋ hrū ƀīṣaṇāƀrā jwalita kadi dilaḥ niŋ ƀaskaraśata*15:35:1455*

wètnyān kagyat tumon hrū sumuluhi rikanaŋ pātāla nitala,maṅkin sandéha tāmbĕk nira dadi ta mĕsat śīǥrāṙ wĕtu ri hèŋ,ton taŋ wré koṭi-lakṣa prakaṭa paḍa humuŋ riŋ pāṙśwa ya sĕsök,kapwānonton Iwak niŋ jalađi kapanasan saṅsāra mahuyaŋ*15:36:1456*

sāmpunyānton ikaŋ wré wulati ta sira saŋ śrī rāmawijaya,muṅgwiŋ tĕmbiŋ nikaŋ sāgara sĕḍĕṅ umurub taŋ krođa ri sira,maṅsö cuṇḍuk ta saŋ hyaŋ baruṇa masidĕkuŋ riŋ wwꜽ makidupuḥ,śīǥrānĕmbaḥ ri saŋ rāǥawa sira ta wawaŋ mojaṙ suwadana*15:37:1457*

hè nāŧa wyaṙŧa déntat haru-hara Umanaḥ wwꜽ niŋ jalaniđi,Āpan tan duṙbbalā yan haliwatana Iké tāsātana tuwi,sakwèḥ niŋ rāt gawéntékana kita maṅĕmit lāwan kita baśa,ndyānuŋ prastāwa niŋ mohita kadi malupèŋ janmottama kita*15:38:1458*

salwiṙ niŋ rāt kitātaḥ Ađipati tumitaḥ byūhanya satata,ndya ṅké mèwĕḥ linakwan ndya taṅ alas asukĕt ndya-ŋ paṙbwata magöŋ,ndyāṅ ādityātitīkṣṇāmanasi Aŧa ca lèn ndya-ŋ bāyu biṣama,māyāmāyānta tékā kakawaśa ya tumūt swécꞓānta ya kabèḥ*15:39:1459*

tan wruḥ nārāyanāṅśāṅdadi maṅĕmita rāt sāđyanta manurun,swasŧā saŋ sāđu lāwan hilaṅa niṅ agawé hāro-hara ya don,Uṅgwantāt wiṣṇu téki-ŋ tasik apa ta guṇanyān sātana kunaŋ,ṅèl-ṅèlĕn dé ƀaṭārākira-kira Apa tan tāpā ta pakaya*15:40:1460*

mwaŋ yan sātanya sāđyān apa wĕnaṅa nikaŋ wré mĕntasa riya,saṅkā yan duṙgga dé niŋ latĕk atiśaya riŋ Āśꞓaṙyya madalĕm,lèn göŋ niŋ lĕmbwara ṅké wĕnaṅa ya humĕlö ƀūmī kṣaṇa tuwi,yékākwèḥ kapwa luṅkāntara nikana kabèḥ malwā katatakut*15:41:1461*

lāwan makwèḥ hana ṅkè kagiri-giri mawān śaṅkādƀuta magöŋ,yan sĕṅkāŋ wānara ṅkā Apa wĕnaṅa niké byaktān kapalĕyö,Akwèḥ téwak liman ṅké ya pinakakarakal niŋ luṅka biṣama,yékā tuŋtuŋ nikā ƀīṣaṇa tuwi katunan ṅ-āditya ya pĕtĕŋ*15:42:1462*

yapwan krīḍānta mintonakĕna ƀaya yaŧālīlā juga ya don,Āpañ jātinta Icꞓā wĕnaṅa kita makakrīḍā triƀuwana,yan yogyā pwaṅkulun wānarabala Atagĕntāmuṇḍuta gunuŋ,tuṅgal sowaŋ kabèḥnyā ṅatĕra watu magöŋ tambak ya gawayĕn*15:43:1463*

tan sandéhā tikaŋ wré wĕnaṅa ya gumawé tambak yan atagĕn,Āpan śaktinta lumrériya hana ri Awak niŋ wānarabala,muṇḍoṇḍāŋ ƀūmi dadyékana wĕnaṅa yadin Ājñāna ya kabèḥ,kāhinyékiŋ samudropama kali sakilan byaktān kawĕnaṅa*15:44:1464*

lāwan sāđyanta sidđā niyata kita jayé śatrunta hilaṅa,hrūtāṅkèn kālamrĕtyū maṅana sahana niŋ mūṙkꝁāđama kabèḥ,sakwèḥ niŋ wré ya kāṅkĕn kalula-kalula niŋ kālāntaka tĕka,byaktan śiṙṇnā sa-lĕṅkā jaya-jaya ƀagawān nārāyaṇa sira*15:45:1465*

{wātoṙmmimālā}

nā liŋ saŋ hyaŋ baruṇāminta jīwa,tuṣṭāmbĕk saŋ raǥuputrān sinĕmbaḥ,saṅhāra-ŋ hrū paḍĕm īŋ Astra bahni,lāwan krođé hati sāmpun sinapwan*15:46:1466*

ménak tāmbĕk nikanaŋ nāga ƀūmī,swaṣṭa-ŋ satwottama muṅgwiŋ samudra*15:47:1467*
sakwèḥnyānuŋ mati dé niŋ śarāgni,tātan malwaŋ Umuwaḥ labđajīwa*15:48:1468*

{drutawilambita ḍan tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}

Aŧa huwus mahurip Ikanaŋ Iwak,wija-wijaḥ ya kabèḥ maṅaluŋ maluy,dadi ta kinon bala wānara maṅkata,maṅatĕra paṙbwata lèn watu tambaka*15:49:1469*

{wĕgawatī}

krama śīǥra mĕsat Ikanaŋ wray,kapwa sadaṙppa mibĕṙ ta ya luṅhā,kumĕlab ta wulunya ya mawyaŋ,tulya dilaḥ nikanaŋ pralayāgni*15:50:1470*

sapĕsatnya kabèḥ taya kantun,pūṙṇna pĕpĕk daśadéśa tĕkapnya,masinaŋ ta sĕnö nikanaŋ wwꜽ,dé ni wulunya satéja ya maƀrā*15:51:1471*

maṅaloṙ sawanèḥ ya maṅulwan,lèn hana wānarawīra maṅétan,diṇunuŋnya Anuŋ gunuṅ āwān,kwèḥ ta watunya śilātala malwā*15:52:1472*

satĕkanya rikaŋ giripāṙśwa,krūra humuŋ prakaṭādƀuta makrak,kadi siṅha sahasra maśabda,tulya gĕrĕḥ gumuruḥ Atiǥora*15:53:1473*

{Aśwalalita}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :23:
ri tĕka nikaŋ kapi prawara wīra kampita ṅ-alas kĕnasnya malayū,Apituwi siṅha niṙƀaya daṅū mĕgil ya ri guhānya gahwara humèt,ṅuni-ṅuni tékanaŋ kĕnas anéka tan Anumané ry-anaknya manusu,mamana-manālayū ya manusup ri śrĕṅga nikanaŋ gunuŋ maṇimaya*15:54:1474*

liman alayū limaŋ puluha yādyus iŋ talaga tan lagèŋ kapibala,Ataha-tahan gaḍiŋnya ya saḍĕŋ malaṇḍĕp inasaḥnya riŋ watu riḍaŋ,punar api tan para pwa ri paran nikaŋ paramatucꞓa satwa maḍĕmit,milu malayū tan éraṅ i-lĕmunya tan paṅapa göŋnya kātara-tara*15:55:1475*

hana ta kapaṙgatan Agati tātan iṅgut agawè ta yoga humĕnĕŋ,ri sĕla-sĕlā nikaŋ watu hanèŋ tatāka kuri tuṣṭa tan prakaṭa ya,Ikana hiḍĕpnya tan katĕṅĕrākwapāk iwĕṅ-iwĕŋ lawan watu magöŋ,sulur aputiḥ paḍā nika gaḍiṅku liŋnya humĕnĕŋ rikaŋ wway ahĕniŋ*15:56:1476*

wwara ta ya wök sukĕt ya malayū sakèŋ patunahanya hīna dahatĕn,makakarasak sasaṙ masusupan ya mosah aṅĕsaḥ ya kāsyasih-asiḥ,Alah atakut ya wèn kaparagèŋ galak nikana taŋ liman ya malayū,wijah aṅĕbak parĕŋ tumĕḍun īŋ lĕbak Ibĕkĕn āmbĕkan tuwi kabĕk*15:57:1477*

ri sĕḍĕṅ ikaŋ kĕnas haru-harālayū masasaran ya tan paśaraṇa,lumĕkas ikaŋ kapiprawara kapwa mambuli Ikaŋ gunuŋ sana-sini,Atiśaya tīkṣṇa tékana kukūnya yéka panĕwĕknya paṙbwata magöŋ,kadi ta ya siṅha sāhasa sahasra saṅꝁya Umatī gajéndra magalak*15:58:1478*

hana ta ya wānarādƀuta makas Ikā karatalanya bajra sadrĕśa,ya ta panĕwĕknya paṙbwata pupak kadi pwa ya cinakra sakṣaṇa pĕgat,Inibĕrakĕnya śīǥra kadi rūpa niŋ Alap-alap katonya sahalab,Upama kapuk hiḍĕpnya rikanaŋ gunuŋ nĕnahakĕn ya riŋ karatala*15:59:1479*

wwara ta wĕkas nikaŋ paramaśaktimānta kapiwīra kādƀuta dahat,tĕpi ni guhā nikaŋ gunuṅ agöŋ ya téka kinawilnya wuṅkal atĕguḥ,dadi dinawutnyan ātiśaya śakti sāra kawĕnaŋ ya dénya sakarĕŋ,milu kadawut pasīnya sumusuk ri soṙ tĕka rikaŋ rasātala-tala*15:60:1480*

Ikana wurinya ƀīṣaṇaluwaŋ gaƀīra kĕlĕwuŋ pĕṅuŋ yan inuṅaŋ,wwara ta ri sor apūṙwwa sumĕnö pwa cūla saṅ anantaƀoga ya katon,kadi ta guhā pasaṅgrahan ikaŋ kapiprawara niścayā jaya tĕkā,hawana nikaŋ watĕk Ađama rākṣasomuliha riŋ Awéci naraka*15:61:1481*

hana ta ya maŋdĕdĕl watu magöŋ sayojana babaknya rodra kumupak,kadi ta gĕlap rikaŋ kasaṅa śabda niŋ watu bĕlaḥ Apuynya sumirat,sahana nikaŋ kĕnas kapĕlĕṅĕn pĕpĕt ya taliṅanya wuntu hibĕkan,kadi ta binajra mūṙccita tibā kabèḥnya kaguliŋ gĕlāna kapati*15:62:1482*

hana ta-tatal-tatālan ikanaŋ śilātala lĕbānya sèwu dĕpa ya,habalaṅakĕn ta yèḥ gagana miṇḍuhuṙ tĕka ri wimba niŋ dinakara,haru-hara saŋ hyaṅ āparan ikāhiréŋ kadi ta rāhu liŋ nira mulat,paḍa ta kapaṙgatan maparikaṙmma saṅśaya sirān tĕkā-ŋ graha wanèḥ*15:63:1483*

kapibala kapwa yāṅibĕrakĕn Anuŋ gunuṅ agöŋ ya ténusuṅ-usuŋ,sakatiga lèn sakarwa sakapat wanèḥ maṅalimé maṅānĕmi kunaŋ,kadi garuḍāṅlayaŋ mibĕrakĕn ƀaṭāra puruṣottamopama nikā,tĕka ta ya riŋ ṇaƀastala gĕlāna taŋ grahagaṇān kasuṇḍuk alayū*15:64:1484*

hana masalaṅgapan gunuṅ anak mahā sahaja yāgawé kaba-kaba,Ikanaṅ i-soṙ mamuṇḍut anĕhĕṙ maṅuṇḍa kadi riṇḍi daṙppa tan aṅèl,Ikanaṅ umuṅgu riŋ gagana yatna ṭan kaluputan widagđa gapitan,sasasawi paŋhiḍĕpnya rikanaŋ gunuŋ ya mahaṅan yan uṅgu ri taṅan*15:65:1485*

{śiꝁariṇī}
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
hanéki wré tuṅgal kagiri-giri göŋnyogra magalak,Ahaṅkārāmbĕknyān guragaḍa tan aṅgān tuluṅana,tinĕmpuḥnyā-ŋ pāṙśwādƀuta kapurupuḥ puḥ kayu pukaḥ,bĕlaḥ bĕntaṙ śīṙṇna-ŋ watu kumalasā syūḥ kabarubuḥ*15:66:1486*

wawaŋ sinwabnyékaŋ gunuṅ atiśayĕŋ göŋnyan aruhur,kadi lwiṙ niŋ kāmī sĕḍĕṅ agul-agul tan wruh iṅ arĕs,gunuŋ yāṅkĕn kanyā kadi ta manaṅis yan rinaƀasa,kalimbak sakwèḥ niŋ talaga kaharan luḥnya humilī*15:67:1487*

saśoka-ŋ haṅsā śā laki-bini muwaḥ sārasa masū,humuŋ lāwan kumbaŋ ƀramita ya mibĕṙ yèṅ awaṅ-awaŋ,manuk mānak monĕŋ muni ya manaṅis kapwa ya humuŋ,ya tāṅkĕn śabdā niŋ gunuṅ alara wètnyān rinaƀasa*15:68:1488*

Aṅin mādrĕs humyus tumama ya rikaŋ gahwara guhā,ya tékośwāsanyān pinĕkul ikanaŋ wānarabala,katūb pwékaŋ méǥa pracalita ri pāṙśwanya mapasaḥ,ya tāṅkĕn kèn-kènyān rusak abayaṅan tulya kawudan*15:69:1489*

maṇik maƀrā lumrāŋ marakata ri himbaŋnya sumawur,ya tāṅkèn kĕṇḍitnyojwala kasarakat tulya ya pĕgat,lumampaḥ pwékaŋ poḥ Asana wariṅin dé nikaṅ aṅin,kadi pwāsāk moré Ikana ta gĕluŋ niŋ śikariṇī*15:70:1490*

{mandākrānta}
