sāmpun moliḥ kapibala muliḥ śīǥra luṅhā kabèḥnya,kapwāwwat-wwat gunuṅ i-sira saŋ rāmadéwān panĕmbaḥ,timbun tékaŋ giri wara kabèḥ mwaŋ śilā mèru tulya,māraryan māri-r irir irikaŋ pāṙśwa māṙ~nĕb kayunya*15:71:1491*

#soḍaśas saṙggaḥ#
<prĕŧwītala>:16
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
^16/1/1482.
huwus tĕka Ikaŋ kapi prawara kapwa moliḥ gunuŋ,madĕg ta sira saŋ nala pratita wiśwakaṙmmātmaja,tumambakakĕnékanaŋ gunuṅ i-mađya niŋ sāgara,Apan sira widagđa Uṇḍahagi niŋ watĕk wānara*16:1:1492*

tibākĕn ikanaŋ gunuŋ Anuṅ agöŋ ya tāmuṅgwi sor,tumūt gunuṅ anak Anékana Ikaŋ Umuṅgwiŋ ruhur,śilātala subadđa kapwa tinatān tinumpaŋ tinap,ya téka tinibān lĕmaḥ ya maratā tumūtaŋ hĕnī*16:2:1493*

huwus winakĕtārĕṣik ya paripuṙṇna malwāratā,sipatnya mabĕnĕṙ lawan watu tĕpinya kapwāpagèḥ,satéja kadi téndranīla lumarap hĕnīnyāhirĕŋ,kadi pwa paṅahā sumāṙgga nikanaŋ jaya śrī n-tĕkā*16:3:1494*

Ukuṙnya kinawistarā nikana saṅgĕpan yojana,dawā ni paṅidulnya pūṙṇna śata yojanātaḥ tĕpĕt,tatan hana kasaṅśayériya subadđa tātañcala,Ah-o saꝑala śakti saŋ nala wĕnaŋ tumambak tasik*16:4:1495*

ri sāmpun ikanaŋ yaśātiśaya sétubanđādƀuta,siraŋ daśamuꝁāṅrĕṅö saƀaya kampitékaŋ hati,maṅĕn-n-aṅĕn ikaŋ samudra Atiƀīṣaṇālwādalĕm,taŧāpi kawĕnaŋ tinambak inupāyan iŋ wānara*16:5:1496*

sahaṙṣa ta naréndra rāma saha lakṣmaṇāṅastuti,samaṅkana ta saŋ kapi prawara sugriwājaṙ sira,lawan sahana niŋ wrayādƀuta manaḥnya kapwāmuji,tumon paṅupakāra saŋ nala Apūṙwwa riŋ rāt kabéḥ*16:6:1497*

madĕg ta sira saŋ raǥūttama wawaŋ Umĕntas sira,lawan sahana niŋ kapi prawara wīra maṅkat kabèḥ,sĕsĕk kakurutug humuŋ kadi ta śabda niŋ Ampuhan,sadaṙppa ya masiṅhanāda sahananya mahyā humuŋ*16:7:1498*

Anantara ḍatĕŋ siré tĕpi nikaŋ mahāsāgara,sumĕṅka ta sirèŋ suwélagiri lor i-lĕṅkāpura,gunuŋ parama-rāmya komala Alasnya konĕŋ Unĕŋ,kadi pwa ya taman hyaṅ indra n-umarérikaŋ mānuṣa*16:8:1499*

maṇik marakatādi yékana śilātalanyojwala,pirak pinakapāṙśwa ƀāśwara sutéja puñcaknya mās,hĕninya maṇi mutyahāra sumĕnö manojñān katon,kadi pwa ya gunuŋ sumèru paḍa niŋ maṇik tan malaḥ*16:9:1500*

Anuŋ hana lanā Umuṅgu riya déwa ganđaṙwwa lèn,sacāraṇa hanāpsarī wwara ta kinnarī-kinnara,mabaṅsi maṅiduŋ makinnara salāwuwīṇā wanèḥ,Ah-o hayu nikaŋ gunuŋ kadi tumīmbaṅi-ŋ swaṙgga ya*16:10:1501*

guhānya Atiśoƀa tulya pasaƀān ƀaṭāréndra ya,satéja hana sūṙyyakānta ya dumèḥnya māwā yawās,maṇik sꝑaṭika candrakānta ya śilātalanyāratā,matīs ya malĕṅis ya toṅgwan ikanaŋ watĕk déwatā*16:11:1502*

Asaṅǥani ya maṅgupit hana sĕḍĕŋ sadaṙppāsiwo,macumbana wanèḥ macaṅkrama wijaḥ ya māmöṅ-amĕŋ,yaŧāsuka manaḥnya muṅgu rikanaŋ suwélācala,kadi pwa Amarāwatī maṅawatāra sākṣāt katon*16:12:1503*

samudra himawān paḍanya paripūṙṇna kalyan maṣik,triđātu ya watunya tulya Alakāwatī taṙ pahī,Asiŋ sakaharĕp hanériya kadi pwa cintāmaṇī,tatan Alaha yan kaḍatwana ƀaṭāra kāmānurun*16:13:1504*

raǥūttama makin sahaṙṣa sira yan panĕk riŋ gunuŋ*16:14:1505*
Anon kayu manoharākiris atis tahĕnyārĕṇĕb,ꝑalanya matasak marūm Arupukan wanöḥ kwèḥ maḍām,sĕkaṙnya sumĕkaṙ prakīṙṇna ya rurū rikaŋ ƀūtala*16:15:1506*

{basantatilaka}
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :14:
mandāra rāmya sumĕkaṙ kadi sāmpun ahyas,mandā ṅ-aṅin ya ta tumūb ya tĕbĕŋ tan olaḥ,mandā Ulaḥ juga kadi pwa masö manuŋsuŋ,mandoni niŋ ƀramara matta Akĕn Ujaṙnya*16:16:1507*

mwaŋ déwadāru ya marūm śuci somya sumrāk,saṅké tuhanya hana rug mati kapwa yātwas,kāwit-kawit ya manibèŋ maṇi sūṙyyakānta,nityān kukus kadi pasaṅgrahan iŋ suwéla*16:17:1508*

lāwan n-ikaŋ kayu kapuṙ ya Apūṙwwa riŋ rūm,saṅké kulitnya tumitis maputiḥ gĕtiḥnya,riŋ sūṙyyakānta katibān i-gĕtiḥnya lumrā,mambö kukusnya kadi đūpa panuŋsuṅannya*16:18:1509*

kaṙ-kolakā mađuka kapwa parĕŋ ya mawwaḥ,lāwan lawaṅga manĕḍĕŋ ya wijaḥ makĕmbaŋ,yékā ta nitya kahawan ri hawan nirākwèḥ,tulyāhṅawit mawitakĕn mukawāsa mawwat*16:19:1510*

malwālilaŋ talaga riŋ giripāṙśwa mahniŋ,rāmyān katon kadi makon umarāṅinum wway,tuñjuŋ kucup wahu kumumbu magöŋ mamuñjuŋ,yékāñjalinya humarĕp kadi gorawāṅliŋ*16:20:1511*

lāwan giliŋ-giliṅ agöŋ makiris kulitnya,tulyānuman marakatottama paŋhiḍĕpnya,mwaŋ haṅsa suswara Uninya malon manojña,ṅké ṅgwāna saŋ praƀu kadi pwa ya maṅkanātaḥ*16:21:1512*

kwèḥ tal magöŋ ri tĕpi niŋ talagātatātöb,wwaḥnyān rurū kadi ta maŋhabalaŋ mamaṇḍĕm,sakrođa riŋ liman alas tamalaḥ marādyus,tuñjuŋ duwĕg_ wahu mĕkaṙ mananāñ ta dénya*16:22:1513*

luṅhā sirāṙ laku sumĕṅka rikaŋ suwéla,mankin kapaṅgih ikanaŋ kayu rāmya makwèḥ,Aṅhiŋ mĕné mara kitān pinaran naréndra,nā liŋnya kapwa masĕkaṙ ta kabèḥ mamĕṅ_pöŋ*16:23:1514*

punnāga nĕp kurawakāṙjjuna kaṙṇnikāra,poḥ cāmpakāsana palāśa Aśoka tañjuŋ,lāwan wuṅū wuṅa kuniŋ wuṅa raṅga paṅgil,sĕntiŋ basantatilakā manĕḍĕŋ kabèḥnya*16:24:1515*

{rucira}
⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
daḍap matöb dalima paḍānĕḍĕŋ kabèḥ,kawèni taŋ mulati ya saṅśayĕŋ Apuy,Apuy niraŋ madana kunĕŋ Ikomurub,maran_ gĕsĕŋ hati nira saŋ wiyoga wèḥ*16:25:1516*

gawé niraŋ madana mawèḥ larèŋ jagat,jagāṅayat laras anihāṅakĕn panaḥ,panāđya riŋ priyawirahātikātara,tatan wuruŋ rucira kataṅga yan kucup*16:26:1517*

kucuṙ nikaŋ wway umĕlĕkaḥ sakèŋ watu,wĕtunya śītala tuwi yālilaŋ maho,Amoǥa téka milu mawèḥ panas Ikā,ri kāla niŋ priyawirahā tatan matīs*16:27:1518*

Atīta saŋ wiraha kariḥ niroṣađa,sađaṙmma lāwan ikana saŋ kĕnèṅ unĕŋ,Upāya tan hana kawĕnaŋ maḍömana,manaḥ kĕnèŋ madanaśarāgni tīkṣṇa ya*16:28:1519*

nayādi tan papakĕna téki niṙguṇa,guṇāṅliput ya kasakitan ta dénya wèḥ,nya wèḥ manaḥ raǥusuta śokamānasa,sasaṙ hiḍĕp nira humĕnĕŋ sirāsuwè*16:29:1520*

suwéla paṙbwata ramaṇīya Uttama,tamāla komala tamalaḥ riké tĕmĕn,taman niraŋ madana hiḍĕpku yānurun,n-ururwakĕn priyawirahāmaṅun Unĕŋ*16:30:1521*

{ƀramarawilaśita}
– – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
lāwan lwaḥ-lwaḥ riya taman adalĕm,kĕmbaŋ bajrojwala Amuja dilĕm,muṅgwiŋ tĕmbiŋnya taruṇa samalĕm,sumrāk rūmnyān kadi puḍak inalĕm*16:31:1522*

jahnī yāhniŋ talaga kadi laṅit,mambaŋ taŋ pās wulan upama nikā,wintaŋ tulya-ŋ kusuma ya sumawur,lumrā pwékaŋ sari kadi jalada*16:32:1523*

molöm ambö suraƀi ya masĕkar,molaḥ dé niŋ haṅin umirir alon,monĕŋ kumbaŋ Umara riya mariŋ,monĕŋ saŋ rāǥawa mulat iriya*16:33:1524*

rāmyān rambat gaḍuṅ anĕḍĕṅ arūm,ṅkāné wit niŋ paḍali paḍa milĕt,kadyaṅgā niŋ Anakĕbi paḍa siḥ,tan saḥ māṅol suku patakuraṅan*16:34:1525*

saśrī yānluŋ hana ta ya maṅunĕŋ,kapwomuṅgwīŋ paḍali paḍa milĕt,kwèḥ kĕmbaŋnyānarawata sumawur,tulyāṅrumbé malara kinawayuḥ*16:35:1526*

māsiḥ taŋ waŋ Umulat i-sulasiḥ,lwiṙnyān polaḥ kadi maṅasih-asiḥ,sumyaŋ kumbaŋ maluyakĕna ṅ-asiḥ,mĕṅgĕp miṅgat kadi manaḍah asiḥ*16:36:1527*

mĕṇḍuṙ mĕṇḍuḥ paḍa-paḍa manĕḍĕŋ,ṅkā tan mandĕl ƀramara kajĕnĕkan,maṅkin monèŋ raǥusuta kaƀaran,māṅè śoka-ŋ ƀramarawilasita*16:37:1528*

{waṅśapatrapatita}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
komala taŋ luruk-luruk atöb masĕkar asisihan,bāŋ sawanèḥ-wanè-ḥ ya maputiḥ kadi ta winasĕhan,paṇḍakaki prakiṙṇna ya mawoṙ wuṅa wari kasihan,kwèḥ ƀramaromarériya lulut kadi kĕna kasihan*16:38:1529*

mwaŋ kayu téja ronya kadi tambaga ya winasĕhan,pāŋnya ya toṅgwan iŋ manuk anéka hana masĕsĕhan,kapwa wijaḥ sadaṙppa masiwo marumah awurahan,syuŋ muni lèn bayan paḍa widagđa kadi winarahan*16:39:1530*

pāṙśwa nikaŋ suwéla ya kabèḥ paḍa makayu-kayu,wwaḥ mamayaŋ payaṅgu masĕkaṙ mrĕdu paḍa rahayu,ṅkā ri tĕgal-tĕgalnya maratottama matata hayu,śudđa sĕkaṙnya yéka maputiḥ kadi ta ya gumuyu*16:40:1531*

mwaŋ hana ho gaḍiŋ ya tumĕluŋ cala ya magiwaṅan,tulya manĕmbahé sira hawisnya ya Upama taṅan,ronya makiŋ tibā maputĕran ta ya Apan ahaṅan,citta niraŋ wiyoga ya paḍanya maha sabayaṅan*16:41:1532*

{dwitala}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
Aŧa ri tĕka niraŋ naréndrātmaja,ri śiꝁara nikanaŋ suwélācala,kalawan ikana taŋ watĕk wānara,kadi-kadi ta sahasra siṅhāgalak*16:42:1533*

prakaṭa paḍa humuŋ masiṅhānada,kadi ta gĕrĕh i-śrĕṅga niŋ paṙbwata,manuk umibĕr apūṙwwa kagyat kabèḥ,makakarasak ikaŋ kĕnas yālayu*16:43:1534*

kapi capala ya jāti moṅsil kabèḥ,tuwi wĕlĕkaṅ aṅèl ya kapwālapā,dadi ya rumaƀasékanaŋ wwa-wwahan,wija-wijah arĕbut lumumpat parĕŋ*16:44:1535*

wwara wuni mamanis ya poh ambawaŋ,wwara wara-waraṅan kapuṇḍuŋ limus,kamalaka wadarālwa wulwan limo,kamalagi calakèt kukap gintuṅan*16:45:1536*

wyu bakula maja luṅga sĕntul duhĕt,panasa kamĕsa baṙkkakan sūkara,rahu kacapi kawista laṅsĕb salak,kalayu kalih asĕm rukĕm taṅgulun*16:46:1537*

nahan ikana samūha niŋ wwa-wwahan,ya pinarĕbutan iŋ watĕk wānara,ꝑala makabarĕbĕl ya kontal wanèḥ,hana rĕmĕk arĕmuk wiśīṙṇnān sirat*16:47:1538*

kayu-kayu ya matöb ꝑalanyātasak,kapibala Umaṅan yayātaḥ warèg,kadi sujana maṅaṙjjanĕŋ mās maṇik,parahita ya ta donya tan bukti ya*16:48:1539*

#saptadaśamas saṙggaḥ#
<basantatilaka>:17
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :14:
^17/1/1528.
tat kāla saŋ praƀu daśānana rāga citta,ṅkāné taman nata manaḥ nira tan patamban,sītā siréka hana riŋ hati nityakāla,Āśā gĕlāna rasa mātya sawèt nikaŋ hyun*17:1:1540*

tātaṙ paṅan marika riŋ wĕṅi tan katurwan,mosaḥ prapañca balisaḥ sira taṙ hanénak,Aṅhiŋ siraŋ nrĕpasutām juga lot cinitta,hāḥ kaṣṭa rāga manakit wiṣayāniwāṙyya*17:2:1541*

mahyas maƀūṣaṇa makumkuma rājalīlā,wastrā nirottama suganđa ginanđa riŋ mās,sĕsrañcuṇinya sumĕnö lumarap maṇiknya,rapwan kinahyunan anéka Ulaḥ nirāhyas*17:3:1542*

māyā gaway nira cĕṅĕl naranāŧa rāma,lāwan cĕṅĕl prawara lakṣmaṇa śudđa sākṣāt,wadwā prawīra ya tikā mawa rodrarūpa,cèṭī nihan mamawa ƀūṣaṇa mās apèni*17:4:1543*

nāhan Ulaḥ nira Apūṙwwa mamañcanātaḥ,saṅkā ya tan kalawanan dadi mèpwiṅ āmbĕk,Aṅgā niraŋ janakarājasutān sināđya,saṅkā ri tībra niran ahyun anékaƀāwa*17:5:1544*

prāptèŋ taman tumama śīǥra taman wikalpa,maṅgā hiḍĕp nira risaŋ wararājaputrī,dényān huwus mati siraŋ nrĕpaputra rāma,mojaṙ sirāmujuki haṙṣa sarāga maswī*17:6:1545*

{punaṙmmada}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
Ari jānakī lihatanā Ikèŋ hulu,takariñ cĕṅĕl nika si rāma tékihĕn,kalawan si lakṣmaṇa nahan huwus mati,Aparan ta liŋta kawĕkas ndya paŋhaḍā*17:7:1546*

pinujinta śakti ni si rāǥawāsama,tuhu yāsamèŋ wĕdi kaniṣṭa tat walĕs,tuwi lumbu lambayuṅ akas ta yénarit,nya kunaŋ bubuṙ paḍa ni rāma lakṣmaṇa*17:8:1547*

ya mataŋnya liṅkwari manaḥta yātĕḍuḥ,taṅ atīta kéwala wuwusku yat patiḥ,Apa tan hanékana lĕwiḥ saké ry-aku,I pĕjaḥ ni rāma Aparan kasaṅśaya*17:9:1548*

Aku cakrawaṙtti jaya riŋ jagat kabèḥ,tuwi rūpawān Aku Udāra saśriya,Aku māsihāri kawaśāku dènta wèḥ,kita rowaṅaṅkwari mamuktya sĕmbahĕn*17:10:1549*

nya ta saŋ hyaṅ indra tuwi ƀakti téry-aku,ratu dibya śakti paricāra ni ṅhulun,tuwi tan sukāmbĕk irikaŋ sukottama,ri sĕḍĕŋnya tan kita siwin lawan Aku*17:11:1550*

yadiyat pituhwa sawuwusku hé priyā,sira saŋ śacī tuwi matimpuhé kita,lawan apsarī Atiśayèŋ halĕp kabèḥ,Umawā guṇanya gawayanya té kita*17:12:1551*

yadiyan naréndra janakāri saṅśayan,yat akona liŋta Umarā ri mꜽŧila,hana wastra dibya kalawan hĕmās maṇik,sira yogya liŋta ya wawan saménaka*17:13:1552*

nya ta ya-ŋ gaṅan sahana pawwaté sira,haliman kĕbo turaga gaṙddaƀéṇḍitĕn,hana moŋ warak wwara ta siṅha pañjaran,hana riŋ waraṅka Ikanaŋ waraṅkakan*17:14:1553*

hana lèn timiṅgila lawan Iwak tuli,kalawan bĕbĕd hyu hana lumba-lumba lèn,tamalaḥ ḍaḍaŋ pĕsut iwak liman wanèḥ,tuwi lĕmbwarékana nahan ya rumpwana*17:15:1554*

yadiyan kuraŋ Ikana liŋta pawwata,Atagĕn siraŋ baruṇa haywa saṅśaya,Umawā ta sési nikanaŋ tasik kabèḥ,Iriṅĕn ya dé nira marā ri mꜽŧila*17:16:1555*

kimutéka sési nikanaŋ Alas magöŋ,Ikanaŋ manuk sahana niŋ kĕnas kabèḥ,hana déwatā ya Atagĕn mawérikā,dulurĕn ya dé nika kinonta pawwata*17:17:1556*

kalawan manuk garuḍa Uttamĕŋ Agöŋ,kuruṅan ya Uṅgwana nikā taman kalèn,hana nāga yékana Umuṅgwa riŋ panay,hana pārijāta ya Umuṅgwa riŋ wakul*17:18:1557*

wwara ratna paṅkaja sahasrapatra ya,ya ta milwa pawwata Apan mahādƀuta,saꝑalān wawan ꝑala sakèŋ kadéwatan,ndya kasaṅśayanta ri kité si rāwaṇa*17:19:1558*

janakātmajāri ya mataŋnya yāsiha,tuluṅĕn ṅhulun malara dènta kāsyasiḥ,kadi tan si rāwaṇa hiḍĕpku riŋ hawak,yadi tat pituhwa Aku hāḥ lĕhĕŋ pĕjaḥ*17:20:1559*

{mālaƀāriṇi}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
Iti nā ta wuwus nirān panomaḥ,sira saŋ rāwaṇa rāga haṙṣa tībra,tuwi sési nikaŋ purī ri lĕṅkā,ya ta winwat ya pawèḥ ri déwi sītā*17:21:1560*

sira saŋ janakātmajāṙ sinomaḥ,humĕnĕŋ tībra gĕlāna mūṙccitāśa,ri pĕjaḥ naranāŧa rāmaƀadra,ya paran niŋ hati milwa mātya tan lèn*17:22:1561*

manaṅis maṅĕsaḥ mahos ya mosaḥ,Ikanaŋ luḥ humilī nirantarādrĕs,katibā wiparīta tār uđāni,kumĕtĕṙ sanđi nikaŋ hawak kabèḥ graḥ*17:23:1562*

mabaṅun matutuṙ masū masambat,Umulat riŋ hulu saŋ naréndraputra,kahiḍĕp pwa huwus hilaŋ sirèŋ rāt,pariśudđa-ŋ hati tan hana-ŋ katrĕṣṇan*17:24:1563*

maṅatīta manāmpur iŋ manaḥ dé,matulaŋ riŋ pati niṙƀayékaṅ āmbĕk,Inujaṙ nira śakti saŋ naréndra,ri sawèt nī lara taṙ lĕgö sudīra*17:25:1564*

A-ha nāŧa ƀaṭāra rāmaƀadra,ndya mataŋnyat mati hāḥ laraṅku dènta,takarin puruṣottamāṅśa déwa,Umahā maŋdadi rākṣakā nikèŋ rāt*17:26:1565*

paraméśwara śakti nāŧa riŋ rāt,tuwi tan sora Ataḥ rikaŋ kaśūran,kala rākṣasa janma Alpaśakti,ndya mataŋnyat mati dénya yālaraṅku*17:27:1566*

{prabođitā}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :10:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
nya ta saŋ ratu ṅūni riŋ saƀā,Asamūhāta rikaŋ swayambara,syapa śakti lĕwiḥ saké kita,kita tuṅgal Umĕṭaŋ Ikaŋ laras*17:28:1567*

nya ta saŋ rĕṣi rāma ƀāṙggawa,Umawit saŋ praƀu ṅūni riŋ hawan,rasikā ta wiśéṣa riŋ raṇa,kita tan lèn ta sumorakĕn sira*17:29:1568*

{mālaƀāriṇi}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
nya wuwus nira saŋ mahāṙṣi ṅūni,kita tan lèn ta baśā rikaŋ triloka,ri wĕnaŋta matī musuḥ rikĕŋ rāt,śaraṇām niŋ magawé ta yajña pūjā*17:30:1569*

riṅ anāgata rakwa riŋ dĕlāha,kita maŋdadya manuṣya Ékacatra,śaraṇā nikanaŋ jagat samasta,Ikanaŋ dꜽtya kalĕṅka patyananta*17:31:1570*

ya tikāna wuwus niraŋ mahāṙṣi,kadi kāwéśa banaspati n-sirātaḥ,mrĕṣawāda ṅ-ujaṙ Asamƀawèŋ rāt,ri patinta praƀu hétu niŋ Awajña*17:32:1571*

nya rĕṅönta naréndra saŋ jaṭāyu,sira māsiḥ tumuluŋ ṅhulun ri ṅūni,Umasö sira sāhasa prawīra,mamatuk bāhu tamaṙ pĕjaḥ jugèŋ praŋ*17:33:1572*

naranāŧa mataŋnya tat tahātaḥ,kita matyāpa tatan pinaṇḍitèŋ praŋ,lalu nisꝑala tan padon larasta,paṅalaḥ riŋ tripuréka niṙguṇa pwa*17:34:1573*

nya ta hétu nikāk wĕnaŋ sahiṣṇu,tumahĕn taŋ lara tak patīyawakku,ri huripta nahan hinèṙku tātaḥ,ri patinta praƀu tan padon huripku*17:35:1574*

saparanta Ataḥ ya tūtanaṅkwa,tak adohāku saké sukunta nīŧa,yadiyan kawawèṅ awécidéśa,tamatan kāntuna ƀaktya nityakāla*17:36:1575*

{swāgata}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
nā taṅis nira ta saŋ nrĕpaputrī,tuṅkulīkana cĕṅĕl naranāŧa,dibya saŋ praƀu Asiḥ nira riŋ rāt,nā winaṙṇnana nirālara Āśā*17:37:1576*

đaṙmma tan hana guṇanya rinakṣa,taṙ wĕnaŋ ya tumuluŋ lara ni-ṅwaŋ,saŋ naréśwara mahāṙdđika sāđu,đaṙmma nitya ginawé nira tan lèn*17:38:1577*

dāna puṇya Aparanta guṇanya,tan wĕnaŋ śaraṇa rākṣaka māsiḥ,saŋ narāđipa sadājapa yogī,dāna puṇya ginawé nira nitya*17:39:1578*

śīla tan hana guṇanya rinākṣa,tan wĕnaŋ ya tumuluŋ lara ni-ṅwaŋ,saŋ naréndra daśaśīla rinākṣa,krođa tan hana jitèndriya śānta*17:40:1579*

ƀakti riŋ guru lawan ta ri saŋ hyaŋ,wyaṙŧa tan hana guṇanya hiḍĕpku,Āṙyyaputra masamāđi mayajña,nitya satwahita sātwika satya*17:41:1580*

nya-ŋ parāṙŧa karuṇātmaka riŋ rāt,wyaṙŧa nisꝑala ya tāpa guṇanya,saŋ naréndra Anumāna rikèŋ rāt,māsih iŋ wiku Udāra guṇajña*17:42:1581*

hyaŋ basunđara jalāgni satéja,hyaŋ haṅin gagana dakṣiṇa sūṙyya,hyaŋ niśākara kitāmrĕtadéha,Aṣṭamūṙtti kita déwa wiśéṣa*17:43:1582*

ninda tāku ri kitékana saŋ hyaŋ,lwiṙ ta-tan wulat i-śīla nikaŋ wwaŋ,rāwaṇāđama durātmaka duṣṭa,wèḥ pwa yāmĕnaṅataḥ tan asiḥ ta*17:44:1583*

saŋ raǥūttama sudānta suśīla,mānawāgama nahan ta tinūtan,ndā taman paguṇa dènta kamuŋ hyaŋ,māsih iŋ kuṭila đik wiđi duṣṭa*17:45:1584*

hāḥ Ariṅku kita lakṣmaṇa sāđu,puṇyamānta manulus kita riŋ rāt,tat kasaḥ ta ri paran naranāŧa,ndā ṅhulun kaluṣa tan Ilu hantu*17:46:1585*

göŋ I-śakti naranāŧa Alaṅǥya,rāma lakṣmaṇa ṅaranta rikèŋ rāt,ndā ṅhulun kunaṅ iké Atipāpa,hétu niŋ pati Amoǥa kitālaḥ*17:47:1586*

Ꜽ prajāđipati rāwaṇa tiṅhal,ndā nihan ya ta wuwusku rĕṅönta,đaṙmma niŋ kadi kamīki taman lèn,satya kéwala patibrata đaṙmma*17:48:1587*

hétu niŋ turida tak mati ṅūni,dénya tan mati siraŋ raǥuputra,riŋ mĕné pwa ya huwus nira hantu,sāhasāku ri huripku Awās ya*17:49:1588*

{puṣpitāgra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
daśamuꝁa ya mataŋnya marya mojar,kadi-kadi jambat ujaṙta jañjan akwèḥ,tuwi-tuwi kita śakti cakrawaṙtti,tat ahalĕpāta makolaha-ŋ wimāṙgga*17:50:1589*

Asama-sama kitèŋ suđīra wīra,praƀu wiƀawādƀuta Uttamèŋ praƀāwa,saꝑala talapanéki jīwitaṅku,Ikana tĕwĕkta tibākĕné gulūṅku*17:51:1590*

kuśala ya ginawènta śāla dibya,yaśa paripūṙṇna ya pūrakèŋ triloka,rikana ta tulusanta mātyanāku,tuhu-tuhu saŋ praƀu ƀūmipālakèŋ rāt*17:52:1591*

yadin agĕlĕha ṅ-astra dèṅku liŋta,saꝑala ta saŋ hyaṅ apuy Umātyanāku,Asiṅ-asiṅa ta lèn mamātyanātaḥ,tak apilihāta marāk paré saṅ āṙyya*17:53:1592*

nahan ikana wuwus nirātisatya,daśawadanāta muwaḥ manaḥ niropĕk,salahasa sira kéraṅan kabāṅan,miṅis awĕṅis laku kāsyasiḥ nirāsiḥ*17:54:1593*

bari-bari ni wuwus niré si sītā,maṅayam-ayam juga mātya tan padondon,tan aṅĕn-aṅĕn iwĕḥ niké dadi wwaŋ,lara-lara niŋ dadi tan baśéry-awaknya*17:55:1594*

ndya kari guṇa nikaŋ patibratātaḥ,kinaharĕpan n-apa tan wuruŋ kapaṅguḥ,mati kita niyatā kari n-katĕmwa,lĕhĕṅa kitāt mahurip mamuktya ƀoga*17:56:1595*

takarin aku Iké praƀūttamèŋ rāt,sakaharĕpaṅkw-Irikaŋ triloka dadya,sapulu-puluha lakṣa séwu sītā,kṣaṇika tĕkā ya mataŋnya tūt ujaṙku*17:57:1596*

hayu-hayu ni wuwusku yogya liṅku,ya juga taman pakalīṅa dénya māmbĕk,Alah alara luluy mahān pamuṇḍuŋ,kaguyu-guyun malaré k-apan mapuṅguŋ*17:58:1597*

Ilu ta laku tuliḥ tan ora téki,Ulih-ulihan riya luṇṭa dénya mojar,wawa ta hulu ni rāma sawyakĕn ṅkā,Abalaṅakĕn ta muwaḥ rikaŋ pacaryan*17:59:1598*

daśamuꝁa ya ta liŋ nirātikopa,Alah awuyuŋ sira héwa tan tinaṅgap,lumaku sira muliḥ tĕkèŋ kaḍatwan,maṅucap-ucap naya cĕṭṭa Ucꞓa caṅkak*17:60:1599*

{swāgata}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
ndā ta tīta sira saŋ daśaśīṙṣa,jānakī sira muwaḥ Ujarĕn ta,mojarājar-ajar iŋ trijaṭāmwīt,mātya tāturun apuy juga tan lén*17:61:1600*

śoka kaṣṭatara saŋ trijaṭāśā,dénya yaṙ pĕjaha saŋ nrĕpaputrī,ndan manaḥnya manulus drĕḋaƀakti,satya riŋ sira ya mātya tumūta*17:62:1601*

tībra saŋ janakarājasutāmrĕm,tan pisan kapati sanđi gupuḥ graḥ,taṙ pahumbarah-araḥ wiparīta,Oṣađā nira ta liŋ nira mātya*17:63:1602*

madyarātri ya sĕḍĕŋ maturū ṅwaŋ,tan hanāta ya mumik paḍa nidrā,ṅkān pamoŋ Apuy apūṙwwa dilaḥnya,mātya rakwa sira kapwa mamūjā*17:64:1603*

jānakī sira surūpa sujanmā,śudđa taŋ hati suniṙmmala ṅ-āmbĕk,śudđa kèn ira suganđa ya somya,śokamānasa sumāđya saṅ āṙyya*17:65:1604*

swasti rāja Umarāđana saŋ hyaŋ,citta tañcala dudug ri ƀaṭāra,saprayojana sira praṇiđāna,prāṙŧanā nira ri saŋ praƀu rāma*17:66:1605*

ndaḥ ƀaṭāra kita bahni ṅaranta,nyāku mātya Apa tad wulat i-ṅwaŋ,taṙ pawèḥ suka-sukā ri manaḥku,ndaḥ patin kasula tāku ƀaṭāra*17:67:1606*

ndā kunaŋ ꝑala-ꝑalā ni patiṅku,ƀukti tāwakun amūṙṣita ri hyaŋ,rāmaƀadra sira téka tĕmuṅkwa,mon sadadya pakurĕnku ya śudđa*17:68:1607*

nī ta liŋ nira manĕmbah i-saŋ hyaŋ,glāna yaṙ wulati saŋ trijaṭāsiḥ,Aśrupāta humilī yaniwāṙyya,mojar épu ya sawèt ni laranya*17:69:1608*

dyaḥku toḥ ndya ta kunĕŋ lara ṅūni,riŋ jagattraya rikaŋ suraloka,riŋ kaŧā carita kāṇḍa Usāṇa,nyāŋ muwaḥ tuladané kita ṅūni*17:70:1609*

ndyèŋ purāṇa niyatèŋ Aji pūṙwwa,maṅkanā kadi laranta laranya,hāḥ Ah-o lalu lalis nira saŋ hyaŋ,taṙ wulat rikaṅ ulaḥ kasusatyan*17:71:1610*

wyaṙŧa kapwa guṇa niŋ guṇa satya, 
niṙguṇa-ŋ guṇa patibrata dé hyaŋ,ndān ikaŋ maguṇa duṣṭa kaniṣṭa,yèka tuṣṭi rikanaŋ wiđi duṣṭa*17:72:1611*

hétu yan kadi wuwusku Awajñā,dé niké pati niraŋ naranāŧa,puṇyamānta guṇamānta guṇajña,ḍū pĕjaḥ pwa sira hāḥ lalu saŋ hyaŋ*17:73:1612*

kāla yan malara tībra makiṅkiŋ,kampitékana matanya ya molaḥ,nā mataŋnyan agiraŋ ta manaḥnya,mājar-ājar i-siraŋ nrĕpaputrī*17:74:1613*

{turagagati}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
ndaḥ nihan śuƀanimitta t-iṅĕt-iṅĕt,kampitékana mataṅku ya ri kiwān,toharaḥ dyah aparan ndya kapuhara,dé nikaŋ mata mahā-haru-hara ya*17:75:1614*

ndak marèŋ giri suwéla ta sakarĕŋ,ndak lawad sira bapaṅku yan ahurip,mājarāku mati milwa ta ri kita,yan huwus mati huwus syapa turidan*17:76:1615*

dyaḥ nihan ya samayaṅku ta ri kita,tāt amātya riṅ apuy kapara-paran,hèrakĕñ juga tĕkāku ya masiha,ṅkāna yan pĕjaha mātya lawan aku*17:77:1616*

{ƀadralalita}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :21:
trijaṭā nahan ya ta wuwusnya yékana pĕsatnya śīǥra ya mibĕr,tĕka yèŋ suwéla giri ratna māya ya ta mèsi wānara kabèḥ,tĕmu saŋ bapāśila rikaŋ śilātala suśīla sādara sira,maharāja rāma hana riŋ palaṅka Ari lakṣmaṇāśila ri sor*17:78:1617*

naranāŧa taṙ kĕna rikaŋ turū mulat ikaŋ wrayādƀuta dahat,paḍa kapwa yāsrama Umĕtwakĕn kanipuṇanya riŋ raṇa kabèḥ,trijaṭā masö mara ri saŋ bapa praṇata gorawāwara-waraḥ,ri laranya yaṙ pĕjaha dèwi riŋ Apuy umātya riŋ kawa-kawa*17:79:1618*

bapa hāḥ Alib hala niraŋ daśānana kalĕṅka bañcana dahat,maharāja liŋ nira pĕjaḥ Ikaŋ hulu kinonakĕn wulatana,ya ta hétu dèwi janakātmajāṙ pĕjaha liŋ nirāturun apuy,ya tikāna donku bapa mājara ṅwaṅ iki mātya milwa ri sira*17:80:1619*

lalu hāḥ laraṅkwanaku yaṇ ḍĕṅö sira ta mātya tātaha-tahan,sira don dumèḥ haji tĕkā dumona I-siraŋ daśāsya taya lèn,ya mataŋnya yatna ta tĕmĕn ry-ujaṙ haji tĕkākĕnanyu ri sira,kalawan ta ƀakti mami tan kalén sira siwin lawan narapati*17:81:1620*

laku tāt Uliḥ Anaku śīǥra-śīǥra ta waraḥ ri dèwi mahulun,ri hurip praƀūttama-tamaṙ wikāra kalawan nihan kami kabèḥ,ya tikā Ibĕṙnya ta ḍatĕŋ manĕmbah awaraḥ ta yālah agiraŋ,Ataruŋ tikaŋ kĕtĕ-kĕtĕg mahosyan ikana swaranya kumĕtār*17:82:1621*

jaya dèwi-déwa ta mulat manĕḥta ya sukā naréndra mahurip,hana riŋ suwéla lawan āṙyya lakṣmaṇa kapīndra bāyutanaya,bapa ni ṅhulun taman adoḥ lawan prawara wīra wānara kabèḥ,Ibĕkan suśīla giri dé nikaŋ prawaga wéga yāsrama parĕŋ*17:83:1622*

mamupak gunuŋ kaparapal mapaŋ kadi gĕlap rikaŋ kasaṅa ya,Atiǥora ǥūṙṇnita gĕrĕḥ rikaŋ pralayakāla tulya ya humuŋ,Ikanaŋ gunuŋ ya kaguluŋ dinĕmwan ahaṅan sinaṅga ri taṅan,tamatan hanā juga kasaṅśayār alaha saŋ daśānana huwus*17:84:1623*

hana manŧarāꝁya giri mandarādƀuta Apūṙwwa paṙbwata magöŋ,kadi tan gunuŋ-gunuṅ inuṇḍa-Uṇḍa kadi siṅgi simban ahaṅan,paḍa makrak atri ya masiṅhanāda kalalaḥ mamātyana musuḥ,Ikanaŋ musuḥ kadi kasay hiḍĕpnya pususĕn ya riŋ kṣaṇika ya*17:85:1624*

paḍa wīra đīra Atiśūra-sāra śaraṇā nikaŋ samara ya,tuwi śakti ƀakti sapakon iraŋ nrĕpati sidđa dénya kadadi,dinawutnya taŋ kayu magöŋ ya téka pabulus-bulusnya lumĕkas,galagaḥ hiḍĕpnya riya yan gamĕl ya tamatan warĕg galigapĕn*17:86:1625*

wwara tāmutĕṙ kayu magöŋ hanāta ya pataŋ puluḥ takuraṅa,kadi ḍaṇḍa-ḍaṇḍa kadi taṙ lĕgön putĕrakĕn ya śīǥratara ya,kapati-ŋ banaspati gĕlāna tībra wiparīta kèlu kaputĕr,tak anon ta maṅkana daṅū Anuŋ paḍa-paḍanya kādƀuta dahat*17:87:1626*

Aparan mataŋnya malarā manaḥta ya pahènakĕn hari-harin,pawĕkas naréndra pituhun huripta kĕmitĕn taman haru-harā,Umulat siré ṅhulun unĕŋ-Unĕŋ nira ri dèwi tībra ta kunĕŋ,winurug ṅhulun muliha mohutĕn pĕjahakĕnta rakwa sakarĕŋ*17:88:1627*

{turagagati}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
dyaḥ mataŋnya ta rahup ta kamaligi,nya-ŋ gurun lĕkas ikaŋ lara lĕpasa,lālanéka hutita-ŋ hati malara,mèḥ mara-ŋ suka tĕkā ri kita huwus*17:89:1628*

nya-ŋ siliḥ ḍiri ḍatĕŋ wulati tadĕg,ndaḥ tibākĕna ri saŋ hyaṅ apuy usĕn,rapwa yan hilaṅ ikaŋ kaluṣa gĕsöŋ,saŋ narāđipa nahan Aṅĕn-aṅĕnĕn*17:90:1629*

dèwi tāgiraṅ amūja sira wawaŋ,puṣpa đūpa saha dīpa ya pinasaŋ,sopacāra caru niŋ raja-rajahan,japyahoma paripūṙṇna ya ginaway*17:91:1630*

wrĕtti saŋ hyaṅ ati śīǥra sira murub,ṅkān panĕmbah umarèŋ kanaka maṇik,jānakī saꝑala ƀakti Atiśaya,prāṙŧanā nira ri saŋ nrĕpati jayā*17:92:1631*

hé hutāśana ƀaṭāra hutipati,déwawaktra kita déwa para wiđi,ƀaktiwatsala ƀaṭāra guṇawiđi,đārakèŋ giri basunđara jalađi*17:93:1632*

déwa Uttama śiwāgni kita lĕwiḥ,Aṣṭamūṙtti kita déwata sakala,dibya Aṣṭaguṇa nityasa ri kita,maṅkana-ŋ triguṇa dènta kakawaśa*17:94:1633*

wīṙyyawān kita wiƀuḥ praƀu balawān,déwa dānawa maṅastuti ri kita,sidđa cāraṇa Umaṙcꞓana ri kita,téja tulya rawi koṭi yan upama*17:95:1634*

mwaŋ jagadđita ta ƀārata karuṇa,ƀakti yékana winèḥta suka magöŋ,tan kalèn kita paran niraṅ atapa,mwaŋ siraŋ krĕtawiwéka suka sadā*17:96:1635*

nitya kāruṇika sātwika ta kita,hétu niŋ suka lawan guṇa ta kita,mwaŋ kitékana mawèḥ wruha riṅ aji,hétu niŋ manĕmu mokṣapada kita*17:97:1636*

Ātmamāntra ta ƀaṭāra suka ya don,hétu niŋ mala kalĕṅka ya hilaṅa,kléśa pāpa nikanaŋ dadi lĕpasa,wètnyasiḥ ta rikanaŋ sakala jana*17:98:1637*

déwa hé triƀuwanéśwara dahana,ndaḥ wulat ry-aku ƀaṭāra Anumata,rāmaƀadra sira wèhĕn amĕnaṅa,māsihéry-aku sukān patĕmu mami*17:99:1638*

{wīralalita}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = :16:
dèwi nahan prayojana nirātidibya ya tĕmĕn,māri mapakṣa mātya ri hurip naréndra karĕṅö,ndan lara niŋ wiyoga ta jugāta tapwan alilaŋ,muṅgu rikaŋ palaṅka gumuliŋ sirāmaca-maca*17:100:1639*

saŋ trijaṭā maṅaswakĕn anékawaṙṇna pinaṅan,pāna sapaŧya māstawa suganđa maṇḍaga puli,laṇḍuga tꜽla-tīla hana modakaṇḍa sagala,nā ta masuk ri dèwi ri sĕḍĕŋ naréndra karĕṅö*17:101:1640*

saŋ trijaṭān pamèt kaba-kabālahāsih atuhan,mépu tumon manaḥ nira makūŋ macaṅkrama ta ya,māmĕṅ-amĕŋ masinđyan agawé kudiŋ-kudiṅ asiŋ,ménak aguywa-guywana nahan gawénya sakulĕm*17:102:1641*

mwaŋ paricārikā paḍa masinđyanādya wihikan,haṙṣa manaḥnya yan pasahuran sarāga magiraŋ,konĕṅ unĕŋ swaranya karĕṅö mawèḥ lulut unĕŋ,rāmya kiduŋnya kapwa sukacitta yān prahasana*17:103:1642*

śrī janakātmajā malara tībra monĕṅ aṅaraŋ,dé ni kiduŋ nikaŋ wwaṅ agawé prapañca ri sira,maṙmma ḍatĕŋ suganđa waṅi niŋ Aśoka bakula,mankin akūŋ manaḥ nira maṅĕn-n-aṅĕn raǥusuta*17:104:1643*

hāḥ lalu niṙǥrĕṇanta hara liṅku manmaŧa wagus,śīṙṇna hatiṅku dènta pinanaḥ tatan sipi pĕgat,ḍīna dudū dahat tamak uđāni riŋ dadi kĕdö,mātya kunĕŋ ya ménaka maran hilaŋ Ikaṅ unĕŋ*17:105:1644*

maṅkana tīs ni téja nikanaŋ wulan Atiśaya,ndan mapanas hiḍĕpku dadi Agni Ujwala murub,puṙṇnama nitya tan kagunĕman sadā ya gumawaŋ,hāḥ ndya ta yaṙ suka-ŋ priyawiyoga nitya linaran*17:106:1645*

mwaŋ ta rikèŋ Aśokawana somya rāmya ya tĕmĕn,bāp ta sĕkaṙ hanériya marūm nirantara rurū,hāḥ ndya dumèḥ wiyoga kasukāna yan hana riya,saŋ wiku mona monĕṅa manaḥ nirāṙ para riké*17:107:1646*

maṅkana taŋ haṅin mrĕdu suganđa komala mirir,ḍū magawé raras hati Unĕŋ ndya dé ya ta kunĕŋ,mātra Ikaŋ gĕrĕḥ ya karĕṅö mawèh unĕṅ agöŋ,hāḥ mata đūṙtta saŋ madana mèdi yāmarimisi*17:108:1647*

ndak wulat iŋ laṅit kilat ikā tinonku lumarap,māṙ hrĕdayaṅku dénya Umaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn priyawara,yéki tĕwĕk niraŋ kusumacāpa tīkṣṇa hinunus,nī tumibé hatiṅku humilī ta rāḥnya ri mata*17:109:1648*

ganđa nikaŋ Aśoka Asanādi Utkaṭa sumār,yéka panaḥ niraŋ madana rodra tīkṣṇa maṅani,śakti ƀaṭāra manmaŧa panaḥ nirāpratihata,hāḥ kadi mātya tāku mapanas hiḍĕpku riṅ umaḥ*17:110:1649*

dèwi nahan ta liŋ nira tumūt sirāta tumurun,maṅkin ikā manaḥnya magiraŋ sahaṙṣa ya kabèḥ,lèn maṅidūŋ makinnara mabaṅsi lèn taṅ aṅigĕl,nitya ṅ-atoṙ lawan mamawa tāmbu-tāmbularasa*17:111:1650*

mwaŋ magawé ta junti karuṇa swaranya karĕṅö,lon magawé sĕmut pupul ataḥ Asiŋ sakaharĕp,dwadwal anékawaṙṇna lakĕtan tapé paṅisi lèn,nā pinaṅanya ménak ahaṅöt bubuṙ caraṇa lén*17:112:1651*

kapwa ta yāsĕkaṙ majĕnu kapwa mahyas asalin,kapwa makèn lalāsa ya dukūla lāka tulalay,kapwa raray rarā rahayu yukti yogya ya kabèḥ,kapwa ta rāgacitta makin uttamèŋ prahasana*17:113:1652*

lèn hana rākṣasī makuru rūkṣa morĕm awĕnĕs,ndan kadurus ya barwaṅ ahuyaŋ maṅèl asiṅ ator,wyāđi magöŋ wĕtĕŋnya kawayan nirantara kĕbĕs,tan dwa gĕlāna sāsiṅ aparö paḍātukup iruŋ*17:114:1653*

yéka pinatryakĕn paḍa kĕkĕl kabèḥ mawurahan,méraṅ umūṙ ya mamrih alayū tinūt ya ginutuk,glāna ṅ-atoṙ mamid mamuk akĕm taman kawulatan,hèwa n-inum batoṙnya mawĕrö warĕg ya maturū*17:115:1654*

dèwi dudū manaḥ nira maṅĕn-n-aṅĕn saṅ ahulun,mèpu marèŋ prasāda gumuliŋ sirāturu-turū,saŋ trijaṭā tumūt pamucaṅan nahan ya winawa,mwaŋ mukawāsa Utkaṭa marūm kapūṙnya karĕṅö*17:116:1655*

saŋ trijaṭā ya tāmupu sĕkaṙ pijĕṙ kajĕnĕkan,cāmpaka yénikĕtnya n-inapus karaŋ bali wanèḥ,nāŋ maṅunĕŋ puḍak ya ta milĕt mawoṙ ta ya gaḍuŋ,dibya hayunya n-aṅwakĕn i-dèwi gorawa ta ya*17:117:1656*

mwaŋ hana nāgapuṣpa tinĕnunya rāga ya wulat,mwaŋ paḍalinya bāp paḍapaḍāputiḥ ya tinĕnun,nāŋ dalimādƀutāmanis abāŋ karaŋ-karaṅ ikā,bāp saruṇinya dibya makuniŋ mikĕt ya taruṇī*17:118:1657*

{candrawilasita}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
paḍa maṅikĕt kĕmbaŋ wwara taruṇī,saruṇi rinantay mwaŋ suka ya marūm,hana manĕnun nīlotpala mahalĕp,hana maṅalap tañjuŋ juga ya tinū*17:119:1658*

hana ta manū kĕmbaŋ śrigaḍiṅ arūm,sĕḍĕṅ arurū lumrā pinarĕbutan,wwara marĕbut mĕṇḍuṙ paḍa mahalĕp,maśiwa-siwo yāsiḥ paḍa masĕkar*17:120:1659*

kañiri kucupnyākwèḥ hana masĕkar,kadi Anumodèŋ mahyun asĕkara,sa-kaya-kayanyāsiḥ mamupu sĕkar,ya ta Inalapnyémpĕn ya tinulaṅan*17:121:1660*

tuluṅi ta rowaŋnyāmilihi sĕkar,lalita lawan sūtrékanaṅ inikĕt,bakula pinolot riŋ puḍak ahalĕp,winawa ri dèwī tuṣṭa sira mulat*17:122:1661*

mulat ikanaŋ lèŋ śīǥra ya maṅalap,kusuma kuraṇṭākwèḥ pada ya matöb,sahana nikaŋ kĕmbaŋ ya ta Inalap,ya ta sinalaṅsaŋ mwaŋ suraƀi marūm*17:123:1662*

rahayu rinantay kapwa ya masĕkar,tumula-tulaṙ yāmèt kusuma mahās,mara riṅ aśokātyanta ya kasukan,kadi grĕha saŋ hyaŋ manmaŧa ya katon*17:124:1663*

maṅucap-ucap yāṅkĕn paḍa Ucapan,Ilu ta tulaṙ dèwī sira Umulat,wulat i-manawwaŋ kapwa malihaṅan,pahayu kĕtā kèn-kènya sĕlĕtakĕn*17:125:1664*

tuhu-tuhu dèwī waṅśaja manulus,sari-sari tan lèn mānawa winuwus,duga-duga dātā sāđu sira putus,tak alaṅ-alaŋ wadwā ri sira huwus*17:126:1665*

madulu-duluṙ yārumpukan asana,maṅiduṅiduŋ yācaṅkrama kasukan,maturu-turū roṇḍon pinakatilam,tumĕṅa-tĕṅā riŋ candrawilasita*17:127:1666*

{kusumawicitra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
kumucur ikaŋ pañcuran atirāmya,parijata muṅgwiŋ parigi paranti,parawan umaṅsö mamupu sĕkaṙnya,mara-marahup tan hana katakutnya*17:128:1667*

wuṅa tali tambil hulur-uluranta,wuṅa wari nīhan wwara I-ruhuṙnya,wuṅa tĕlĕṅ akwèḥ kadi ta rinĕṅga,wwara wuṅa raṅgādƀuta pacarĕṅga*17:129:1668*

makuliliṅan riŋ talaga kabèḥnya,paḍa mamupak paṅkaja sahananya,sulur inalapnyāmĕṅ-amĕṅa donya,paḍa masĕkaṙ kéśara rinurūnya*17:130:1669*

tamala-malaḥ Utpala Inalapnya,Ulih-ulihanyātiśaya halĕpnya,ya tikana winwatnya ri sira dèwī,lumaku muliḥ sokya-tara tar āgya*17:131:1670*

Umirir alon-lon ikaṅ anilārūm,kadi ta lum iŋ saŋ malara wiyoga,kusuma rurū riŋ hawan atirāmya,kadi pasĕgĕḥ niŋ kayu-kayu tuṣṭa*17:132:1671*

hayu nira dèwī saꝑala sinĕmbaḥ,tuwi sira satyātiśaya suśīla,malara tuwin tan malupa ri saŋ hyaŋ,tĕka ta mamūjèŋ kusumawicitra*17:133:1672*

{mālinī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
Aŧa rahina ya sānpun māwa taŋ déśa rāmya,dadi marahup amūjā jānakī satyaƀakti,satata tan alupātaḥ satya riŋ déwapūjā,tuhu-tuhu sira dèwī-déwatātaḥ cinitta*17:134:1673*

hana ta wahu tawan strī kāsyasiḥ wwaŋ sujanmā,priyawiraha ya monĕŋ tībra sambéga ṅāmbĕk,Atiśaya ta manaḥnyāhyun ta riŋ sātwikāsiḥ,saꝑala nira ta dèwī ƀakti nāhan ta liŋnya*17:135:1674*

ya tikana hiḍĕpĕntā liṅku saŋ hyaŋ śarīra,kita karika riyāpan janma mānuṣya hīna,sakawĕnaṅa nikā taŋ kāya riŋ yuktikrĕtya,sari-sari warahĕn tā tékanaŋ citta ƀaktya*17:136:1675*

wulati kari ya kĕdwa ndan hanĕŋ Āgamokta,tuwi carita rĕṅönta ꝁyāti riŋ kaṇḍaparwa,saka-saka ṅuni tékiŋ kléśa saṅsāra ni ṅwaŋ,ndan ikana ginawé taŋ ƀakti dé suŋ wiśéṣa*17:137:1676*

ya ta Ikana wuwusnyātyanta sambéga māsiḥ,maṅĕn-aṅĕn ikanā yan tan lanèŋ sokya sampat,wulati ta sira dèwī wèt nikāmbĕknya ƀakti,satata ta sira śoka ṅkām ri soṙ niŋ Aśoka*17:138:1677*

#Aṣṭādaśamas saṙggaḥ#
<mālaƀāriṇi>
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
^18/1/1666.
nda tatīta sira-ŋ naréndraputrī,sira saṇ ƀūpati rāwaṇojarĕn ta,magawé naya bañcanātiduṣṭa,kalaran śoka kasoran iŋ kaśūran*18:1:1678*

śuka sāraṇa śīra sāra śakti,śaraṇā riŋ raṇa yogya wīra đīra,ya ta cāra kinon iraŋ daśāsya,mahasa ṅkāna rikaŋ gunuŋ suwéla*18:2:1679*

milaṅa-ŋ bala wānara prawīra,wruha riŋ śakti lawan dudū manaḥnya,kalawan kapirāja yan subadđā,wĕnaṅomātyaŧawā yaŧāsukātūt*18:3:1680*

ya Ikā ta pakon iraŋ daśāsya,dadi luṅhā śuka sāraṇātiśīǥra,tĕka yèŋ giri riŋ suwélanāma,tĕmahan wānararūpa bañcanātaḥ*18:4:1681*

Umulat ta siraŋ wiƀīṣaṇāꝁya,dadi maṅsö sira đīra sāha sojar,śuka sāraṇa Ꜽ-mapéki donmu,Apa mĕṅgĕp wray iké Atīta duṣṭa*18:5:1682*

ya Ikāna wuwus nirān patakwan,humĕnĕŋ taŋ śuka sāraṇāṙdđa méraŋ,Inasö ya Inambulan tinonton,sinikĕp yénapusan wawaŋ ta winwat*18:6:1683*

Umulat naranāŧa rāmaƀadra,dadi mojaṙ ta sirèŋ wiƀīṣaṇādi,wrayapéki ta kāsyasiḥ binanđa,Apa doṣanya lukan laraṅku dénya*18:7:1684*

jaya hé nrĕpa tan watĕkta téki,ya Iké rākṣasa cāra saŋ daśāsya,śuka sāraṇa ya prawīra riŋ rāt,tuwi yāwānara bañcanéki donya*18:8:1685*

ndya kunaŋ pwa wuwus ƀaṭāra tātaḥ,ya tikānuŋ taḍahĕn taman kalèna,ya mataŋnyan inaswakĕn ya winwat,yadiyan patyana yan mapā gatinya*18:9:1686*

tamatan kĕna téki patyananta,syapa tékāwarahé tuhanya wrĕtta,luputīkana banđananya tosĕn,mara yan śīǥra tĕké tuhanya mojar*18:10:1687*

Iti nā ta wuwus ƀaṭāra rāma,mari taŋ rākṣasa kāpusan sutrĕpta,Umasö ya wawaŋ madĕg manĕmbaḥ,Umuliḥ śīǥra huwus ḍatĕŋ ri lĕṅkā*18:11:1688*

satĕkanya satuṣṭa māri śoka,Umasuk tèŋ wataṅan wawaŋ ta mojar,satinonya yaŧāṙŧa dénya mājar,I siraŋ rākṣasa rāwaṇāđirāja*18:12:1689*

maharāja kamīkihĕn kinonkon,Umara ṅkā ri musuḥta rāmaƀadra,Ibĕkan wray ikaŋ gunuŋ suwèla,tĕka riŋ pāṙśwa kabèh i-soṙ sĕsĕk-sök*18:13:1690*

paḍa śakti ya kapwa tan pahīṅan,mamupak paṙbwata mèrutulya riŋ göŋ,paripūṙṇna subadđa sétubanđa,ya tikāpūṙwwa gawénya kādƀutèŋ rāt*18:14:1691*

Umuliḥ Ikanaŋ gunuŋ kadi lwaḥ,Ikanaŋ sāgara tulya paṙbwatāwān,ri sawètnyan agöŋ ta śakti niŋ wray,taya mèwĕḥ taya duṙgga dénya kabwat*18:15:1692*

sahananya ta ƀrĕtya śakti ƀakti,ri siraŋ rāǥawa yālilaŋ manaḥnya,pawanātmaja tan dudū hiḍĕpnya,tuwi saŋ Aṅgada tan surud ya māsiḥ*18:16:1693*

{Aparawaktra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
gawa-gawaya gawākṣa jāmbawān,saha nala nīla suséna késari,śaraƀa wrĕṣaƀa Indrajānu lèn,kumuda darīmuꝁa ganđamādana*18:17:1694*

{puṣpitāgra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
dwiwiđa panasa ƀīmawaktra tāra,winata śuƀodara kālawaktra đūmra,śatabali kalawan sꝑuṭākṣa mꜽnda,đruwasa đanuṙđara dāma mattahasti*18:18:1695*

nahan ikana wiśéṣa muꝁya niŋ wré,Atiśaya rodra ya kālamrĕtyu sākṣāt,kagiri-giri Ulaḥnya lèn wulatnya,gumuyu maśabda masoṙ gĕlap ta dénya*18:19:1696*

{Aparawaktra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
Ikana ta ya kabèḥnya tan kalèn,Ikana manaḥnya ta ƀakti kéwala,raǥusuta sira liṅga déwatā,rikana hatinya kabèḥnya wānara*18:20:1697*

sagila mati kacidra ta ṅhulun,Inamah-amaḥ nira saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,raǥusuta sira sāđu taṙ pawèḥ,sira humurip ri patikta hé praƀu*18:21:1698*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
mataŋnya hé ƀūpati yogya tāpĕsa,nihan ta-taṅguḥ mami karwa yālapĕn,lanā mahārāja mamuktya don iké,tatan sakèŋ drohaka ƀakti hétuka*18:22:1699*

matūta tātaḥ maharāja ménaka,lawan siraŋ rāma maran lanā ṅ-inak,sitā sirékāna wawan mĕnèŋ gĕlĕk,Apan sirékā ta dumèḥ tukaṙ hana*18:23:1700*

{Upajāti waṅśa}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
nahan wuwus niŋ śuka sāraṇāhayu,mataṅguh iŋ yukti Asiḥnya mapraƀu,sakrođa saŋ rāwaṇa yaṙ tinaṅguhan,mojaṙ kabāṅan sira wèt nikaŋ galak*18:24:1701*

hāḥ đik mahākaśmala ƀrĕtya tan waras,tuhun ṅaran rākṣasa tan pasāra ya,Alaḥ magöŋ tībra takutmu riŋ musuḥ,makon ta ko ƀaktya taman wruh īŋ Iraŋ*18:25:1702*

tan déwa tan rākṣasa tékanaŋ musuḥ,ya wānarātyanta kaniṣṭa yāđama,sawèt niké pāpamu tan prawīra ko,Alaḥ dudī cittamu ƀakti riŋ musuḥ*18:26:1703*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
pratīta riŋ sāra ya śūra riŋ daṅū,mĕné pwa yāsāra ya cāra duṙyyaśa,milag pwa yuḥ mūṙ laku ko parèŋ musuḥ,wĕgil Ikaŋ hīna wiƀīṣaṇāđama*18:27:1704*

nahan wuwus saŋ daśaśiṙṣa yāgĕlĕŋ,madĕg manĕmbaḥ śuka sāraṇātakut,praƀuṅku tātan huniṅan wuwus salaḥ,Apan-n-asiḥ ƀakti ya donya tan kalèn*18:28:1705*

kunaŋ pwa yan papraṅa budđya saŋ praƀu,nya saṅhulun mātya rikaŋ raṇāṅgaṇa,byayā mahārāja Iké hurip mami,ꝑalā ni kāsiḥ ta magöŋ ri saṅhulun*18:29:1706*

lawan ndya yatnā maharāja riŋ musuḥ,Anuŋ Upāyā gawayĕn mĕnèŋ gĕlĕk,nihan patik saŋ praƀu tan Alāṅ-alaŋ,Ujaṙ mahārāja kunaŋ nahan rĕṅön*18:30:1707*

ndya dona niŋ nīti lawan nayojarĕn,Apan kaniṣṭéka musuḥta wānara,Atag tikaŋ śāwara mĕtwa riŋ raṇa,tulup panaḥ yéka wawan lawan Asu*18:31:1708*

lawan n-ikāṅhiŋ guṇa yogya saṅgrahan,huwus katon śīṙṇna nanānya dé nikā,Ikā pwa wèḥ kwèḥnya kunaŋ hanāluput,nahan kayatnākĕna saŋ mahābala*18:32:1709*

{prĕŧwītala}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
nahan n-ikana liŋnya riŋ daśamuꝁātiđīra-ŋ manaḥ,nda tīta rasikā siraŋ nrĕpati rāmaƀadrājarĕn,prayatna maṅulī-huliḥ sira mamèt upāyāhayu,wiƀīṣaṇa kapīndra māruti nahan ta rowaŋ nira*18:33:1710*

saṅ aṅgada Uliḥ naréndra maṅaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn tan kalèn,suđīra balawān prawīra sira śūra sārāsama,sirékana ta dūta saŋ praƀu kinon marā riŋ musuḥ,tumaṅguhana saŋ daśānana Asiḥ nirèŋ rāt ya don*18:34:1711*

saṅ aṅgada kinon lumakwa parituṣṭa tāmbĕk nira,ri ƀakti nira hétu tan n-alaṅ-alaŋ ri saŋ rāǥawa,ya tékana pĕsat nirāṙ laku mibĕṙ lumumpat sira,haṅin nira sarodra kādƀuta Ikaŋ sa-lĕṅkāpura*18:35:1712*

Ikaŋ đwaja tikĕl katon awanimitta séṇḍuŋ riwut,pĕtĕŋ katatakut ya gĕntĕr atirodra guntuṙ kĕtug,gĕrĕḥ pwa ya magĕnturan maputĕran tikaŋ handaru,lĕbū ya ta mĕlĕk mawū mawalikan tikaŋ rākṣasa*18:36:1713*

Anantara pĕtĕŋ hilaŋ mĕtu ƀaṭāra sūṙyyāsinaŋ,ḍatĕŋ ta siraṅ aṅgadākya mahawan tatambak masuk,pragalƀa sira đīra niṙƀaya tataṙ lĕgö riŋ saƀā,sawismaya siraŋ daśānana tumon ulaḥ sāhasa*18:37:1714*

rikaŋ wataṅan uṅgu saŋ daśamuꝁāta taŋ ƀrĕtya bāp,Ikaŋ Awanimitta tātan iniwö wiśāta-ŋ manaḥ,masö ta siraṅ aṅgadāśila wawaŋ ta mojaṙ sira,Ikaŋ swara malon prakāśa karĕṅö mawās ƀyakta ya*18:38:1715*

daśānana kitaŋ prajāđipa wuwusku yékin rĕṅön,nihan n-aku ta bāliputra karĕṅö pratītāṅgada,ƀaṭāra raǥuputra rāma sira nāŧa niŋ rāt kabèḥ,sirékana makon marā ri kita hétukanya-k para*18:39:1716*

kumona kita ƀaktya donku saha ƀrĕtya tānĕmbaha,huripta tadahĕn maran kita lanā mamuktya-ŋ śri ya,samūlya hana riŋ kaḍatwan alapĕn wawan pawwata,Apèni maṇi ratna mādulura dèwi sītā r-uliḥ*18:40:1717*

yadin wihaṅa tat t-anĕmbaha mawā siraŋ mꜽŧilī,siraŋ nrĕpati rāmaƀadra biṣamān sumīṙṇnānana,mawās ta kita mātya đūlya tamatan paśéṣā kabèḥ,Apan sira lĕwiḥ parākrama nirèŋ jagat wīṙyyawān*18:41:1718*

lawan ndya kari dona ni-ṅwaṅ aƀimāna tātaḥ sadā,ṙyya nitya nikanaŋ hurip tuwi kayowanan tan lanā,Ikaŋ suka kilat paḍanya lumarap taman śāśwata,tuwin priya samāgamāsama-saméki riŋ cañcala*18:42:1719*

Ah-o lalu lalista mūṙkꝁa ri gulūnta saŋ rāwaṇa,Amoǥa kita moha mūḋa paradāra momo manaḥ,panaḥ nira ƀaṭāra rāma Atitībra tīkṣṇāpanas,tamat hiḍĕp ikā haraḥ guragaḍāƀimāna-ŋ manaḥ*18:43:1720*

nahan ya ta wuwus saṅ aṅgada sakontukānaṅguhi,daśānana mabāŋ prakampita ṅ-awak sawèt niŋ galak,halis nira ya cāla kumrut ikanaŋ lalāṭārĕṅū,wulat nira ya tāwĕlū tudiṅi téka saŋ Aṅgada*18:44:1721*

{śiꝁariṇī}
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
Ah-o niṙlajjékiŋ plawaga kadurus pāpa ya dahat,bali pwékī đīrèṅ aṅĕn-aṅĕn apan bālitanaya,luluy jañjan tꜷn mèraṅ ikaṅ umulat ri ṙyya Ađama,rumūg taŋ đaṙmmāgöŋ mawara-warah iŋ wīṙyya balawān*18:45:1722*

Alaḥ damƀāƀaṅga Agati ya tan olin kakawaśa,kaniṣṭanyān pāmbĕk sumiwi Ikanaŋ śatru kaluśa,taman sūpĕn tékā hatimu ri pĕjaḥ niŋ bapa kunaŋ,guru drobātyantèŋ kanaraka Ikèŋ wānara lumud*18:46:1723*

tatan wis tāwaknyān mahala ya mamèt milwa kahalā,waliŋnya ṅwaŋ mūḋā kawĕnaṅa ta dényān paṅujari,ƀaṭārātaḥ sākṣāt sira tuwi kumonāku Umawā,Ikaŋ sītā ṅkāné raǥusuta tak aṅgā kimuta ko*18:47:1724*

t-uliḥ tosĕn pājāri ratumu tak aṅgān pamatiha,lawan kon tomaṅswāgĕlara malagā kon lumĕkasa,sahasrā rāmānuŋ tĕka pariƀawā tak matakuta,kahī tuṅgal mwaŋ wré tuhaburu nahan murwa juga ya*18:48:1725*

nahan tojaṙ saŋ rāwaṇa muman-uman dūta saƀaya,malĕs mojaṙ saŋ bālitanaya madĕg krođa ta sira,pamĕṅpöŋ pojaṙ ko kalana kadi tan mātya ya huwus,katon lwiṙmun śīṙṇnā saha bala ta dé saŋ raǥusuta*18:49:1726*

nahan tojaṙ saŋ Aṅgada dadi muliḥ niṙƀaya sira,daśagrīwātyantèŋ saƀaya saha ƀrĕtyāṅulih-uliḥ,Ulaḥ lèn lwīṙ tātan kadi daṅu-daṅū Aṙdđa masĕnĕḥ,sawèt niŋ mānāgöŋ kadi tan atakut đīra yan adĕg*18:50:1727*

nda tīta lwiṙ saŋ rāwaṇa Ikana saŋ Aṅgada t-ujar,wawaŋ prāpta ṅkānĕŋ giriwara masuk śīǥra ri dalĕm,manĕmbaḥ maṅsö sādara sira ri saŋ rāmawijaya,wawaŋ mojaṙ mājaṙ ta sira ri Ujaṙ saŋ daśamuꝁa*18:51:1728*

mulat maṅsö saŋ lakṣmaṇa milu ta saŋ nīla nala lén,masuk saŋ sugrīwānilasuta susénākya winata,tumūt sakwèḥ niŋ wré maśila maduluṙ kapwa ta humuŋ,kinon muktyékānaŋ ꝑala saꝑala muṅgwiŋ śiꝁariṇī*18:52:1729*

#nawadaśamas saṙggaḥ#
<praharaṇakalika>:19
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :14:
^19/1/1718.
krama huwus amaṅan ꝑala sahana nikaŋ,kapibala paripūṙṇna ya tan alah-alaḥ,makin atiśaya sāhasa paḍa magalak,kalalah umahĕm ahyun amususa musuḥ*19:1:1730*

tuwi-tuwi bala rākṣasa paḍa kalalaḥ,sĕḍĕṅ amaṅan agoṣṭi ya wijah aṅinum,manĕwĕri ya maƀūṣaṇa kanaka maṇik,muꝁa ḍaḍa Ibĕkan jĕnu paḍa masĕkar*19:2:1731*

dadi maṅadĕg anambutakĕna si gadā,curiga krĕtala lori muśala paraśu,bulusuligi sa-lāṅgala śarađi laras,triśika paṭiśa sapraharaṇa kuliśa*19:3:1732*

mĕtu ta ya rikanaŋ kuṭawara waṅunan,đwaja tuwi tĕṅĕran ya paḍa pinasaṅan,kuda ya rinasukan gaja ya kinawacan,raŧa ya Inibĕkan praharaṇa kalikā*19:4:1733*

{Upendrabajra}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
sĕḍĕŋ nikaŋ rākṣasawīra yāwū,humuŋ ya mahyā kalalaḥ ya maṅhèr,saśoka saṇ rāwaṇa mohacitta,ṇ-ḍĕṅö siraŋ rāma hanèŋ suwéla*19:5:1734*

rajaḥ tamaḥ niŋ hati tībra wrĕdđi,lawan nikaŋ mātsara rāga Iṙṣyā,Iké si sītā ya ta patyanaṅkwa,tatan riko tan ry-aku liŋ nirāśā*19:6:1735*

r-aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn kaśmala duṙyyaśèŋ rāt,ri pāpa niŋ strīwađa yātiǥora,madĕg g-ahĕṅkāra lawan kađīran,manaḥ manāṅdé pĕjahèŋ raṇāṅga*19:7:1736*

r-atag ta saŋ mantri patiḥ prahasta*19:8:1737*
lawan mahāpāṙśwa ǥaṭodarākya,tumūt wirūpākṣa wilohitākṣa,yupākṣa kānĕm nira mantri muꝁya*19:9:1738*

{Upajāti bajra}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
Anuŋ mahāśakti balaprađāna,mitraǥna lāwan praǥasa prajaṅǥa,saŋ jambumāli Aśanipraƀākyas,đūwrākṣa Ākampana bajramuṣṭi*19:10:1739*

déwāntakānak nira saŋ daśāsya,narāntaka mwaŋ triśiraḥ trikāya,Anuŋ Anak saŋ Ari kumƀakaṙṇna,praśāsta riŋ rāt si nikumƀa kumƀa*19:11:1740*

Ikā ta saŋ mantri bala prawīra,wadwā ni wadwā nira koṭi-koṭi,mahöm mahāśūra ya sāra riŋ praŋ,tīkṣṇāyuđanyogra kadīndrabajra*19:12:1741*

{sragđara}
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :21:
tat kālanyān inājñan sahana-hana nikaŋ rākṣasomĕtwa riŋ praŋ,tinyup taŋ śaṅka saṅꝁyānya ya Inatus-atus koṭi lakṣā parāḍya,śabdanyātyuǥra mapyak prakaṭa kadi gĕlap sapta pātāla molaḥ,lyab taŋ rāt ƀūṙ-ƀuwaḥ-swaḥ kadi ta ya śiwakaŋ Aṇḍa koṇḍākyakāṇḍĕk*19:13:1742*

lèn kĕṇḍaŋ koṭi-koṭyaṙwuda niyuta humuŋ ǥora gambīra śabda,yan ginwal méǥa samwaṙttaka juga gumuruḥ ƀūmi méṅguŋ gumĕntĕr,trus twas niŋ wwaŋ pwa dényānarawata kumĕtĕṙ kātara-ŋ kāla-kāla,monīkaŋ maṙddalādrĕs saha paṭaha mahāsāra masraŋ makaṅsi*19:14:1743*

maṅhrik taŋ tuṅgaṅan kwèḥ paḍa tahu mamusuḥ syuḥ masāk sénasönya,maŋhrĕṅguŋ taŋ gajaḥ ǥūṙṇnita rasa lĕbura-ŋ rājya lĕṅkā mawāgyut,kāgyat tékaŋ kĕnas riŋ wana gahana-hanan glāna mūṙcꞓān kagöman,dé niŋ śabdātiǥorādƀuta kadi rubuha-ŋ paṙbwatārūga śīṙṇna*19:15:1744*

saŋ śūrātyanta tuṣṭān uni sahana nikaŋ śaṅka kĕṇḍaŋ Asaṅꝁya,maṅkin magyā Umĕtwèŋ raṇa hana maṅadĕg kapwa tāsiṅhanāda,sāmbut kontaṙnya lāwan karatala pinĕniŋ śūla lèn candrahāsa,tan dwān tindak tumandaŋ wijah aṅigĕl ikaŋ wīra pañcāyuđajña*19:16:1745*

saŋ wruḥ riŋ hastiśikṣā sira Ika mamanèk riŋ liman matta daṙppa,yatnānuṅgaŋ manāmpil curiga Ikana saŋ paṇḍitèŋ śālihotra,lèn tékaŋ rākṣasānuŋ suƀaga winihikan rī đanuṙwédaśāstra,kapwādandan Umuṅgwiŋ raŧa hana humaḍaŋ sāraŧinyātisāra*19:17:1746*

krorākārékanaŋ rākṣasa mamawa Arug kapwa maswāṅga ƀinna,wintaŋ-wintaŋ ni kantaṙnya ya kanaka mabāŋ lèn maṇik ry-āntaranya,tan swaŋ swaṅganya siṅhākrĕti ya katatakut mrĕtyu yomrĕm tumon ya,saŋ hyaŋ kālāta kolāhala mawĕdi tumon lwiṙnya rodrātirodra*19:18:1747*

maṅkat saŋ śaktimāntākawaca wĕsi sĕsök wuntu taŋ māṙgga dènya,toḥ tuṇḍuŋ taŋ panĕṇḍas laku-laku ta huwus liŋnya saṅké sĕsöknya,maṅkā tékāyuđanyojwala paraśu magöŋ lwānya gaṅsal ḍĕpā ya,yāwat yāmraŋ musuḥ riŋ samara daṅu-daṅī tan papiŋ rwéka dénya*19:19:1748*

sāṅkat niŋ wīra mahyā paḍahi paḍa humuŋ tūt hawan śaṅka tinyup,tuṣṭékaŋ wīrapatnī gumuyu ya magiraŋ n-ton siraŋ swāmi mĕtwa,suṇḍaŋ téka priyanyān laku maṅatĕrakĕn ṅkā ri hèŋ niŋ kaḍatwan,swāmī ndaḥ yatna-yatnāmriha ta yaśa nahan liŋnya mamwīt manĕmbaḥ*19:20:1749*

tātan maṅkā Ikaŋ strī wĕdi-wĕdi manaṅis kwèḥ kapöyöḥ Umĕṇḍĕk,kapwān tiṅhal tumuṅkul makiḍupuh akuśā kāsyasiḥ wètnyasiḥnya,saŋ wīrāsiḥ tumiṅhal hati nira kalaran kāsyasiḥ luḥ kumĕmbĕŋ,mantuk tuntun ta kāsiḥnyan arĕki sakarĕŋ kolakĕn pèri luḥnya*19:21:1750*

śrĕṅgārārum Ikaŋ strī wahu kĕna riṅ asiḥ yāsayut śīǥra mojar,swāmī taṅhèṙ pwa tāḍū lalu tan anumatanté sĕḍĕŋ glāna monĕŋ,haywāgyā milwa mātya ṅhulun aturun apuy yaṙ pĕjaḥ nā ta liŋnya,trĕṣṇā saŋ wīra maṅhèṙ dadi sira sumĕlaŋ lālanékaŋ wara strī*19:22:1751*

molĕm maṅliḥ hanékiŋ wahu sĕḍĕṅ aṅiḍam komalārūm wulatnya,mapway-pway somya saśrī wulat agawayasiḥ maŋdudut citta rāgi,rumbé tékā gĕluŋnyāhirĕṅ alĕṅis alit rāmyan uṅgwī pipinya,sambé saŋ swāmi mamriḥ lumaku ya kumĕtĕṙ tūṙnya māpĕs wĕtisnya*19:23:1752*

swāmī toliḥ pwa ta ṅwaŋ lalu takarih iké tan Asiḥ tātar onĕŋ,ndā tan karyāku milwa ṅhulun umĕtu tamak sāha saṅké sukunta,Aṅgānyāt mātya tādé Aku ta pĕjahanāwakku mātyātamūka,saṅké ƀaktiṅku yāṅhiŋ kita juga kaharan liṅga muṅgwiŋ hatiṅku*19:24:1753*

lāwan yan kāntunātaḥ syapa ta kadi kitānuŋ mahāté tuwuḥku,mwaŋ maŋ­rākṣā kitātaḥ taṅisana śaraṇā yan tĕkāŋ duḥkakāla,Āpan tā mitra kāsiḥ Aku tamak akadaŋ taṙ wulat rāma-réṇa,saṅké doṣaṅku k-āŋlĕs mara ri kita Alaḥ tībra mahyun tak amwīt*19:25:1754*

nā liŋnyāsiḥ manĕmbaḥ drawa ta hati nikaŋ wīra masnéha māsiḥ,wèt ni hyunyékanānuŋ Umawaya ri sirānlud sĕḍĕŋ gaṙbƀinī ya,puḥ ṅ-āmbĕk luḥ tan ampĕt r-aṅĕn-aṅĕn ikanāsiḥnya lèn kāsyasiḥnya,göŋ niŋ sambéga lāwan Asih umulahakĕñ citta ni-ṅwaŋ dadi wwaŋ*19:26:1755*

dèwī tā-trĕṣṇa tātaḥ t-ulih ari ri Umaḥ kapwa taṅhĕṙ tamolaḥ,Āmbĕktātyanta maṅliḥ tuwi kita maṅiḍam komalāpĕs sukunta,ṅwaŋ mapraŋ priṅga muṅgwī hĕlak-ĕlakan ikaŋ mrĕtyu mèwĕḥ Uripnya,méman hé dèwi hat-hat hayu nikanaṅ awak lyan wĕtĕṅtāri mèsi*19:27:1756*

lāwan tak mātya tāntĕn musuh ata pĕjaha byakta saŋ rāǥawālaḥ,Āpan nāŧanta śaktīŋ triƀuwana ya huwus ƀakti ya ṅké ri lĕṅkā,ndaḥ taṅhèṙ tāri tāsiḥ tak alaha t-arĕki swāmi mamwīta mĕtwa,nā liŋ saŋ wīra luṅhā ta sira mĕtu lawañ citta saṅhāra tan saḥ*19:28:1757*

glānékaŋ rākṣasāsiḥ tinaṅisan iṅ anak syūḥ manaḥnyālah āsiḥ,śīǥrān hĕmban ta yan kolĕn arĕki sakarĕŋ wèhakĕn té priyānya,dèwī-t hĕmban Anakta-t harih-arihĕn iṅūn haywa tan yatna ri ṙyya,byaktāk mātyèŋ raṇātaḥ kaḍasih ikaṅ anak nā panononananta*19:29:1758*

nā liŋ niŋ rākṣasojaṙ kadi ta ya ginitĕs twas nikaŋ strī kapūhan,tan pojaṙ tātan ambil ṅ-anak apan aṅĕliḥ luḥ tibā sāk ta siḥnya,graḥ sanđinyān pĕkul taŋ suku patakuraṅan manda māsrĕt taṅisnya,saŋ wīrātyanta māsiḥ dadi sira mamĕkul r-uṅgwakĕn yèŋ palaṅka*19:30:1759*

hé dèwī taryakĕŋ taŋ lara Apa tan ikā hétu ni ṅwaŋ mapaṅguḥ,tan kiṅkiŋ kāraṇāntāt anĕmu suka mĕné mwaŋ sukantèŋ paratra,Aṅhiŋ satyanta tékā ya ta lumĕpasakĕn riŋ kadi lwiṙta dèwī,yan tan satyékanaŋ strī niyata ya mapasaḥ mwaŋ tibā riŋ Awéci*19:31:1760*

maṅkā lwiṙ niŋ kadī māmi ya pinakapatik séwaké jöŋ naréndra,sojaṙ sājñā nirātaḥ ya ta ginawayakĕn dé nikaŋ ƀrĕtya nitya,yapwan tan maṅkanātaḥ niyata ta ya kĕlān riŋ kawaḥ riŋ dĕlāha,nāhan hètunya k-amwit ri kita makĕlatomĕtwa riŋ praŋ mamūka*19:32:1761*

sāmpun saŋ wīra mojaṙ majar-ajar irikaŋ strī lwiriŋ đaṙmmaśāstra,ménak tékā manaḥnyomari manaṅis anūt sojariŋ swāmi satya,makrīḍāsnéha sāmpun Umĕtu ta sira saŋ wīra mārin kamāran,mahyas tékaŋ wara strī dadi maṅadĕg akèn sragđarā yan panĕmbaḥ*19:33:1762*

{rajanī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
ri wĕtu nikaŋ prawīra bala rākṣasa matri humuŋ,dadi ta kinon madūma sira saŋ mapatiḥ mamatiḥ,prakaśita saŋ prahasta matuhātuha riŋ samara,sira ta Umuṅgu wétan ikanaŋ nagarān pagĕlar*19:34:1763*

{prĕŧwītala}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
ǥaṭodara sirodarèŋ raṇa patiḥ mahāpāṙśwa lèn,sirékana ta sāra rākṣaka kidul huwus saṅgraha,prawīra wara méǥanāda tinitaḥ sirāṅraṅkĕpi,sĕnadđa siran uṅgu kulwan agĕlaṙ siromuṅgu lor*19:35:1764*

{śiꝁariṇī}
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
wirūpākṣāpakṣākĕmita ri dalĕm niŋ pura sira,waraḥ tékā rowaŋ nira ya masukātuṅgwa wataṅan,t-aṅanti ṅké tuṅgwa t-wawa sahana niŋ Āyuđa kabèḥ,kabèhīkaŋ śatrun tĕka taya malaywan pinanahan*19:36:1765*

nahan liŋ saŋ mantrī ri bala nira śīǥrān tama ta ya,tayānuŋ tan saṅkèp sama-sama rĕgĕp śakti matahĕn,ta hĕntyan sakwèhtottama kita kabèḥ liŋnya maṅatag,Atag tékaŋ wadwā ya ta kakurutug rodra gumuruḥ*19:37:1766*

murub krođanyāgyā misanana Ikaŋ wānarabala,balātkāra krūrāṅgĕtĕm aṅikikan ƀīṣaṇa maṅaŋ,maṅārèmƀāmbĕknyāmĕjahana siraŋ rāmawijaya,jayātaḥ liŋnyāpan guragaḍa mahāmūṙkꝁa satata*19:38:1767*

tatan wruḥ yan ƀraṣṭā tuwi sakulagotranya hilaṅa,hilaŋ sandéhanyān pamulati gagak lèn Asu hasaŋ,Asaṅꝁyāpūṙwwékin tĕka muni humuŋ lwiṙnya magiraŋ,giraŋnyān mātyékaŋ kalajana watĕk rākṣasa kabèḥ*19:39:1768*

{prĕŧwītala}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
samāpta bala saŋ daśāsya humaḍaŋ kabèḥ sāyuđa,raǥūttama sirāṅrĕṅö dadi mulat sirèŋ lakṣmaṇa,widagđa sira saŋ Arin winulatan wawaŋ wruḥ sira,prayatna maṅadĕg ta sādara r-atag tikaŋ wré kabèḥ*19:40:1769*

Anuŋ pramuꝁa śaktimānta tinuhèŋ watĕk wānara*19:41:1770*
saṅ aṅgada suséna nīla nala jāmbawān māruti,sahasra hari mꜽnda ƀīmamuꝁa mattahaṣṭī gaja,gawākṣa winaténdrajāna śaraƀākya sampāti lén*19:42:1771*

lawan śatabalī đruwa drawiḍa đūmra tārapraƀa,śuƀodara karālawaktra kumuda pralambodara,wisaṅkaṭa putākṣi lèn wrĕṣaƀa krĕṣṇa siṅhānana,darīwadana ganđamādana đanuṙđarākrandana*19:43:1772*

nahan ta ya tuha n-nikaŋ kapibala prawīrèŋ raṇa,sadaṙppa ya masiṅhanāda paḍa gaṙjjitāhyā humuŋ,parĕŋ ya mamupak gunuŋ śiꝁara niŋ suwélācala,lawan kayu-kayunya yéka dinawutnya niśśéṣa ya*19:44:1773*

śilātala makas ya tīkṣṇa binabaknya tan pātya ya,ya téka pinakāyuđanya winawanya sāmpun mawit,sahaṙṣa siraṅ āṙyya rāǥawa tumon ya saṅkĕp kabèḥ,maṅaṙcꞓana siré ƀaṭāra śatarudra mamwīt sira*19:45:1774*

wwarāṣṭaśata maṅgalastawa gaway niraŋ kośala,padèḥ ri sira Ātmarākṣa ri sĕḍĕŋ nirāṙ wālaka,pawitra ya ta hétu niŋ jaya lawan kadiṙgǥāyusan,ya tékana Inunyakĕn nira samāpta maṅkat sira*19:46:1775*

Adĕg nira Amoǥa molah ikanaŋ lĕmaḥ kampita,hudan ruđira tūt hawañ jaya nimitta rakwékana,kidaŋ ya malayū kiwā nira hawanya kapwāhayu,lawan Uni nikaŋ manuk mrĕdu manoharāṅdé suka*19:47:1776*

tibā ri harĕpan nirādƀuta kĕtug nikaŋ handaru,lawan Asu hasaŋ masaṅꝁya manaṅis sumuṅsuŋ sira,Ikaŋ śuƀa Ataḥ tinon ira taŧāpi tan niścaya,swaƀāwa nira saŋ mamèt hayu Atéka göŋ saṅśaya*19:48:1777*

wiƀīṣaṇa wicakṣanèŋ Aji nimitta mojaṙ sira,naréndrasuta hé raǥūttama-taman hana-ŋ saṅśaya,Awās ya hilaṅa-ŋ musuḥ kita Ataḥ jayā riŋ raṇa,katona nikanaŋ nimitta ya dumèḥ ṅhulun niścaya*19:49:1778*

nahan n-ika wuwus nirātiśaya haṙṣa tāmbĕk haji,lawan sahana niŋ kapiprawara wīra kapwāgiraŋ,makin ya kalalaḥ makoliha Ikaŋ watĕk duṙjjana,ṇ-ḍĕṅö pamuji saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa rikaŋ nimittaṙ jaya*19:50:1779*

tĕkanya ri samīpa niŋ nagara déśa lĕṅkāpura,parĕŋ ta ya masiṅhanāda kadi siṅha rodrāgalak,matanya ya lumöŋ kukunya ya makas sihuŋnyāluṅid,kadi pwa yamakiṅkarāṅalapi jīwa niŋ rākṣasa*19:51:1780*

masö ya humarĕp kidul dadi madan madūm déśa ya,sĕsök sumarasaḥ sumāṙ kumuliliŋ ya kulwan kidul,wanöḥ hana ta muṅgu wétan ikanaŋ kaḍatwaṇ ḍĕḍĕt,Apūṙwwa kadi wāḥ plawaṅga gumuruḥ humuŋ ǥūṙṇnita*19:52:1781*

hĕnī ri tĕpi niŋ tasik syapa wĕnaŋ sumaṅꝁyā Ikā,ya tékana paḍā nikaŋ kapibalālah akwèḥ dahat,nda tan paligaran ya wuntu matitip matap loṙ kidul,kakūṣa kaliput kakaṇḍa kakasut sa-lĕṅkāpura*19:53:1782*

tatan papatĕṅaḥ tikaŋ tĕka Anéka ta pwaṇ ḍatĕŋ,lakunya tamatan pĕgat saka rikaŋ suwélācala,wanèḥ wahu sumĕṅka riŋ giri suwéla tan pāntara,katon ya makatap-katap hana sĕḍĕŋ Umĕntas wanèḥ*19:54:1783*

samaṅkana Ikaŋ hanèŋ giri mahèndra ta pwan laku,sahasraśata koṭi lakṣa niyutāṙwuda kwèḥ nikā,Aṅèl ya maṅadĕg humèrakĕn ikaŋ Umĕntas kabèḥ,maṅöb ta ya wijaḥ mamaṅkuk amiré maṅantuk wanèḥ*19:55:1784*

makin tĕka makin ya wāgyu gumĕtĕṙ ya kolāhala,matuṇḍuṅ atuguṙ mawū mawalikan sawètnyān sĕsök,kadi pwa bĕlaha-ŋ lĕmaḥ kadi ta guntura-ŋ paṙbwata,laṅit kadi ta rūga dé nikana śabda niŋ wānara*19:56:1785*

humöŋ ya humaḍaŋ mahöm rumĕbuta-ŋ watĕk rākṣasa,sawètnyan agalak taṅanya pinususnya kapwāṅgĕtĕm,wulunya madawā malit kapilawaṙṇna kumlab kabèḥ,kadi pwa ya tasik Apuy tĕka tumunwana-ŋ rākṣasa*19:57:1786*

Anéka ta Ulaḥnya tan duga-dugālah agyāpraṅa,manāmbay aṅadég umaṅswa maṅigĕl tumindak masö,maṅañjali wijaḥ wanèḥ maṅujiwat Alaḥ gaṙjjita,rarāhayu ya paŋhiḍĕpnya rikanaŋ musuḥ niṙƀaya*19:58:1787*

kinon ta ya maṅantya haywa rumuhun masö maŋlagé,Apan tuhu ya wīra rakwa mamalĕs huwusnyān kanin,Ikaŋ rumuhun amraṅ iŋ raṇa ya tékahĕn mađyama,tatan pinakamāṙgga dé nikana saŋ prawīrottama*19:59:1788*

kapīndra winaraḥ riṅ āgama winèḥ wruhèŋ loṙ kidul,tatan hana ta sambawanya matihékanaŋ śāsana,Apañ capala jāti mūḋa ya taŧāpi tan laṅǥana,praƀāwa nira saŋ raǥūttama wĕnaŋ śumikṣāŋ sarāt*19:60:1789*

patiḥ ta sahananya tan hana wihaŋ ri Ajñā nira,kapīndra magiraŋ sahaṙṣa Inĕnĕb tĕḍuḥ niścaya,maṅanti ya humèrakĕn nikana sāṅswa niŋ rākṣasa,taŧāpi kalalaḥ manaḥnya panagiḥ nikaŋ kawrayan*19:61:1790*

daśānana sirénajaṙ tĕka maṅĕmbuli-ŋ wānara,makin ta kumĕtĕṙ manaḥ nira nirāśrayāśātakut,nda tan prakaṭa yan kĕnèŋ ƀaya sajāti ni-ṅwaŋ praƀu,ginopita Asiŋ kaduḥkan i-manaḥnya tātan katon*19:62:1791*

madĕg ta sira śīǥra yaṙ wĕtu ri hiŋ maniñjo sira,mulat ta sira ri pradéśa nikanaŋ kaḍatwan kabèḥ,nda tan hana tĕgal tatan hana ṅ-alas lĕbak tan katon,Apan kasaputan ya pūṙṇna Ibĕkan kabèḥ wānara*19:63:1792*

Ikaŋ ƀaya ya koƀayan mulat i-kīṙṇna niŋ wānara,tatan patĕpi yan katon kadi tasik sĕḍĕŋ ǥūṙṇnita,lawan gunuṅ anak ya téka pinupaknya yāṅkĕn karaŋ,juraŋ kariwutan hiḍĕp nira rikaŋ purān kāmbulan*19:64:1793*

tatan hana Upāya yār aṅĕn-aṅĕn ya tan pélagan,madĕg taṅ aƀimāna jāti karatun Ahĕṅkāra ya,makon ta sira maṅswa riŋ bala mamūka riŋ papraṅan,Apan punagi saŋ huwus manĕmu rājya muktyèŋ raṇa*19:65:1794*

balèđika watĕk prawīra maṅasö ri saŋ Indrajit,ya pūṙwwaka kinon umaṅswa hinamĕs ya śūrèŋ raṇa,masö ya humarĕp ta loṙ paḍa ta kapwa saṅkĕp kabèḥ,kinaṇḍa tinatā tinap ya tinitaḥ dinūmdūm kabèḥ*19:66:1795*

Anuŋ pramuꝁa riŋ tĕgal raŧa paḍāti lèn tuṅgaṅan,magaṇḍi mapanaḥ ya tékana kinon Umuṅgwèŋ sukĕt,liman pramuꝁa riŋ rĕnĕk mapakĕnèŋ lwah alwādalèm,watèk makawacātisāra rikanaŋ juraŋ riŋ gunuŋ*19:67:1796*

Ikaŋ Umĕtu riŋ tĕgal paḍa madan ya mabyūha ya,padāti ri tĕṅaḥ kabèḥ panaliṅa-ŋ watĕk tuṅgaṅan,ri puṅkuran ikaŋ padāti matatā-ŋ raŧāṅrākṣa ya,ṅaranya makarānana pratita muꝁya niŋ byūha ya*19:68:1797*

watĕk makuda nā dinānan atatā ya muṅgwī tĕṅaḥ,Ikaŋ bala padāti yāta humapit ya kapwātatā,tumūt ta Ikanaŋ watĕk raŧa limāṅ atus rākṣakā,ṅaranya ya ta bajra pañjara jayèŋ musuḥ duṙjjana*19:69:1798*

padāti ya winöḥ kahundula lakunya muṅgwiŋ tĕṅaḥ,watĕk makuda paŋhapit nda tan asö dahat tan madoḥ*19:70:1799*
Ikaŋ raŧa ya rākṣakèŋ kuda nahan ya sūcīmuꝁa,praśāsta ya daṅū wĕnaŋ malahakĕn sa-prĕŧwītala*19:71:1800*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
nāhan byūha nikaŋ balāđika madan madwandwa tandwān asö,hūmrĕŋ siṅha jugèŋ galak katatakut kālāntakāṅiṇḍarāt,mawyaŋ mèkĕl ikā wulunya makusut sākṣāt dilaḥ niṅhapuy,malwābāŋ mawĕlö matanya mawĕlū wā tulya yan löŋ lanā*19:72:1801*

molaḥ tānak-anaknya cañcala kilat tulyanya rodrān wulat,méǥèŋ rĕŋrĕṅ ataḥ paḍanyan ahirĕŋ woknyākusut yāsukĕt,séṇḍuŋ ƀīṣaṇa bāyubajra sadrĕśoswāsanya humyus mĕsĕs,mākrak matri masiṅhanāda kumisik śabdanya yāṅkĕn gĕlap*19:73:1802*

sāmpun matri makin masö ya mawĕrö śīǥrān maraṅkĕp kabèḥ,mamraŋ riŋ krĕtalāṅaruk ya mamulus maṅduk mañakrānuhuk,maŋḍaṇḍāmupuh iŋ gadā ya maṅalā maṅduk rikaŋ lāṅgala,saglisnyān panĕwĕk rikaŋ curiga lèn maŋlori riŋ lori ya*19:74:1803*

sāra-ŋ sāraŧa wīra đīra mamutĕṙ ḍaṇḍé taṅanyé kiwān,pāśomuṅgu rikaŋ taṅanya ri tĕṅĕn śīǥrān habĕt taŋ kuda,lumpat niŋ kuda tandwa tan dadi wuruŋ moliḥ kabèḥ maŋdĕmak,lāwan saŋ hana riŋ raŧāŋlĕpasakĕn kontāṅĕné pyaḥ paraḥ*19:75:1804*

yatna-ŋ wīra watĕk manuṅgaṅ umasö sāṅsönya tan wyaṙŧa ya,kapwa wruḥ rikanaŋ musuḥ mati lawan tan mātya tan swaŋ masö,sèp taŋ wwaŋ Umulat riyān tĕka wawaŋ n-ton wré kahundul manūb,tulyanyālap-alap gĕlap juga ya riŋ śīǥrāṅalāṅhīrakĕn*19:76:1805*

lèn wīrākawaca pracaṇḍa magalak sāmbĕknya tan paṅgalĕŋ,gumrut krođa hatinya lèn kumĕrĕkĕt lambénya dényānahut,kapwāmöki manūb mamūk ya manuruŋ kombak tikaŋ wré kabèḥ,ma-ṙyyak-ṙyyak maparĕk rikaŋ kali juraŋ makwèḥ kakuṙcyat kapök*19:77:1806*

krođékaŋ balawānarān kapipitan rowaŋnya śīǥrān walĕs,māmrĕp māmrĕkĕsĕt manampyal anahut kapwāmubat riŋ Ikū,waṅkiŋ-waṅkiṅ ikaŋ musuḥ ya tinaṅan karwanya pik yāmpisit,śīǥrénantĕpakĕn ta yān upat-apit bāhunya rĕmpak rĕmuk*19:78:1807*

lèn taŋ wré manĕwĕk rikaŋ kuku makas kāścaṙyya dènyānĕwĕk,pyaḥ niŋ rākṣasa ya trusan ri walakaŋ sāmbut ta buñcit nikā,tunduk tiṅhal ikaŋ wanèḥ dadi tibā kāṅgĕk kalĕṅgak kalaḥ,rāḥ muñcaṙ I-tutuknya śīṙṇna pinugut mūṙcꞓān linūd riŋ watu*19:79:1808*

lāwan wānara śaktimānta ya Ikā muñcaŋ kudāsiŋ masö,jambākĕn ta ya riŋ śilātala makas tīkṣṇogra bajropama,rĕmpū syūḥ pipi niŋ kudādƀuta mĕsat miṅsil matanyān sirat,mwaŋ tĕṅgĕknya tikĕl hatinya ya rurū rāḥ rodra rīruŋ mulĕk*19:80:1809*

krora-ŋ wré mamuliṙ gulū Agul-agul Andul ya munduṙ mĕsat,śūra-ŋ rākṣasa yan n-asö mamurugul tĕṇḍasnya sāmpun hilaŋ,mūṙ taŋ wré maṅidīdi mèdin inusī dé niŋ kawaṇḍāgalak,luṅhā yan purugul rikaŋ kali kalaḥ tan wruḥ tibā riŋ juraŋ*19:81:1810*

wré wīrādƀuta maŋdudut suku saké śaktinya tan kabwatan,hiṙ tékaŋ bala rākṣasèŋ watu riḍaŋ kāsaḥ ḍaḍanyānanā,wré moṅsil prakrĕtinya tulya ya raray kapwāmanèk yārĕbut,tuṅgaŋ té walakaŋ nikaŋ kala hiniṙ-niṙ wismayāhyā humuŋ*19:82:1811*

lèn taŋ wānara maŋlayaŋ ya sumuyug sāmbut taṅan niŋ musuḥ,yékā krora tĕmĕn taman wruh iṅ asiḥ n-iṇḍit tikaŋ rākṣasa,saṅsārān sinaranta śīṙṇna ya rujit Āwaknya tan lwiṙ Awak,dé niŋ wānara riŋ naƀastala sĕsök sakrođa kapwānahut*19:83:1812*

sākṣāt siṅha Ikaŋ kapīndra mamĕrĕp tékā taṅanyānĕpak,rāḥ wuṅkal tumapĕl rikaŋ karatalāṅrĕṅgut tĕpak taŋ muꝁa,mūṙkꝁāmūk mamĕkul gumanti manahut héwān tinampyal malĕs,pinriḥ pīnrĕp iruŋnya pik Inuwahan huntunya rĕmpak pupak*19:84:1813*

lāwan rākṣasawīra mapraṅ iṅ alas Atyanta riŋ ƀīṣaṇa,gaṇḍéwanya magöŋ satal satakuraŋ taṅgwanya sawwaḥ magöŋ,lèn lwā niŋ warayaŋ muꝁanya sadĕpā pūṙwwanya laṇḍĕp mĕṅĕs,yékānuŋ pamanaḥnya tulya ya sihuŋ niŋ kāla sākṣāt katon*19:85:1814*

glāna-ŋ wré pinanaḥ parĕŋ kaparapal sĕmpal cĕṅĕlnyèŋ lĕmaḥ,lèn tékaŋ kĕna saṇḍaṅanya rikanaŋ saṇḍaŋ sinuṇḍaŋ Umūr,kwèḥ taŋ wré sipi tékanaŋ Ibab-ibab lambuŋnya tambis pĕgat,mĕṅgaḥ ta pwa maṅĕntak-ĕntak inusuŋ saṅsāra sārèŋ lara*19:86:1815*

lèn taŋ wwil mamanaḥ rikaŋ taji tajĕm tujwanya kapwāṅĕnè,mwaŋ nārāca panaḥnya sök kakĕrĕcĕk kāntĕp Ikaŋ wré kĕna,tīkṣṇa-ŋ hrū hitu waṅkiṅ alwat atĕguḥ rodrāṅgaluṅgaŋ ri tūr,rĕmpak syūḥ ta Igā nikaŋ kĕna muṭu kwèḥ puḥ pupūnyān paraḥ*19:87:1816*

maṅkin duṙbbala tékanaŋ kapibalā glānānanākwèḥ kĕna,māṙ maṅkĕp kanin iŋ kĕnĕŋ tĕtĕk urat hototnya sāmpun pĕgat,mūṙcꞓā mūṙ sawanöḥ mĕsat ya sinawat wètnyān paraḥ kwèḥ tibā,mosaḥ mosik asāk tinūt ya malayū munduṙ tinūtan panaḥ*19:88:1817*

tat kālān kasuruŋ katūb ya kasĕsĕṙ soṙ śīṙṇna taŋ wānara,kombak kāmbah akik Ikaŋ wray aḍĕmit kāntĕp katuṇḍuŋ wanèḥ,mahyā-ŋ rākṣasa riŋ Alas ya mamalĕs gut-gūtĕn aṅhruk humöŋ,moŋ tulyanya manon kidaŋ ya maṅusī maswī ya moliḥ hulu*19:89:1818*

śaŋ sugrīwa tumon ikaŋ kapi katūb mojaṙ siré saŋ nala,Āy-āy saŋ nala haywa hīna yan alaḥ rowaŋta kon mamriha,saŋ nīlānilaputra haywa humĕnĕŋ protsāhana-ŋ wré kabèḥ,Āpan tan palayū swaƀāwa nira saŋ śāṙddūlawikrīḍita*19:90:1819*

{kusumawicitra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
Aŧa ri huwus saŋ kapiwararāja,mujar i-siraŋ māruti nala nīla,dadi Umasö saŋ tiga paḍa đīra,lumaki-lakī wānarabala maṅsö*19:91:1820*

mpu laki kitaŋ wānarabala wīra,kita karĕṅö đīratara rikèŋ rāt,Ikana yaśaṅtātiśaya ya śudđa,pinahagĕlĕḥta pwa ya lalu héman*19:92:1821*

bali winaraḥ riŋ Aji kita pūṙwwa,pinacaritākĕn ta kita śinikṣā,Apa ta paran Iŋ wĕdi-wĕdi liŋta,Apa Ulihan saŋ laki-laki riŋ praŋ*19:93:1822*

Aparan ikaŋ praŋ karika hiḍĕpta,takarin ikèŋ swaṙgga wahu kapaṅguḥ,Ikana kaśūran ta ya pamĕnĕṙnya,yaśa kalawan mokṣa ya ta ꝑalanya*19:94:1823*

Ikana kunaŋ yaṙ wĕdi-wĕdi rakwa,niyata Ikaŋ pāpa tumuwuha ṅké,Ika hariṅĕt ta drawa ya mĕnö ya,naraka lawan duṙyyaśa ꝑala ƀuktin*19:95:1824*

kalawan iké yogya ya gawayĕnta,prakrĕti tinūtan mamuhara sidđi,yadin agĕlĕḥ riŋ prakrĕti gawénta,naraka lawan duṙyyaśa kita riŋ rāt*19:96:1825*

Apa pakĕnantāt pinakahulun kwèḥ,ya tan ikanājñā nrĕpati kasidđā,Apan ikihĕn samƀawa gawayĕnta,pituhu pakon saŋ praƀu gawayĕnta*19:97:1826*

mati kita tan wyaṙŧa yaśa tĕmunta,ṅuni-ṅuni yan sorakĕna musuḥta,niyata kiténastuti nikanaŋ rāt,yaśa suka lèn wiṣṇupada kapaṅguḥ*19:98:1827*

wiku sira satyèŋ Aji japa pūjā,ratu sira śūrāpaḍa sira riŋ rāt,masawaha saŋ wꜽśya baṇijakaṙmmā,kita pi pakon saŋ praƀu gawayĕnta*19:99:1828*

bala ya mataŋnyāmriha sahananta,pulihi pakoliḥ nikana musuḥta,hana kari mèwĕḥ ri sira saṅ amriḥ,Asiṅ ata sāđyā niyata kasidđā*19:100:1829*

jalaniđi lāwan gagana tan alwā,Alas asukĕt ƀīṣaṇa tuwi māwā,śikara nikaŋ méru tuwi mahāṇḍap,ri hati saṅ utsāha saṅ aƀimāna*19:101:1830*

masuka ri pātāla nitala dadya,Aŧa ca guhā pomahan ikanaŋ moŋ,kumĕlĕma riŋ rorawa baḍawāgni,Ikana kabèḥ tan mawĕdi saṅ amriḥ*19:102:1831*

kimuta Ikaŋ rākṣasabala wāḥ ya,pisani pusus saṅhara ya kabèhi,ꝑala ni kaśūranta tuwi ya dadya,mati mamĕnaŋ riŋ raṇapada mokṣa*19:103:1832*

nahan ikanojaṙ saṅ anilaputra,nala kalawan nīla milu mataṅguḥ,dadi mapuliḥ wānara sahananya,prakrĕti niraŋ wīra n-inuđahanya*19:104:1833*

rasa-rasa niŋ lālana rinasanya,kadi hinĕnö riŋ Amrĕta hatinya,Ikana kaśūranya makin atāmbĕḥ,kadi ta sinapwan Ikana takutnya*19:105:1834*

maluy aṅalap Āyuđa sahananya,hana mamupak paṙbwata ya sadaṙppa,kayu-kayu māwān ya ta dinawutnya,makakarasak taŋ kusumawicitra*19:106:1835*

{śiꝁariṇī}
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
huwus saṅkĕp kapwātiraƀasa masö wānarabala,tumindak maṅduk riŋ kayu-kayu lawan tal hana hano,hanān paṅduk riŋnyū ya ta pinakalorinya sawanèḥ,mamaṇḍĕm maŋḍaṇḍāmarupuhi hanānampuhi gunuŋ*19:107:1836*

gĕlānèkaŋ mūṙkꝁāmanahi hinabĕt hrūnya sinawat,wawaŋ konduṙ kèdĕṙ tinuju kĕna bāhunya ya dinuk,hanāmĕṇṭaŋ laṅkap ya wahu tumihaŋ hrūnya sinikĕp,rĕmĕk rĕñcĕm cūṙṇnān pinalu winalātkāra pinupuḥ*19:108:1837*

kalĕṅgak lèn kāntĕp karĕpa kahiriŋ kwèḥ kasuririŋ,kariṅkèl tan polaḥ kapati kapisan-sanđi wipayoḥ,hanāṅohan mohān pinalu ya parĕŋ rwāṙdđa ya sipī,linūdan dé niŋ wré winatu mĕtu totĕknya sumirat*19:109:1838*

hanāmūk momo moŋ juga yadiya tan mātya yan asö,Alaḥ héwāmbĕknyān sinikĕp amĕkul mamrih anahut,kapīndrādrĕs molaḥ humaluyamĕluk maŋdĕha gulū,jalākĕn taŋ mūṙkꝁèŋ watu katutu tĕṇḍasnya kasĕsĕḥ*19:110:1839*

hanāṅduk riŋ laṅkap hana manĕwĕk iŋ hrū Inupasan,sahīṅan niŋ drĕsnyān pamalu ri larasnyālah agalak,suđīra-ŋ wré śīǥrān rĕbuti ta Ikaŋ rākṣasalaras,tibā mūṙcꞓā muṙkkān winalĕsan i-laṅkapnya kapisan*19:111:1840*

makin makwèḥ lwaŋnyān sinikĕp ananānékana kanin,nda tañjriḥ kapwāmriḥ mamulihi mahöm moliha musuḥ,marin wĕṇṭaŋ laṅkapnya dadi mamĕniŋ kadga paraśu,manāmbut kontārug krĕtala kalawan lāṅgala kalā*19:112:1841*

masö manraŋ mamraŋ manuruṅ aṅusī yāṅutitakĕn,nda tan kagyat taŋ wray tuwi ya manuruŋ sāra sinuruŋ,malĕs māmrĕp krorān panahut anuhuk riŋ kuku makas,ginaṇḍyaglis taŋ wré ginala kinalā glāna kaguliŋ*19:113:1842*

tumandaŋ tékaŋ rākṣasa humalu riŋ wré kĕna kalā,sinuŋsuŋ riŋ śūlā n-rinug inuwahan pyaḥnya tinujaḥ,wanèḥ kontal kāntĕp tinuju rikanaŋ konta katibā,widagđékaŋ wré wruḥ mamalu mamalĕs tan kawalĕsan*19:114:1843*

makin sakrođāŋ rākṣasabala lawan wānarabala,tinūb yānūb moliḥ hana ta pinakoliḥnyan apuliḥ,marok wré wwil rodran kadi ta ya hari wyāǥra magalak,kađīranyātyantādƀuta kadi tĕguḥ niŋ śikariṇī*19:115:1844*

{jalodđatagati}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
samaṅkana Ikaŋ liman kinawacan,gaḍiŋnyan atitīkṣṇa malyus aluṅid,sadaṙppa ya maśabda matta magalak,Apūṙwwa kadi diggajéndra juga ya*19:116:1845*

yatéka malagé rĕṇĕk ya matĕgĕl,tĕgal tuwi ya papraṅanya sawanèḥ,wanèḥ malaga riŋ juraŋ lawan alas,Alas sĕsĕk anéka tan ginaṇita*19:117:1846*

nanāsiṅ inasönya lāgi lĕkasan,kasanmata ya śakti kapwa ya masö,masö ta Ikanaŋ kapīndra sumahab,mahöm ya paḍa mahyunolih aliman*19:118:1847*

manāmbutakĕn ugraḍaṇḍa ya sakol,manaṅhara parĕŋ ya kapwa mamalu,manambiriṅakĕn śilātala wanèḥ,manĕmpuhi gunuŋ Ikaŋ wray umibĕr*19:119:1848*

Anuŋ wray atiśakti yékana manèk,Anuṅgaṅi paḍāṅadĕg ri walakaŋ,Anuṅkak atisāhasāṅdĕdĕl igā,Anuṅgali hanāṅdĕdĕl hulu gulū*19:120:1849*

wanöḥ wwara tĕkāmutĕṙ palu-palu,pupuḥ ta tulalay nikaŋ liman agöŋ,gaḍiŋnya kinayuḥnya kapwa ya pupak,tujaḥ tuju matanya tan pabiṣa ya*19:121:1850*

gĕlāna Ikanaŋ liman ginurumuŋ,winūk ya rinĕbut ḍinaṇḍa dinĕdĕl,masāk ta kawacanya cūṙṇna ya tĕñuḥ,praƀāwa nikanaŋ wrayadƀuta dahat*19:122:1851*

samaṅkana Igā nikaŋ gaja tikĕl,Uḍul ta ḍalĕmanya rāḥnya malĕbĕk,tibī katubab iŋ tĕbĕŋ ya kabubat,maṅohan umĕhāḥ ya mohita pĕjaḥ*19:123:1852*

wanèḥ hana winèḥ lumāha makakaŋ,wĕhaŋnya kalawan gulūnya tinĕhak,dinuk ya dinugaŋ ḍaḍanya dinĕdĕl,sukunya pinuliṙ pĕgat ta ya kapāt*19:124:1853*

lawan hana sĕbit silitnya dinuwĕl,wawaŋ kasuluyuŋ tibā kasidĕkuŋ,gulūnya kapĕluk Awaknya makukuŋ,gaḍiŋnyan aputiḥ tikĕl kadi bakuŋ*19:125:1854*

Asiŋ gaja masö pĕjaḥ ya kapisan,nda tan kṣaya Anéka yātitih atap,lawan hana ta mapraṅ iŋ lwah adalĕm,gajéndra tahu riŋ jalodđatagati*19:126:1855*

{Aśwalalita}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :23:
Aŧa ri sĕḍĕŋ nikaŋ bala parĕŋ mataṅkĕp atuguṙ ndatan hana surud,saraƀasa niṙƀayékana manaḥnya mo mati hiḍĕpnya tār alaṅ-alaŋ,paḍa ta nanānya śīṙṇna ya winūk mamūk mamurugul malĕs winalĕsan,hana kapisan hanan sipi pĕjaḥ ya mānaṅ-anaṅan maṅohan umĕkĕḥ*19:127:1856*

mata Umalik Ilatnya ya malā Ususnya ya mulū ta rāḥnya mĕlĕbĕk,ruđira sumök rikaŋ muꝁa rĕmĕk-rĕmuk ya pinĕrĕp pipinya kapalu,kapulir ikā gulūnya kumĕtĕṙ taṅanya kumĕdut sukunya kumĕdal,ḍaḍa ya ḍaḍal ḍinaṇḍa ḍinuḍuk ḍuhak ya tinuhuk buhak ya tinuhuk*19:128:1857*

jariji rujit nanā ya sinahut nikaŋ plawaga nārasiṅha juga ya,susu ya sasat-sayat ya śata śīṙṇna taŋ kulit alit ya tan patĕmahan,walakaṅ ikaŋ karaṅkaṅ inidĕk tĕṅaḥnya dinĕdĕl tikĕl ya kakayaŋ,makabulacak cacal kaparacal ta tūṙnya karagöt rikaŋ kuku makas*19:129:1858*

hana hinabĕt ya hīna ya hinosakĕn Inabalaŋ tibā ya kahalaŋ,kahala kalaṅkahan pinulihan taman padalihan Umūṙ ya mawĕṅis,hana muriṅis maṅas-maṅasulāsa līṅa riya yan mawĕdya pĕjaha,wahu maṅadĕg masö malĕsa liŋnya sèp rinuhunan sinaṅhara winūk*19:130:1859*

maparaśu śūra sāra ya surākṣa-rākṣasa wiśéṣa-śéṣa ya biṣa,baśa-baśa sāhasānĕba sawāta dénya maṅawasŧa wānara rĕbaḥ,saka sapuluḥ rikaŋ kṣaṇa pĕgat gulūnya pinugut cĕṅĕlnya gumuluŋ,makaparupuḥ mawantah apagut Apan satata yan tibā kabarubuḥ*19:131:1860*

makin atitip tikaŋ śawa sawaŋ-sawaŋnya sawanèḥ t-ajaṙ sakawĕnaŋ,śata-śata lakṣa koṭi niyutāṙwuda prayuta koṭi-koṭyaniyuta,patĕmu ni rāḥ nikaŋ mati samaṅkanādƀuta dalĕmnya hīṅan i-ḍaḍa,gaja raŧa lèn padāti matunaḥ gĕlāna kapĕtĕk taṅ aśwalalita*19:132:1861*

{rajanī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
Atiśaya ƀīṣaṇāŋ samaraƀūmi mabāŋ ya kabèḥ,Ahalĕpa maṅkanāŋ talaga saŋ yama yan panurun,ruđira ya ta wwayanya malĕtuḥ mahaṅī mahariŋ,đwaja mahirĕŋ mabāŋ hana putiḥ kaharan wĕrĕha*19:133:1862*

cĕṅĕl ikanaŋ prawīra pinugut Umulat mĕlĕlö,ya ta tumalaḥ kumambĕṅ i-tĕṅaḥ kadi padma mĕkar,madarawayan Ususnya mawilĕt ya ta tulya sulur,Atiśaya śudđa yan talaga tulya nikaŋ palagan*19:134:1863*

#wiṅśati saṙggaḥ#
<citrālaya>:20
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
^20/1/1847.
kadi guntur ikaŋ ruđira ya humilī,rikanaŋ giri gahwara kali madalĕm,kahilī śawa niŋ gaja turaga pĕjaḥ,gumulumpuṅ apūṙwwa kadi watu magöŋ*20:1:1864*

Atiǥora hilīnya satata gumuruḥ,tuwi miśra lawan wuduk utĕk awĕrĕḥ,ya dumèḥ ya makin katatakuta tĕmĕn,kadi wꜽtaraṇī juga sakala katon*20:2:1865*

gaṇa ƀūta piśāca maṅigĕl agĕlar,rikanaŋ raṇaƀūmi mamaṅan aṅinum,mawĕrö ya warĕg ruđira paḍa humuŋ,kadi siṅha muꝁanya ya kagiri-giri*20:3:1866*

{mānawakakrīḍita}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :8:

wīra kabèḥ tībra maṅèl,wètnyan asowé n-papupuḥ,kapwa ta munduṙ mapasaḥ,rākṣasa mĕṅgaḥ ya mĕhāḥ*20:5:1868*

maṅkana taŋ wānara wèḥ,māṙ ya mararyan maṅĕliḥ,kapwa mapèpèṙ hariṅĕt,mānawakākrīdita ya*20:6:1869*

{śālinī}

munduṙ pwékaŋ wīra saṅkā ri ṅèlnya,kapwomaṅsö saŋ balānuŋ prađāna,Utsāhèŋ praŋ saŋ prajaṅǥa prawīra,śaktyaƀyāsèŋ pādayudđātiwrĕdđi*20:7:1870*

kadyaṅgā niŋ bajra yākas malaṇḍĕp,tadwat maṅkā taŋ wĕtis bajra sākṣāt,sāk śīṙṇna syūḥ taŋ musuḥ yan dĕdĕl ya,prastāwanyā ꝁyāti māran prajaṅǥa*20:8:1871*

malwākandĕl pāwakan göŋ manĕṅgö,malwat mokĕt mo tibā mo kasuṅsaŋ,tan swaŋ tan sor iŋ galak wyāǥra māwak,twas-twas tus-tus his nikaŋ wīragotra*20:9:1872*

maṅsö taŋ wré wīra sampāti nāma,sāmpun sampat riŋ yaśātyanta śūra,wīrān wīṙyyan wruḥ ta yèŋ śatru śakti,māsrĕŋ mèntĕṙ māntĕb āmbĕk nirèŋ praŋ*20:10:1873*

maṅsö saŋ sampāti pātrān tinonton,r-uṇḍoṇḍékaŋ ḍaṇḍa göŋnyāpraméya,munduṙ muṅkuṙ tékanaŋ pātra tindak,līlālīlā lola laṅgūla molaḥ*20:11:1874*

śīǥrāraṅkĕp kapwa tonan widagđa,yatnāṅintay cidra tātan kacidra,saŋ sampātyutpāta lumpat nirādrĕs,yan mèḥ prāptā-ŋ pāda niŋ wwil prajaṅǥa*20:12:1875*

maṅkā tékā saŋ prajaṅǥa prayatna,yan mèḥ prāptā-ŋ ḍaṇḍa mamriḥ lumumpat,mosyan maswī kapwa tāmèti cidra,wèt niŋ tonan tan hanātaḥ kacidra*20:13:1876*

saṅké sowé soṙ titiḥ saŋ prajaṅǥa,mèḥ maŋdūkèŋ pāda kāntĕp ḍinaṇḍa,kontal tĕṇḍasnyan linūdan katimpal,muñcaṙ taŋ rāḥ mwaŋ Ikaŋ jīwa luṅhā*20:14:1877*

{bramitākṣara}

sumirat ta tèja ni matanya mabāŋ*20:16:1879*

sꝑutadākṣi yéka sinikĕp nira ya,tinĕpak muꝁanya ya pĕjaḥ kapisan,Inusī niraŋ pratapanākṣi mĕsat,sinikĕp sukunya kawĕnaŋ wĕkasan*20:19:1882*

{sragđara}

tat kālanyān pĕjaḥ rākṣasabala-balawān wīra wānīŋ raṇāṅga,Ambĕknyāyudđa tātan Alaṅ-alaṅ atulaŋ tan wĕnaŋ mātya riŋ praŋ,cihnanyān śūra ṅ-āmbĕk tuhu-tuhu manulus tan Alaŋ tan kalĕṅka,méṅguŋ taŋ swaṙgga muṅkab babahan ika mĕṅā rakwa dé saŋ prawīra*20:21:1884*

mosik sakwèḥ nikaŋ kinnaragaṇa kalawan kinnarī kapwa haṙṣa,lāwan widyāđarī bāp paḍa madulu-duluṙ mwaŋ ta widyāđara kwèḥ,kapwānuŋsuŋ sukāmbĕknya mamawa panamuy ƀoga pañcopacāra,Āpan yékī ta ācāra nira ta hana riŋ swaṙgga nāhan byawaṣṭā*20:22:1885*

mahyun tāmbĕk niraŋ déwagaṇa rĕṣigaṇèṅ antarikṣān panonton,kapwārampak humuŋ riŋ gagaṇatala sĕsök tan katon antarikṣa,haṙṣāmbĕk saŋ mahāṙṣi priyaraṇa sira saŋ nāradānuŋ panĕṇḍas,sokyātūt tuṣṭi saŋ tumburu milu ta siraŋ gotamātyanta mahyun*20:23:1886*

Atyantèŋ ǥora yāǥūṙṇnita palaga nikaŋ rākṣasa mwaŋ Ikaŋ wré,kahyun-hyun yan tinonton paḍa-paḍa magalak tan masor iŋ kaśūran,saṅké wīranya đīranya malaga mapupuḥ kapwa tāsiṅhanāda,śabdanyātīta riŋ ƀīṣaṇa kagiri-giri n-pūrakèŋ dig widéśa*20:24:1887*

maṅsö saŋ jambumālī mamulihi ya mahāśūra tan dadya mundur,saṇḍaŋ wèt kwèḥ butinyān lagi malaga gahan riŋ galak tā paḍanya,kadganyātyanta tīkṣṇa n-parupuhi ta Ikaŋ wré dinuknyĕŋ krĕtāla,yāṅsö saŋ bāyuputrān pisani ya katibā yan tibèŋ paṙbwatāgöŋ*20:25:1888*

raǥūttama kapīndra lakṣmaṇa mulat ri saŋ Aṅgada,maṅastuti manāđukāra ciha bāliputrottama,wiƀīṣaṇa miṅis sawismaya sahaṙṣa tuṣṭān wulat,humuŋ ya matalaṅkup atri Ikanaŋ watĕk wānara*20:37:1900*

samaṅkana rikaŋ naƀastala humuŋ watĕk déwatā,tumon sira saṅ indrajit katĕk apan paḍāṅadwakĕn,wiǥūṙṇnita Ikaŋ laṅit saƀaya taŋ watĕk rākṣasa,kucĕm muꝁa saṅ indrajit dadi muliḥ Alaḥ kéraṅan*20:38:1901*

{Aparawaktra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:

ya Ikana ta hilaŋ mĕné ṙ-hiḍĕp,yaśa nira śīṙṇna ri śīṙṇna niŋ raŧa,pati ni kuda nirāṙ kadi pwa sor,ya Ikana hétu nikā Iraŋ nira*20:40:1903*

Aŧa huwus umuliḥ saṅ indrajit,taya ta surākṣa nikaŋ balāđika,raǥusuta tahu riŋ musuḥ pĕjaḥ,panahi ta yèŋ śarawaṙṣa tīkṣṇa ya*20:41:1904*

kadi Atĕp atitip panaḥ nira,gagana pĕtĕŋ ya pĕpĕt taman katon,Anarawata tibānya yāṅĕné,dadi mananā balawīrarākṣasa*20:42:1905*

hana kĕna warayaŋ pĕgat pisan,kadi ta cinakra ḍaḍanya tan salaḥ,hana ta katuluyan parĕŋ pĕgat,kadi binabad ya parĕŋ pĕjaḥ kabèḥ*20:43:1906*

tatan ujarĕn ikaŋ kĕné taji,mati kapisan kĕna maṙmma tan sipi,laru-laru tumibā rikaŋ Apuy,ya paṅupaméka patinya sakṣaṇa*20:44:1907*

tuwi satata tibā nikaŋ panaḥ,kadi sinĕsĕb śataśīṙṇna taŋ śawa,hana ya hinibĕkan tutuknya sök,Ikana tutuknya kadi pwa taṅkulak*20:45:1908*

hana ta lagi kĕnānanā dahat,tumuluyataḥ Ikanaŋ panaḥ riya,sana-sini ya kanin ruwĕd rujit,raga-raga tulya Awaknya śīṙṇna ya*20:46:1909*

sahana-hana nikaŋ balāsura,ya tika mamūk tamatan paśéṣa ya,hana ta wĕdi-wĕdīŋ raṇāṅgaṇa,mamana-manā para cakra yālayū*20:47:1910*

{rajanī}
