taya kasalaḥ rikaŋ bala kabèḥ śata wikṣata ya,makatiritis ta rāḥnyan inusī ya gĕlāna mĕhāḥ,puyu-puyuhĕn gĕyuḥ ya maṅĕliḥ sawanèḥ katibā,Inamah-amaḥ pinatryakĕn ikaŋ bala wānara ya*20:49:1912*

Aŧa mapasaḥ samāpta sahananya taman papuliḥ,paḍa ta mĕgil rikaŋ kuṭa Atīta lalu-ŋ diwasa,dadi sumurup ƀaṭāra rawi śīǥra kadi pwa humöt,Alah alĕmöḥ tumona Ikanaŋ bala yan palayū*20:50:1913*

{ƀujaṅgaprayāta}
⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
surup saŋ hyaṅ āditya luṅhā sirosĕn,makin manda-mandékanaŋ téja māwā,tĕka-ŋ kāla sanđyā mabāŋ téja kulwan,kadi lwiṙ nikaŋ papraṅan dé nikaŋ rāḥ*20:51:1914*

nda tītékanaŋ kāla sanđyā ta luṅhā,pĕtĕŋ taŋ jagat loṙ kidul tan patonan,kadi pwānapiḥ lwiṙ nikaŋ Anđakāra,rasanyānta riŋ wīra mapraŋ ta dénya*20:52:1915*

rikaŋ kāla sakrođa taŋ méǥanāda,masĕṅhit pĕjaḥ tuṅgaṅan mwaŋ raŧāsāk,masuk tèŋ padéwāharan ṅkān pasāđya,mamūjā ta yèṅ astra saṙppāstrapāśa*20:53:1916*

huwusnyān pamūjā rikaŋ nāgapāśa,pasaŋ tékanaŋ yoga māyān Adrĕśya,malit tékanāwaknya Ākāśa tulya,manon tan katon śakti niŋ yoga māyā*20:54:1917*

ri sāmpunnya sampūṙṇna yoganya sidđi,miṅis niścayāmbĕknya tan dadya sora,sināmbutnya laṅkapnya Atyanta riŋ göŋ,lawan hrūnya tīkṣṇāgra nāgāđidéwa*20:55:1918*

tĕkanyèŋ raṇaṅgātri ya krora makrak,gĕrĕḥ ǥora gamƀīra śabdanya mādrĕs,gumĕntĕṙ lĕmaḥ pūṙṇna ṅ-ākāśa dénya,mataŋnyān praśāstèŋ jagat méǥanāda*20:56:1919*

gĕlānékanaŋ wré kapūhan ya kagyat,tatan wruḥ ri saṅkā nikaŋ śabda ǥora,kapūhan mulat loṙ kidul tan tinonya,sawètnyāpĕtĕŋ Anđakārékanaŋ rāt*20:57:1920*

lawan sūkṣma tāwak nikaŋ méǥanāda,tuhun siṅhanādanya yèkātiǥora,makin kātrĕsan wréṇ ḍĕṅö śabda ǥora,tatan wruḥ ri déyanya tan ton musuḥnya*20:58:1921*

śĕḍĕŋ ǥūṙṇnita-ŋ wré paḍāwū ya māwrĕg,mamĕṇṭaŋ laras ṅ-indrajit tā tumon ya,panaḥ tékanaŋ wré rikaŋ nāgapāśa,madadyan Ulā nāga sakwèḥ nikaŋ hrū*20:59:1922*

mapañjaŋ magöŋ lèn kiwiknyādƀutālwā,lumöŋ ƀinna cūlanya lāwan matanya,wiṣanyomĕsat nitya saṅké tutuknya,Ah-o ǥorarūpa-ŋ ƀujaṅga prayāta*20:60:1923*

{waṅśapatrapatita}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
nā tĕmahan niṅ āstra nika saŋ daśawadanasuta,koṭi sahasra saṅꝁya ya tikāṅapusi kapibala,wānara kapwa kāpusan akik saka pitu saka pāt,kāsih-asiḥ makudyat anaṅis paḍa ta ya muriṅis*20:61:1924*

maṅkana saŋ raǥūttama lawan Ari nira pinanaḥ,riŋ śara nāgapāśa kapisan ta sira Inapusan,bāhu subadđa kapwa kabĕbĕt tĕka ri suku nira,sanđi kabèḥ rapuḥ kaṅĕlihan kadi ta pinupuran*20:62:1925*

mūṙccita yāṙ tibā kapati riŋ kṣaṇa Awak alupa,mrĕm wiparīta taŋ mata kadi pwa manĕhĕra pĕjaḥ,lèn muꝁa tan patéja kadi candra juga karahinan,tulya sawaṅśapatra patita-ŋ hati ya ta kumĕtĕr*20:63:1926*

{wīralalita}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = :16:
kāla nirāṙ tibā dadi humuŋ tikaŋ kapibala,maṅkin akik makiṅkiṅ atikaṣṭa kapwa manaṅis,lèn ta laranya yan Inapusan Awaknya wipayoḥ,lèn pwa Asiḥnya mapraƀu Ah-o hatinya karuṇa*20:64:1927*

hāḥ raǥuputra nāŧa kita déwatā mami kabèḥ,mèḥ kami ƀoga tan hana wanèḥ kitéka śaraṇa,kapwa yak āmbalĕs hilaṅakĕn laranta nrĕpati,wyaṙŧa Ikā hurip mami kabèḥ winèḥ suka magöŋ*20:65:1928*

ṅhiŋ kita ta praƀūttama Anuŋ wĕnaŋ parahita,saŋ wiku sāđu sajjana rinakṣa dènta satata,duḥka nikaŋ jagattraya sināđya dènta hilaṅa,hāḥ syapa maṅkanā paḍa-paḍanta riŋ guṇa magöŋ*20:66:1929*

kāruṇika swaƀāwa kita māsih iŋ dadi kabèḥ,dīna Anāŧa Anđa śaraṇāgaténanumata,tan hana pakṣapāta ni hatinta śudđa malilaŋ,krođa musuḥ magöŋ tuwi lanānukūla ri kita*20:67:1930*

nī ta Ujaṙ nikaŋ kapibalān pasambat anaṅis,luḥ humilī humīs kabarabas paḍāṅisĕk-isĕk,sambatakĕn nikā guṇa niraŋ raǥūttama kabèḥ,wĕt ni tutuṙnya riŋ paṅupakāra dibya satirun*20:68:1931*

lèn hana wānarātiśaya wīra đīra dahatĕn,tan panaṅis kĕnèŋ ƀujagapāśa wètnyan agalak,mamrih akuṇḍah aṅgĕtĕm alaḥ masĕṅhit abutĕŋ,luḥnya nirantaré pipi humīs hatinya ya lumöŋ*20:69:1932*

yékiṅ awak tan ora pakĕnanya yan hinuripan,tan hana śakti ri ṙyya lĕhĕṅa-ŋ pĕjaḥ pwa kaśula,liŋ nikanaŋ wanèḥ r-uman-uman Awaknya kalaran,duṙyyaśa paŋhiḍĕpnya Apa tan pati-ŋ musuh agöŋ*20:70:1933*

hāḥ lalu mandaƀāgya ni huripku kaśmala dahat,pāpa gawéṅku ṅūni ta kunaŋ sumèru ya magöŋ,déwa Ah-o lalis nira nahan ta liŋnya sawanèḥ,kapwa kabanđa budđi ya Uđāni riŋ wiđiwaśa*20:71:1934*

śèṣa nikaŋ kĕnèŋ ƀujagapāśa towi manaṅis,mépu taman wĕnaŋ ya tumuluŋ siraŋ raǥusuta,byakta pĕjaḥ niraŋ nrĕpati rāma lakṣmaṇa huwus,ndyékana dèya liŋnya maṅadĕg kapūhan umulat*20:72:1935*

tan ya katon ikaŋ musuh araḥ nihan kita kabèḥ,tan surudèŋ raṇāṅga paḍa mātya yogya dadaha,jīwita ya byayanta makahīṅanāŋ pati kita,nā ta wuwusnya kapwa ya Umèri luḥnya humilī*20:73:1936*

krođa ta saŋ kapīndra manahut ta lambay aṅadĕg,Āṙyya wiƀīṣaṇéka ta masö musap mata nira,n-ton ta saṅ indrajit hana rikaŋ naƀastala mawās,sāmbutakĕn ta śūla nira tīkṣṇa śīǥra lumarap*20:74:1937*

wruḥ pwa saṅ indrajit dadi ta mūṙ muliḥ sira huwus,prāpta masö sirāwara-waraḥ ri saŋ daśamuꝁa,sāmpun alaḥ musuḥ mati kapāśa tan pabiṣa ya,rāǥawa lakṣmaṇātiśaya hīna tan paguṇa ya*20:75:1938*

nā ta Ujaṙ nirārajarakĕn raǥūttama pĕjaḥ,niścaya tan kasaṅśaya sawèt nikaŋ guragaḍa,haṙṣa ta saŋ daśānana manāđukāra mamuji,sāđu Anakku dibya saꝑalān prawīralalita*20:76:1939*

{lakṣmīwati}
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
nā liŋ niraŋ daśawadanāṙ puji ṅ-anak,saṅké giraŋ gĕrĕmĕ masö maṅolakĕn,tan saṅśayāṙ winara-waraḥ manaḥ manūt,wètnyān lanā pracaya ri śakti niŋ Anak*20:77:1940*

ndānékaƀoga kanaka ratna ƀūṣaṇa,yékā pamuṙṣita dĕmakan saṅ indrajit,sāmpun sinĕmbahakĕn ikaŋ pamūṙṣita,śīǥrāṙ wĕtu-ŋ dĕmaki kabèḥ watĕk nira*20:78:1941*

tuṣṭékanaŋ bala rumĕṅö sirājaya,kapwāmaṅan maṅinum agoṣṫi riŋ kulĕm
salwiṙ nikaŋ Aƀinawaƀoga Uttama,sèṣṭīṣṭi niŋ hati humaḍaŋ huwus hana*20:79:1942*

kĕmbaŋ jĕnūttama wĕḍihan malit marūm,raṅkaŋ hĕmās jamanika bidđa nāga lén,molĕs tilām wara taruṇī warāpsarī,lakṣmīwatī mrĕdu paḍa paṇḍitèŋ siwo*20:80:1943*

{dođakawrĕtta}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
nā ta ƀinukti nikaŋ bala wīra,tan paturū rikanaŋ wĕṅi jāgra,lèn mamijaḥ maṅigĕl ya sawaṙgga,lèn ta macumbana kāmuꝁa daṙppa*20:81:1944*

#Ĕkawiṅśati saṙggaḥ#
<tiḍak ḍikĕtahui>
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
^21/1/1926.
nda ta tīta Ikaŋ balān pamukti,sira saŋ śrī janakātmajojarèn,Iṇusuŋ ta sirèŋ wimāna ratna,winawèŋ dèśa nikaŋ raṇāṅgaṇa*21:1:1945*

sinaranta winèḥ tumona saŋ śrī,raǥuputrān kĕna pāśa mūṙccita,Umulat pwa siré saṅ āṙyya rāma,makuśāsū marusak ta kèn ira*21:2:1946*

ri ḍasaṙ nikanaŋ wimāna ratna,katibā mūṙccita tan paṅumbaraḥ,wiparīta sawèt nikaŋ larāgöŋ,kadi waṅkay humĕnĕŋ saniścala*21:3:1947*

mawĕnĕs muꝁa lèn mata pwa yomrĕm,Ikanaŋ jīwa kadi pwa tan hanā,tuwi tan patahĕn gulū nirāṅliḥ,taṅan akwāŋ malupaŋ Awak kabèḥ*21:4:1948*

I sĕḍĕŋ nira mūṙccitèŋ wimānā,manaṅis taŋ trijaṭā mĕkul suku,suku saŋ janakātmajā ta māpĕs,mapa yan moǥa makas wataŋ juga*21:5:1949*

ginugaḥnya sirāpi rājaputrī,ndya kita dyaḥ ta wuṅu pwa t-aṅlilir,nya hulunta gĕlāna tolihĕnta,haliwat dwānta kariḥ ta ri ṅhulun*21:6:1950*

ndya ta liŋ ni wuwusta ṅūni dèwī,trijaṭā ndā huniṅan wuwuskwari,saparanku kita nda tan kasāha,tuwi tag dadya tak ājaré kitā*21:7:1951*

ya tikādi nikā Ujaṙta yādwā,Apa tan wwīt aku tak madoḥ tuwi,ndi paran ni takut ta riŋ Asatya,ri paṅipyan tuwi tat kabañcana*21:8:1952*

ri mĕné ta hilaŋ bratanta dénta,kita luṅhā tamatad waraḥ ṅhulun,winuwusta kabèh asiḥ ta ṅūni,tuwi sojaṙta tamat wĕnaŋ wihaŋ*21:9:1953*

parimāṇa bapaṅku lén ibuṅku,taya trĕṣṇākw-i sirān hané kita,kita rāma kitāđidéwataṅku,kita cintāmaṇi kalpapādapa*21:10:1954*

siniwiṅku paṅöbanaṅkwu tan lèn,kita tātaḥ hinarĕp-harĕp tĕmĕn,syapa māsiha lèn yadin taya dyaḥ,Ikanaŋ lèn niyatanya sampaya*21:11:1955*

sahananya ta rākṣasī paḍāmid,Apan aṅhiŋ Aku sèwaké kita,tuwi tan malawas hanè sukunta,ya mataŋnyāt taḍ asiḥ wulat ry-aku*21:12:1956*

yadiyan tuhu mātya liŋta maṅkè,tuwi tak kāntuna dènta sakṣaṇa,ya mataŋnya t-uđāni dèwi tāṅhèr,Apa tak sāha Ataḥ sakè suku*!

{Upajāti bajra}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
nā liŋ nikā saŋ trijaṭān pasāmbat,saṅkā ri ƀaktinya lawan Asiḥnya,dèwī masowè sira tār uđāni,maṅkin ta yāsū makusān saśoka*21:13:1957*

sanālikā yaṙ wiparīta mūṙcꞓā,śanꜽḥ-śanꜽḥ moluh uđāni dèwī,nda taṙ wĕnaŋ molah alaḥ gĕlāna,Ahos Ah-o tībra nikaŋ larāgöŋ*21:14:1958*

nda taṙ dĕliŋ pūḥ Ati sanđi yāṅliḥ,luḥ nityakāla drawa riŋ muꝁādrĕs,Abāḥ mabāŋ taŋ mata dé nikaŋ luḥ,muwaḥ sirāsū wĕkasan masāmbat*21:15:1959*

hāḥ jīwitātyanta bĕtaḥnyu tan mūr,hiḍĕp Ikaŋ duḥka Atīta duḥka,lukan satrĕṣṇanyu rikèŋ śarīra,saranta saṅsāra sadā laranya*21:16:1960*

samaṅkanékiŋ hati Adwanāsiḥ,tuhun nikāṅ āmbĕk ataḥ satrĕṣṇa,pĕjaḥ pwa saŋ nāŧa hananta maṅhèr,hāḥ đik Iwĕḥ niŋ manulus Asiḥnyu*21:17:1961*

Asiḥku trĕṣṇaṅku ya liṅku tan swaŋ,taŧāpi tan tūt mati hé naréndra,yan bajra sākṣāt pwa kunaŋ hatiṅku,mataŋnya tan syūḥ ri pĕjaḥta nāŧa*21:18:1962*

{Upajāti bajra}
⏓ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
Alib ta pamriḥta laranta ṅĕlta,Umèt ṅhulun ṅūni rikèŋ Alas göŋ,huwus kitād wruḥ hana wèḥ ri lĕṅkā,mamèt kitopāya sawètnyasiḥ ta*21:19:1963*

sahīṅan iŋ nīti dinadyakĕnta,tat tolih at toliha satwahiṅsā,matī balī wèḥ kita rakwa ṅūni,ṅhulun Ataḥ don i-Ulaḥta tan lèn*21:20:1964*

Anéka taŋ wré milu duḥka dènta,tumūt makiṅkiŋ ri laranta dèṅku,Iké wĕnaŋ mĕntas ikaŋ samudra,Atīta riŋ kléśa Uliḥta mamriḥ*21:21:1965*

huwus Umĕntas pwa rikaŋ samudra,makabyaya-ŋ jīwita riŋ raṇāṅga,hīṅanya tan lèn Inaṅĕn-n-aṅĕnta,si mandaƀāgyā ta pinèt kininkin*21:22:1966*

Ikā sahīṅan niṅ asiḥ-Asiḥ ta,wĕnaŋ pĕjaḥ lāwan arinta satya,nāri pwa kāntun ri patinta nāŧa,kala ṅhulun niṙǥrĕṇa nīca duṣṭa*21:23:1967*

tamak panon lèn tuhu satya māsiḥ,Aṅhiŋ bapantékana sāđu satya,kasaḥ nirèŋ sakṣaṇa mātra dènta,mataŋ nirāsiḥ mati tībra monĕŋ*21:24:1968*

ṅhulun pwa maṅké ta tumon patinta,wĕnaŋ pwa tan tūt mahurip tan éraŋ,Awās ya tan kapracayāna tékā,strī sāđu tāpan kapapas ya dèṅku*21:25:1969*

ṅhulun hana ṅké ta humèṙ tĕkanta,Anéka taŋ duḥka kinölakĕnku,mĕṅgĕp makāmbĕk Ikanaŋ kasatyan,tan tūt pĕjaḥ hāḥ bali tuhwasatya*21:26:1970*

Aho Awak kéraṅ-iraŋ hananya,taman wĕnaŋ satya wĕnaŋ matiṅgal,Asiḥ nikā saŋ naranāŧa ri ṙyya,magöŋ tĕmĕn ndā tan aṅĕn-n-aṅĕnya*21:27:1971*

hāḥ-Āḥ si sītātiśayèṅ aƀāgya,duṙllakṣaṇāgöŋ pagawému pāpa,ndā tan pakāwakta Awakmu nīca,hāro-hara-ŋ rāt milu pāpa dému*21:28:1972*

mapa pwa pāpamwi dĕlāha sowaḥ,Apan sarāt duḥka ya dému maṅké,Awās ya kiñkiŋmu n-agöṅa dénya,ry-uwaḥmu maŋjanma sahasrajanma*21:29:1973*

Aho hawaknyan ta kariḥ gĕlĕḥnya,bali pwa māhīṅan ikā laranya,Aho lalis niŋ wiđi tan pahīṅan,mataŋnya wéḥ duḥka mahānaranta*21:30:1974*

dèwī nahan liŋ nira wèn pasambat,sĕsöl ikaŋ dꜽwa lawan swakaṙmma,tĕñuḥ wiśīṙṇna-ŋ hati tībra duḥka,r-aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn kaśmala niŋ śarīra*21:31:1975*

makin masowé ta sirān pasāmbat,taṅis nirāsrĕt mapĕyĕḥ ya mandra,gulū kasātan masĕkĕl kakīṅan,maṅaŋ makuṇḍaḥ juga taṙ paśabda*21:32:1976*

hana ṙ-bĕṅaŋ tan panaṅis kapūhan,tatan kĕḍap niścala tātar āmbèk,binanđa niŋ duḥka Ikaŋ śarīra,surat tapĕl lèn pratimā paḍanya*21:33:1977*

Apuy murub tulya nikaŋ larāgöŋ,Umuṅgu riŋ citta panasnya tīkṣṇa,gĕsöŋ katunwan hati dénya cūṙṇna,kadīkanaŋ wrĕkṣa kĕnéndrabajra*21:34:1978*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
tibā ta dèwī Umuwaḥ wimohita,dinagđa riŋ duḥka hilaŋ hurip nira,gĕlāna tékaŋ trijaṭā tumon sira,maluy ta yāsū Atiśoka mānasa*21:35:1979*

ri maṅkananyān wiparīta mohita,wawaŋ pinuṇḍutnya siromĕsat ta ya,ḍatĕŋ riṅ udyāna Aśoka śīǥra ya,n-ĕnaḥ sirèŋ ratna palaṅka niṙmmala*21:36:1980*

gugaḥ tikāwak nira kapwa yālupa,n-usap muꝁātī tuwi bāyu tan hana,gagap tikā twas nira moǥa yā makas,makin ta yākrak trijaṭānaṅis mawū*21:37:1981*

wulat pwa ta dyaḥ ndya kitāta wèt para,t-uđāni-đāni pwa manaḥta taṅguhi,Ah-o mahīṅan ta kariḥ tikèṅ asiḥ,Apan hinūṙ taŋ pati tad wulat ry-aku*21:38:1982*

ƀaṭāra tāsiḥ pwa tasö tuluŋ ṅhulun,nihan sira śrī janakātmajā-t hurip,sira prasādaṅku ta rūg waṅun muwaḥ,hilaŋ pukaḥ tā wariṅinku yan taya*21:39:1983*

nahan ta liŋ ni trijaṭā ya kāsyasiḥ,samantarođāni sirāṅrĕṅö taṅis,tĕbĕŋ ta molaḥ maṅĕliḥ taṅan nira,ta molah ūmrĕm mawuwus tĕbĕŋ mugĕm*21:40:1984*

taṅèha duḥkanta ya dèṅku yat hana,mataŋnya mātyāku huwus misan-misan,ndya dona ni ṅwaŋ mahurip nirāśraya,Ariṅku maŋlampwapawās ṅhulun pĕjaḥ*21:41:1985*

lawan ndya déyaṅku kariḥ rikèŋ hurip,Apan pĕjaḥ śrī naranāŧa rāǥawa,Alib tĕka hyunkwapi mātya ṅūnikā,hurip nirātaḥ ya hinèṙku tan pĕjaḥ*21:42:1986*

pĕgat pwa tuntun ni huripku tan hana,mawās ta yan sāka huwus mĕnèŋ gĕlĕk,Apan sirékī tali tulya banđana,panū ri jīwaṅku mataŋnya tan hilaŋ*21:43:1987*

Iké pwa yan sŧitya Ikā huripkwari,huwus pĕgat tūnya tatan masāka ya,taŧāpi sākĕnkwa ya téka sāhasan,kaṭuṅka duṣṭākw-ari yak hanā tataḥ*21:44:1988*

piréka trĕṣṇaṅkwa kunaŋ rikèŋ hurip,lawan sirékā ta sukākwa yak hanā,tĕmuṅkwa yāṅhiŋ lara pāpa kéwala,mataŋnya đik jīwita mātya ménaka*21:45:1989*

kunaŋ yaŧānyan saꝑalān patiṅkwari,taman samaṅké ya dĕlāha riŋ jĕmaḥ,ƀaṭāra wꜽśwānara yéka Oṣađā,mataŋnya tāsiḥ trijaṭā pamoṅyapuy*21:46:1990*

nahan Ujaṙ śrī janakātmajāpagĕḥ,saniścayékaŋ hati mātya tan kalèn,makin gĕlāna-ŋ trijaṭātiduḥkita,wawaŋ ya mojaṙ manaṅis samantara*21:47:1991*

Alib kita dyaḥ tan asiḥ ta ri ṅhulun,mapanta yat sāhasa mātyanaŋ Awak,tamat t-anoliḥ tat aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn ṅhulun,Atīta kaṣṭān kawĕkas nirāśraya*21:48:1992*

lawan tatan byakta naréndra yaṙ pĕjaḥ,Asamƀawān mātya binanđa riŋ Ulā,siraŋ hanūmān tuwi ṅūni kāpusan,taŧāpi taṙ māti luput sirāhurip*21:49:1993*

samaṅkanātaḥ naranāŧa rāǥawa,kĕnèŋ mahāpāśa mahān sirān hiḍĕp,harĕp niran wrĕdđya ta haṙṣa niŋ musuḥ,Agöŋ pwa haṙṣanya mawās ta yan Alaḥ*21:50:1994*

mataŋnya tāṅhéra tamat harohara,pahénak āmbĕkta tamat makiṅkiṅa,Iké hurip duṙllaƀa tan pasambutan,sĕḍĕŋ ta yat mātya sira pwa tan pĕjaḥ*21:51:1995*

kunaŋ ya tat niścaya yaṙ hanāhurip,ṅhulun marā riŋ raṇaƀūmi méṅgala,huwus nirān byakta pĕjaḥ saliŋta taḥ,nihan ṅhulun dyaḥ tamak antuné kita*21:52:1996*

lawan sĕḍĕŋnyān niyatan sirāṙ pĕjaḥ,ṅhulun marāmwīta ri saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,nyapan tahan tan wruha wèn pĕjaḥ ṅhulun,tumūtakĕn höb ni sukunta tan kalèn*21:53:1997*

nahan Ujaṙ niŋ trijaṭā mĕsat ta ya,mibĕṙ ya luṅhā mara riŋ raṇāṅgaṇa,ḍatĕŋ manĕmbaḥ ri siraŋ wiƀīṣaṇa,Ulaḥnya waṅśa sŧiti ƀakti riŋ bapa*21:54:1998*

{puṣpitāgra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
Aŧa tĕka ya ri saŋ wiƀīṣaṇāsiḥ,Umawa taṅisnya humīs ta luḥnya mādrĕs,kadi Ikana hatinya śudđa ya syūḥ,ya matĕmahan Amrĕté matanya mahniŋ*21:55:1999*

ṅhulun ikana Anakta mandaƀāgya,taya ta wanèḥ trijaṭā ṅaranku riŋ rāt,maraha kita ya donku haywa tāśā,pĕjaha Anakta nihan ṅhulunta mamwīt*21:56:2000*

ṅhulun alara tumon naréndraputrī,janakasutāṙ winawèŋ raṇaṅga ṅūni,Inusuṅ-usuṅ awū sirākuṣāsū,wulati siraŋ raǥuputra wèn kapāśa*21:57:2001*

dadi ta sira tibā rikaŋ wimāna,kapati-patibrata satya sāđu māsiḥ,I lara nira tumon ƀaṭāra rāma,kĕna rikanaŋ ƀujagāstra nāgapāśa*21:58:2002*

tar uđani masuwé sirān wimūṙccā,Inulihakĕnku sirèŋ taman-taman wruḥ,samana nira r-uđāni mamrih amwīt,pĕjaha sawĕtnya Asiḥ niré naréndra*21:59:2003*

nahan ikana ta donku wèk para ṅké,kita tat akiṅkiṅa yan pĕjaḥ Anakta,maturun apuy umilwa mātya tāku,janakasutā duluraṅkwa tan kasāha*21:60:2004*

nahan ikana wuwusnya wèn panĕmbaḥ,dadi sumahuṙ ta siraŋ wiƀīṣaṇāsiḥ,lalu kita hara putri niṣṭuranta,pĕjaha ta liŋta Amoǥa tan satrĕṣṇa*21:61:2005*

Apa kita wiparīta matta médan,Apa sumaput kita yan piśāca yakṣa,grahagaṇa gaṇa ƀūta yāṅawéśa,rikana hatinta mataŋ ni kon wimoha*21:62:2006*

hana kari gamaṇā ƀaṭāra rāma,pĕjaha rikèŋ raṇaƀūmi liŋta putrī,triƀuwana lĕburékaṅ aṇḍa rūga,yar alaha saŋ raǥuputra riŋ raṇāṅga*21:63:2007*

Atiśaya riṅ aƀāgya tékanaŋ rāt,yar upahatā naranāŧa rāmaƀadra,sira mara puruṣottamāṅśa māwān,nipuṇa pinaṇḍita riŋ sarāt riṅ astra*21:64:2008*

nahan ikana kaniścayaṅku putrī,niyata sukānta mataŋnya haywa śoka,laku tat ulih arébu santwa dèwī,sahana niké sawuwusku nojarĕnta*21:65:2009*

Uhuti ta sira sāhasèŋ śarīra,biṣama naréndra yadin pĕjaḥ sudéwī,I pati nrĕpati tan hanā Ikéŋ rāt,Aku tuwi mātya yadin tayā naréndra*21:66:2010*

guṇa nira Ikanaŋ guṇajña tātaḥ,ya ta kalulutku mataŋ nikān hana ṅkè,tamak anĕmu paḍā ƀaṭāra rāma,Ikanaṅ ahāta manon guṇālpa towi*21:67:2011*

ri pĕjaha nira taṙ wanèḥ mahītaḥ,syapa ta tumona guṇaṅku dibya héman,kadi kayu ri tĕṅaḥ nikaŋ Alas goŋ,kamaga tĕwas manĕḍĕŋ ya puṣpatāgra*21:68:2012*

{ratodđata}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
nā dumèh aku tamak Anona lèn,yaṙ tayā nrĕpatiputra rāǥawa,ndaḥ wĕkaṅku ya mataŋnya wèḥ tuliḥ,jānakī sira ta rākṣa taṅguhi*21:69:2013*

saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa nahan Ujaṙ nira,riŋ Anak mari ya śokamānasa,sādara praṇata yan paṅañjali,śīǥra yaṙ laku muliḥ tĕkèŋ taman*21:70:2014*

saŋ raǥūttama sirojarĕn muwaḥ,taṙ wĕnaŋ mawuṅu tībra mohita,graḥ rĕmĕk Ikana sanđi niŋ Awak,dé nikaŋ ƀujagapāśa duṙjjaya*21:71:2015*

maṅkananya dadi maŋliliṙ sira,maŋhiḍĕp lara mĕkĕḥ siromĕhāḥ,mār umaṅkĕp ikanaŋ Awak kabèḥ,rāḥ sumār i-muꝁa yāpanas sumöŋ*21:72:2016*

duṙbbala-ŋ mata pĕtĕŋ panon ira,citta kéwala Uđāni yātutur,tulya muṅgu ri dalĕm wĕtĕŋ sira,jīwamātra juga śākti tan hana*21:73:2017*

mꜽliliṙ pwa siraṅ āṙyya rāǥawa,saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa masö sirāwaraḥ,wrĕtta saŋ janakarājaputrikā,yékanénajarakĕn nirān asö*21:74:2018*

glāna saŋ raǥusutāṅrĕṅö sira,mꜽŧilī winawa riŋ raṇāṅgaṇa,byakta mātya rasikā si kāsyasiḥ,n-ton akuk kapati ṅūni mūṙcꞓita*21:75:2019*

hāḥ priyé janakarājaputrikā,tan salaḥ Aṅĕn-aṅĕnta yogya ya,mātya wèt nikana hīna ni ṅhulun,tan wĕnaŋ mĕjahi śatru niŋ sarāt*21:76:2020*

rāt kabèḥ kita hiḍĕpku yat hana,wèt ni göŋ nikana taŋ guṇé kita,yadyapin sari nikaŋ jagat kabèḥ,taṙ paḍā ya kalawan kita priyā*21:77:2021*

śrī ratiḥ girisutā saraswatī,nī sirānuṅ atidibya déwatī,yan tarajwana lawan kita priyā,sora ƀāra nira dènta yak hiḍĕp*21:78:2022*

tan kahĕntya saguṇanta waṙṇnitan,Apraméya kadi ratna riŋ tasik,nā mataŋnya tamatak Alāṅ-alaŋ,mèt kita priya makabyaya-ŋ hurip*21:79:2023*

ndān aƀāgya ta kunaŋ ṅhulun Ari,déwa mèdi malalis tamaṙ wulat,mèḥ mapaṅguha Ataḥ kitomuwaḥ,moǥa wiǥna tĕka tan pawèḥ jaya*21:80:2024*

kaṣṭa đik wiđi ya duṣṭa niṙǥrĕṇa,yéki māra sumarik kita priyā,tan saniṣṭura ta yaṙ pawèḥ lara,duṣṭa tuṣṭa ya manon larāpasaḥ*21:81:2025*

mwaŋ Ikaŋ wiđi yaŧéṣṭa yāmidi,niṙguṇa-ŋ guṇa patibratériya,wwaŋ sulakṣaṇa suśīla tan salaḥ,lèn Ikaŋ wiđi biṣāma sāhakĕn*21:82:2026*

tā paḍanta rikanaŋ sulakṣaṇa,riŋ Ulaḥ lima taman kuraŋ kita,taṙ sayogya wirahāpasāha taḥ,wālakāra kari dé nikiŋ wiđi*21:83:2027*

lèn manaḥta maṇi tulya śudđa ya,ƀakti taṙ paṅawanèḥ kitèŋ priya,satya nitya ri hatinta yātĕguḥ,yadyapin wahu sĕḍĕŋ ratodđata*21:84:2028*

{swāgata}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
ndaḥ priyé Asiha niŋ wiđi tāṅdé,riŋ paratra ta kunaŋ palarĕnta,ṅkā ta paṅguha dĕlāha ta rāri,wèt nikaŋ guṇa patibrata hétu*21:85:2029*

nyā ṅhulun pĕjaha lāwan arinta,taṙ wanèḥ pratita lakṣmaṇa ātaḥ,satya sāđu satirun drĕḋaƀakti,đīra riŋ lara tumūt saparanku*21:86:2030*

lakṣmaṇāri karĕṇan Aku dènta,dé ni tūt ta saparanku tat aṅluḥ,tīs panas lara lapā wĕlĕkaŋ ṅèl,nā lanā katĕmu dènta ya dèṅku*21:87:2031*

hāḥ Ariṅku saꝑalān pinakāntĕn,sāntĕn īŋ Asih-asiḥ taya ƀāra,jīwitanta pinakabyaya dènta,donta tan hana pi kéwala satya*21:88:2032*

tan hanéki pamalĕskwi kitāntĕn,klèśa duḥka juga nitya pawèḥku,hāḥ kakanta ya tuhun matuhātaḥ,tan wĕnaŋ Umupakāra Arinya*21:89:2033*

haywa tākwari Umèḥ kita ƀoga,yā matan Aku dumèḥ kita mātya,đik huripkwari krĕtaǥna ya pāpa,wwaŋ mahāṙdđika tumūt mati dènya*21:90:2034*

riŋ trilokya tak anona paḍanta,đīra wīra wirati-ŋ hati śānta,prajña satwika guṇajña suśīla,dakṣa dānta mrĕdu sāṙjjawa satya*21:91:2035*

nītimānta matakut riṅ ayogya,yogya yéka larapan ni Ulaḥta,pojaranta ya hitapriya satya,swāgatèṅ atiŧi mitra sagotra*21:92:2036*

{turagagati}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
nā guṇanta ya Ananta hana ta lèn,kwèḥnya taṙ sawinilaŋ salah inujar,paṙbwatopama kitékana malaya,tulya candana guṇanta śuci marūm*21:93:2037*

yadyapin hana guṇanta tuwi magöŋ*21:94:2038*
tan ya paŋhaḍa-haḍanta tat awĕrö,ƀakti ta pwa kita riŋ kaka kawaśa,tan pahī lawan ikaŋ pinakahulun*21:95:2039*

nā dumèḥ Aku makin kapihutaṅan,n-ton kita praṇata séwaka satata,mèru tulya ta rĕṇaṅkwi rari kita,tan kahĕntya sahurĕn sa-Iwu tahun*21:96:2040*

prāṙŧanākwari yat aṅdadi ya muwaḥ,sānakāta kita haywa ta mapasaḥ,ndan kitāta matuhā Aku raraya,ƀaktya tāku ri kitāmalĕsa guṇa*21:97:2041*

saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa samaṅkana ta kita,tasyasiḥ ta śaraṇāgata Agati,yogya kāsihana sajjana guṇawan,wāni riŋ sukrĕta duskrĕta katakut*21:98:2042*

loƀa riŋ guṇa lawan Ulah ahayu,hīna śakti rikanaŋ gawayahala,mūḋa tan wruh agawé dwa duga-duga,bwat pramāda riṅ ulaḥ kuṭila kabèḥ*21:99:2043*

yékanādi ni guṇanta sapinuji,yéka momah i-hatinta ya sumusuk,tapwa yan wĕnaṅ umèhi kita suka,tan patī mala nikaŋ ƀuwana kabèḥ*21:100:2044*

saŋ daśānana kakanta tuwi sira,tan satrĕṣṇa hrĕdayanta I-rasikā,wèt ni göŋ ni hrĕdayanta parahita,rāt kabèḥ ya kaharĕpta juga sukā*21:101:2045*

tat Anolih apasāha lawan anak,wwaŋta sānak aŧawānakĕbi kadaŋ,kapwa tan hana katrĕṣṇan ika kabèḥ,ṅhiŋ jagadđita Ataḥ Inaṅĕn-aṅĕn*21:102:2046*

wruḥ kitāñcala Ikaŋ matĕmu-tĕmu,nyā-ŋ hurip tuwi lawan suka sakarĕŋ,ṙyyak kilat ya Upamā nikanaṅ inak,riŋ hiṅā paḍa lawan turagagati*21:103:2047*

{ƀramarawilaśita}
– – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
nā hétunyād laku Umĕgil aku,saṅké hyuntèŋ parahita karuṇa,ndā tan sidđékanaṅ inaṅĕn-aṅĕn,tāđé tā déwata Aṅanumata*21:104:2048*

don-doni-ṅwaŋ mamĕgil aśaraṇa,śatrunyātaḥ ya ta hilaṅakĕna,lāwan wèhĕn wiƀawa suka magöŋ,yan tan maṅkā lĕhĕṅ umari maṅöb*21:105:2049*

tapwan paṅguḥ ꝑala niṅ aśaraṇa,saṅké pāpaṅku ya Asama-sama,hāḥ đik rāmāđama manalahasa,Āmbĕk māsiḥ bali kari wĕnaṅa*21:106:2050*

göŋ niŋ kléśéryaku giri sadrĕśa,tuŋtuŋ niŋ duṙyyaśa ka-Iraṅ-iraŋ,Āpan saŋ sajjana Umĕgil aku,tapwan sapwīkana salara nira*21:107:2051*

saŋ sugrīwāṅgada pawanasuta,ndaḥ mamwīta ṅhulun i-kita haraḥ,haywākiṅkiŋ kita laku tat uliḥ,Āpan sāmpun ta mamalĕsi guṇa*21:108:2052*

nèl tan mamriḥ lumaku masusupan,mèt saŋ sītā tatan alita tasik,tā lwaḥ tātas taya gunuṅ aruhur,tā digdéśāntara gahan asukĕt*21:109:2053*

lyab-lyab lwaŋnyāŋ ƀuwanatala pĕnuḥ,dé niŋ wadwā plawagabala sumār,sāmpun déwī katĕmu sira pinĕt,tambak tambĕḥ niṅ atiśaya yaśa*21:110:2054*

saŋsiptan sāgara hinaliwatan,maṅkin daṙppèŋ raṇa kita Umahöm,sakwèhtāmriḥ malaga taya surud,tātan lèn don rĕṇa ta ya panahur*21:111:2055*

sāmpun tékaŋ Inaƀimata dadi,tan sandéhan huwus amalĕs asiḥ,sakwānantāku taman atĕṅĕta,sojaṙttātaḥ yat uliha laku ta*21:112:2056*

nā liŋ saŋ rāmawijaya mawĕkas,tan lèn āmbĕk nira pĕjaha Ataḥ,saŋ sugrīwa drawa ta hati nira,juḥ nityomīs tĕka ri ḍaḍa nira*21:113:2057*

hāḥ nāŧa-t hèṙ kami pinakahulun,tonĕntātaḥ praṇata mami kabèḥ,lāwan pamriḥ mami ya wulatana,paŋliṅganté hati mami malilaŋ*21:114:2058*

nyānuŋ hèrĕn narapati sakarĕŋ,śatruntātaḥ ya pĕjahana mami,yapwan śakti-ŋ musuh atiraƀasa,tādé mātya-ŋ pinakahulun usön*21:115:2059*

sāmpun śīṙṇnā sahana-hana mami,ṅkā tat yogyāṅaṅĕn-aṅĕna pati,mwaŋ lwiṙ tan ton waluya mami muliḥ,tātan yogyékana Apa tan asiḥ*21:116:2060*

Āpan yan kāntuna kami ri kita,byaktān nindā sahana niṅ umulat,đik wré tīṙyyak tuhu-tuhu Ađama,tan wruḥ riŋ rāt nahan ujara nikā*21:117:2061*

nā prastāwanyan ujarĕn ahurip,yan tuhwékiŋ pati ri kita tĕkā,ndan sidđā don mami puwi rumuhun,đwastā niŋ śatru ya punagi mami*21:118:2062*

yan niśśéṣa pwa ya huwus alilaŋ,riŋ swaṙggantānuturakĕna kami,lwiṙnyan sāmpun mati si daśamuꝁa,yékā pawwat-wwata mami ri kita*21:119:2063*

tātan saṅkĕŋ guragaḍa mawuwus,cihnanyāmbĕk mami juga mapagĕḥ,tān imbātaḥ ri suku narapati,ṅkāné janmāntara huluna Ataḥ*21:120:2064*

nā liŋ saŋ wānarapati sumahur,wèt nī satyé hati nira malilaŋ,tātan liṅgaṙ Ikanaṅ aṅĕn-aṅĕn,tan trĕṣṇèŋ jīwita satiru-tirun*21:121:2065*

sāmpun mojaṙ sira dadi humĕnĕŋ,pèrīkaŋ luḥ drawa makabarabas,niśśabda-ŋ wré taya wĕnaṅ anaṅis,saṅké göŋ niŋ lara kadi ta surat*21:122:2066*

tat kālanyānta paḍa kahĕnĕṅan,maṅkin luṅhā-ŋ wĕṅi haṅin umirir,nityān tĕmpuḥ ṅ-ĕbun anarawata,yāṅkĕn luḥ niŋ wĕṅi milu kalaran*21:123:2067*

mèḥ-mèḥ māwā-ŋ wĕṅi rahina masö,kapwātaṅhi-ŋ manuk umuni humuŋ,sambégānon malara ya manaṅis,tulyāsāmbat ƀramarawilasita*21:124:2068*

{wīralalita}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = :16:
kāla ƀaṭāra rāma humĕnĕŋ humuŋ rĕṣigaṇa,riŋ gaganān paṅañjali maṅunyakĕn stuti sira,śakti ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu winuwus nikaŋ stuti kabèḥ,dadya nikā Uđānya nira saŋ raǥūttama ya don*21:125:2069*

hé mađusūdanāmriha ƀaṭāra haywa malupa,wiṣṇu Awakta jāti puruṣottamottama kita,satwa ya satya nitya ri Awakta tan dadi hilaŋ,moha kariḥ hanā tuwi rajaḥ tamaḥ pwa kawaśa*21:126:2070*

kwèh i-dadinta tan dadi yataḥ wimohita daṅū,ṅūni riṅ ādisrĕṣṭi kita rakwa maŋdadi Iwak,kūṙmma warāharūpa narasiṅha wiṣṇu ta kita,bāmana jāmadagni dadi rāmadéwa ta kita*21:127:2071*

nā ta dadinta donta puwi dadya niŋ parahita,janma Anuŋ Anāgata tĕmun ƀaṭāra taya lèn,kabwatakĕn nikaŋ dadi Anéka tātan alupa,nitya tutuṙku tan katutupan Apan praƀu kita*21:128:2072*

wyāpaka riŋ jagat kita ta jīwa niŋ dadi kabèḥ,Ādi kitāta mađya pinakānta Antaka kita,kāraṇa niŋ sŧiti pralaya samƀawèŋ triƀuwana,mwaŋ maṅanugrahé kita mahéśwarèŋ surawara*21:129:2073*

riŋ sumĕnö kabèḥ kita ta sūṙyya nitya dumilaḥ,riŋ Aji sāma wéda kita riŋ hyaṅ indra ta kita,riŋ watĕk indriya pwa ya manaḥ Awakta ya lĕwiḥ,rudra kabéḥ kitékana ta śaṅkarāgaway inak*21:130:2074*

riŋ dadi yakṣa rākṣasa kabèḥ kitāta danawa,riŋ dadi mānuṣa prakaṭakīṙtti ƀūpati kita,riŋ maruhuṙ suméru kita riŋ Akampya himawān,riŋ madalĕm samudra kita bođi riŋ kayu-kayu*21:131:2075*

riŋ paśujāti lĕmbu kita mèhakĕn sakaharĕp,riŋ Umibĕṙ kitékana ta wꜽnatéya taya lèn,siṅha kitèŋ kĕnas makara riŋ Iwak yan aḍĕmit,yapwan iwak magöŋ kita Anuŋ praƀunya baruṇa*21:132:2076*

nāga kabèḥ kitékana Anantaƀoga karĕṅö,saṙppa kabèḥ kitékana ta bāsuki prakaśita,riŋ lwah agöŋ pawitra śuci jāhnawī kita sadā,riŋ laku śīǥra lèn gati lanā kitéka pawana*21:133:2077*

riŋ maṅadĕg kitékana ta waṙṣakāla sakala,lèk rwawĕlas kitékana ta māṙggaśīṙṣa kalima,riŋ rĕtu nĕm kitéka mađumāsa manmaŧasakā,riŋ magawé prajā kita ta đātrĕ māṅulahakĕn*21:134:2078*

riŋ pitaraḥ kabèḥ kita ta Āṙyyamā pitrĕwara,yajña kabèḥ kitāta japa yoga Uttama tĕmĕn,Oṃ riṅ ujāriṅ akṣara Akārarūpa ta kita,riŋ caturāśrama pwa ya grĕhasŧa Aśrama kita*21:135:2079*

đaṙmma magöŋ ꝑalanya taya duṙyyaśanya ta kita,nyāya nimitta yan katĕmu ṅ-aṙŧa yékana kita,kaṙmma manūt i-Āgama lawan jagadđita kita,maṅkana riŋ Ulaḥ Anuṅ anūt i-yogya ta kita*21:136:2080*

mona kitèŋ rahasya kita wāda saŋ wruh acĕṅil,saŋ wihikan rikaŋ naya kitā ta kīṙtti rasikā,téja kitèŋ sutéja jaya niŋ jayèŋ raṇa kita,śakti nikaŋ maśakti kita budđi saŋ winihikan*21:137:2081*

wyāsa kitèŋ munīndra kita śukra riŋ kawiwara,riŋ rĕṣi sidđa tan hana wanèḥ kitāta kapila,déwarĕṣi praśāsta kita nārada priyaraṇa,brahmarĕṣi prasidđa ƀrĕgu siđđawāk sira kita*21:138:2082*

riŋ nayawit pratīta ƀagawān wrĕhaspati kita,riŋ maṅĕnākĕn ātiśaya ḍaṇḍa saŋ yama kita,bajra Awakta Uttama riṅ āyuđāpratihata,riŋ wihikan riṅ astra kita rāma wīralalita*21:139:2083*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
riŋ nakṣatra kabèḥ kitékana wulan riŋ Aśwa Uccꜽḥśrawa,riŋ sènāpati saŋ kumāra rikanaŋ widyā kitāđyātmikā,riŋ ganđaṙwwa kitāta citraraŧa lèn prahlāda riŋ dꜽtyawān,riŋ strī śrī smrĕti kīṙtti śānti đrĕti điḥ méđā kṣamā wāk kita*21:140:2084*

saŋ hyaŋ pāwaka riŋ watĕk wasu waṣaṭ swāhā kitātaḥ pawèḥ,gāyatrī kita Uttamottama rikaŋ candénujaṙ saŋ kawi,dwandwāwakta rikaŋ samāsa kita ta dyūtèŋ calātaḥ kita,saŋ Ꜽrāwaṇa riŋ gajéndra magalak śāṙddūlawikrīḍita*21:141:2085*

{basantatilaka}
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :14:
riŋ wrĕṣṇiwīra kita rakwa dĕlāha krĕṣṇa,kaṅśādidꜽtya trĕṇatulya ya patyananta,riŋ pāṇḍawa pwa kita Aṙjjuna Ujwala ṅkā,duṙyyođana prakrĕtiduṣṭa ya patyananta*21:142:2086*

nā ta prakāra ni Awakta ƀinéda-ƀéda,kintu pwa tan hana palè-nan ikā Awakta,tuṇgal kitékana pĕnuḥ rikanaŋ triloka,Ātmā nikaŋ dadi carācara Ucca-nīca*21:143:2087*

tātan dadi-ŋ dadi kabèḥ yadiyat tayātaḥ,Āpan kitékana ta jīwa kitéka saṅkan,brahmādi niŋ sakalaƀūta trĕṇānta towi,tuntūni jīwita nikā kita cétananya*21:144:2088*

Aṅhiŋ samaṅkana hiḍĕp mami hé mahātmā,gamƀīra-ƀāra ta Awakta Atīta sūkṣma,dé saŋ mahāṙṣi maha simpĕn ikā Awakta,saŋsipta mātra paṅujaṙ mami mantramātra*21:145:2089*

saṅké Iwĕḥ nika Awakta Acintyagamya,saŋkṣepa saŋ rĕṣi n-usī taṅ ujaṙ masimpĕn,yāwat mahāṙdđika mahābala mapraƀāwa,tāwat ƀaṭāra puruṣottama liŋ mahāṙṣi*21:146:2090*

ndan don ikojara ni tatwa ƀaṭāra tan lèn,swaṣṭā nikaŋ ƀuwana duṙjjana yādahānya,saŋ sāđu maṅguhakĕna-ŋ suka taṙ pakāla,Aṅhiŋ basantatilakādi sĕkaṙ makāla*21:147:2091*

{jagatpramudita}
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = :16:
nā ta Ujaṙ niraŋ rĕṣi kabèḥ maṅastuti humuŋ,mwaŋ sura sidđa cāraṇa maṅunyakĕñ jaya-jaya,Utkaṭa puṣpawaṙṣa sumawuṙ lawañ jĕnu marūm,riŋ gaganāntarāla I-ruhuṙ niraŋ raǥusuta*21:148:2092*

paŋhuniṅan nirĕŋ stuti tatas tikaŋ Apus-apus,pāśa pasèwu śīṙṇna ya pĕgat taman pahamĕṅan,maṅkana pāśa niŋ kapibalāpasaḥ kasarakat,dé ni haṅin niraŋ garuḍa śīǥra yaṙ tĕka masö*21:149:2093*

sādara yan panĕmbah i-ƀaṭāra rāmawijaya,mwaŋ siraṅ āṙyya lakṣmaṇa manaḥ nirāsih agiraŋ,kol suku saŋ naréndrasuta karwa kapwa Inusap,śudđa maluy śarīra nira niṙwikāra mari mār*21:150:2094*

swasŧa saṅ āṙyya kālih umuliḥ ta saŋ garuḍa wèḥ,Adƀuta saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa kapīndra Aṅgada tuwi,mgāmruti nīla lèn bala sahaṙṣa kapwa magiraŋ,n-ton nrĕpaputra sāmpun apasaḥ ta pāśa nira sāk*21:151:2095*

maṅkana taŋ kapiprawarawīra kādƀuta tĕmĕn,tan bali sāka taŋ ƀujagapāśa ṅūni matĕguḥ,sāk pwa Apus-Apusnya wĕkasan sawismaya ta ya,tātan i-rāt hiḍĕpnya kadi Indrajāla juga ya*21:152:2096*

wruḥ pwa ya-yan siraŋ garuḍa mèḥ ya jīwita masiḥ,māmri ya saṅśayātiśaya haṙṣacitta ya kabèḥ,maṅkin agöŋ ta ƀakti ni manaḥnya tan n-alaṅ-alaŋ,n-ton ikana praƀāwa nira saŋ raǥūttama magöŋ*21:153:2097*

byakta ƀaṭāra wiṣṇu sira mānuṣākrĕti katon,saŋ garuḍađwajāṅdadi sirāṙyya rāma ta kariḥ,tan hana saṅśayān hilaṅa śatru niŋ triƀuwana,rāma namostu nāŧa nikanaŋ jagat pramudita*21:154:2098*

{malinī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :15:
nahan ikana wuwus niŋ wānarātyanta tuṣṭa,dadi ya madĕg adandan daṙppa yāsiṅhanāda,saraƀaṣa ya lumumpat gaṙjjitāgyā manaḥnya,muwahana Ikanaŋ praŋ prāṙŧanānya byayātmā*21:155:2099*

Aŧa rahina ya mésuk mèh umĕtwa hyaṅ aṙkka,kapibala ya Umaṅkat kapwa sāmpun sĕnadđa,krama tĕka ya ri hèŋ niŋ rājya lĕṅkā ya mahyā,gaganatala ya limpad dé ni śabdanya mādrĕs*21:156:2100*

daśamuꝁa sira kagyat maŋ­rĕṅö śabda ǥora,tĕka tumama ya mājaṙ wrétta taŋ cāra śīǥra,saha bala maṅĕsaḥ sāk đꜽṙyya saŋ rāwaṇāsiḥ,hati saƀaya kapūhan kātrĕsan śoka māśā*21:157:2101*

muꝁa nira mawĕnĕs nistéja wètnyāṙ kapūhan,kĕtĕ-kĕtĕgĕn umaṇḍĕḥ taŋ Ahĕṅkāra piṇḍaḥ,ƀaya ya ta pinakāwak niŋ mahāmoha wrĕdđi,ya sumaput i-kađīran niŋ manaḥ māna śīṙṇna*21:158:2102*

pamĕnaṅa nira riŋ praŋ taṙ hiḍĕp yaṙ kasidđā,Alaha nira ya téka byakta yaṙ ton ya dadya,dadi ta sira Umājñèŋ wīra đūmrākṣa mĕtwa,pamuni nira yatanyān taṙ katonan pakiṅkiŋ*21:159:2103*

tuwi-tuwi saṅ inājñan wīra đūmrakṣa đīra,tar alaṅ-alaṅ i-sojaṙ saŋ praƀu prāṇatulya,pĕjaha dadaha riŋ praŋ prāya niŋ citta tan lèn,saꝑala-ꝑala niṅ āmbĕk ƀakti maswāmi māsiḥ*21:160:2104*

Umĕtu ta sira riŋ praŋ dāni wadwā nirākwèḥ,gaja raŧa kuda sāmpun yātitaḥ mwaŋ padāti,wwara ta raŧa nirāgöŋ ꝁyāti siṅhāsya nāma,kuda nira si wrĕkāsyānuŋ humīṙ yāniwāṙyya*21:161:2105*

sawĕtu nira manambĕṙ taŋ gagak krora śabda,đwaja nira ya kabuñcaŋ dé nikaŋ bāyubajra,hati nira nirupékṣān ton ikaŋ duṙnimitta,tar awĕdi tar akiṅkiŋ riŋ Awak mātya donya*21:162:2106*

Apa katakuta ni-ṅwaŋ yan huwus sidđakāṙyya,Inanumata sakahyun-hyunya dé saŋ naréndra,winarĕgan iniṅū riŋ wastra ratnopaƀoga,wiƀawa wiṣaya sécꞓā Apsarī mālinī kwèḥ*21:163:2107*

{widyutmālā}
– – – | – – – | – ⏓ = :8:
nāhan tojaṙ saŋ đūmrākṣa,sāmpun śudđāṅ āmbĕk mātya,saṅké göŋ niŋ ƀaktyaswāmī,tātañ cāla-ŋ cittātyucca*21:164:2108*

tat kālanyān prāpta ṅkānè,hèŋ niŋ rājyān tonton taŋ wré,kapwāgyā yan wĕtwa-ŋ śatru,maṅhrĕŋ maṅhrik kapwāṅambul*21:165:2109*

maṅsö rowaŋ saŋ đūmrākṣa,krūrākārākrĕm-krĕm mākrĕp,kadyaṅgā niŋ méǥāröŋrĕŋ,kadganyā ṅkèn widyutmālā*21:166:2110*

{mattamayūra}
– – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
sāṅsö niŋ wwil kapwa tumindak ya tumandaŋ,mwaŋ kantaṙnyāty-ujwala patranya widagđa,śudđālaṇḍĕp ƀinna krĕtālanya mapañjaŋ,rodrān paṅduk ry-antara niŋ kantar aniñjo*21:167:2111*

śīǥrān pamraŋ taŋ makrĕtālān kadi kāla,yatnān lumpat yā kapisan dénya kapökan,buŋ lumbu wwé tulya nikaŋ wré ri hiḍĕpnya,kapwārimpuŋ wānara waṅkwaŋnya tiniṅhas*21:168:2112*

makwèḥ taŋ wré wīra rikāścaṙyya tinonton,taṙ wruḥ sĕmpal pinraṅ ataḥ daṙppa rikaŋ praŋ,mèḥ maŋḍaṇḍā liŋnya kalĕṅgak ya lumĕṅhèḥ,sumyūk taŋ rāḥ ṅkā ri wĕtĕŋnyāṙ kĕna pinraŋ*21:169:2113*

saṅsāra-ŋ wré śīṙṇna śarīranya kanin kwèḥ,kārug kāṅkus lèn kalipuŋ mwaŋ kĕna ḍaṇḍa,kāmbaḥ kèdĕk duḥkita yākik ya kakuṙcyat,glānomĕṅgaḥ mosah aṅĕmbus hana mūṙcꞓā*21:170:2114*

manṅkin daṙppa-ŋ rākṣasa sāk syūḥ sawinuknya,maṅsö taŋ wré śakti daṅū śūra rikèŋ praŋ,siṅlaṙ pinraŋ yan pamalĕs tan dadi madwā,rĕmpak rĕmpū dénya tumampyal muꝁa niŋ wwil*21:171:2115*

dényāmaṇḍĕm riŋ watu tātan sipi riŋ drĕs,rampal sĕmpal bāhu nikaŋ rākṣasa dénya,maṅluḥ taŋ wwil kapwa kapĕṅhĕl ya pinaṇḍĕm,cūṙṇnān rĕñcĕm yan tinibān paṙbwata māwān*21:172:2116*

waṅkay niŋ wwil tan hana tan syūḥ śata śīṙṇna,wèt niŋ glisnyèŋ wānara maŋḍaṇḍa mamaṇḍĕm,saṅké sĕṅhitnyāṙ kĕna pāśé wĕṅi ṅūni,nā hétunyān tan panĕpöŋ tībra galaknya*21:173:2117*

wré gut-gūtĕn tan hana tékā katakutnya,tātan wèḥ wwil mālĕsa maṅkin sinuruŋnya,māmrĕp man~wĕk riŋ kuku sakrođa ya maṅduk,konduṙ kèdĕk duṙbbala taŋ rākṣasa kosī*21:174:2118*

saŋ đūmrākṣa glāna tumon rākṣasa śīṙṇna,maṅsö gumrit taŋ raŧa siṅhāsya maśabda,haṙṣān paṅhrik taŋ kuda kaꝁyāti wrĕkāsya,tan dwān lumpat taŋ wray alumpat dinĕmaknya*21:175:2119*

saŋ đūmrākṣāṅuṇḍa gadā riŋ raŧa r-uṅgu,r-ambaḥ taŋ wré mawri ya māwrĕg ya Umundur,yékāṅsö saŋ māruti kapwāta sahaṙṣa,kadyaṅgā niŋ mattamayūrān panĕmūlā*21:176:2120*

{prahaṙṣiṇī}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
maṅsö saŋ pawanasuta prahaṙṣacitta,sāmbut taŋ watu sagunuŋ makas malaṇḍĕp,r-uṇḍoṇḍé taṅan i-tĕṅĕn kiwān makañjar,bāhwalwā ya ta winiwiṙ supatra līlā*21:177:2121*

đūmrākṣodđata Umasö mĕsat lumumpat,sakrođān pamalu-maluy ta yé raŧanya,taṙ kagyat saṅ anilaputra yaṙ ḍinaṇḍa,taṙ polaḥ tar alara taṙ tulaṙ tataṙ köl*21:178:2122*

đūmrākṣāmalu Umaluy maliḥ ya kontal,saŋ pinriḥ pinalu pi niṙwikāra đīra,līlātaḥ makin amiwiṙ ḍaḍāṇ ḍinaṇḍa,mahyun riŋ yaśa Umahā mahöm sirèŋ praŋ*21:179:2123*

saṅkā yan lagi ginadā madan ta mundur,yékāṅsö nira wĕkasan wawaŋ mamaṇḍĕm,đūmrākṣān winatu mĕtu-ŋ kaṭuṅkabudđi,tan đīromilag atakut kĕnā kanīna n*21:180:2124*

sèlagnyān kĕna ta raŧanya śīṙṇna cūṙṇna,ƀasmīƀūta matĕmahan hawūn pinaṇḍĕm,tātan lwiṙ kuda si wrĕkāsya-kāsyasiḥ syūḥ,dé saŋ māruti mati yātĕñuḥ Awaknya*21:181:2125*

đūmrākṣomari maraŧomasö masĕṅhit,ḍaṇḍātaḥ ya ta pinakāyuđèŋ raṇaṅga,saglisnyān pamalu siraŋ marutsutāmriḥ*21:182:2126*
hūmrĕŋ mamrigigih alaḥ humöṅ ikaŋ twas*21:183:2127*

saŋ bāywātmaja sira taṙ calāṇ ḍinaṇḍa,ndā taŋ jriḥ pamalu masö maluy tayolap,tan ṅèḥ yan hĕnĕṅakĕnéki hīnaśakti,nā liŋ saŋ pawanasutāṙ sikĕp sukunya*21:184:2128*

sampunnyān kasikĕp inīrakĕn Inandul,kāṅgĕk yèŋ watu karĕpārĕmuk wĕhaŋnya,tuṅgak téka rahu-rahunya pūḥ hatinya,rāḥ wuṅkal makabĕlĕbĕk saké tutuknya*21:185:2129*

đūmrākṣa-kṣaṇika huripnya yéka luṅhā,hāhaḥ śabda haru-harālayū-ŋ watĕk wwil,mahyāhyaŋ mamuji wijaḥ manāđukāra,déwā riŋ gagana mulat prahaṙṣiṇī kwèḥ*21:186:2130*

{sragđara}
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :21:
đwasta-ŋ đūmrākṣa đuṙttāđama makabalasaḥ đūli rowaŋnya śīṙṇna,dé niŋ wré wīra yāwoṙ wariṅutĕn abutĕŋ yaṙ pamuk tan panon rāt,nyā-ŋ rāt rokĕn ya dadyāŋ hawu kimuta Ikaŋ rākṣasāsāra rūkṣa,kosī sāk śéṣa-śéṣanya ya Ikana muliḥ mājar-ājaṙ ya wrĕtta*21:187:2131*

Āśā saŋ rāwaṇāmsiḥ winarah i-pati niŋ wīra đūmrākṣa riŋ praŋ,ṅ-kon taŋ Ākampanāmriḥ-mriha tan uliha yan tan hanoliḥnya śatru,śatru ƀrasŧā ta dé saṅhulun aŧawa nihan saṅhulun mātya nāŧa,nā liŋ niŋ wīra Ākampana punagi nikā saṅka-saṅka byayèŋ praŋ*21:188:2132*

sāmpun sampūṙṇna ṅ-āmbĕk praṇata ri sawuwus saŋ praƀū ƀakti matwaŋ,yékān lampaḥnya mĕtwèŋ raṇa hana humaḍaŋ taŋ raŧāgöŋ gaƀīra,hrū tīkṣṇānuŋ Isinyénatus atitip atap tīka tamyaŋnya m-akwèḥ,mwaŋ gaṇḍéwanya gaṅsal ḍĕpa sasaka sakol göŋnya sawwaḥ talinya*21:189:2133*

sāṅkatnyāñcāla bāhunya kumĕdut i-kiwān lèn haṅin ǥora séṇḍuŋ,krūra-ŋ piṇḍuŋ manuŋsuŋ Asu hasaṅ ajugug ǥūṙṇnitèṅ uṇḍuṅ-uṇḍuŋ,nā lwiṙ niŋ duṙnimittāhala ya tinĕmu niŋ wīra Ākampanākwèḥ,tātan kagyat gatinyodđata maṅapa kariḥ moha momo ya mūṙkꝁa*21:190:2134*

tat kāla prāpta ṅ-ākampana pinapagakĕn dé nikaŋ wré kabèḥnya,wĕṇṭaŋ tékī larasnyān panahi ta Ikanaŋ wānarèṅ astra tīkṣṇa,hrūnyātap taṙ panonan gaganatala pĕtĕŋ pūṙṇna limpad hibĕk hrū,rampal rampuŋ tikaŋ wré kĕna panah ananī tan hana wré wĕnaŋ mūr*21:191:2135*

krođāmbĕk saŋ hanūmān dadi sira manikĕl tal magöŋ twasnya wuntu,yékāṅkĕn lori līlā lalita ya pinutĕṙ tan wikārān putĕṙnya,yatnāṅ ākampanāmriḥ mamanahi hinabèt hrūnya dé saŋ hanūmān,kontal maṅsul kawaṅsul kapalu-kapalupuy pūḥ pupug syūḥ panaḥnya*21:192:2136*

maṅkin maṅsö ta saŋ māruti wirati tamaṙ pawyat āpan widagđa,pinriḥ sinwī tinuṇḍĕs pinanah inuwahan tan kanin taṙ kĕnātaḥ,r-aṅsö ṅ-ākampanāṅduk taya dadi katibā tan papiṇḍwan pinaṇḍĕm,mūṙcꞓān mañcuṙ ta rāḥnyèŋ ḍaḍa-ḍaḍal apasaḥ sāk bĕhak bāhu sĕmpal*21:193:2137*

munduṙ rowaŋnya mawrī binuru-buru rusānĕmwakĕn moŋ paḍanya,kapwāmwriḥ jīwitanyācik-icik i-lalayū śīǥra mājaṙ ya wrĕtta,dīnāśā saŋ daśāsyāṅĕsah asih asĕkĕl kölakĕn taŋ ƀayāgöŋ,göṅ āmbĕk caṅka-caṅkak ta sira daṅu-daṅū ndan mĕné māna mona*21:194:2138*

tātan maṅgĕḥ paluṅguḥ nira haru-hara taŋ citta maṅgaŋ tan andĕl,maṅkat saṅkèŋ palaṅkāṙ kuliliṅi Ikanaŋ rājya r-ājñékanaŋ wwil,kon saŋ mantrī prahastomasuka tumitahāŋ rākṣasānuŋ matuṅgwa,mwaŋ taŋ konĕn Umĕtwèŋ raṇa sira śaraṇā niŋ watĕk wīra riŋ praŋ*21:195:2139*

nā liŋ saŋ rāwaṇojaṙ saraƀaṣa malayū tékanaŋ wwil kinonkon,gumyāmkĕn saŋ prahastomasuka dadi masuk saŋ prahastātiśīǥra,prāptānĕmbaḥ siré saŋ daśawadana wawaŋ saŋ daśāsyāsi mojar,ndaḥ dānīkaŋ matuṅgwā laki kita ta Ikomĕtwa riŋ praŋ ta liṅku*21:196:2140*

nojaṙ saŋ rāwaṇāgyā sumahur ikana saŋ mantrimuꝁya prahasta,sojaṙ śrī ƀūmināŧāparan ikana kasandéha lāwan kakiṅkiŋ,đīrā saŋ swāmi haywāwĕdi kadi matakut lwiṙ mahārāja maṅké,Āpan makwèḥ Ikaŋ rākṣasabala makĕmit moǥa saŋ nāŧa śoka*21:197:2141*

nyānuŋ lwiṙ niŋ matuṅgū satata ya tinitaḥ saṅhulun rākṣakā ṅké,Āmbĕknyālyus tan imbā maṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn ikā śrī mahārāja tan lèn,tan loƀèŋ mās tan ahyun riṅ anakĕbi tuwin kölan iŋ tīs panas ṅèl,śūrātaṅhi prayatnĕŋ rahina wĕṅi lanātātitaḥ saŋ matuṅgu*21:198:2142*

sāmpun pwékī dinānān sahana niṅ akĕmit taṙ kasandéha ri ṙyya,mamwītomĕtwa riŋ praŋ pinakahulun ikā mātya mamriḥ mamūka,Āpan doniŋ kadi lwiṙ mami hana Iniṅū dé mahārāja tan lèn,Aṅhiŋ mātyèŋ raṇātaḥ punagi mami yadin tan n-ikaŋ śatru śīṙṇnā*21:199:2143*

nā tojaṙ saŋ prahasta praṇata dadi madĕg dāni taŋ dāna dibya,salwiṙ niŋ puṇya-puṇyénatĕrakĕn i-siraŋ brāhmaṇācāṙyya sidđa,mās lāwan mutyahāra sꝑaṭika marakatādinya dīnottamākwèḥ,luṅsiṙ déwāṅga dodot wrĕṣaƀa kuda liman kanyakā sragđarārūm*21:200:2144*

{suwadanā}
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :20:
sāmpun pwaŋ puṇya-puṇyātiśaya dadi Ināśīṙwwāda ta sira,dé ḍaŋ hyaŋ Aṣṭasénīnanumata ta sirān swasŧèŋ raṇa jaya,lèn pūjā riŋ pahoman satata saha wiđi mwaŋ maṅgalagĕlar,saŋ hyaŋ Astra pracaṇḍénawatakĕn iṅĕnaḥ riŋ Āyuđa kabèḥ*21:201:2145*

mahyā taŋ wīra rowaŋ nira huwus aṅinum kapwājĕnu marūm,salwiṙ niŋ mūlyadodot ya ta wĕḍihan ikā mwaŋ kuṇḍala maṇik,lantaŋ-lantaŋ gĕlaŋ mās kiriwili calanāswaṅgāsama-sama,kantaṙ tan kāri lāwan karatala ya tĕlas muṅgwiŋ karatala*21:202:2146*

lèn sāṅkat niŋ manuṅgaŋ saha raŧa kalawan n-āđoraṇa muꝁa,gamƀīra-ŋ ƀèri ginwal murawa kala-kalārāwèŋ daśa-diśi,haṙṣāmbĕk saŋ prahastāhuti nira hinatuṙ dīpākṣata miñak,saŋ hyaŋ wꜽśwānarénaṙccaṇa nira manĕhĕṙ mamwit mĕtu sira*21:203:2147*

wĕt niŋ gyā śīǥra muṅgaḥ sira ri raŧa nirālwāgöŋ kadi gunuŋ,pahyas sāmpun sĕnadđākawaca hinĕmasan jwālanya kumĕñar,maƀrī taŋ ratna muktā-ŋ kanaka tapu-tapu ṅkāné hulu nira,Ādityomuṅgwi puñcak niṅ udaya sumĕnö nā topama nira*21:204:2148*

maṅkin haṙṣékanāmbĕk niran inarak-arak niŋ rākṣasabala,kapwāhyā ǥūṙṇnitā yaṙ laku kadi ta-tasik śabdanya gumuruḥ,tan kraḥ taŋ taṇḍa-taṇḍojwala kaharan alun n-ālola kumĕlab,tulyéwak lumba-lumba-ŋ kuda krĕtala Akĕn hyu praŋnya mawilĕt*21:205:2149*

cihnanyān mātya riŋ praŋ krama dadi ta manon aswāsaṅ apupul,yānuŋsuŋ saŋ prahastāṅhalulu ya maṅalup kapwāṅuliliṅi,gĕntĕṙ taŋ rāt hudan rāḥ kagiri-giri tikĕl taŋ taṇḍa kumupak,nā lwiṙ niŋ māra wiǥnāmarahakĕn i-pati byaktāhala daṅū*21:206:2150*

đīrāmbĕk saŋ prahastāṙ wulat iriya tapa-ŋ sandéha ri sira,tā trĕṣṇā tā kakiṅkiŋ Ikaṅ awak aparan yogyanya kari lèn,yan lènānuŋ matīŋ praŋ niyata ya naraka mwaŋ duṙyyaśa tĕkā,yapwan yajñān pamūjèŋ raṇa pĕjaha mamūk mokṣā ya lĕpasa*21:207:2151*

nā citté saŋ prahastāpratihata matĕguḥ taŋ đꜽṙyya ri hati,prāptāṙ sambé Ikaŋ wré mapagakĕna Ikā rowaŋ nira masö,mwaŋ byūhanyāṙdđacandrāṙdđa kawĕtu ri tĕṅaḥ saṅké panaliṅa,saŋ kīṙṇna byūha niŋ wré bari-bari majĕmuṙ yāwoṙ tar apiliḥ*21:208:2152*

sāṅsö saŋ sꜽnya sénāpati maṅarahakĕn wīrāṅatagakĕn,Uttuṅgottuṅga niŋ wwil malayu-layu masö kapwāṅlaki-laki,tan dwānyāṇḍĕm maraṅkĕp kaparupuh amupuḥ mosyan silih usī,sinraŋ manraŋ ya mamraŋ manuruṅ aṅicipiṙ cidranya gapitan*21:209:2153*

wwil mamraŋ wwil mañakrāñuriga ya maṅarug yānūla manuhuk,wré māmrĕp wré mamaṇḍĕm mamalu ya manahut maṅduk ya manikĕp,kapwālwaŋ kapwa moliḥ paḍa ya mapulihan kapwā kaninanā,ndā tañ jriḥ kapwa đīrodđata taman atakut gumrut garĕgĕtĕn*21:210:2154*

moŋ mwaŋ siṅhātirodrénatus-atus atukaṙ nāgéndra masahut,himpĕṙ niŋ wwil lawan wray malaga taya lĕgö göŋ māna magalak,manwī manwab maṅambaḥ mara ya mamurugul taŋ wwil Agul-agul,maŋḍaṇḍa-ŋ wré pracaṇḍa pracalita capalān luñcat maṅicipir*21:211:2155*

sākṣāt kālékanaŋ wwil mawila-wila wĕlaŋ tāwaknya manisiḥ,yan taṇḍaŋ tan dadīkā kamaga daṅu-daṅū moliḥ ta ya cĕṅĕl,yatna-ŋ wré wruḥ maṅinté Inayatan irikaŋ kadgāyuđa magöŋ,taṅgul taŋ rākṣasāmriḥ misani ya rikanaŋ muṣṭi kṣana tibā*21:212:2156*

lèn wwil maṅrug tumandaŋ dadi dinudutakĕn tārugnya sinikĕp,ginyat kāṅgĕk kahaṇḍĕm kahala kahilaṅan yārugnya kawĕnaŋ,ṅkāliḥnyoliḥ nikaŋ wré mati ta ya Inarug ry-ārūgnya wĕkasan,limpad pyaḥnyān paraḥ trus saha ruđira rujit tosusnya ya mulū*21:213:2157*

Aṙdđāsoṙ śakti niŋ rākṣasa Asiṅ umasö yātaḥ pinugutan,krođāmbĕk saŋ prahasta krama dadi ta masö gumrit raŧa nira,wĕntaŋ laṅkap nirāgöŋ śarawara ya huwus sampūṙṇna tumihaŋ,tuṇḍĕs tĕṇḍas nikaŋ wré kaparapal apasaḥ hrū tīkṣṇa tumuluy*21:214:2158*

mèwwīwu-ŋ wré parĕŋ yan katuluyan ananānékmā hana kĕna,jaṅgutnyéruŋnya timpal ḍaḍa-ḍaḍal anuḍul waṅkwaŋnya tumihuk,bāhunyégānya kārit ruđira ya mĕlĕbĕk muñcaṙ ya sumirat,Akwèḥ taŋ wré pipinyān sipi maṅawir-awiṙ đīrāmrih anahut*21:215:2159*

maṅkin śīṙṇnān piniṇḍwan pinanahan ananā nānāwiđa kĕna,saṅkā ri kwèḥ nikaŋ hrū daśadiśi ya sĕsök mānak mapasurup,tuṅgal mānak ya sātus tuwi satata tibānyèŋ wānara rujit,tan pās~lāŋ hrū tumaṅgö katatakut atitip mākrĕp kacĕrĕcĕb*21:216:2160*

waṅké niŋ wré tatan lwiṙ malara Umulat i-lwiṙnyan kĕna panaḥ,raṅké-raṅké jugāpan taji makatulajĕg tan pāntara riya,saŋ sugrīwālarān ton kapibala kabalik yāsoṙ kawalĕsan,sambé saŋ nīla līlān taṅan ira mawajik mojaṙ suwadana*21:217:2161*

{basantatilaka}
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :14:
hé nīla haywa humĕnĕŋ mananā Ikaŋ wré,tāṅsö-huwus papagakĕnta Ikoŋ prahasta,yèko patiḥ pati-patiḥ Umatīkanaŋ rāt,tā rāt hiḍĕpnya kamakāra kuraŋ wiwéka*21:218:2162*

nyojaṙ niraŋ plawagarāja wawaŋ maṅajñé,saŋ nīla tār alaṅ-alaŋ malilaŋ riṅ āmbĕk,śīǥromasö sira mataŋnya malap ta ḍaṇḍa,raṇḍö magöŋ ya madawā sapuluḥ dĕpā ya*21:219:2163*

nityāmanaḥ manakitīkana saŋ prahasta,koṭyaṙwudāyuta Anuŋ mati dé nira-ŋ wré,saŋ nīla nīti hinabĕt nira tékanaŋ hrū,hrū saŋ prahasta malilaŋ ta hilaŋ ya kontal*21:220:2164*

saŋ nīla nīti pinanaḥ ta sirénarāraḥ,ndā taṙ kĕnèŋ panah ataḥ kimutaṙ kanīna,wètnyāṙ wicitra tahu cĕtta macitraḍaṇḍa,syūḥ pūḥ katimpal apĕluḥ kapĕluk tikaŋ hrū*21:221:2165*

ǥora-ŋ raṇāṅgaṇa tasik Upamanya riŋ lwā,hrū saŋ prahasta kumisik ya Akĕn wwayanya,saŋ nīla tulya waḍawāmuꝁa rodrabahni,jwālā paḍā nikana ḍaṇḍa nirāmaṅan hrū*21:222:2166*

tulyāpuyiŋ pralaya Astra niraŋ prahasta,tīkṣṇāpanas sakĕna dénya gĕsöŋ Ikaŋ wré,sambaṙttakopama niraŋ kapi nīla méǥa,nāŋ ḍaṇḍa tulya ya hudan pamaḍĕm nirèŋ hrū*21:223:2167*

piŋ sèwu yaṙ pamanahīkana saŋ prahasta,tan kālarañ juga siraŋ kapi nīla wīra,towin tinuṇḍĕs aparö saparan kĕnītaḥ,tātaṙ kĕna-ŋ kapi Apan paramèŋ widagđa*21:224:2168*

polaḥ ni ḍaṇḍa nira taṙ katĕṅĕṙ putĕṙnya,lwiṙnyan katon kadi papan mawĕlū jugālwā,jāwan taṅan nira taman katĕṅĕṙ kĕtĕṙnya,kāścaṙyya hāḥ haha-hahāḥ hah-ah-o Apūṙwwa*21:225:2169*

tātan tuluy kapalupuy kawaluy tikaŋ hrū,puṅkanya yéka kumĕné ḍaḍa saŋ prahasta,tulyāƀicāri ri siraŋ bahumantra sidđi,Aṅhiŋ Ikaŋ maṅaƀicāra paranya tan lèn*21:226:2170*

Aṙdđāṅĕliḥ kĕli-kĕlin nika saŋ prahasta,mamriḥ Ataḥ tar akĕlé mamanaḥ tar aṅlé,wètnyān maṅèl makin atīs ta tibā nikaŋ hrū,saŋ nīla maṅkin aparö tuwi wèḥ tumindak*21:227:2171*

tandaŋ nirāṙ palu baṅus nikaṅ aśwa méṅas,kèṅĕl cĕṅĕlnya kacĕkĕl ya tikĕl kapĕṅhĕl,runtuḥ rubuḥ kaburubuḥ raŧa saŋ prahasta,dé saŋ kapiprawara nīla ḍinaṇḍa piŋ rwa*21:228:2172*

wruḥ saŋ prahasta Umĕsat ta sirātiśīǥra,sāmbut Ikaŋ muśala sāra putus ya riŋ twas,taṙ kātrĕsan kahilaṅan raŧa tan kagöman,göŋ mānamānasa sirodđata đīrabudđi*21:229:2173*

r-uṇḍoṇḍa taŋ muśala nīla maṅuṇḍa ḍaṇḍa,līlā Ulaḥ nira ta kālih alaḥ sadaṙppa,sakrođa yaṙ pamalu kapwa tatan hanāwyat,wètnyān mahābala Awak nira bajra tulya*21:230:2174*

lāwan nikā kawaca saŋ mapatiḥ prahasta,mokĕt-t-ukĕt ya cumĕkĕḥ sira yaṙ ḍinaṇḍa,saŋ nīla towi wĕsi tulya Awak nirālwat,tātaṙ lĕgö pinalu riŋ muśalāprakampya*21:231:2175*

kabwat nikā taya kanin ri sirāsi kāliḥ,tañ jriḥ siliḥ palu humöŋ paḍa śūra hūmrĕŋ,mālap maluy maluwaran ta parĕŋ Umundur,mindĕṙ sirāmutĕrakĕn muśalograḍaṇḍa*21:232:2176*

patrā niraŋ prawara mantri patiḥ prahasta,tindak nikaŋ suku supatra pĕsatnya śīǥra,Āpan Awak nira maluŋ mawĕlū malambat,masriŋ makas mamĕsi mésyabĕnĕṙ la muṅsir*21:233:2177*

saŋ nīla wèḥ lalitagātra mapatrayūđa,lumpat supatra ya tĕbĕŋ manapak tumindak,māpĕs Ikū nira ya komala lola molaḥ,luṅgaḥ lumuŋ calita dé niṅ aṅin paḍanya*21:234:2178*

sāmpun mapatra Umuwaḥ ta maḍaṇḍa-ḍaṇḍan,nīla prahasta masiluṙ matuguṙ kakĕṙ~tĕg,kāṅgul maṅaṅgul amubat binubat siliḥ gyat,maṅduk dinuk paḍa tibā Umuwaḥ maraṅkĕp*21:235:2179*

kapwāṅusī maputĕran sira tulya cakra,humyus haṅin nira tumūt umutĕṙ ya mādrĕs,roṇḍon lĕbū ya ta mĕlĕk Umilu ƀramanta,tātan katon sira Apan hibĕkan lĕbū-ŋ rāt*21:236:2180*

Indĕṙ nikaŋ prawara mandara riŋ samudra,bun méǥa kapwa sumaput riya kapwa mindĕr,nā tulya saŋ prawara nīla lawan prahasta,posyan nirān paputĕran maduluṙ lĕbu m~lĕk*21:237:2181*

mwaŋ lwiṙ nirān silih-usī kadi cakra mindĕr,miṅsor umiṇḍuhur alaḥ paḍa kapwa daṙppa,tonan tinūtakĕn-anūtakĕn os-ahosyan,mamriḥ mataṇḍaṅan ataṇḍiṅan iŋ kađīran*21:238:2182*

saŋ nīla nīti sira nitya mamèti cidra,śīǥrānusī sira mĕsat tumĕḍun prahasta,yapwan prahasta I-ruhuṙ kapi nīla miṅsor,tulyāyunan riṅ ayunan puliṅañ jugādrĕs*21:239:2183*

piṅsoṙ niraŋ prawara nīla rikān panīti,sāmbut tikaŋ watu magöŋ kadi bajra riŋ kas,ndā tan katon r-alap ikaŋ watu wèt nirādrĕs,yatnomĕsat sira muwaḥ Umusī prahasta*21:240:2184*

mantri prahasta tumĕḍun Inusī Umiṅsor,ṅkānan kacidra tinibān watu tan papiŋ rwan,kāntèp gulū ya kapĕtĕk hulu śīṙṇna bĕntar,multak ṅ-utĕk mata kawiṅsil adoḥ kasiṅsal*21:241:2185*

waṅkwaŋ tikĕl kawaca yénĕmasan masāk ya,rāḥnyèṅ awak ya sumirat kadi đātu muñcar,tātan pahī lawan ikaŋ wĕsi yan tinunwan,maƀrā mabāŋ ya pinupuḥ sumirat Apuynya*21:242:2186*

sāmpun prahasta mati mūṙkꝁa mahāwrĕg awrī,kagyat kagöman umulat muliṅānya méṅas,saŋ nīla ƀinna maṅusī manuruŋ maṅambaḥ,siṅhopamāmuru kĕnas juga duṙniwāṙyya*21:243:2187*

{Upendrabajra}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
katūb ikaŋ rākṣasa tan pasāra,muliḥ kabèḥ tan papuliḥ paḍāṅliḥ,mĕhāḥ mahosyan tama riŋ kaḍatwan,tĕkānaṅis mājar-ajaṙ ya wrĕtta*21:244:2188*

#dwāwiṅśati saṙggaḥ#
<rajanī>:22
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
^22/1/2168.
Aŧa winaraḥ ta saŋ daśamuké pati saŋ mapatiḥ,makin atakut manaḥ nira-nirantara kampita ya,gupu-gupurĕn siré gupura niŋ pura yaṙ paṅadĕg,tuwi mawĕnĕs Ikaŋ muꝁa wawaŋ ta sirāṙ pawuwus*22:1:2189*

sahana-hananta rākṣasa wuṅu pwa Ariṅku gugaḥ,Ikana si kumƀakaṙṇna wiparīta dahat maturū,maṅinak-inak tayāṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn riya tulya kĕbo,sinaputan iŋ tamaḥ taman akiṅkiṅ atīta wuta*22:2:2190*

daśamuꝁa nā ta liŋ nira madĕg sahananya kabèḥ,tĕka manabĕḥ ta kèṇḍaṅ anulup kalaśaṅka wanèḥ,murawa tuwuŋ rĕgaŋ paḍahi mandra mahāswara lèn,ya ta tinabĕḥnya ǥūṙṇnita parĕŋ masamūha humuŋ*22:3:2191*

patĕmu ni śabda niŋ paḍahi ǥora gĕrĕḥ juga ya,karatala tālaśabda nikanaŋ kala tulya gĕlap*22:4:2192*
punar api tan hanāta rinĕṅö nira saŋ winuṅu,malĕs alisuḥ taṅan niṅ anabĕḥ murawāwurahan*22:5:2193*

haru-hara tékanaŋ mamuṅu saŋ winuṅunya makög,paḍa ta Umĕtwakĕn kira-kiranya hanan panahut,hanan anĕwĕk rikaŋ kuku-kukuḥ ta kukūnya pupug,hana maṅarug-Arugnya kapĕluk tĕmahan ruwaga*22:6:2194*

hana ta watĕk prawīra mahawan kuda śīǥragami,mamuṅu parĕŋ maṅambah i-Awak nira tan maharis,limaṅ atusaŋ liman tuwi Inambahakĕn ri sira,maṅupuk-upuk hiḍĕp nira rikaŋ panapaknya suka*22:7:2195*

wwara raŧa paṙbwatopama magöŋ ya Inambahakĕn,mamisili tulya tékana guluŋ-guluṅanya lanā,pakĕna ni śabda niŋ paḍahi ǥora Uyūyu juga,makin atĕgö pakög nira humuŋ gumuruḥ gumĕtĕr*22:8:2196*

tuwi ya tĕlas ṅ-upāya kinĕnākĕn anékawiđi,tatan ika hétu niŋ mawuṅu kāwit-awit juga ya,I tĕka ni paŋliliṙ nira ya hétu nirāṙ pawuṅu,dadi Inusap niraŋ mata-mataṅhi wawaŋ mawuwus*22:9:2197*

Aparan iké prayojana mataŋnya Akug winuṅu,dadi sumahuṙ sahaṙṣa sahananya kabèḥ praṇata,Ikana ta Ājña saŋ praƀu kinonakĕn osakĕna,ri tĕka nikaŋ musuḥ mati siraŋ mapatiḥ matuha,
ya Ikana liŋ nikaŋ bala kabèḥ ya makon tumama,dadi marahup sirāhyas asalin masĕkaṙ majĕnu,krama Umasö sĕkul kĕpĕ-kĕpèl nira yaṙ pawuṅu,Iwu-Iwu lakṣa koṭi kukusan ya ta hĕnti pisan*22:10:2198*

kĕla-kĕla māṅsa siṅha haliman ya winaṅkrah atap,saka sapuluḥ puluk pisan ikaŋ kṣaṇikān pinaṅan,Ikaṅ ininum-Inum sira gucinya kunaŋ pira taŋ,pisan ininum nirādƀuta masāt rikanaŋ sakarĕŋ*22:11:2199*

huwus akĕpĕl-kĕpĕl dadi masuk maśilā ri dalĕm,satama nirān tĕmu-ŋ kaka kakiṅkiṅanāṅĕn-aṅĕn,muꝁa mawĕnĕs mahos hati kĕtĕg-kĕtĕgĕn rumaras,panĕṅĕr i-göŋ nikaŋ ƀaya wuwus nira manda malon*22:12:2200*

{tiḍak dikĕtahui}
– – ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :9:
Antĕnku halib moha kita,nidrā wiparītāt paturū,tan wruḥ tĕka śatrunta kariḥ,mwaŋ wānara wadwānya sumār*22:13:2201*

makwéḥ mati dényèŋ palagan,mitraǥna si kumƀādi nikā,đūmrākṣa wirūpākṣa wanèḥ,Ākampana lāwan praǥasa*22:14:2202*

yékādi nikaŋ wīra pĕjaḥ,śūrātiśayèŋ śakti daṅū,mwaŋ saŋ mapatiḥ wrĕdđa tuwi,sāmpun mati tātan pabiṣa*22:15:2203*

Aṅhiŋ kita nāŧāṅkwa Ari,mraṣṭākĕna śatrunta kabèḥ,rāmāđama yékān pisani,mwaŋ lakṣmaṇa sugrīwa pusus*22:16:2204*

nké k-tona Asiḥ tāt makaka,yan śīṙṇna musuhtālilaṅa,wīṙyyanta katonèŋ palagan,lumrā ta yaśantèŋ ƀuwana*22:17:2205*

byaktālaha niŋ dāśaraŧi,Āpañ jaya jātinta daṅā,nya hyaŋ bali ƀaktīri kita,trꜽlokya ya matwaŋ matakut*22:18:2206*

saŋ rāwaṇa sāmpun mawuwus,saŋ Antĕn irāgyā sumahur,tag wruḥ ry-ujaraṅkwéri kita,képwan Aku riŋ déya huwus*22:19:2207*

mwaŋ dona nikaŋ śabda hita,swasŧā ni sawaṙgganta kabèḥ,makwèḥ pwa Ikaŋ wīra pĕjaḥ,tādé kasulākĕnta huwus*22:21:2209*

ṅūnin winaraḥ riŋ rahayu,kālanta mahöm moha kita,sakwèḥ saṅ ataṅguḥ winahil,saŋ mājar-ajaṙ nīti pinid*22:22:2210*

bāhulya hanā taŋ hiḍĕpĕn,maṅsul sawuwus saŋ mawaraḥ,mānanta magöŋ tulya tuli,yékā ta Umuṅgwiŋ taliṅa*22:23:2211*

drĕṣṭānta paminton ri kita,ndā tan kahiḍĕp dènta masiḥ,śabdāmrĕta héman kahilī,n-uṅgwī hrĕdayantāsiluhuŋ*22:25:2213*

Olīṅa ya taṙ w~naŋ matuhā,tan katwaṅa saŋ sāđu kunaŋ,tātan wruha riŋ śāsana wèḥ,ṅkāsamƀawa tātaŋ hiḍĕpa*22:26:2214*

tuŋtuŋ mata riŋ tatwa sira,kahyun nikanaŋ rāt pinuji,tan lèn kaki riŋ réṇa tuwi,sampat saꝑalātaḥ pituhun*22:27:2215*

tapwan pituhu ṅwaŋ matuhā,taṙ ƀakti ri saŋ yogya siwin,sojaṙ nikanaŋ mūrꝁha tinūt,ndaḥ ƀukti ꝑalanyéki ḍatĕŋ*22:28:2216*

tan wruḥ kakarĕm riŋ jalađi,yékiŋ mada malwā madalĕm,loƀanta lanā tulya Alun,rāganta Akĕn ṙyyaknya magöŋ*22:29:2217*

sambéga ya samboŋta bĕlaḥ,jñānanta lunas naṣṭa nanā,ƀaktinta tihaŋ ƀagna tikĕl,śīlanta layaṙ śīṙṇna rujit*22:32:2220*

nā liŋ saŋ Ari kumƀakaṙṇna manĕsĕl sakrođa saŋ rāwaṇa,hāḥ đik đūṙtta niké wĕnaŋ mujarakĕn sāmbĕknya tan paṅgalĕŋ,kot pèt kot hayu tan pataṅguha lawan tak pājarĕn riŋ naya,yapwan wāni lakun pamūk aku kunaŋ wūkĕnmwi yan krođa ko*22:41:2229*

saŋ nīlāṙṣaƀa ganđamādana đanuṙđara gawa-gawaya, 
tārā krĕndana Indrajānu kalawan śatabali winata,mwaŋ saŋ đūmra gawākṣa ƀīmamuꝁa mꜽnda śaraƀa wrĕṣaƀa,saŋ sampāti darīmuꝁādi nikanaŋ prawagabala masö*22:58:2246*

saṅkĕp kapwa maṅuṇḍa paṙbwata wanèḥ mamawa watu magöŋ,tūta-ŋ wānara miśra masraṅ anikĕl kayu-kayu kumupak,kapwā tā Umasö maṅĕmbuli parĕŋ saraƀasa mamalu,naṅduk lèn manibèŋ gunuŋ kaparupuḥ watu malatu-latu*22:59:2247*

taṙ pawyat sira saŋ dinuk ginurumuŋ sana-sini liniput,bĕntaṙ paṙbwata lèn śilātala Asiŋ tĕka ri sira rĕmuk,ƀasmīƀūta lĕbūnya ƀīṣaṇa mĕlĕk gaganatala pĕtĕŋ,mèṅguŋ rāt kumĕtug hudan Awu sĕḍĕŋ nira pinarĕbutan*22:60:2248*

ǥora-ŋ bāyu riwut-śiwat-siwut awū-ŋ bala ya mawalikan,tan ton déśa nikaŋ raṇāṅgaṇa pĕtĕŋ patigaga-gagapi,sakrođodđata kumƀakaṙṇna magalak kadi liman awĕrö,Ambaḥ taŋ kapipil ya kèdĕkan akik saka pitu saka pāt*22:61:2249*

lèn taŋ wré pinaṅan wanèḥ pinipitan hana ta hinapitan,mwaŋ tĕṇḍasnya rĕmĕk-rĕmuk tinĕlisik mata mĕtu kapicil,lèn kontal riṅ awaŋ-ṅ-awaŋ mati tinūb ry-aṅin-aṅiniṅ iruŋ,kwèḥ kèsöp kapisan kagĕntus iṅ upil kadi ta watu ridaŋ*22:62:2250*

śīṙṇna-ŋ wré ginilut hanénigit-igit manahut analuki,ndā tan pamyati tan Ari-n mati kulitnya cacal alulunan,mamwas rāḥnya humīs wanèḥ kaputihan-hana ta katitihan,dé niŋ wuṅkal agöŋ kasaṇḍuṅ i-kaliṅkiṅan i-suku nira*22:63:2251*

jriḥ taŋ wānara tan wĕnaŋ ya mapuliḥ mawĕdi giri-girin*22:64:2252*
n-ton rowaŋnya Asiŋ masö mati Ataḥ taya maluyahurip,tātan rākṣasa paŋhiḍĕpnya Alapanta ya juga sakala,yékonduṙnya muwaḥ katūb kapalupuy taya ta mamulihi*22:65:2253*

tat kālān palayū tikaŋ kapibalāmana-mana-mananā,mojaṙ tékana saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa ri saŋ raǥusutawijaya,yatnā saŋ praƀu haywa nāŧa humĕnĕŋ biṣama tĕmĕn iké,byakta-ŋ wānara hĕntya dénya yadiyan hĕnĕṅakĕna Iké*22:66:2254*

yéko rākṣasa kumƀakaṙṇna jaya riŋ triƀuwana karĕṅö,saŋ hyaŋ Indra huwus Alaḥ baruṇa wꜽśrawaṇa yama tuwi,śaktinyopama bāyubajra rikanaŋ pralaya katatakut,śīṙṇnāsiŋ kahawā ta dénya ya mataŋnya lĕkasana huwus*22:67:2255*

{Upajāti bajra}

minaṅkana śrī naranāŧa rāma,r-ajñéka saŋ wānararāja maswa,sugrīwa mahyun mayaśā rikèŋ praŋ,kinon pwa maṅkin ta sirātihaṙṣa*22:68:2256*

dawut Ikaŋ wrĕkṣa sahīṅan iŋ göŋ,tĕkā ya sātus takuraŋ Ukuṙnya,gamƀīra gambiṙnya lawan dawānya,bajropama twasnya Atīta riŋ kas*22:69:2257*

tilil ya taṅkil ya sakol milĕt ya,walū kumĕṇḍuŋ mawilĕt ri pāŋnya,pĕgat karantan kadudut ḍawutnya,banaspatinyān mawĕnĕs kagöman*22:70:2258*

r-uṇḍoṇḍa tékaŋ kayu ǥorarūpa,kadīkanaŋ takṣaka nāgarāja,raṅgaḥ nikā wwadnya ya tèlatanya,tāmbinya malwā pamiwiknya tulya*22:71:2259*

babak-babak ƀinna kulitnya makras,Akĕn sisiknyādƀuta kaṙkkaśākral,lĕmaḥ nikā wwadnya mĕlĕk lĕbūnya,ya téka Uśwāsa wiṣopamanya*22:72:2260*

tandaŋ nikā saŋ kapirāja tandwa,duk tékanaŋ rākṣasa kumƀakaṙṇna,tātaṙ pahī mwaŋ garuḍātirodra,mantīṅakĕn nāga rikaŋ girindra*22:73:2261*

hyaṅ indra tulyā nika saŋ kapīndra,nāŋ wrĕkṣa paṅduk nira yéka bajra,saŋ kumƀakaṙṇnācala mèru tulya,đīrātĕguḥ niścala niṙwikāra*22:74:2262*

{prahaṙṣiṇī}

ndā tapwan wiǥani siraŋ dinuk Akampya,saŋ sugrīwa sira wawaŋ muwaḥ ta maṅduk,riŋ wrĕkṣātiśaya wiśéṣa sāra riŋ twas,ndā tan pamyati juga puḥ pupug kawaṅsul*22:75:2263*

maṅkin krođa ta magalak siraŋ kapīndra,mindĕṙ taŋ mata mawĕlū halis ya kum~rut,maṅhrĕŋ rodra sira maṅaŋ maṅékapāda,mwaŋ ḍaŋṣṭrā nira lumarap lanā kilatnya*22:76:2264*

molaḥ tékana ta Ikū nirādawāgöŋ,rūg taŋ wrĕkṣa sakaparĕk tĕbĕŋ kahambĕŋ,sāmbut tékana ya huwus rĕbaḥ pukaḥ kwèḥ,kānan kéri taṅan irān paganti maṅduk*22:77:2265*

ndā taṙ cāla ta sira saŋ dinuk manaṅgul,mankin Ujwala Atiƀīṣaṇātirodra,tulyāpuy sĕḍĕṅ umurub magöŋ pracaṇḍa,śīṙṇnāsiŋ tĕka riya tan paśéṣa hĕnti*22:78:2266*

wètnyān duṙbbala baribin dinuk pinaṇḍĕm,līlātaḥ sira mamĕniŋ ta konta tīkṣṇa,ḍaṇḍanyātiśaya kinaṇḍa-kaṇḍa riŋ mās,twas-twas niŋ wĕsi Iwu lakṣa koṭi-koṭi*22:79:2267*

huntunyādƀuta kadi bajra tan mayākas,maƀrā yan pinutĕrakĕn murub dilaḥnya,tulyanyékana ta sihuŋ ƀaṭāra kāla,kālanyān suka maṅigĕl maṅaŋ maṅan rāt*22:80:2268*

maṅkin yādƀuta Umurub lipuŋ putĕṙnya,jwālā niŋ kawaca mawās lanān kasĕnwan,mwaŋ mérūpama juga Ujwalān katéjan,dé niŋ dwādaśaśata sūṙyya riŋ yugānta*22:81:2269*

maṅsö sāhasa sira daṙppa yaṙ paṅonta,pyaḥ saŋ wānara wararāja yénarāraḥ,mèḥ kontā ḍatĕṅa ri saŋ kapīndra wīra,ṅkānan yatna dadi mĕsat ta saŋ hanūmān*22:82:2270*

sāmbut taŋ lipuṅ atiśīǥra yèka humyus,saṅké göŋnya dadi pinaṅkwakĕn pinuṇḍut,luṅhā riŋ gagana sirāṙ tikĕllakĕn ya,puṅgèl-puṅgĕlakĕn ikā tĕṅaḥnya riŋ tūr*22:83:2271*

mahyā-ŋ wré sahana-hananya kādƀutāwū,hāh-āḥ māruti winuwusnya wīra riŋ praŋ,lāwan ǥūṙṇnita rikanāṅ awaŋ-ṅ-awaŋ sök,dé saŋ sidđawara humuŋ manāđukāra*22:84:2272*

saŋ hyaŋ Indra sira mulat Atīta tuṣṭa,kapwāṅastuti sira liŋnya sāđu dibya,Āpan ṅūni sira masoṙ huwus palaṇḍuŋ,dé niŋ konta mataṅ ikā prahaṙṣacitta*22:85:2273*

pahyā niŋ sakala jagat kabèḥ ya matri,héwa-ŋ rākṣasa kalawīra kumƀakaṙṇna,méraŋ tékana pinawūwakĕn masĕṅhit,sakrođāṙ dadi mamupak ta paṙbwatāgöŋ*22:86:2274*

śīǥrékāna balaṅakĕn ri saŋ kapīndra,rĕñcĕm mūṙccita sira yaṙ tibā kalĕṅgak,tātan wruḥ sira pinalaywakĕn pinuṇḍut,dé niŋ rakṣasa warawīra kumƀakaṙṇna*22:87:2275*

byakta ta hĕntya niŋ kapibalān hĕnĕṅakĕna Iké,rākṣasa kumƀakaṙṇna waḍawāmuꝁa muꝁa nikana,!=
nā ta mataŋnya patyana ta dé narapati huwusĕn,liŋ nira saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa manaṅguhi maṅasihi rāt*23:1:2279*

rāǥawa lakṣmaṇèŋ kṣaṇa madĕg parĕṅ anihaṅakĕn,lakṣmaṇa pūṙwwakāŋlĕpasakĕn śarawara dumilaḥ,sāk kawacanya śīṙṇna makuṭanya kanaka pinanaḥ,maṅkin amūk si mūṙkꝁa Umasö tan awĕdi pĕjaha*23:2:2280*

niścaya saŋ raǥūttama tumon ya mari makawaca,hrū si Amoǥa sañjata daṅū lagi linĕpasakĕn,yéka matī kara triśira dūṣaṇa rikanaṅ alas,nā pamanaḥ nirériya samantara Inigit-igit*23:3:2281*

göŋ ni wĕtisnya karwa pinanaḥ kaŧam api ya pĕgat,tūṙnya ya paŋlakunya wĕkasan lumaku makĕdĕpĕk,n-uṇḍa taṅ ugraḍaṇḍa dumilaḥ wĕsi kati ya sakol,wāhu mamalwa liŋnya pinanaḥ ta ya ri takĕlĕkan*23:4:2282*

timpali saṇḍaṅanya ri tĕṅĕn tuhun i-kiwa hana,sāmbutakĕn tikaŋ kayu magöŋ ya ta pinakagadā,wyaṙŧa kasèp pĕgat t-inuwahan pinanahan i-kiwan,tan pataṅan huwus tuhun awak hulu jaga ya hana*23:5:2283*

kabwatakĕn Ikān pinapasan makin agalak ataḥ,tan karĕrĕp matanya dumilaḥ kadi Apuy umurub,rodra sihuŋnya tīkṣṇa makilat Umaṅaṅ aṅikikan,ƀūta kuƀāṇḍa pūtana paḍanya ya kagiri-giri*23:6:2284*

kāla nikā Aṅaŋnya pinanaḥ muꝁa ya hinibĕkan,sök ta tutuknya tan wĕnaṅ aśabda tuwi kapĕpĕkan,yan pinanaḥ muwaḥ pinisanan ta ya Inarah-araḥ,rākṣasa tan salaḥ ya tumanĕm hati ya ta kinĕnan*23:7:2285*

Aŧa sāmpuniŋ suƀaga kumƀakaṙṇna mati dé niraŋ raǥusuta,manaṅis ta saŋ daśamuꝁātitībra wiparītacitta saƀaya,maṅadĕg ta saŋ Anak anuŋ manūti ri saṅ indrajit ya mapuliḥ,triśiraḥ sirātuha tumūt narāntaka hana trikāya sawanèḥ*23:10:2288*

wwara déwatāntaka kapātnya kapwa ya mahāprawīra taruṇa,rwa Amaŋnya rākṣasa rumākṣa yālaga bĕtaḥ rikaŋ samara ya,karĕṅö si mantaka ṅaranya riŋ samara matta matri ya parĕŋ,mawĕrö warĕg laga lagi n-panorakĕn asiŋ musuḥ lagi-lagi*23:11:2289*

sa-Asönyanak nikana saŋ daśānana nanā katūb kapibala,pinapag nikaŋ wahu siṅī rĕbaḥ ya rinĕbut Apan huwus aṅèl,Umadĕg saṅ aṅgada gadādi ta pwa ginĕgö humöŋ hati nira,Ikanaŋ narāntaka tinandaṅan nira minuṣṭi naṣṭa kapisan*23:12:2290*

triśiraḥ trikāya ya makāya mamrih apuliḥ masĕṅhit abutĕŋ,kalawan Arinya ta si déwatāntaka tĕkān paṅĕmbuli parĕŋ,kaliput saṅ aṅgada tuwin luput sira widagđa đīra gapitan,wihikan milag sira humöṙ ḍinaṇḍa drĕḋa tan kĕḍap mata nira*23:13:2291*

kapi nīla lèn pawanaputra śīǥra tumuluŋ saṅ aṅgada masö,giriśrĕṅga yékana sinaṅga sañjata daṅū taman pamuruṅi,triśiraḥ siréka mamanaḥ rikaŋ śarawarāstra yānarawata,mapĕpĕs pupug kapalupuy Apan papagakĕn rikaŋ gunuṅ akas*23:14:2292*

dumilaḥ gadā wĕsi ni déwatāntaka tĕkapnya yāmalu lalis,mapupuḥ pupū lawan igā gulū ya ginĕlisnya tan ya kahiḍĕp,baribin ta saŋ pawanaputra dénya dinudut dinīna nira ya,kinuṭuk ya naṣṭa wĕkasan minuṣṭi tan iniṣṭi mātya linaran*23:15:2293*

mwaṅ amaŋnya matta mati dé niraŋ śaraƀa tan pasāra ginadā,kalawan Ikaŋ samaramatta nīla Umipis rikaŋ gunuṅ agöŋ, 
triśiraḥ saroṣa maṅusiṙ yaśāmutĕrakĕn krĕtāla makilat,kawĕnaŋ pwa pinraṅ i-tĕwĕknya dé saṅ anilātmajénalihakĕn*23:16:2294*

kawĕśas makas taṅ atikāya māhyuna Ikā laganya masuwè,kuda sèwu yékana humiṙ raŧanya kadi paṙbwatādƀuta magöŋ,wray akik lacak ya kapicil ri cakra nikanaŋ raŧādrĕs aṅusī,hana kèdĕkan sinahut iŋ kudākidat akuṇḍah amrih adudut*23:17:2295*

karuṇā ta saŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇèŋ wray asakit winūk winalĕsan,Inasö nirā taṅ atikāya kāya sira kapwa śakti mamanaḥ,kumisik panaḥ nira lawan panaḥnya maharas mawantah atĕmu,dumilaḥ parĕŋ mapulihan rikaŋ gagana tan hanāmyati gĕsöŋ*23:18:2296*

hana sora lèn hana mahéndrasāyaka Iṣīka pāwakaśara,ya panaḥnya lèn ya pamanaḥ nirātĕmu taman hanāta maṅani,matutuṙ ta saŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇè kamalajāstra śūrawijaya,yatikāmatīkaṅ atikāya tan tuhu makāya dé nira pĕjaḥ*23:19:2297*

sapĕjaḥ nikaŋ Anak anuŋ Umaṅsĕ kalawan n-amaŋnya kawĕnaŋ,kawĕnaŋ hiḍĕp nikana saŋ daśānana huwus mawās pati nira,nirapékṣa riŋ pamĕnaṅan mapök hati mapakṣa mātya taya lèn,taya lèn Anak nira wanèḥ saṅ indrajit aniṅgilis ya kawĕkas*23:20:2298*

wĕkasaṅkwa téki bapa mātya tāku yadiyan musuḥ mamĕnaṅa,wĕnaṅāku maŋlawapa rāma sèwu ramĕsĕnkwa śīṙṇna huwusĕn,huwusĕn lumakwaku makoliha-ŋ makulamitra wānara haraḥ,harasènkwa rūga yadiyan gunuŋ kimuta yan manuṣya kaluṣa*23:21:2299*

ruṣa rūkṣa tulya ya śaśā hanĕŋ Alas-alas Umĕṅgĕp atapa,tapa tan tuhu n-tapasi pāpa duṙyyaśa ya hiṅśaka brata baka,wiku hantĕlū swaṅ aputiḥ ri hèŋ pila-pilū hisinya mahaṅi,ya paḍā ni rāma rumasèŋ bratāmati-matī mataŋnya ya pati*23:22:2300*

ya huwus saṅ indrajit asiṅhanāda maṅadĕg suđīra magalak,mari saŋ bapālara tumon ya rodra kadi siṅha śīǥra lumaku,mĕtu riŋ raṇāṅgaṇa huwus mahoma Inanugrahan raŧa magöŋ,kalawan wimohanaśarāstra yékana pawèḥ ƀaṭāra Iriya*23:23:2301*

I wĕtunya riŋ raṇa surup ƀaṭāra rawi Anđakāra sumaput,daśadéśa kapwa ya pĕtĕŋ sadaṙppa ta saṅ indrajit puji-puji,ya manon taman hana tumon kaśaktiniṅ adrĕśya tantra pinasaŋ,pinanaḥnya taŋ wray ikanaŋ wimohanaśarāturū ya karĕrĕp*23:24:2302*

sapijĕṙ nikaŋ kapibalāturū gumuyu ṅ-indrajit baśa-baśa,taya saṅśayanya mĕjahi-ŋ makög curi tĕkapnya tan pracura ya,śata lakṣa koṭi mati dénya wānara nirantarān panahi ya,Ikanaŋ madoḥ ri sira saŋ raǥūttama-taman hana wray ahurip*23:25:2303*

wray anuŋ wiśéṣa maṅaran ya téka maparö ri saŋ raǥusuta,ya jugāhurip kunaṅ ikā matanya maharip kĕnèṅ aji sirĕp,tuwi saŋ raǥūttama-tamaṙ salaḥ rikanaṅ astra mohanaśara,karĕrĕp karöpan aṅajap parĕŋ maguliṅan lawan Ari nira*23:26:2304*

ri huwus narāṙyya kĕna mohanāstra malayū muliḥ si maliṅan,ri takutnya kawruhana dé niraŋ bapa wiƀīṣaṇāmalĕsana,sira taṙ kĕnèṅ aji sirĕp tamaṙ kĕlu masāmparan sapu mata,mata nitya Ujwala mataṅhi jāgra jaga yatna nīti nipuṇa*23:27:2305*

Aji dīpasañjata na nāma-nāmalahakĕn Ikaŋ Aji sirèp,ya Ikā hané sira mataŋnya taṙ kĕna rikaŋ wimohanaśara,ya lanā mĕnĕŋ maṅĕn-aṅĕn nikaŋ Aji nirantarāmrih ajapa,tumahāŋ mahākalana Indrajit ya ta tĕka Apañ curi raṇa*23:28:2306*

tĕka tandwa saṅśaya sirāmasaŋ pwa ya suluḥ katon ta nrĕpati,kadi rūpa niŋ kĕna piśāca kāwiśa muꝁāmĕrĕḥ mata malik,Umĕkĕḥ milūmilu salaḥ hiḍĕp kadi hiḍĕp nikaŋ kapasukan,ginugaḥ kinon marahupātutuṙ sira Uđāni māri karĕrĕp*23:29:2307*

tuwi saŋ kapīndra ginugaḥ marutsuta nilāṅgadāta winuṅu,dumĕliŋ sirāṙdđa mawĕliŋ kataṅgama manon suluḥ paḍa miṅis,tumulaṙ suluḥ nikana saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa katon tikaŋ mati matap,sahananya wānara madoḥ huwus pinĕjahan nikaŋ curi raṇa*23:30:2308*

Atitībra kāruṇa ta saŋ raǥūttama tumon ikaŋ maguliṅan,kapatinya tan kapati niŋ prawīra minaliŋ-maliŋ mati pijĕr,dadi saŋ marutsuta kinon maṅambila mahoṣađāmrĕtamaya,maluyā hurip śawa sawèt ni sidđi nikanaŋ mahosađilatā*23:31:2309*

kahanān ikaŋ paramahoṣađī śikara niŋ gunuŋ himagiri,tuwuhan niṅ oṣađilatā ṅaranya karĕṅö wiśalyakariṇī,mrĕtajīwanī braṇitasanđinī ya ta kinonakĕn susupana,tamataṙ wihaŋ lumaku saŋ marutsuta mibĕṙ tĕkèŋ himagiri*23:32:2310*

sira ta pwa yaṙ wruh irikaŋ mahoṣađi gĕlāna képwan aṅadĕg,wĕkasan pupak ta Ikaṅaŋ gunuŋ n-ibĕrakĕnya sakṣaṇa ḍatĕŋ,saha mūla mūlya milu taŋ mahoṣađi katūt katon ya tamalaḥ,Inalap ta dé nira narāṙyya yéka panirām irèŋ mati kabèḥ*23:33:2311*

satitis niṅ oṣađi rikaŋ paratra sahananya kapwa mawuṅu,murĕṅaŋ samāṅhwab umusap matanya kadi tāturū warurutĕn,dinilātnya ṅ-āmrĕta ya mātra muntaraṅ asiṅhanāda ya parĕŋ,kalalaḥ manaḥnya maluyèŋ raṇāṅgaṇa paḍāṅgĕgö palu-palu*23:34:2312*

ri sawèt ni héwa ni manaḥ nikaŋ kapibalān pinatyan aturū,n-apuyīkanaŋ nagara rāwaṇojwalita tan paśéṣa ya gĕsöŋ,bala saŋ daśānana kapūhan adƀuta tumon kaḍatwan atunu,makucĕm saṅ indrajit asiḥ wawaŋ kawalĕsan mulat kawĕnĕsan*23:35:2313*

mĕtu taŋ rwa sānak aduluṙ si kumƀa kalawan nikumƀa mapuliḥ,kadi kumƀa tambaga matanya ƀīṣaṇa mabāŋ wiśāla mawĕlū,tuwi kumƀakaṙṇna makaputra yātiśaya göŋnyawaknya sagunuŋ,saguṇèŋ raṇāṅgaṇa daṅū taman hana Anuŋ wĕnaŋ mapaga ya*23:36:2314*

wwara rākṣasottama ṅaranya kampana Akampanākya nipuṇa,kalawan prajaṅǥa śi wilohitākṣa karĕṅö đwajākṣa sawanèḥ,ya tikā rumākṣa si nikumƀa kumƀa Umakuŋ watĕk wrayalaha,Alah olih iŋ raṇa daṅū mamūkana Ikaŋ manaḥ mamĕnaṅa*23:37:2315*

sapamūk nikaŋ pitu pĕpĕk mapakṣa pati tan panolih apagĕḥ,mapanas panūbnya kadi Antakāgni Umurub muruŋ kapibala,bala wānarāsiṅ inasönya śūra kasuruŋ surākṣa kasĕsĕr,milu mosah-osik apasaḥ kadi pwa ya tasik surud Umari sök*23:38:2316*

nrĕpaputra rāǥawa wawaŋ makon sira makolihékaṅ aburu,taya lèn saṅ aṅgada kĕdö sirāta paragul lanā mamulihi,drĕḋaƀakti satya ri siraŋ raǥūttama-taman pahīṅan iṅ asiḥ,tar aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn kapatiniŋ bapāparapacāra cāmpur iṅ ulaḥ*23:39:2317*

kalawan winèḥ ta yuwarāja rāja sadrĕśāṅinak kadi ratu,ya dumèḥ sirāmriha rikaŋ raṇāṅgaṇa kadi priya wruh iṅ asiḥ,satatékanaŋ rĕṇa rinākṣa riŋ hati rinūpa paṙhyaṅan agöŋ,sira saŋ raǥūttama maṇik pratiṣṭa ri dalĕm Inaṙccaṇa lanā*23:40:2318*

mapagĕḥ pwa ƀakti niraṅ aṅgadāṙ pisani taŋ Akampana paśu,kasikĕp si kampana wanèḥ sinĕmsĕmakĕn iŋ śilātala makas,tuluy i-prajaṅǥa tinĕwĕk nirèŋ karatalé kiwān kawĕlĕlö,tinĕpak muꝁanya kapĕtĕk Iruŋnya kapicil matanya kawicil*23:41:2319*

r-alapi đwajékana ta si đwajākṣa hinabĕt nirèŋ đwaja tibā,dinĕkuŋ tĕṅaḥ ni walakaŋnya yaṙ pulirakĕn gulūnya pinĕgat,dwiwiđāwiḍaŋ drĕḋa Ikaŋ ḍuḍāṙ pamaḍa ṅ-uṇḍa ḍaṇḍa manulak,si wilohitākṣa kadi takṣakèŋ galuk amūk rĕmuk ya pinalu*23:42:2320*

kapi mꜽnda mindĕr amutĕṙ gadā Umilu maŋlagé haga-hagaḥ,kapĕgan sirān pinanahan n-i kumƀa sagilān pĕjaḥ kĕna taji,sira Aṙdđa duṙbbala rikaŋ raṇāṅgaṇa lanā sirénadak-adak,dumadak tumandaṅ amutĕṙ gadā bali kariḥ sirāsi malara*23:43:2321*

kabaran saṅ aṅgada tumon paman pwa nira mꜽnda mandaśaraṇa,giriśrĕṅga yékana sinaṅga sèṅgita masiṅgi tulya tar aṅèl,Inarā-haraḥ muꝁa ni kumƀa dé nira saṅ aṅgadāṙ pamugari,niyatān pĕjaḥ ya tinibān gunuŋ yadiya tan wruhāmalĕsana*23:44:2322*

wihikan pwa yèŋ praharaṇa pratīpa na ṅaran niṅ astra panulak,kawaluy gunuŋ kawalikut saṅ aṅgada bali pwa tuhwamalĕsa,malisuḥ taṅan nira-nirantarāmaluyakĕn nikaŋ pamugari,mawaluy-waluy gati nikaŋ gunuŋ kadi macaṅkramāmija-mijaḥ*23:45:2323*

kapirāja lajjita tumon kawalwan ira bāliputra kabalik,takarin sirātah umatī si kumƀa kapisan minuṣṭi nira ya,mapuliḥ kakanya si nikumƀa ƀinna maṅawasŧa riŋ palu-palu,pawanātmajādƀuta Alāp-alap juga r-alap gadānya tinikĕl*23:46:2324*

kadi siṅha yaṙ sahut ikā gulū ni Anikumƀa tulya haliman,U lukān imān i-kapatinya dé nikana saŋ samīraṇasuta,pati niŋ rwa sānak ahĕnĕk manaḥ ni kalulanya līna kalulun,binuruñjakĕn milu jurunya duṙjjana julig taman n-ilu pĕjaḥ*23:47:2325*

{suwaṅśapattra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :18:
daśamuꝁa késisan kasiharĕp kawĕkas aṅililan,Akara-karā tĕkā nikanaṅ antaka ri sira huwus,ri pati nikaŋ prawīra wiratī dadi yar aṅĕn-aṅĕn,kapasukan āmbĕk āpĕs anaṅis ta sira Udahani*23:48:2326*

Ah-ah aparan prayojana nikaŋ sukan inaṅĕn-aṅĕn*23:49:2327*
Apa pakĕnā nikaŋ wiƀawa ƀaṅga wirasa rinasan,tuhu-tuhu māwasāna wiṣa taŋ wiṣaya maṅawaśa,si pati sipat-sipat niṅ ahurip syapa luput irikā*23:50:2328*

nahan ikanādi niŋ Ujar adīna dinadak i-hati,wahu-wahu yaṙ kĕnèŋ lara-larad siga si galak alök,dadi saṅ anak manaṅguhi manuṅgĕṅa riṅ aṅĕn-aṅĕn,kalaki-lakinya riŋ raṇa ya tékana lĕkasakĕna*23:51:2329*

huwus amaṅun manaḥ nira saṅ indrajit aṅaji hĕnĕŋ,tar awĕdi mātya matri ta sirāṅusira kapuruṣan,mĕtu mapuliḥ palaṙ kapalisa-ŋ musuh awisa pisan,Alaha mĕnaŋ maganti ya gatāgata gati nikana*23:52:2330*

sawĕtu saṅ indrajit-jitasaƀā suƀaga saha bala,lawan ikanaŋ striyottama-taman dadi sira kapasaḥ,Anakĕbi dibyarūpa ǥariṇī nira Asama-sama,wĕka-wĕka Apsarī saꝑala dibya sira tiru-tirun*23:53:2331*

pitu ta sirāpisānak aduluṙ drĕḋa hati matĕguḥ,manah anulus rikaŋ pati-patibrata tar alaṅ-alaŋ,tuhu-tuhu waṅśajāti malilaŋ Ikanaṅ aṅĕn-aṅĕn,muliha riṅ indraloka maluy āpsari suƀaga muwaḥ*23:54:2332*

paḍa ta suđīra wīra Ikanaŋ bala maluy umasö,gaja raŧa sāraŧi stiŧi titaḥnya tahu tan inutus,satata tikān titik makana riŋ raṇa pakĕna lanā,butirĕn awaknya woknya makusut suku ya bakikulĕn*23:55:2333*

sapalaga niŋ balā mabalaṅan makĕkĕr akalaṅan,makaparupuḥ ri puṅkuran i-wiṅkiṅ analibukuṅi,kapibala Aprakampya kapahūṅ inamah-amah amīk,pinarĕbutan Inambulan inumbanan uwal anuwul*23:56:2334*

watĕk apapan tĕkānĕwĕk apan tahu turuṅ inamĕs,masinapi ƀūṣaṇanya masinaŋ sana-sini lumarap,mahulap ikaŋ watĕk kapibalān wulati ya mahalĕp,kadi tuhu-tuhwa tan n-alaha yan parĕṅ anuwul anūb*23:57:2335*

lawan agalaḥ manimbaṅi manāmbĕhi halĕp aṅiriŋ,kagiri-giri n-tihaŋ ri harĕpan niṅ apapan aparö,haga-haga tékanaŋ wray agalak ginulumi ginalak,wahu kaguliŋ linūd iṅ apapan n-apan agalak ataḥ*23:58:2336*

saṅ apapan aṙdđa daṙppa maharĕp r-ahata mamuguti,winatu ya riŋ śilātala tikĕl saka tĕlu kaguliŋ,Ayak-ayak iŋ kuyaŋ-kuyaṅ asāk kayu-kayu pamalu,hana katibān gunuŋ matĕmahan ta payag arawayan*23:59:2337*

watĕk agadā madan ya maṅadĕḥ mapapan apan aṅèl,Ikanaṅ alori lot ya mamupuḥ mamalu maṅimulu,makrĕtala matri kinrakan ikaŋ kapi ya kapĕlĕṅĕn,naṅawur añakra makrama ṅ-acakra kakrĕcik aṅĕné*23:60:2338*

pijĕr atuguṙ bĕtaḥ bala saṅ indrajit atĕguh ataḥ,sira kalalaḥ ri kālaha nikaŋ musuh awisa masö,nrĕpasuta lakṣmaṇékana lawan nira maṅadu yaśa,paḍa kinawiḥ riṅ astra nipuṇĕŋ panah apanas atīs*23:61:2339*

praŧama narāṙyya lakṣmaṇa huwus mamanahi rumuhun,hana ta ya bāruṇāstra pamanaḥ nira salilamaya,maya Ikanaŋ tĕgal taya ṅ-upāya riya dadi tasik,bala niraṅ indrajit kalĕbu duṙbbala paḍa kapĕlĕk*23:62:2340*

jwalita murub śarāgni pamalĕs nira maṅalad-alad,ya ta Umuruŋ wway adway alayū kapanasan anasar,huwus ikanaŋ wway adway ikanaŋ Apuy-apuy apuliḥ,ri taya nikaŋ tahĕn ya tamatan patahĕn apulihan*23:63:2341*

maluy amanaḥ saṅ indrajit anéka mĕtu riya mulĕk,prakaśita Āsurāstra ya mamĕtwakĕn asi muśala,paraśu gadā triśūla masuluŋ-suluṅ adulur apuy,wugari halaŋ mawoṙ watu lĕbū mĕlĕk alatu-latu*23:64:2342*

Apa paṅalaḥ rikā hana mahéśwaraśara-śaraṇa,panah umaṅan Asiŋ pinakasañjata linĕpasakĕn,ya ta pamanaḥ niraŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇa maṅalahakĕn,hilaṅ apasaḥ sa-sañjata saṅ indrajit asiṅ umĕsat*23:65:2343*

kapariƀawān maṅèl kapuritĕn satata pinanahan,kucĕm aku liŋ nirāṙ daṅu-daṅū bali kari balawān,gaja raŧa Aśwa sāraŧi saṅ indrajit inarah-araḥ,pralaya-layaḥ kabèḥ nirawaśéṣa sira juga salaḥ*23:66:2344*

Aṅilil anéka paṭṭaka paḍāmrihata sira masö,taya raŧa tā paśāraŧi ya kéwala ta sira mamūk,dadi pinanaḥ riṅ indraśara rudraśara winarayaŋ,ya mĕgatakĕn gulū nikana saŋ daśawadanasuta*23:67:2345*

kalawan ikā ta ǥāra nira saŋ pitu mati ya kabèḥ,brata nikanaŋ patibrata nahan ya ta ginawayakĕn,mamuji sahaṙṣa saŋ rĕṣi tumon i-kapati rasikā,jĕnu saha puṣpawaṙṣa tumibā satata ya sumawur*23:68:2346*

ri pati saṅ indrajit jaya-jayèŋ gaganatala humuŋ,Umuji saṅ āṙyya lakṣmaṇa wĕnaŋ maṅalapi kasusuk,suka hati niŋ hyaṅ ahyun aṅalĕm-lĕmu-lĕmu magiraŋ,manawurakĕn ta ganđa riṅ awaŋ-ṅ-awaṅ-awaṅi marūm*23:69:2347*

daśawadanātidīnatara tā śaraṇa nira huwus,pati niṅ anak lawan bala kadi pwa kayu tinutuhan,tuhun ikanaŋ Awak hana Iwĕḥ nikana mahuripa,niyata tibā nikāta waduṅĕn nikana saṅ atahĕn*23:70:2348*

taya Ilagan lumakwa malagā juga saꝑala mamūk,mabĕnĕr awās ya ṅ-antakawasāna samara-maraṇa,dadi mari dīna dāni ta manaḥ nira-niratiśaya,Umaluy amuntaraŋ taṅ atakut pĕjah aciha-ciha*23:71:2349*

tumama mahoma riŋ śiwasaƀā grĕha padiwaharan,parama-gurūgra ƀīṣaṇa sirékana Inawatakĕn,mĕtu ta mataṅkil iŋ waruga saŋ dwijawara humaḍaŋ,Umadĕg aśānti maṅgala nagéri pañarita nira*23:72:2350*

kala saha śaṅꝁa śaṅǥaṇi kanānuni mamawa suka,paḍahi paḍāṅiriŋ Ati hatuṙ nikana n-uni parĕŋ,suka hati saŋ daśāsya ri siraŋ dwija majaya-jaya,manawurakĕn ta dāna Atigorawa ri sira kabèḥ*23:73:2351*

bala mabalèm umanti wĕtu saŋ praƀu daśawadana,Upakaraṇèŋ raṇāṅgaṇa huwus hana hinaḍaṅakĕn,pinasuk iraŋ rasuk hana rukuḥ nira kanaka maṇik,dumilah abāŋ sĕnönya mahĕniŋ kadi ta hati nira*23:74:2352*

{wiśwalalita}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
krama Umanèk sirèŋ raŧa magöŋ kinūṣa riṅ ĕmās,kadi ta ya śrĕṅga niŋ giri sumèru kāñcana maya,kuda kadi ratna maṙkata katon awaknya mahijo,ya ta Umadĕg Ikaŋ raŧa sirāta sūṙyya sadrĕśa*23:75:2353*

bala nira ƀāra Ujwala paḍārasuk Inĕmasan*23:76:2354*
ya ta lumiput tumūt marawayan marĕk raŧa nira,wulu ni papanya cāmara miraḥ madanta ya muré,kadi ta ya méǥa yan wahu kĕné sĕnö hyaṅ aruṇa*23:77:2355*

kanaka karat-karatnya kumilat-kilat kagurilap,tabĕ-tabĕhanya ǥūṙṇnita tĕkèŋ diśāntara humuŋ,đwaja kadi waṅkawāsĕmu kuwuŋ-kuwuŋ Ubar-abir,kadi ta hudan magöŋ wiṣa panaḥnya tīkṣṇa mapanas*23:78:2356*

tĕka ta Umaṇḍĕm āṅrĕpa maṅaŋ ya maṅhrik aṅakar,tuwi bala saŋ raǥūttama masö tumindak aṅigĕl,paḍa ta galaknya yan patĕmu kapwa đīra mapupuḥ,kadi bubula-ŋ lĕmaḥ n-inidĕkan matĕmpuh atugur*23:79:2357*

Umĕlĕk ikaŋ lĕbū dadi pĕtĕŋ raṇāṅgaṇa pĕpĕt,taya ta tumon lawan ya majĕmuṙ muṅuṙ-muṅur arok,pati ta masö patiḥnya n-aṅusī Asiŋ tan apiliḥ,sakatĕmu dénya dīna dinudut tĕwĕknya kawatĕk*23:80:2358*

wray aku ta liŋ nikaŋ wray i-paḍanya wānarabala,sy-anu Aku rākṣasa prih aku rākṣa liŋnya sawanèḥ,ḍĕh apa kariḥ Asiŋ sakasikĕp pramāda ya pati,tak aharĕp iŋ hurip pati patĕmwaniŋ saƀuwana*23:81:2359*

makakĕrĕcĕk makik hana maṅaŋ maṅaṅgul anukĕr,hana kawilĕt gulūnya riṅ ikū Ikaŋ kala wanèḥ,kasiku wĕhaŋnya bāp kapisahut sihuŋnya maṅani,kapacilu lèn kapik kapihĕḍĕs tĕḍas kĕna hiḍi*23:82:2360*

paḍa ta nanīnya téka mati rāḥnya rodra humilī,ya ta maḍĕmi-ŋ lĕbū mari mĕlĕk hilaŋ pĕtĕṅ awās,Akara-karā Ikaŋ kalana rākṣasénarah-araḥ,mati saka sèwu śīṙṇna pinanaḥ niraŋ raǥusuta*23:83:2361*

jaga-jaga saŋ daśānana tumon balāṙdđa mananā,raŧa nira śīǥra gumrit umasö Amoǥa kawaluy,pinakanimitta niŋ Alaha riŋ raṇékana huwus,tĕka taṅ aṅin riwut makaduluṙ gagak malimunan*23:84:2362*

{sragđara}
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :21:
ndā taṙ kagyat tar āśā rasika ta saṅ amūk mūṙkꝁa rājā daśāsya,ṅ-kon taŋ wadwāmrihātaḥ krama dadi ta masö saŋ wirūpākṣa nāma,muṅgwiŋ hastin panuṅgaŋ mamawa ta ya lipuŋ tīkṣṇa ƀinnāṙ putĕṙnya,saŋ sugrīwā mapag yèŋ raṇa mati kapisan taṙ pasārān tinampyal*23:85:2363*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
saŋ đūmrākṣa masö masĕṅhit apuliḥ tan polih amriḥ Ataḥ,saŋ sugrīwa siromatī ya tinibān wuṅkal kariṅkĕl rĕmuk,mahyāmuk Ika saŋ mahodara masö mahyun tumĕmwaŋ yaśa,pīnrĕp dé niraṅ aṅgadèŋ raṇa rĕmuk-rĕmpū hulunyāpasaḥ*23:86:2364*

{Indrayuđa}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏓ = :21:
ri pati saṅ apatiḥ tigaŋ waŋ wirūpākṣa đūmrākṣa māhodara,makin alilaṅ awās awaśyaŋ baśā ṅ-antaké saŋ daśāsyèŋ raṇa,mĕtu sakala galak nirāṙ wuk Ikaŋ wānarānékanā duṙbbala,tutug apagĕh ikaŋ kaśūran rasé tan surud-rudra tulyèḥ galak*23:87:2365*
