tat kālān kadi kālamrĕtyu sakalātyantèŋ galak yaṙ pamuk,yékāṅsö nira saŋ raǥūttama tumūt saŋ lakṣmaṇāṅimbaṅi,lāwan saŋ guṇawān wiƀīṣaṇa paḍāmĕṇṭaŋ laras niṙƀaya,raṅkĕp riŋ guṇa Agra niŋ kakawihan Agrèŋ kawīran sira*24:1:2366*

sāṅsö saŋ tiga déwata tripuruṣa pratyakṣa māwak katon,saŋ hyaŋ tryagni murub paḍā nira dilaḥ tulya-ŋ manaḥ tan paḍĕm,maṅkin đīra Aho Ahaṅkrĕti nikā saŋ krūra lĕṅkāđipa,taṙ kéwran lumagèŋ tigaŋ waṅ amanaḥ māna-ŋ manaḥ nimna ya*24:2:2367*

lwiṙ niŋ hrū nika saŋ daśānana katon atyanta riŋ kādƀuta,siṅhā wyāǥra Ulāgalak mĕtu mulĕk saṅkèŋ panaḥ ṅ-āsura,tan kāntun ṅ-asukanta ƀīṣaṇa Asiŋ satwāgalak nā mulĕk,Agnéyāstra panaḥ Apuy pwa pamalĕs saŋ rāma lĕs līna ya*24:3:2368*

mowaḥ hrū nika saŋ daśāsya mamanaḥ riŋ Astra rodrādƀuta,multak taŋ muśalā triśūla krĕtalārūg ry-agra niŋ hrū mĕlĕk,wuṅkal lèn alaṅan hilaŋ haliliṅĕn sāsiŋ kĕnā dé nikā,ganđaṙwwāstra panaḥ pratīta panulak saŋ rāma riŋ maṅkana*24:4:2369*

{prahaṙṣiṇī}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
yan soṙ bāṇa nira ta saŋ daśāsya śīṙṇna,pahyā niŋ rĕṣigaṇa riŋ naƀastalāwū
ndā tañjriḥ Inalah-alaḥ masö tar olaḥ,puṅgĕl taṇḍa nira pĕgat pisan kĕnāstra*24:5:2370*

tan pamwas kuda nira dé niṅ astra rimpuŋ,lāwan sāraŧi nira tan pasāra śiṙṇna,rĕmpak taŋ raŧa pinanaḥ manaḥ tar énĕḥ*24:6:2371*
sāmbut taŋ lipuṅ umasö lĕpāsakĕn ya*24:7:2372*

mèḥ prāptāŋ lipuṅ i-narāṙyya rāmadéwa,yatnāntĕn nira sumawat sawèt nirāṙ wruḥ,Aƀyāsèŋ samara mariŋ wulat nirāwās,hétunyān kĕna pinanaḥ lipuŋ ya puṅgĕl*24:8:2373*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
muntab krođa niraŋ daśānana tumon kontāsi kontal tikĕl,sāmbut konta wanèḥ kinon ira ta saŋ rāma prayatnā huwus,Ꜽ rāma nda wulat prayatna ta kĕmit héman n-ikuŋ lakṣmaṇa,byaktā yan mati dé nikiŋ lipuṅ apan sy-āmoǥa tan wyaṙŧa ya*24:9:2374*

nā tojaṙ nira niścayāŋlĕpasakĕn tékaŋ lipuŋ tan luput,limpad pyaḥ niraṅ āṙyya lakṣmaṇa tibā tībrānaṅis saŋ kaka,Āśāsū sira saŋ kapīndra kapĕgan Āmbĕk nikaŋ wré kabèḥ,n-ton saŋ lakṣmaṇa mūṙccitāṅĕsah asiḥ saŋ sidđa muṅgwiŋ laṅit*24:10:2375*

prajñā saŋ kinawiḥ wiƀīṣaṇa wawaŋ puṇḍut ta saŋ lakṣmaṇa,munduṙ mūṙ sakarĕŋ watĕk ta Ikanaŋ kontā r-alap ṅ-oṣađi,pöhīkaŋ kani niṙwikāra mabaṅun saŋ lakṣmaṇāṅañjali,sakwèḥ saŋ manaṅis miṅis mari maruk maṅhrūk watĕk wānara*24:11:2376*

hāḥ saḥ māruti dibya māraṇa hilaŋ dèntār alap ṅ-oṣađi,śudđékā suyaśanta sidđi satirun riŋ maŋ hurip rāt kabèḥ,nā liŋ niŋ bala wānarāmuji wijaḥ n-ton jīwa saŋ lakṣmaṇa,saŋ rāmāta maṅolakĕn gĕmĕ-gĕmĕn göŋ niŋ giraŋ riŋ Ari*24:12:2377*

tan poliḥ Amĕṅan niraŋ daśamuꝁām poliḥ ḍatĕŋ tā-muliḥ,maŋhundaŋ raŧa sāra-sāraŧi wanèḥ śīǥrāṙ panèk riŋ raŧa,Agyā mātyana mātya mo tar apiliḥ dényān puliḥ liŋ nira,gumrit taŋ raŧa gūmrĕhīta hati saŋ śīrāŋ kudāṅhrik masö*24:13:2378*

sandéhāta manaḥ hyaṅ indra tumahā saŋ rāma sorèŋ raṇa,yatnāwèḥ ta sirāstra guhyawijaya brahmāstra lāwan raŧa,tan lèn sāraŧi mātalīkana kinon nityé karākṣān nira,muṅgaḥ saŋ raǥuputra riŋ raŧa maṇik saśrī lawan saŋ Ari*24:14:2379*

{mađulinda}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :24:
Anantara naréndraputra hana riŋ raŧottama pawĕḥ hyaṅ indra ri sira,watĕk rĕṣi riṅ antarikṣa Anumoda maŋhudanakĕn ta ganđakusuma,mulat ta sira saŋ daśānana sawismayāmaya-mayājayā nrĕpasuta,daśāsya sira đīra wīra tuhu jāti śūra sira tan surud tar arusuḥ*24:15:2380*

masö ta masiliḥ panaḥ paḍa mamĕtwakĕn kanipuṇan niṅ astra sakala,naréndra raǥuputra pūṙwwa mamanaḥ ta pāśupatapāśa śūla ya mulĕk,daśāsya mamanaḥ rikaŋ ƀujagapāśa yéka Umĕlö panaḥ nrĕpasuta,saroṣa sira dénya śīǥra mamanaḥ muwaḥ hibĕk ikaŋ naƀastala pĕpĕt*24:16:2381*

paraḥ kĕna ta saŋ daśānana nanā tĕḍas ḍaḍa nirāṙdđa mūṙccita tibā,mulat saƀaya śīǥra sāraŧi nirālayūmĕgil awaknya ḍuṣṭa matuhan,samantara Uđāni saŋ daśamuꝁāṅadĕg sira suđīra mamrih atahĕn,haro-hara si ḍuṣṭa sāraŧi manèk rikaŋ raŧa muwaḥ takutnya ri sira*24:17:2382*

hanādƀuta sutīkṣṇa sañjata nira triśūla ya pawèḥ ƀaṭāra ri sira,yatéka pinĕniŋ nirojwala marab murub mĕtu ṅ-apuy nirantara ri ya,naréndra raǥuputra śīǥra mamutĕṙ lipuŋ Inaƀimantra Indrakuliśa,parĕŋ mapulihanya yaṙ lĕpasakĕn ya kapwa dumilaḥ gĕsĕŋ dadi hawu*24:18:2383*

muwaḥ sira mamèti sañjata wanèḥ Anèka masiliḥ-siliḥ paḍa puliḥ,yamāstra hana nꜽnrĕtāstra baruṇāstra guhyaka guhāstra Āsuraśara,sarūpa nikanaŋ sinañjata tataṙ tutug Aṅĕn-aṅĕn nirāmanah ataḥ,suđīratara tan kacidra paḍa lakṣitān sira linakṣa siṅlar akalis*24:19:2384*

makin ta maparö sirāṙ silih-usī siliḥ-palu siliḥ-tuhuk tahu-tahu,ƀramanta kadi cakra cañcala lanā mataṇḍaṅan ataṇḍiṅan maputĕran,muwaḥ maluwaran sirān tar aṅĕliḥ tar aṅlu tar aṅĕl karug-rag asuwé,tawaŋ-tawaṅ awak nirār aṅĕn-aṅĕn ya ta pwa mahaṅan haṅiñ juga mibĕr*24:20:2385*

kĕdö sira kadi kya mindĕr aŧawā kadi pwa sapu Ujwalénutitakĕn,tatan sira katon-katon taṅ awĕlū jugākuliliṅan mawās makalaṅan,kadi pwa kalaṅan ƀaṭāra yama kālamrĕtyu manawuŋ sirāṅadu laga,Asiŋ Umasukérikā niyata yan pĕjaḥ kapipisèŋ raŧān paputĕran*24:21:2386*

ri maṅkana nirāṙ pijĕṙ maputĕran kadi pwa maliha-ŋ lĕmaḥ magiwaṅan,girīndra gumĕgör iṅ agra kadi rūga rūpa ni gĕrĕḥnya ǥora gumuruḥ,lamad-lamad amèt paran paḍa kasamburat kasarakat hilaŋ marawayan,ƀaṭāra rawi manda-manda makucĕm samudra kumucak kakuñcaṅ atugur*24:22:2387*

rikaŋ gagana saŋ gaṇāgĕnĕṅan iŋ grahāgraha takut sirāmrih ajaga,sasaṅśaya sirāṙ kasuṅsaṅa tumoñ jagat riga-rigu grahāgraha kunaŋ,tatan sawuwusĕn takut nikana taŋ watĕk wray akiḍampĕlan ya rumĕpa,rikaŋ watu śilātalān pagĕnĕṅan wanèḥnya mĕgĕgĕḥ kagöman aṅadĕg*24:23:2388*

susāraŧi suśakti mātali sirāṅgĕgö tali niṅ aśwa duṙbbala mahos,mahos kĕtĕ-kĕtĕg nirān kadi tinampyal iŋ haṅin aṅèl maṅañjali sira*24:24:2389*
makon lumĕkasāmĕkāsana laga ndya dona niṅ ataṇḍaṅan tĕwas aṅèl,jagat juga ya kāsih-āsihi naréndra sugyan uḍula-ŋ lĕmaḥ pwa katĕrag*24:25:2390*

musuḥta ya matīs hiḍĕpta riya haywa maṅkana kĕnākĕna-ŋ naya huwus,salaḥ linawanan mataṇḍaṅan apan mamèt kira-kirékanāmala-malar,ya mūṙkꝁa paracidra yānuru-nurū mururwakĕn i-saŋ narāṙyya juga ya,yadin palĕ-palĕḥ piliḥ kita puliḥ panumpala nikā kunaŋ mamĕnaṅa*24:26:2391*

damaṙ maṅaraman Umèḥ pĕjaha hĕntya duḥnya dumilaḥ murub sapinaḍĕm,nahan paṅupamé pamūk rasika mūṙkꝁa wiṣṭi biṣamĕŋ sumaṙdḍiṅ iriya,mataŋnya pahawās huwus-huwusi taŋ lagā pĕjahi ṅ-aṅjahit triƀuwana,panaḥ ta ya tumampanèŋ kapanasan kabèḥ kapana téki yan lĕkasana*24:27:2392*

gĕgön ikanaṅ astra guhyawijayāpraméya ya Apan naƀastalamaya,susūkṣma tuwi yātiƀāra kadi mèru winđya himawān bwatanyan inagag,Ikaŋ mata si bāyubajra makasub Iṅ agni warayaŋnya sūṙyya sakala,hĕlaṙ nikana saŋ kagéndra ya wulunya rudra sira muṅgwi puṅka nikana*24:28:2393*

nahan n-ikana liŋ niraŋ prawara mātali ṙ-habĕt iṅ aśwa riŋ tali wĕsi,madan ta siraṅ āṙyya muṣṭi ta laras nirāṙ tihaṅakĕn śilīmuꝁa huwus,Ujaṙ ta juga makramé sira tamaṙ katon lĕpasakĕn ya sèp ṅwaṅ umulat,daśānana paraḥ gulū nira parĕŋ pĕgat kasapuluḥ tibā kabarubuḥ*24:29:2394*

{praharaṇakalika}

Aŧa ri pati niraŋ praƀu daśawadana,kapibala kadi sāgara gumuruh awū,maṅigĕl akupik atri paḍa wija-wijaḥ,puji-puji ya mabiñcaluka kadi raray*24:30:2395*

haṅin umirir aǥūṙṇnita ƀuwana tĕḍuḥ,jĕnu kanaka sumāṙ sumawur ata marūm,Agaru gugula đūpa satata kumukus,suragaṇa karuṇā sira maṅinakakĕn*24:31:2396*

haṙṣāmbĕk rĕṣigaṇa sidđa yaṙ paśānti,riŋ méǥāṙ hana sukamātra taṙ pagātra,mwaŋ puṣpāñjali nira nā katon manojña,lumrā taŋ ƀramara mariŋriṅ antarikṣa*24:32:2397*

{prĕŧwītala}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
wiƀīṣaṇa sirātitībra kabaran gĕlānāṅaraŋ,manaḥ nira ya kāsrĕpan wulat i-saŋ kakāsiḥ pĕjaḥ,drawa-ŋ hati kamānuṣan kapasukan ṅ-asiḥ luḥ tibā,tibākĕn ikanaŋ sĕkaṙ I-suku saŋ kakāṅañjali*24:33:2398*

kakaṅku kita hāḥ daśānana nihan ṅhulun tiṅhali,kṣamākĕna taman kĕnā ta riṅ upadrawāṅiṅgati,Apak para ri saŋ parāṙŧa paramāṙŧa doni ṅhulun,mahāhuluna saŋ mahāṙdđika mahāt sirèŋ rāt kabèḥ*24:34:2399*

nihan mahala yan paṅiṅgati Anuŋ parèŋ duṙjjana,tan ora yaśa dona niŋ wiraha kéwala drohaka,ṅhulun pwa makakāṙyya kāruṇika rakṣakā niŋ sarāt,mataŋnyan apagĕḥ hatiṅku kapasāha lāwan kita*24:35:2400*

kunaŋ pwa kalaraṅku dènta mati dé nikaŋ duṙnaya,Ujaṙkwahayu ṅūni tat pituhu riŋ saƀāpad wihaŋ,Ujaṙ nikana saŋ prahasta kĕna téki maṅké tĕka,patinta saha mīla yèki ta ꝑalanya sākṣāt katon*24:36:2401*

makin ta mapagĕḥ Iké pamituhuṅku riŋ Āgama,tumon ꝑala ni duṙnayanta riṅ ihatra saḍyāṇ ḍatĕŋ,dĕlāha kari tan pawèha lara duḥka janmāntara,mĕné tuwi nihan ya hĕnti kita hantu wèt niŋ wihaŋ*24:37:2402*

Apan ṅwaṅ umahā mahöm Umahawās raṣā niŋ naya,Adun saguṇadoṣa ṣaḍguṇa ya dānanānuŋ kĕnā,Awās hayu ni wastu niŋ wuwus awās ya yékālapĕn,tatan n-asiṅ-asiŋ hanā nika nayotpĕnāténayu*24:38:2403*

kita pwa mituhu-ŋ salaḥ salahasāku dèntèŋ saƀā,suƀāga tuwi tan hanāta Inalapta śabdāhayu,hayunta kaharĕpku wrĕdđya ya mataŋnya kojaṙ hita,hatinta wiparīta wèt ni kawĕrönta wīrĕŋ raṇa*24:39:2404*

tatan sapituhun n-apan rarayasiḥ sumaṅkyé kita,kakinta tuwi yukti katwaṅa samaṅgalān sĕmbahĕn,sirāwara-waraḥ rikaŋ hayu-hayun hiḍĕpté sira,tan ora rinĕṅönta śabda nira tulya tīban humuŋ*24:40:2405*

wihaŋta ya tĕwas maṅèl mara-maraḥ sirèŋ wwaŋ bahaŋ,Anéka Upamé pamaṅsita nirèŋ wuwus yālapĕn,Apan n-alĕpakĕn tamat t-alap ikā kĕnoḥ liŋ nira,sayogya pituhun tuhun matuha tan tinon tan tinūt*24:41:2406*

gĕlāna kabaran tumon ṅwaṅ awamānacittāmahil,r-uliḥ ta manaṅis Asiḥ maṅĕsah ènĕh āśā sira,muwaḥ Aku mataṅguh amrih awaraḥ Umās-wās kita,wahil matĕmahan galak gĕlĕṅi tāku moǥāṅdĕdĕl*24:42:2407*

Ađā kalana līna riŋ hati hilaŋ panontāt-hiḍĕp,tan ora hiniḍĕp wuwus suśaraṇa ṅwaṅ èwö ṅhayu,ri göŋ ni tan asiḥ ta göŋ galak alök hiḍĕp ni ṅhulun,kaliḥ ta kasulāpa tat pituhu nīti saŋ nītimān*24:43:2408*

lukan tuhun ikā tahāṅku ta halād wihaŋ saŋ tahu,Apan ṅwaṅ aƀimāna riŋ wwaṅ atuhāsahāsāsahaŋ,hilaŋ hayu hĕlinya duḥka pati pātakāgöŋ tĕka,Ah-o kaka nihan katon kita katuŋtuṅan dūṙyyaśa*24:44:2409*

{sariṇī}
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ = :11:
wiƀīṣaṇa nahan ta sāmbat nira,raǥūttama wawaŋ mataṅguḥ sira,wiƀīṣaṇa huwus ta haywālara,Apan saꝑala saŋ daśāsyāṙ pĕjaḥ*24:45:2410*

praśāsta sira ṅūni sāmpun tapa,gahan ta sira cakrawaṙttīŋ jagat,pĕjaḥ sira taman surud riŋ raṇa,Asiŋ mati mamūk ya mokṣātmaka*24:46:2411*

Atīta rasikā tamat kiṅkiṅĕn,Apan mati mahāprawīrèŋ raṇa,kunaŋ kita Iké gumantya praƀu,praƀāwa ni guṇanta śudđānulus*24:47:2412*

puliḥ pahayu taŋ sa-lĕṅkāpura,kitékana siwin nikaŋ rākṣasa,muḋanyana manaḥ nikaŋ duṙjjana,sacaṙmmin awĕniŋ manūtāgama*24:48:2413*

tatat sawarahĕn ri dé niŋ ratu,Apat nipuṇa puṇyawān śīlawān,taŧāpi warahĕṅkwa tātaḥ kita,pagĕḥ-pagĕha niŋ hiḍĕp don iké*24:49:2414*

nihan krama ni dé niṅ aṅdāni rāt,Awakta rumuhun waraḥ riŋ hayu,tĕlasta mapagĕḥ magöm Āgama,tĕkérikaṅ amātya mantrī tumūt*24:50:2415*

patiḥ saṅ apatiḥ patiḥ satya ta,saƀrĕtya paricāra kapwācara,tĕkèṅ anak anīt ulaḥ tan salaḥ,prajā ya milu jāgra nītī hayu*24:51:2416*

prayatna riṅ ulaḥ Ataḥ ṅwaŋ praƀu,mawèha tuladan tirūn iŋ sarāt,yadin salah-ulaḥ sasaṙ rāt kabèḥ,panaṇḍa pada saŋ mawaŋ rāt tinūt*24:52:2417*

lawan sira kinonakèn katwaṅa,Apan hana ƀaṭāra muṅgwīŋ sira,wwaluŋ hyaṅ apupul ry-awak saŋ praƀu,dumèḥ sira mahāpraƀāwāsama*24:53:2418*

hyaṅ indra yama sūṙyya candrānila,kuwéra baruṇāgni nāhan wwalu,sirā ta maka-Aṅga saŋ ƀūpati,mataŋ nira Iniṣṭi Aṣṭabrata*24:54:2419*

nihan brata ni saŋ hyaṅ indrālapèn,sirāṅhudanakĕn tumrĕptīŋ jagat,sirāta tuladĕnta Indrabrata,sudāna ya hudanta maŋlyābi rāt*24:55:2420*

yamabrata ḍumaṇḍa kaṙmmāhala,sirékana maluŋ maliŋ yaṙ pĕjaḥ,Umilwa kita malwa ṅ-olaḥ salaḥ,Asiŋ Umawarāŋ sarīt priḥ pati*24:56:2421*

ƀaṭāra rawi maŋhisèp wwꜽ lanā,ndatan kara śanꜽḥ-śanꜽh è-nira,samaṅkana kitat Alap paṅguhĕn,tataṙ gĕlisa yéka sūṙyyabrata*24:57:2422*

śaśibrata humaṙṣuka-ŋ rāt kabèḥ,Ulaḥta mrĕdu komalā yan katon,guyunta mamanis ya tulyāmrĕta,Asiŋ matuha paṇḍitāt swāgatan*24:58:2423*

haṅin ta kita yan paṅinté Ulaḥ,kumawruhana budđi niŋ rāt kabèḥ,sucāra ya panonta tātan katon,ya dibyaguṇa sūkṣma bāyubrata*24:59:2424*

mamuktya ṅ-upaƀoga sambi ṅ-inak,taman panĕpĕṅèŋ paṅan mwaŋ Inum,manaṇḍaṅa maƀūṣaṇā mahyasa,nahan ta đanada-bratānuŋ tirun*24:60:2425*

ƀaṭāra baruṇāṅgĕgö sañjata,mahāwiṣa ya nāgapāśāṅapus,sirāta tuladĕnta pāśabrata,kitomapusana-ŋ watĕk duṙjjana*24:61:2426*

lanāṅgĕsĕṅi śatru bahnibrata,galakta ri musuḥta yékāpuya,Asiŋ sa-Inasönta śīṙṇnāpasaḥ,ya tékana sinaṅguh agnibrata*24:62:2427*

nahan ta guṇa saŋ rumakṣèŋ jagat,ginorawa lanā ginoṣṭīniwö,ya tūtana ya tū maṇiktékana,Ulaḥ masĕsĕran ya sĕs~ran magöŋ*24:63:2428*

Ikaŋ sugati gantiṅan tāpagĕḥ,suśīla salayanya tan siṅsala,twaṅ iŋ maguru gorawāṅkĕn garit,śiwāṙccana cininta cintāmaṇi*24:64:2429*

si satya mata mutya Atyanta ya,gĕlaŋta taya niŋ gĕlĕŋ riŋ hati,suka-ŋ hrĕdaya tan makuṅkūṅana,wiśiṣṭamakuṭān kaṭuṅkālapi*24:65:2430*

masimsima samāđi śudđāŋ manaḥ,si jāgra japa nā paṅadwāpaḍèn,si sajjana ya tāñ janāṅkĕñ jĕnu,yaśānta śayacitta mutyāputiḥ*24:66:2431*

Umaḥta ṅ-ulah āmahaywaŋ jagat,si tañcala lanā palaṅkāpagĕḥ,syupékṣaka sakānya yākas dahat,si kāruṇika nā ta watwan nikā*24:67:2432*

salönya samatā si mꜽtrī wanèḥ,parāṙŧa paramāṙŧa paṭṫāraṇa,subudđi ya ta bidđanāgé ruhur,paṅöban ira saŋ Umöbīŋ jagat*24:68:2433*

nahan suƀaga ƀūṣaṇānta praƀu,ya mūlya ya maṇik taman pabwati,tataṙ kawĕnaṅénalap niŋ maliŋ,maliḥ ya kinĕmit ya nityāṅĕmit*24:69:2434*

hĕmās pinakaƀūṣaṇèŋ wwaŋ kabèḥ,ya mūlya riya hétukanyāṙ maṅèl,hanān laku layaṙ ya wadwāsawaḥ,sawètnyan atidamƀa riŋ ƀūṣaṇa*24:70:2435*

ri saŋ praƀu taman wiśéṣā ṅ-ĕmās,ya tā pahupaƀoga muṅgwiŋ saƀā,Ikaŋ guṇa kunaŋ kinuṇḍaŋ lanā,ya maŋhalĕpi tan kasaḥ sāparan*24:71:2436*

Ikaŋ wiƀawa tan wawékān pati,hananya sakarĕŋ huméṙhéṙ ṅhurip,pĕjaḥ pwa kita duṣṭa mantun nikā,guṇanta ginĕgönta yānūtakĕn*24:72:2437*

ya rākṣaka rikaŋ hawan duṙggama,parahwa nikanaŋ paratran paran,suluḥ salawah iŋ jagat tan paḍĕm,ya maŋdunuṅakĕn ṅ kamokṣan tĕmĕn*24:73:2438*

tatan pariƀawèŋ wanèḥ don ikā,Asiŋ katakutātakut ton ikā,Ikaŋ magalak iŋ daṅū yāsiha,praƀāwa nikanaŋ guṇān ƀūṣaṇa*24:74:2439*

biṣā wiṣaya taṙ biṣāté kita,si kāmuꝁa sikākĕnāṅkĕn Asu,jitèndriya ya ǥāra kāsiḥ kulé,Anakta Inak iŋ samāđīniṅu*24:75:2440*

tĕṅĕn nika panonta nityojwala,ya pañjut atĕḍuḥ taman kāṅinan,pĕtĕŋ pitu patapnya yékāmpĕti,patimbunan ikaŋ gĕlĕḥ t-āmbili*24:76:2441*

nihan praŧama niŋ pĕtĕŋ tiṅhali,wĕrönta puji dé nikaŋ kawwaṅan,wĕgig ta kita dé nikaŋ śaktyagöŋ,si damƀa kawĕrönta dé niŋ hĕmās*24:77:2442*

sahaŋta kita yat prawīrèŋ raṇa,kawiḥ pwa kita kāwiśāṙdđāmiṣa,si moha ya wĕrönta yat yowana,wanèḥ litu-hayunta yāṅdé wĕrö*24:78:2443*

nahan ta si pĕtĕŋ pitu priḥ tutup,duluṙnya si lulut ya lolyāmulut,ya tā sahana sūhakĕn dohakĕn,samāđi sumĕnö śumudđāŋ tamaḥ*24:79:2444*

Alaḥ sahana niŋ musuḥ ṅké ṅ-awak,Awīs ya kawaśā musuḥtā yawā,yawat niyata śakti śūrèŋ raṇa,Asiŋ malahakĕn malālwat malit*24:80:2445*

samasta talu taŋ musuḥ jriḥ kabèḥ,ri hèŋ mwaṅ i-dalĕm ya kapwārarĕm,jagat praṇata ƀakti tan laṅǥana,siwin kita sumiwya saŋ hyaŋ śiwa*24:81:2446*

bratā prĕŧiwi yéka mabwat tĕmĕn,Asiḥ ta maratā rikaŋ rāt kabèḥ,halāhayu nikaŋ jagat haywakĕn,syasiḥ guṇa gunuŋ magöŋ saṅǥa ta*24:82:2447*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
prihĕn tĕmĕn đaṙmma đumāraṇa-ŋ sarāt,sarāga saŋ sāđu siréka tūtana,tan aṙŧa tan kāma pi donya tan yaśa,ya śakti saŋ sajjana đaṙmmarākṣaka*24:83:2448*

sakā nikaŋ rāt kita yan wĕnaŋ manūt,munūṣadéśa prih ataḥ rumākṣa ya,kṣayā nikaŋ pāpa nahan prayojana,janānurāgādi tuwin kapaṅguha*24:84:2449*

guhāpĕtĕŋ taŋ mada moha kaśmala,malīdi yolānya magöŋ mahāwiṣa,wiśāta saŋ wruḥ rikanaŋ juraŋ kali,kalīṅan iŋ śāstra suluḥ nikāpraƀā*24:85:2450*

praƀā nikaŋ jñāna suśīla đaṙmma wèḥ,mawèḥ kasidđyan paḍa mukti niṙmmala,malā milĕt tan pamatuk makiŋ mariŋ,mari-n wiśéṣāŋ yaśa sidđa tāpasa*24:86:2451*

pasaŋ putiḥ tulya nikaŋ malāṅliput,luput siraŋ sāđu yakĕn pasaŋ tuju,tuju-ŋ suka ṅké mamunuḥ taman muliḥ,muliḥ sirèŋ mokṣa lĕpas rikaŋ muliḥ*24:87:2452*

mulik patūt niŋ Aji nā gawé nira,nirantarāwèḥ hayu đaṙmma riŋ para,parāṙŧa tan lèn juga don irèŋ jagat,jagat ṇ-ḍĕṅö sājar-ajaṙ nirèŋ hayu*24:88:2453*

{puṣpitāgra}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ = :12:
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
nahan ikana wuwus ƀaṭāra rāma,Umuḍahanī sira saŋ wiƀīṣaṇāsiḥ,drĕḋa mapagĕh ikā manaḥ nirānūt,winara-waraḥ rikanaŋ sayukti dè yā*24:89:2454*

kadi gati nikanaŋ lĕmaḥ kalahrūn,bĕlah atĕlā tumibāŋ hudan n-isĕpnya,ya ta paḍa ni manaḥ niraŋ sinantwan,rumĕsĕp asiḥ sumusuk rikaŋ swacitta*24:90:2455*

tunu ta kaka nirāṙ paśoca sāmpun,sira ta gumanti rinatwakĕn ri lĕṅkā,suƀaga sira saśoƀa sāƀiṣéka,maśila huwus masalin wulat salīlā*24:91:2456*

rĕṣigaṇa Anumoda déwatānūt,magiraṅ anon ratu catra niŋ triloka,gĕrĕmĕs ira gĕrĕḥ manojña hrĕŋ-hrĕŋ,Amrĕta tibā mapuliḥ rikaŋ sa-lĕṅkā*24:92:2457*

ciha-ciha hati saŋ hyaṅ indra haṙṣa,brata nira dāna hudan magöŋ mawaḥ-waḥ,sa-mahala kahilī hilaŋ ya luṅhā,kawĕkas ikaŋ śuci śoƀa ƀūmi rāmya*24:93:2458*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
tampuḥ niŋ paramāmrĕté sapinasuk riŋ rājya lĕṅkāpura,maṅkin wrĕdđi hayunya Ujwala muwaḥ salwiṙnya dé saŋ kaka,sampūṙṇna-ŋ giri riŋ mahéndra katĕkān rĕŋrĕŋ ya rāmyāpuliḥ,sakwèḥ-kwèḥ nikanaŋ nanā ya hinĕnö dé saŋ hyaṅ indrāmalĕs*24:94:2459*

tātan déśa jugāpuliḥ hinuripan taŋ wré pĕjaḥ riŋ raṇa,tan palwaŋ bala saŋ raǥūttama Aho đaṙmmāmrĕtāwèḥ hurip,swasŧa-ŋ wré mati māṙ baṅun kahudanan kapwāṅinūm āmrĕta,kagyat yan mahurip hiḍĕpnya maturū ṅūnī pĕjaḥ yāṅipi*24:95:2460*

lāwan taŋ mati riṇ ranāṅgaṇa kabèḥ riŋ wīralokān dunuŋ,ṅkānāŋ ƀukti Ikaŋ sukottama magöŋ nānāwiđèṅ apsarī,salwiṙ niŋ Upaƀoga ƀūṣaṇa maṇik Atyanta riŋ kādƀuta,nāhan swaṙgga niraŋ prawīra paramèṅ uttuṅga toṅgwan nira*24:96:2461*

{suwadanā}
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :20:
sāmpun sampūṙṇna sampat sira ratu sumiliḥ lĕṅkādipa gahan,saŋ hyaŋ ƀūtādƀutānon saguṇa wahu madĕg kādĕg sira mulat,Ākāśāṇin Apuy wwꜽ lĕmah umilu mulat nā-ŋ pañcakuśika,cihnānyāmbĕk ƀaṭārāṙ paṅanumata matīs söb-söb nira marūm,
Ambö niŋ ganđa lumrā haṅin-aṅin ikanaŋ trꜽlokya ya mirir,saśryaṅlimbé panāmbé śriya maṅaway-away sāmbé ya muliha,haṙṣanyān ton ikaŋ rāt wahu rahayu muwaḥ sāmpun sasuraƀi,maṅsö taŋ rājya lakṣmī masĕmi ya masĕwö ṅ-udyāna masĕkar*24:97:2462*

wadwad luṅgaḥ lumaṅgé lalita ya maṅigĕl dé niŋ haṅin alon,roṇḍon anwam manumpak manuk iriya n-unīnāyun-n-ayun aṅèl,satwé sor aṙdđa map~ḍay mata ya kalilipĕn dé niŋ sari rurū,képwān uṅsiṙ lakinyā liku-liku riṅ ikā yāṅkĕn sapu matā*24:98:2463*

śudđāmbĕk saŋ mawaŋ rāt tuhu-tuhu guṇawān wwaŋ sidđapuruṣa,śīǥrawwaḥ wwa-wwahan bāp wawaṅ atasak arūm dé niŋ tapa magöŋ,māmbö ḍūṙyyan diṅāṙyyan paḍa mamaḍa rasé dwadwal ǥrĕtapura,glāna-ŋ wré kapwa képwan manĕmu ꝑala matöb matwab juga warĕg*24:99:2464*

punnāgāśoka tañjuŋ Asana sana-sini śrīnyāsama-sama,kumbaŋ-kumbaŋnya luṅhā mahas iṅ asiṅ arūm ṅkānān kajĕnĕkan,kāsyāsiḥ śrīgaḍiŋ pūḥ kawĕlas-arĕp akūŋ yènāryakĕn asiḥ,nā hétunyān tibā riŋ lĕmah arawa-raway somyāṅaway-away*24:100:2465*

padmārūm rāmya lumrèŋ parigi paraga niŋ rāgāgaway unĕŋ,milwāpĕs téka ronyānipis amaya-mayā Āpan maṇimaya,lit-lit niŋ mās sarinyomirir apaḍa kuniŋ ṅkānèŋ natar ĕmās,Aṅhiŋ hiṙ niṅsarin saṙ mawaṅi mawa ṅ-inak ƀogèŋ mađukara*24:101:2466*

ṅkānèŋ kaywāra yāriŋ manuk anak-anakan riŋ ƀūmi kanaka,jīwā-jīwāwajik yāŋ-jawat ajulay aḍèŋ riŋ kinnara-rarā,syuŋ tan swaŋ wruḥnya mèdī kĕna madana madan médan milu masö,suŋsuŋ tékā bayanyāṅaway-away agawè rāgériya mada*24:102:2467*

sāṅsönyèŋ śūnya-śūnyāṅikis aṅĕkĕs unĕŋnyāsyaŋ masĕnĕṅa,prāpta ṅkā tan Isin riŋ Atat atakut ataḥ tan tūt tula-tuli,lwiṙ niŋ syuŋ hyunya tan swaŋ ya sumĕḍĕku masö wiśwāsa manisik,késyan kāruṇya kériŋ siniwi-siwi ṅ-atat tūtut ya wĕkasan*24:103:2468*

satwāsaṇḍiŋ masuṇḍaŋ laki-bini saparan kapwāśiwa-siwo,mosyan masnéha māsiḥ manusu-nusu n-usiṙ taŋ cumbana rasa,n-ambuŋ taŋ lambuṅ éñjuḥ puji-puji sahajān paŋjiŋjaṅ ajaṅĕl,tuṅgaŋ-tuṅgaŋnya maṅgaŋ maṅagagi gigirĕn śaktin kahaṅĕtan

haṅsāsyaŋ-syaŋ maṅumbaŋ ri tĕpi-tĕpi nikā ƀoganya talaga,tan ton swāminya luṅhānilĕmi sulur adoḥ wĕtwanya wĕkasan,śīǥrāŋ haṅsān usiṙ taŋ laki-laki ya wujuk muṅkuṙ malĕk-alök,lwiṙ niŋ kāsiḥ nikāsiḥ mamirimisi mahāṅdodohi sakarĕŋ*24:104:2469*

kĕmbaŋ niŋ jambu kériṙ sumawur i-walakaŋ niŋ mrāk ya maṅigèl,yāṅkĕn jĕnwanya madyus riya makin agiraŋ daṙppān kararaban,līlā ƀāwān wugatnyāŋ-jiriṅ i-maṅicipiṙ yan kéḍak akĕcĕk,nāŋ nĕp mās tulya maṅliŋ kadi pamugari niŋ kaywāra kabaran*24:105:2470*

jātīkaŋ pārijātānarawata marurū riŋ kuṇḍi kanaka,simsim gantiŋ magantiŋ gagana kadi hudan ṅkā tulya sumawur,byaktāwĕḥ ƀūṣaṇā niŋ mrak agĕlĕm aṅigĕl ta wwaŋnya sugĕma,méṅin mamriḥ mamaṇḍak ḍarapati wĕlu wok yékā pipi ruṣa*24:106:2471*

satwātūt budđi satwa prasama tan asuwé ta wwaŋnya mapalöŋ,siṅhāsiŋ siṅha kāsiḥ tĕka kadi ta kadaŋ kāriŋ kidaṅ ariŋ,saṅkā yan trus nikaŋ priḥ praŧama nikana saŋ maŋ­rākṣa ƀuwana,taṙ mèwĕḥ dé niṅ āmbĕk makaka muḍi ṅ-asiḥ mꜽtrī ya banawā*24:107:2472*

moŋ taŋ moŋ sosyanāmoṙ camara mari n-usī kañcil kacula mik,sākṣāt sosyan pasuswan sasusu-sasusupan somyān ruṣa śaśa,wut kāwu wwawwa mawwaŋ lutuṅ atali-talī paŋ niŋ duhĕt atöb,tañ jīṙṇnājīṙṇna méñjuḥ ṅ harawa hariwuwun wèḥ-wèḥ wuru-wuru*24:108:2473*

katkat luklak sa luklik-lika-lika lulut iŋ larwan ni wiwalik,puk-puk pakṣāṅupikṣāṅipik-ipik i-pijĕṙ taṅkwak kupu-kupu,Ujña-ŋ prit sāṙjjawojaṙ maṅicap i-puḍaṅan yāpūḍiṅan aḍèŋ,nityāniṅtiŋ maniṅtiŋ riṅ alap-alapa riŋ lūṅan lagi maliŋ*24:109:2474*

mapritya-ŋ prit rikaŋ priḥ prakutut atat atūt tuṣṭātat atatā,tiṅkik-tiṅkik ya tékākaka-kakatu kakaḥ baṅkak makah-akaḥ,swaṅgāsaṅgĕm sĕgĕḥ yāsiga sagula wĕtiḥ mwaŋ tor atitira,humwaŋ pūdyanya mahniŋ haliliṅan abalĕm dè niŋ patuk agöŋ*24:110:2475*

manyaŋ-manyaŋ ya méṅālalula ṅ-alula riŋ prajñojwala jalak,prĕñjak-prĕñjak tumañjak ṅ hiji maṅajir umaḥ tiñjo puyuh i-sor,dé niŋ budđyaṙdđa mūḍān pakidupuh akipū tan pomah aramĕḥ,kuwwaŋ kéndo kuwuŋ ṅké Aku makuwu-kuwuŋ liŋnyān uni kuwoŋ*24:111:2476*

līṅan lūṅan ya hūṅan muni manuk uyakanyékāmidu-midu,sambégā niŋ kuwoŋ tékana hinaṅĕn-aṅĕn donyān pamĕjahi,koŋ taṇḍaŋ koŋ kaniṣṭākuṭa makuwu-kuwuŋ koŋ kaśmala kuwoŋ,tan pomaḥ tā katrĕṣṇān laku widu mawayaŋ kom guṇya saguṇa*24:112:2477*

ko tākuŋ kéwalāsā makuwu-kuwu rikā saŋ śréṣṭi puhiji,kāsyāsiḥ koŋ jalak ko mamaṅun umah umāt tonton tiru-tirun,ṅèl-ṅèlĕn swaŋ ya mamriḥ makuwu-kuwu tĕwas saṅsāra kawilĕt,tĕkwan kuṇḍaŋ ta liṅku d-laku ta wiku kuwuŋ kuwwanta ta-tapa*24:113:2478*

nā liŋ niŋ pakṣi widwan manuk uyaka n-akon wikwāsusupana,konan taŋ kokilānūt n-uni kakuli-kulik śabdanya masulit,kokilya-ŋ kokilāpan maṅinaki kalawan lagnāmutusana,ƀuktī ƀaktèṅ alas göŋ makula-kula kulit molĕs kuli-kulit*24:114:2479*

kabwatnyan sor ujaṙ niŋ manuk uyaka n-akĕn kwanyāmĕja-mĕjaḥ,saṅkā riŋ haṙṣa donyāṙ wulat i-hayu nikaŋ rajyojwala muwaḥ,moliḥ Āmbĕknya maprāṙŧana n-uwah apuliḥ ṅ-udyāna saꝑala,hétunyān aṙdđa médan mamidu-midu dumon rowaŋnya pikatan*24:115:2480*

joḥ koŋ jaṅkuŋ maraṅkuŋ mara kumira-kirāmor iŋ huraṅ-ariŋ,riŋ kaṅkuŋ kom pamaṅkuk katĕlĕguk aharĕp riŋ duṅkil aṅilu,koŋ kuntul koŋ manuṅkul milu maṅilu mulat riŋ mĕlĕm amulay,wéśanyātaḥ wiśéṣān bisu si bĕsi biṣān paŋhĕlwi sisili*24:116:2481*

tān olĕg tan wutaḥ dĕḥ si wĕla haya-hayān doyan n-itĕk-itĕk,kèkĕt cittanya yaṙ ton kuḍuk aḍĕp aḍuḍuk ṅkāné puḍak aḍas,mĕṅgĕp cuṇḍuk cumidrèŋ dĕlĕg amulay i-koŋ caṇḍāla si baka,baṅkak-baṅkak mamĕṅkĕk mamaṅana ya sĕpat hīnān karĕnĕhan*24:117:2482*

nāŋ méṅā Aṙdđa médan hĕlaṅ ahala hilaŋ luṅhā maṅuy-aṅuy,wruḥnyān doyan tan andĕl lagi ta ya mamatuk đik dūṙtta si hĕlaŋ,kālaṅkyaŋ ko lanākūŋ saƀaya mabayaṅan ko taḥ mapa kunĕŋ,koŋ gāgak ndin pinaṅgaŋ kagĕsĕṅan ahirĕŋ hémanmun agĕsĕŋ*24:118:2483*

tucꞓāṅicꞓān paṅantuk walatuk aṅarutuk tan māsih apatuk,hémanmun śakti saktèŋ gaway apatuk akas-kas mun n-inuhutan,swaŋ suṅsaŋ satwa kalwaŋ satata taman aṅèl tūt riŋ brata tatiŋ*24:119:2484*
mūṙkꝁāmaṅsö masĕṅhit maṅilabi mahapĕk koŋ pāpa lalawā*24:120:2485*

caṅgigyaṙgyānyan iṅgat Igar-igar atakut dé niŋ brah ahawok,hāḥ taṅhèḥ yan prawīrāpa ta kawĕdi nikān lumpat si suluwug,citrékaŋ cakrawākāṅacak-acak ucapan riŋ cikruk umacak,wiśwāsān wiśwasowus waliwis awalikan sinyaŋnya ri pĕluŋ*24:121:2486*

döh aṇḍaḥ tan papiṇḍaḥ bwat atĕmu ri tĕṅaḥ niŋ wwꜽ hila-hila,nāŋ tan méraŋ kapéṅin si tilil i-luwag ag wāg agya wagugĕn,matrī trik trĕpta méraŋ ri si tilil alayū luṅhā malulunan,cūcuṙ-cūcuṙ curīkaŋ cucur umuni cucud mélik ri si tilil*24:122:2487*

lĕŋlĕŋ luŋluŋ lumaṅlaŋ tumuluy alalayan riŋ saṅkuliṅ arĕn,caṅkak cod caŋ-ciṅan yākĕcĕk acala-calan caṙccāñ cucu-cucud,don taŋ dok dīna yāṅdoḥ mamĕdi-mĕdi Ataḥ mèdī wĕdi-wĕdi,daryas miṅgus kasiṅkuḥ milu winijah ajoŋ kampid tukaṅ akūŋ*24:123:2488*

wruḥ taŋ w~ruk n-awri wok bris kulumur-umuruṅut rūkṣorup-urupan,miṅgat mélik ri kabwat wĕdi Umilu milag log-log wuraṅ-utan,đīrékaŋ binturun yan turun aturu-turū riŋ toraṇa maṇik,saṇḍiŋ laṇḍak surākṣāmawa panah arasuk taŋ tiṅgiliṅ ariŋ*24:124:2489*

nā taŋ satwātisatyādulu-dulur adilat tulyāśapaŧa ya,Aswāsaŋ wyāǥra barwaŋ baraṅ agalak arūm rūpanya wĕkasan,tūsnyāmbĕk saŋ mawaŋ rāt ya ta dumulurakĕn satwāsiṅ atukar,kāhinyékaŋ kaḍatwan drĕḋa hati mapagĕḥ ƀaktinya ri sira*24:125:2490*

sakwèḥ niŋ mūṙkꝁa mārin paṅimur-imur amor iŋ sajjana jĕnĕk,māƀyāsèŋ ƀāṣitāsiŋ guṇa pinahagĕnĕt pinriḥ ginuṇita,tā botoḥ tā pajudyan gaṇita nita mĕné tāŋ syāsa sinawuŋ,tā māśā tāmasāsakta tama sahana niŋ śāstrottama kabèḥ*24:126:2491*

soƀāgyan ƀāgya yāgöŋ I-sira saṅ umadèg tā ƀīṣaṇa mrĕḍu,saṅkā yan śānta tā ƀīṣaṇa ya mataṅ ikè kyātīṅaran arūm,r-andĕl riŋ rājya lĕṅkā kadi taru kanakā riŋ nandanawana,cāyācāyā nirātīs katitisan amrĕtékaŋ rāt suka maṅöb*24:127:2492*

{Udgatawisama}

⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
nda t-atīta saŋ praƀu gumanti tujara ta siraŋ marutsuta,sādara sira mara maŋlawada,para tèŋ taman katĕmu dèwi jānakī*24:128:2493*

praṇatāṙ panĕmbah atiƀakti jaya-jaya namostu maṅgala,dèwi wijaya naranāŧa huwus,pahawās hiḍĕpta tĕka niŋ sukékihĕn*24:129:2494*

ndya kunaŋ Anugraha pininta dĕmakana pawèha ni ṅhulun,ndak pĕjahi sahana niŋ magĕlĕḥ,kala rākṣasī sasinipat ya patyana*24:130:2495*

Ikanaŋ dumīna kita ṅūni marimisi kitat kĕnèṅ unĕŋ,mojar amĕjahana yāmrakatak,yatikā tĕkāna ri gĕlĕṅku séṣṭawan*24:131:2496*

janakātmajātiśaya dibya hati nira tamaṙ kĕnèŋ gĕlĕŋ,kabwatakĕn ikana sampay asiḥ,yaśa māsihāta kaharĕp nirériya*24:132:2497*

pawanātmajālapi gĕlĕŋta t-upaśama samāđi māsiha,yadyapin ahala wuwusnya kabèḥ,mawĕlas Ataḥ haṅĕn-aṅĕnku kāsihan*24:133:2498*

kalawan ndya dona ni patinya Anakĕbi taman paśakti ya,śatru biṣa Anuṅ asāra Ataḥ,ya ta yukti patyan ika dènta hĕntyakĕn*24:134:2499*

nya kunaŋ pakonku laku dadyakĕna para ri saŋ raǥūttama,pājarakĕn aku tĕkā praṇata,kalalaḥ sumuṅsuṅa sirāṙ huwus jaya*24:135:2500*

tamataṙ wihaŋ pawanaputra r-ujar i-sira saŋ raǥūttama,hé nrĕpati sira tĕkā haḍaṅĕn,janakātmajā sira marā manĕmbaha*24:136:2501*

sumahuṙ ta saŋ nrĕpati rāma Ah-u laku waluy waraḥ sira,ndan maradina sira śucya katon,mahaśudđya citta nira saŋ mahājana*24:137:2502*

janakātmajā saduga sāđu mituhu sawuwus naréśwara,niṙmmala malilaṅ awak makila,kinĕnan lulūd awak irāsalin wulu*24:138:2503*

gĕluṅan đinūpa masĕkaṙ ta majĕnu masalin makèn wahu,sāmpun aradin aṅadĕg ta sira,mara té naréśwara manĕmbahèŋ saƀā*24:139:2504*

saḍatèŋ nirāṙ tĕmu naréndra humĕnĕṅ abunĕk manaḥ nira,dīna masuma masamun makucĕm,makĕcap tumuṅkul anurat-nurat lĕmaḥ*24:140:2505*

janakātmajā tĕka manĕmbah akiḍupuh uḍū rapuḥ huyuŋ,sanđi kadi pinupuran maṅĕliḥ,lara niŋ dinīna tĕka tan liniŋ linūd*24:141:2506*

suka don irān para hilaŋ pwa mahĕli lara lèn iraŋ nira,tuṅkuli ta kaluṣa niŋ kadadin,tinukĕl ta kaśmala nikaŋ śarīra bāp*24:142:2507*

Ah-a duḥka tan patĕpi tībra bali kari samaṅkanaŋ lara,tan lara ta karih ikaŋ mapasaḥ,nya ṅ-iraŋ magöŋ ya pamĕkas nikaŋ lara*24:143:2508*

marabas ta luḥ nira gĕlāna kadi ta tinĕkĕk gulū nira,ndīŋ daśa-diśi pamawāna wulat,syapa sĕmbahĕn Anumané ry-awak nira*24:144:2509*

sira saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa kapīndra pawanasuta nīla jāmbawān,Aṅgada sira milu gadgada bāp,mĕgĕgĕḥ sirāṙ wulat i-saŋ raǥūttama*24:145:2510*

bala wānaromilu lumuḥ ya mulat i-janakātmajānaṅis,tan bali sira katĕkāna gĕlĕŋ,sira doniṅ apraṅ iniraŋ-Iraŋ pwa wèḥ*24:146:2511*

masuwé siraŋ nrĕpati dīna mabunĕk ahĕnĕk wulat mabos,kāsihan umulat anon manaṅis,mawaraḥ satorasi sirèŋ kasaṅśaya*24:147:2512*

janakātmajā ta huwusan ta pahalilaṅ aṅĕn-n-aṅĕntari,haywa malara kita haywa makūŋ,Apa tat t-apaṅguha muwaḥ lawan n-aku*24:148:2513*

kasusuk niké haṅĕn-aṅĕnku kita ta malawas hanèŋ musuḥ,ya pwat uwaha ri tuwuḥku hana,niyatādulög ni hati niŋ mulat ry-aku*24:149:2514*

śuci niskalĕṅka raǥuputra taya ta pacalā nirèŋ jagat,yadyapi-t uwaha kunaŋ makurĕn,kahawā kulaṅku lumĕtuḥ lilaŋ nira*24:150:2515*

ya mataŋnya tañcala ni dèwi pakatapa tikaŋ larāpasaḥ,citta sapihi pahawās huwusĕn,tĕwasākuru-ŋ kuraṅa riŋ paṅan turū*24:151:2516*

ta piliḥ saliŋta saparāna sarahayu saménakèŋ manaḥ,yāt uliha ri miŧilā saꝑala,tĕhĕrā kunaŋ hana ri saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa*24:152:2517*

yadiyan si lakṣmaṇa saliŋta si ƀarata kunaŋ paṅöbana,yan wĕgila kunaṅ i-saŋ kapirāt,tamatad gulaŋ-gulaṅa riŋ saménaka*24:153:2518*

paramāṙŧa tékana wuwusku tatan ujariṅ aṅlulū Iké,duṙyyaśa niyata kitāt mapasaḥ,yaśa māsihéry-aku ya sāđya niŋ dadi*24:154:2519*

yatikā wuwus nrĕpati rāma dadi ta sumahuṙ priyā nira,ƀūpati kita raǥuputra putus,tumatas ṅ-asiḥ masiha haywa maṅkana*24:155:2520*

lalu tan takut ta ri ƀaṭāra hana sira paḍomulat kabèḥ,pañcakuśika sira sakṣi sadā,mulat iŋ maṅāmbĕk i-salaḥ lawan kĕna*24:156:2521*

tuhu yak tamolah i-musuḥta kagamĕl aku ṅūni dé nikā,tan kawawa riya pi déwa mulat,sira sākṣi sūkṣma mulat iŋ patibrata*24:157:2522*

prĕŧiwīki téka pinakébu kumisapu sapiṇḍa niŋ jagat,tiṅhali kĕta sa-Ulaḥku salaḥ,kuśalālilaŋ haṅĕn-aṅĕnku liṅku piḥ*24:158:2523*

kita saŋ hyaṅ āpah aparan ta yan ahala Ulaḥku tiṅhali,wyāpaka kita riṅ inak Ininum,pinakāmrĕtèŋ ƀuwana déwa mānuṣa*24:159:2524*

sahananta téja ri jagat ndat iṅĕt-iṅĕtakĕn pwa ta ṅhulun,yak mahala maharĕpèŋ wipaŧa,kita téja Ujwala suluḥ tumon adoḥ*24:160:2525*

hyaṅ aṅin kitékana ta jīwa sumurup i-sarūpa niŋ jagat,sūkṣmagati kita tumon sagati,sagatiṅku tiṅhali yadin hanāhalay*24:161:2526*

kita saŋ naƀastala t-ulad wruhi hala-hayu ni ṅhulun ta ṅꜽ,lyab kita I-ruhur i-sor i-yawā,ri dalĕm śarīra śaraṇāṅkwa mīsiha*24:162:2527*

Ari lakṣmaṇād wulati tāku kasiharĕp asiḥ nirāśraya,wyaṙŧa hanan iki huripku tĕmĕn,pinahidwakĕn mamuharā dulög hati*24:163:2528*

lĕhĕṅa-ŋ pĕjaḥ juga hiḍĕpku kaśula saꝑalāku yak taya,rwā ꝑala katĕmu yadin pĕjaha,priya rāma tuṣṭa Aku marya méraṅa*24:164:2529*

ya mataŋnya tāsyasiha rāri dilahi taṅ apuy tamèt tahĕn,mātya maturun apuyāku huwus,ꝑala niŋ patibrata palaṙ kapaṅguha*24:165:2530*

trijaṭā masö sira ri dèwi wulat i-sira tībra duḥkita,tan Alaṅ-alaṅ atiƀakti sadā,drĕḋa tan tulā r-aṅĕn-aṅĕnya tañ cala*24:166:2531*

trijaṭāri hāḥ wulati tāku Atiśaya ṅ-aƀāgya kaśmala,ḍū hara Apa ta kalīṅan iké,kita kéwala wruh irikéry-ulaḥkwari*24:167:2532*

tawaraḥ saniṣṭura kitāri ri sira ta bapanta paṇḍita,yogya ta sira warahĕn saꝑala,wihikan sirèŋ Aji kuṭāramānawa*24:168:2533*

ya tikā wuwus nira sudèwi dadi ta sumahuṙ ya mānasā,tībra ya malara masū manaṅis,Atiđīra niṙƀaya ya mojar iŋ saƀā*24:169:2534*

{punaṙmmada}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ = :13:
kadurus ƀaṭāra wuta tulya taṙ panon,takarin hiḍĕp wara-waraḥ niṅ āgama,sira dèwi tā paḍa-paḍā nirĕŋ sarat,rikanaŋ susatya drĕḋa ƀakti mapraƀu*24:170:2535*

tamataṙ paṅan marasa taṙ kĕnèŋ turū,satatānaṅis maguliṅan rikaŋ lĕmaḥ,lara duḥka tan patĕpi tībra kāsyasiḥ,kadi kāwiṣan sira sawèt nikāṅ unĕŋ*24:171:2536*

kita nitya kéwala Iniṣṭi niŋ hati,Ikanan pamūja ri ƀaṭāra tan kalèn,ri jayā naréndra kalawan mapaṅguha,ya Ikā prayojana nirāṙ paṅaṙccaṇa*24:172:2537*

ya tikā Ulaḥ nira Atīta riŋ hayu,lalu hāḥ Alib salahasāku dé nira,ri tĕkanta nāŧa kadi taṙ kama ṅkanā,tamatan hanā-ŋ rasa kariḥ Ikèŋ dadi*24:173:2538*

kita liṅku yogya śaraṇā nikaŋ jagat,wruha riŋ salaḥ kĕna ƀaṭāra tan kalèn,wĕgilĕn Ikaŋ Agati pāpa kāsyasiḥ,kita tāmrĕtĕŋ ƀuwana yukti Oṣađā*24:174:2539*

{waṅśasŧa}
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
taŧāpi yan mūṙkꝁa hatinta niṙǥrĕṇa,kalĕṅka tātaḥ hrĕdayanta tan padon,Alāṅ-alaŋ dènta đumāraṇa-ŋ prañā,Apat t-ala d-dé nikanaŋ malānaput*24:175:2540*

lukan gĕlĕḥ tālapakĕn kita praƀu,swaƀāwa niŋ déwata tan hané kita,hilaŋ pwa đaṙmmanta yaśanta riŋ jagat,Apan grĕhītāṅhala tat t-alap ṅ hayu*24:176:2541*

mataŋnya tātaṙ hana śāśwatānulus,śuƀāśuƀātaḥ suꝁa-duḥka taṙ wuruŋ,dumèḥ manaḥ niŋ dadi tan saniścaya,Apan Ikaŋ kaṙmma lĕwiḥ lawan wiđi*24:177:2542*

sawèt ni yāśā ni manaḥku tékihĕn,tumon sira śrī janakātmajālara,hilaŋ takut twaṅku ri saŋ naréśwara,tak olya yak mātya sadénya yaṙ pĕjaḥ*24:178:2543*

mapāpa ta lwiṙ nira saŋ sukānulus,lanā mamukti-ŋ śriya tan kĕnèŋ lara,naréśwarāṅhiŋ sira liṅku Uttama,taŧāpi yaṙ śoka nihan sirāpasaḥ*24:179:2544*

kahīnya tékiŋ dadi mānuṣāđama,huwus katon byakta Umaḥ nikaŋ lara,mataŋnya saŋ paṇḍita sāđu sajjana,tamaṙ kabadđèŋ śriya mūṙ sirātapa*24:180:2545*

tatan wiśéṣa-ŋ wiṣayāta dè nira,nirākulékaŋ hati budđi śudđa ya,wiśéṣa taŋ citta samāđi đāraṇī,Umuṅgu riŋ śūnya suđīra mabrata*24:181:2546*

Apan huwus wruḥ ri wiwéka niŋ dadi,dumèḥ sirāwās ya makāmbĕka-ŋ tapa,wiratyasambéga manaḥ nirālilaŋ,rikaŋ kawikwan drĕḋa tār alaŋ-Alaŋ*24:182:2547*

Ah-o mahādibya niraŋ wĕnaŋ wiku,luput rikaŋ Indriya-rāga tan hana,warĕg nirèŋ janma Anitya hétuka,pĕgat t-akĕn taŋ mala ƀakti kéwala*24:183:2548*

laraṅku dé saŋ janakātmajékihĕn,tatan tahāŋ duḥka magöŋ tĕké sira,Apan sadā satya lanā patibrata,k-uđāni té saŋ wiku saŋ wĕnaŋ tapa*24:184:2549*

mataŋnya wikwāku ƀaṭāra déwata,manaḥku sambéga tumon ikèŋ dadi,saranta saṅsāra saśoka kāsyasiḥ,huripnya tan nitya sukanya tan lanā*24:185:2550*

samaṅkanékaŋ pakurĕn n-aṅĕn-n-aṅĕn,Inaknya tan śaśwata jāti duḥka ya,mataŋnya saŋ hyaŋ tak alākya yāsiha,Agöŋ wirāgyaṅku tumon gatī sira*24:186:2551*

nahan Ujaṙ niŋ trijaṭā rikaŋ saƀā,tumohi satyā nira dèwi jānakī,huwusnya mojaṙ manaṅis ta yāṅĕsaḥ,humīs ta luḥ niŋ Umulat paḍālara*24:187:2552*

muwaḥ ta dèwī mawuwus saniṣṭura,huwus hĕnĕŋ saŋ trijaṭā tĕwas maṅèl,samaṅkanāriṅku si lakṣmaṇād wulat,t-amoŋ Apuy tāsiha ri ṅhulun Ari*24:188:2553*

{prahaṙṣiṇī}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
nojaṙ saŋ janakasutāṙ paminta mātya,saṅké göŋ niṅ iraṅ-iraŋ lawan kasatyan,saŋ rāmāṅanumata taṙ wihaŋ ta winwīt,ṅkān saŋ lakṣmaṇa matĕra-ŋ tahĕn panunwan*24:189:2554*

Āśā saŋ lumaku kinon sawèt nikaŋ twaŋ,timbun taŋ kayu tamalaḥ ta luḥ kamantyan,wèt niŋ bāp sira n-aharĕp tumūta mātya,képwan tan tĕmu naya saŋ kakāmikalpa*24:190:2555*

woŋ tékaŋ Apuy umurub dilaḥnya māwās,māwāmbĕk nira saṅ aminta mātya satya,nis trĕṣṇā taya katakut masö manĕmbaḥ,saŋ sītā makuliliṅan ri saŋ hyaṅ agni*24:191:2556*

ndaḥ saŋ hyaŋ jwalana kitāta sākṣi niŋ rāt,yak duṣṭāhala gĕsĕṅa ṅhulun wiśīṙṇnā,yak satya pwa ya kĕmitĕn ṅhulun tĕkapta,nā sāmbat nira tumĕḍun ri saŋ hyaṅ agni*24:192:2557*

{rajanī}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = :17:
Aŧa ri tĕḍun niraŋ paramasatya ri saŋ hyaṅ apuy,nda tan agĕsĕŋ manaḥ niṅ umulat juga śīṙṇna gĕsĕŋ,salahasa dényaṅĕn-n-aṅĕn iraŋ raǥuputra salaḥ,kadi ginitĕs tikaŋ twas umarèŋ mata luḥ tumibā*24:193:2558*

paḍa ta mulat rikaŋ Apuy apūṙwwa dilaḥnya murub,kaŧamapi moǥa yan paḍĕm ah-o tuhu satya sira,tĕmahan ikaŋ Apuy kanaka paṅkaja tuñjuṅ ĕmās,dadi dala taŋ dilaḥ kukus arūm tĕmahanya sari*24:194:2559*

mĕtu ta ƀaṭāra bahni puruṣākrĕti dibya katon,maṅadĕg i-mađya niŋ kanaka paṅkaja sāƀinaya,janakasutā matimpuh i-samīpa nirātiśaya,ciha-ciha dibya niŋ brata susatya mahāsaꝑala*24:195:2560*

dadi mawaraḥ hyaṅ agni ri naréśwara dāśaraŧi,nrĕpasuta hé raǥūttama-taman katamāna tamaḥ,Apa ta kitāt sasaṅśaya ri saŋ ǥariṇinta śuci,kadi raray aṙdđa mohita hatinta salaḥ panahā*24:196:2561*

kita malawas pwa ṅūni makurĕn tĕka riŋ satahun,wruha ta kité sulit nira salèk pwa katona nikā,kimuta kitān tĕkèŋ rwa tĕlu pātta tahun tat atūt,tat iṅĕt-iṅĕt Ataḥ tĕṅĕ-tĕṅĕn n-i manaḥ rasikā*24:197:2562*

nya ta ya paṅawruhé hayu ni citta nirāṙ wulati,sakala ƀaṭāra śaṅkara nihan sira rin gagana,maraha kité ry-awakta ya ta dona nirān panurun,mara t-atutuṙ tatad waluya saṅśaya śucya lanā*24:198:2563*

tuwi sira rāma saŋ nrĕpa nihan sira wèd wulati,milu manurun siraŋ daśaraŧa praƀu nāŧa sira,maśila sirèŋ wimāna manapĕl ri ƀaṭāra śiwa,makajuru saŋ hyaṅ indra sira mitra nirèŋ sakala*24:199:2564*

{śāṙddūlawikrīḍita}
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = :19:
nāhan liŋ nira saŋ hyaṅ agni tumurun sākṣāt ta saŋ hyaŋ śiwa,lāwan déwaganāpramèya hibĕkan ṅ-ākāśa sök loṙ kidul,muṅgwiŋ ratna wimāna maṅkin aparö ṅkāné ruhuṙ niŋ saƀā,sakwèḥ niŋ Umulat sahaṙṣa muririŋ kāścaṙyya kapwārarĕm*24:200:2565*

saŋ rāménujaran ƀaṭāra winaraḥ ry-āwak nirān déwata,hé nārāyaṇa hé raǥūttama-taman béđékwawaktāt hiḍĕp,saŋ hyaŋ wiṣṇu kĕtā kita priyatamā sītā sira śrī-maya,taṙ saḥ sātmaka śudđa satya pihakanyāwakta yat dampati

haywātaḥ kita saṅśayé sira muwaḥ sāmpun kaśudđyan sira,dontāt aṅdadi dadyakĕn tulusakĕn kīṙttinta riŋ rāt kabèḥ,swasŧā niŋ ƀuwanatrayékana Iwön nāhan ꝑalantāt jaya,cihnānyān kita saŋ janāṙddana dinésaŋ hyaŋ dumīkṣa-ŋ sarāt*24:201:2566*

nā tojaṙ paraméśwaré sira wawaŋ śīǥrān panambaḥ sira,Antaṙ-līna ƀaṭāra sukṣma kawĕkas saŋ rāma tuṣṭa-ŋ manaḥ,saŋ sītā śuci satya śodđa satirun santāna lumrāŋ yaśā,saṅkrānta prakaṭa praśāsta kinudaŋ tan lèn kiduŋ niŋ sarāt*24:202:2567*

{prabođitā}

Aŧa sāmpun awās sirāṙ śuci,sira saŋ śrī janakātmajénapi,parituṣṭa siraŋ raǥūttama,malawas tākaḍasiḥ suniṙmmala*24:203:2568*

kramakāla kulĕm Umèḥ tĕkā,Umuliḥ saŋ milu sākṣi riŋ saƀā,raǥuputra lawan wiƀīṣaṇa,tumamèŋ rājya sirānaḍaḥ kabèḥ*24:204:2569*

milu saŋ kapirāja māruti,nala nīlāṅgada jāmbawān tuwi,paripūṙṇna makaṙmma ƀojana,dadi mojaṙ naranāŧa rāǥawa*24:205:2570*

pawanātmaja yaḥ t-asö ry-aku,krama niŋ māṙgga ya pājaré kita,kita liṅku haraḥ laku t-ruhun,ri Ayođyā ta waraḥ n-alaḥ musuḥ*24:206:2571*

waluyī ta gĕlista maŋlayaŋ,Umusī méǥa makandĕl iŋ laṅit,haliwat pwa kitèŋ mahodađi,tĕmu taŋ rāmya mahéndrapaṙbwata*24:207:2572*

paṅaloṙta muwaḥ tĕmu-ŋ gunuŋ,malayā ꝁyāti manojña komala,giri winđya ya loṙ nikāparö,tuwi kiṣkinđa gunuŋ ya saśri ya*24:208:2573*

kalawan giri mālyawān tĕmun,wulatī daṇḍaka kānanāsukĕt,katutuṙ Aku ṅūni dé nikā,manusup ṅkāna lawan si lakṣmaṇa*24:209:2574*

wiparīta sukĕt nikaŋ Alas,paramĕŋ đīra si lakṣmaṇā lara,kawilĕt karawit Ikaŋ gulū,suku tan lwiṙ suku rāḥ nirantara*24:210:2575*

manusup kami śoka kāsyasiḥ,malapāpus kurapas jugākurū,kadi tag waluyāpuliḥ-t hiḍèp,Irikaŋ daṇḍaka kānanāk hana*24:211:2576*

paṅaloṙ tĕmu ṅ-āśramottama,patapan hyaŋ rĕṣi saŋ sutīkṣṇa ya,hana rāmya tĕmĕn taman śuci,patapan saŋ śaraƀaṅga ƀāgiya*24:212:2577*

rĕṣi Atri pawitra sĕmbahén,sĕpĕri ṅkā patapan nirāparö,tĕmu taŋ giri citrakūṭa lor,suƀagèŋ śoƀa ƀaradwajāśrama*24:213:2578*

yamunā ya wĕnaŋ mawèḥ hayu,ta sibū budđi ya śudđi dé nikā,tĕmu taŋ lwah agöŋ suniṙmmala,ratu niŋ tīṙŧa pawitra jāhnawī*24:214:2579*

silĕm iŋ lwah ah-o mahādƀuta,śuci gamƀīra hilīnya ƀīṣaṇa,kadi nīla lawan śilāñjana,tamasāk yomasĕh iŋ katāmasan*24:215:2580*

sarayū palayū parériya,śitala wwꜽnya suganđa yākuniŋ,kinĕbuṙ niṅ ayođya kanyakā,masibū syūḥ jĕnu kumkumé susu*24:216:2581*

tumamā ta kité dalĕm pura,tĕmu tébuṅku sukān kitān tĕka,pawaraḥ pwa kitān alaḥ musuḥ,ƀaratāwaś ya giraŋ nikāṅrĕṅö*24:217:2582*

siraṅ āṙyya wiƀīṣaṇāṅadĕg,sumiliḥ ƀūpati nāŧa pājara,kapirāja sirāta waṙṇnitan,priya mitraṅku dumèḥ ṅhuluñ jaya*24:218:2583*

ri wurinta kamīki maṅkata,sukacittāku nihan panūtwuri,ri waluy tat-uḍik manuŋsuṅa,Irikākun kapapag kapaṅguha*24:219:2584*

Iti nā ta wuwus naréśwara,sira saŋ māruti taṙ wihaŋ kinon,Umibĕṙ sira śīǥra maŋlayaŋ,kawĕkas ƀūpati saŋ tigāṅinum*24:220:2585*

kapirāja lawan wiƀīṣaṇa,tumĕkāŋ mastawa yaṙ tinakwanan,kita karwa ta liṅku māsiha,ri Ayođyā dulurĕn ṅhulun muliḥ*24:221:2586*

prakrĕtīkana riŋ kamānuṣan,malulut riŋ priyamitra yan kasaḥ,niyatāku makūṅa yat taya,ya mataŋnyāt ilu tūta ri ṅhulun*24:222:2587*

tĕlu pāt lima nĕm pituŋ kulĕm,lawasantéri Ayođya nāgarī,mulihāta kité samaṅkana,Aku maŋlampwa ƀawīṣya yāt uliḥ*24:223:2588*

taya lāƀa pi déśalāƀa don,wruha riŋ rājya ya sāđya niŋ milu,ri pawitra nikaŋ guṇé kita,suyaśā śudđya ṅ-ayođya yat parā*24:224:2589*

ya pawitra ya tīṙŧa yāśrama,saparan saŋ paripūṙṇna riŋ guṇa,saṅ anū mara ṅūni na-ŋ yaśa,suƀagārūm pamĕkasta riŋ pura*24:225:2590*

nya pi lāƀa tĕmén tĕmun riya,priyamitrāŋ ƀarata prayojana,ya kĕtā ꝑala Uttamaŋ praƀu,patĕmunta priyamitra māsiha*24:226:2591*

yat anĕmwa maṇik wiƀūti lèn,kabaran ṅwaŋ kumĕmit tikān hana,priyamitra ya rākṣakāṅĕmit,ya mawèḥ ƀoga maṅöbi maŋlyabi*24:227:2592*

{mālaƀāriṇi}

ya wuwus naranāŧa rāma masyaŋ,Umarā milwa muliḥ marèṅ ayođyā,sumahuṙ sira saŋ rwa kapwa mojar,kapi sugrīwa wiƀīṣaṇātihaṙṣa*24:228:2593*

naranāŧa kitāgĕlĕm maṅājñé,kadi maŋrwa-rwa Ujaṙta sāṙjjawāsiḥ,Aparan kari tan tĕmun mami ṅkā,syapa molin paripūṙṇna taŋ Ayođyā*24:229:2594*

tan ikaŋ ꝑala dona niŋ mara ṅkā,kami trĕṣṇā malulut jugé naréndra,wĕṅi tan pawulan Awās pĕtĕŋ ya,paḍa niŋ kāri makūŋ wiyoga māśā*24:230:2595*

manukāna kari-ŋ wulan satéja,rasa niŋ candana tan panīsi citta,Asĕpĕn wway atīs tatan ya tambā,ri paṅāwéśa nikaŋ Unĕŋ kunĕŋ ya*24:231:2596*

ya winaṙṇnita saŋ purāṇa kāwya,lara niŋ kāri ri saŋ narāṙyya māsiḥ,praƀu saṅgama yāmrĕtātidibya,sumukèŋ wwaŋ kadi saṅhulun hanāṅhöb*24:232:2597*

Upaman kadi kāga cakrawāka,mapasaḥ riŋ wĕṅi đik śaśaṅka liŋnya,rahina pwa ya piḥ bĕtaḥ ya mapwśé,hana niŋ saṅgama tan hiḍĕp panasnya*24:233:2598*

katuluy madawā wuwusku nāŧa,kalarān iŋ mapasaḥ kaŧāprasaṅga,ya mataŋnya kanugrahékanaŋ syaŋ,syapa tan haṙṣa rikā pakonta milwa*24:234:2599*

kadi liŋ naranāŧa ṅūni tuṅgal,Ikanaŋ monĕṅ-unĕŋ laranya tan swaŋ,si masaṅgama yéka dibya ƀoga,tan inum tan pinaṅan mawèḥ sukĕŋ waŋ*24:235:2600*

ri katona nikā sukunta nāŧa,ya tumrĕptī kami nityakāla tūṣa,ri hatiṅku maṇik kita pratiṣṭa,Anuṅ īniṣṭi wiśéṣa déwatāṅkwa*24:236:2601*

Iti nā ta wuwus niraŋ tinakwan,sira kāliḥ kapirāja rākṣaséndra,paḍa milwa muliḥ maréry-ayođyā,Ikanaŋ citta kadīnisĕp tumūta*24:237:2602*

hĕlĕm ésuk ataḥ sirāṙ payātrā,wĕṅi yénantin inantyakĕn mataṅhi,ri sawèt ni suwé nirāsiwo ṅkā,manĕhĕṙ tan paturū mijil hyaṅ aṙkka*24:238:2603*

kramakāla sirārahup masanđyā,majapāṅaṙccaṇa kapwa ƀakti satya,brata saŋ praƀu mrĕdđyakĕn praƀāwa,saparan sélwana ƀakti muꝁya mūlya*24:239:2604*

{swāgata}
– ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = :11:
maṅkas-aṅkas aṅadĕg ta sirādan,dampatī nrĕpati rāǥawa sītā,śrī janāṙdđana katon sira sākṣāt,tulya kāma rati ratna nikaŋ rāt*24:240:2605*

ꝁyāti puṣpaka wimāna manojña,mās maṇik kanaka tan maya māyā,yāta Uṅgwan ira kālih aluṅguḥ,ratnajampana wimāna manojña*24:241:2606*

saŋ wiƀīṣaṇa kapīndra kapuṅkur,maŋ­rakĕt ri sira kèn kadi sānak,lakṣmaṇāṅgĕnĕṅi cāmara saśrī,Aṅgadāṅisapu pāda riṅ ambyan*24:242:2607*

sahya cĕṭṭa kapi mꜽnda makampil,saŋ nalāmayuṅi yatna tan imba,wīra nīla makaluŋ Umawaŋ wwaḥ,jāmbawān mamawa kadga masaṇḍiŋ*24:243:2608*

saŋ suséna sira wédya widagđa,na-ŋ pahidwan aradin ya dinānan,saŋ gayāgaway anaṅga capāru,krandanāsiga mawa-ŋ curigābwat*24:244:2609*

ruṅki mās ginawa saŋ gawayāmsiḥ,saŋ gawākṣa mamawāta payuŋ wyaḥ,puṇyawān tar apanas-panas aṅhöb,riŋ payuŋ wuluṅ aluṅguh agĕgwan*24:245:2610*

śoƀa sāƀinaya saŋ wrĕṣaƀārūm,yaṙ wawāṅirira mās ramaṇīya,saŋ mabāhu mawiḍaŋ dwiwiḍāḍèŋ,ratna ḍaṇḍa ri ḍaḍanya sumaṇḍa*24:246:2611*

sāraƀāra śaraƀāmawa lankap,tībra kābrĕkĕkĕ kabwatan amriḥ,đūmra dum nira duwĕg mamawa hrū,taṅkulak kanaka nā salayanya*24:247:2612*

wīra tāra rasikākurug éraŋ,yaṙ kasènwan ahulap mata kāprĕm,kéśarāṅakusarāṅusirèŋ drĕs,taṙ sukĕṙ kisapu taŋ rasuk abwat*24:248:2613*

ƀīmawaktra mawa ƀakta sirārūm,laṇḍugādi hana kuṇḍi kinuṇḍaŋ,saŋ đanuṙđara diné tar aṅèla,śukti mās winawa sokya taṅ āmbĕk*24:249:2614*

saŋ darīmuꝁa muꝁāṅgupi đārī,hyun niré kalula saŋ trijaṭāṅliŋ,Indrajānu sahajāṅgupi lambuŋ,maŋjawil maṅujiwat sajiwāhyun*24:250:2615*

kāmadrĕṣṭi kumudomilu sinta,miṅsĕr-iṅsĕr aṅusiṙ wulatolĕm,ganđamādana madan-madan aswaŋ,taṙ wulat winaya saŋ winatātwaŋ*24:251:2616*

dibya saŋ śatabalī bali milwa,riŋ Ulaḥ mamiṣa-maṅga-maƀāmī,mūṙ maré saṅ abalun mabalāmrĕm,raṅkĕp iŋ kapi makampil akampya*24:252:2617*

sāmpun iŋ wray umanĕk sahananya,kapwa yātitih adan matatātap,puṣpakān pakahawan gaganādrĕs,tulya ƀūmi kadi paṙbwata maṅkat*24:253:2618*

tan masoṙ tan aruhuṙ ta Ibĕṙnya,byakta dé nira tumon ikanaŋ rāt,saŋ naréśwara sahaṙṣa tumuṅkul,waṙṇnana krama nikaŋ sakapaṅguḥ*24:254:2619*

mꜽŧilī taṅa-taṅā tasik alwā,lwiṙ nikā kadi laṅit malilaŋ ya,sétubanđa Umalaŋ ri tĕṅaḥnya,yan katon kadi ta méǥa kumĕṇḍĕŋ*24:255:2620*

nāŋ mahéndra mahalĕp wahu rāmya,duṙbbalāhala ya ṅūni ta kāmbaḥ,rūg rĕbaḥ kayu-kayunya watunya,yénatĕṙ ya ta sinūk nikanaŋ wré*24:256:2621*

hāḥ hyaṅ indra lalu dibya nirāsiḥ,göŋ nikā hudan irāri tĕkā ṅké,tan hudāni ta hudan n-ira liṅku,wiśwakaṙmma juga yan pamuliḥ rāt*24:257:2622*

nyaŋ lĕmaḥ mari lĕbak ta ya késyan,nā-ŋ galintuṅ aruhuṙ maratā ya,wrĕkṣa rūg mawuṅu kapwa makĕmbaŋ,hāḥ ṅ hudan praƀu jugān pahayu-ŋ rāt*24:258:2623*

ndaḥ hyaṅ indra kami kālih anĕmbaḥ,hyun mamī hayu nikā suyaśanta,yak parā kunaṅ araḥ riṅ ayođyā,swāgatā kami manuŋsuṅa ƀaktya*24:259:2624*

malaya maluyakén kūŋ kokilanyān paśabda,kuya ta ya kayu koliŋ candanākwèḥ riyārūm,satata mawaṅi māmbö mimbuhī kūŋnya tékā,mrisakiti ṅ-apadohan mrāknya maṅhrūk manawwaŋ*24:260:2625*

#pañcawiṅśati saṙggaḥ#
<mattamayūra>:25
– – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏓ = :13:
^25/1/2598.
nā taŋ winđyā tiṅhali śröṅanya manojña,yékā mahyun rakwa rumūgāŋ pada kéndran,puñcaknyāwānnyā tumuwuḥ nitya matāmbĕḥ,maṅkin māwān duṙbbala taŋ swaṙgga kasuṇḍul*25:1:2626*

saŋ hyaŋ śakra glāna tumon swaṙgga kasuṇḍul,sĕmbaḥ saŋ hyaŋ śaṅkara kārūṇya sirèŋ rāt,mopāyākon saŋ hyaṅ agastī jawa r-uṅgu,rwaŋ don sāđya swaṙgga sukā taŋ jawa śudđya*25:2:2627*

saṅké kꜽlāśa hyaṅ agastin paṅidul ta,pintan tékaŋ winđya hawan haywa kitāwān,wèt ni twaŋ niŋ winđya ri saŋ sidđa Agastya,maṇḍĕḥ mĕṇḍĕk māri manuṇḍul suka taŋ rāt*25:3:2628*

{turagagati}

{suwadanā}

{drutawilambita}

{prahaṙṣiṇī}

{bramitākṣara}
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = :12:
śaraƀaṅga ƀoga patapan rasikā,patiganya kapwa tinanĕm-tanĕman,sulasiḥ sakaṇḍa hana kaṇḍuyuhan,dalimānya paṇḍakaki mĕṇḍur arūm*25:8:2633*

kasihan si haywa masĕkaṙ kañiri,pacaraṅga-raṅga nikanaŋ racana,Anujājajaṙ saruni ranti talĕs,tĕbu bāp pisaŋ saṅu saṅ ugratapa*25:9:2634*

giri citrakūṭa kuṭajanya matap,kala yaṙ kuyaŋ kayu kuñit kawalot,kayu cāmaromara maṅöb camara,paḍa jaṅgutan wuraṅ-utanya manèk*25:10:2635*

walatuk ri tuŋtuṅ anabĕḥ murawa,mrĕdu māṙddawān paṅurugĕm Aḍawa,puputĕṙ makūli kumĕtĕṙ satata,puji jīwa-jīwa ya marujyawajik*25:11:2636*

rĕṣi saŋ ƀaradwaja nahan đwaja sor,tĕṅĕran ni Āśrama nirāta tĕhĕr,sumanohara wwara padéwaharan,kuya tākukus mawaṅi ganđa miñak*25:12:2637*

jawa jahli loṙ kidul ikaŋ pamacan,pikatan tatan mawĕdi dibya mariŋ,I ruhuṙ niraŋ rĕṣi darān paturū,masisik sĕsĕk ri sisi niŋ patiga*25:13:2638*

sahajāŋ hiji n-pasĕsĕh iŋ dalima,salimā ri soṙnya hana sĕṇḍi pasaŋ,ya pasaṅgrahé tamuy amukti sadā,wadarārurū I-ruhur iŋ mapasaŋ*25:14:2639*

Apa saṅśayé sira mahāṙṣi kariḥ,matasak ta śakti ni samāđi nira,nirapékṣa sakṣana mĕtu-ŋ kaharĕp,marĕgi-ŋ maré sira mariŋ magiraŋ*25:15:2640*

tuhu sidđawākya wiku tan papaḍa,paḍa paṇḍitāsiṅ aparö ri sira,tuwi satwa satya mamicāra kĕcĕk,syuṅ asaṅǥanīŋ paṅajaran-n-ajaran*25:16:2641*

kimuta-ŋ mahātma tapa-tāpa cuṭul,śuci cĕṭṭa-cĕṭṭa Ucapan riṅ aji,Aji niŋ hĕniŋ hana hĕnĕŋ ginĕgö,Apawaṙgga māṙgga mapagĕḥ ginĕnĕŋ*25:17:2642*

tuhu taṙkka taŋ Atat atatwa humuŋ,macĕṅil cumodya si jalak magalak,paḍa niścayèṅ aji winiścaya ya,kumupak ka-pakṣi nika pakṣa nika*25:18:2643*

puḍaṅan maḍaṅhan inusī yan alaḥ,si maniṅtiṅoni ya manaṅtaṅ atoḥ,macĕṅil wawil wujil aṅas si ṅaṅā,si walik kĕkĕl kawĕlikan lik-ĕlik*25:19:2644*

wataṅan atiśayāhĕnī mās maṇiknéka waṙṇnānataṙ tāratamyātirāmya-ŋ mahāmandapāpūṙwwa śoƀāhatĕp mās pirak ratna mutya pralĕmbanya lambénya yābāŋ sinindūra duḥ niŋ duray ṅkān uray cāmarāṅkĕn kumisnyāhirĕŋ rĕṅganānā wanèḥ tūt ata ṅkān tatiŋ taṅluh ātap lawan kya-kya lèn waḥ nikaŋnyū gaḍiŋ Ādya Uttuṅga ƀinnāniṅis wismayāpan mahārāja muṅgwiŋ mahāratna siṅhāsanātyujwala,

⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:44: = :138:
narapati sira dampatī prāpta sāmpun maluṅguḥ tumūt saŋ tamuy makrama ꝁyāti lĕṅkāđipa mwaŋ siraŋ wānaréndrāśilèŋ ratnasiṅhāsanānūt i-saŋ kékayīputra somitra śatruǥna sāmpun makĕmbaŋ mamuṇḍut pasuṇḍuk nikā saŋ matutwan matūtan halĕp dé niṅ aṅdāni hantrantri gaṇḍaŋ mahāmāṅsa sèsī nikaŋ sāgara lwaḥ Alas lwā niṅ āmbĕk rahasyad wuwus tat wĕnaŋ maṙṇnitékaŋ Umuṅgwiŋ limas mās masowé magantiŋ mawèwèḥ lanā,
{daṇḍaka}
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | [ – ⏑ – ] ×:42: = :132:
kapibala riṅ alun-n-alun loṙ dinānan niraŋ jāmbawān agra paŋktī tatātūt susénādi tan sénujaṙ śrī mahārāja kapwānaḍaḥ yaṙ taḍaḥ taŋ Umuṅgwiŋ gĕḍaḥ drāk sasīđu-ŋ sumāṙ māsawâtyanta jaṙṇniḥ hapènī mahāpāna muṅgwiŋ pané mās Inaṅsū nikā saŋ matoṙ sök tĕké soṙ ṅ-atoṙ Īṅitū pūṙṇna gémpor ikaŋ wré sawèt niŋ wĕrö waṙṇna sindūra tékā ḍaḍanyāḍaḍut yātĕnĕŋ ḍaḥ kahīsan Asiŋ séninumnyāturaḥ,

{mahā daṇḍaka}
 [ ⏑ ⏑ – ] ×:476: = :1428:
naranāŧa raǥūttama ƀoga ƀinukti lawan ǥariṇī nira pūṙṇna pĕnuḥ pinaṅan pinagantyakĕn iŋ mananĕk dinadak-dadak énak-inak ya ta-tambul ikaŋ sumĕḍaḥ sakarĕŋ sinaranta paranti nirantara taŋ malariḥ maṅaliḥ masiliḥ-silihan sumĕlaŋ sumiliḥ mamaṅan maṅinum sakarĕŋ saka rĕmba nikā sakarĕŋ Umaluy pwa matoṙ maduluṙ mawuwuḥ-wuwuhowah-uwaḥ ta paṅan nira dé niṅ anékarasādƀuta ṣadrasa dibya suganđamahā mahaṅĕt mĕrĕṅĕt sira dénya mĕtu-ŋ hariṅĕt kĕna mađya madĕg madarāga masö saṅ awèḥ jĕnu kumkuma candana tīsnya marūm panirām nira rāmya rikaŋ ḍaḍa bāhu gulū tĕka riŋ twas atīs rumĕsĕp śuci cāmara somya mirīŋ ramaṇīya ṅ-ĕmās sumuké sira yaṙ pasĕkaṙ suka baṙ pulaṅ utpala cāmpaka bolu gaḍuŋ puḍak utkaṭa sāri Arūm tumurun ta sirèŋ natar ériṅ-iriŋ kalawan ta siraŋ Ari ƀāra guṇottama saŋ ƀaratāṙ para té sira saŋ tinamuy r-adĕg iŋ bala wānara yaṙ panaḍaḥ maṅinum wwara baṇḍa si ƀaṇḍira nāma parö ri siraŋ ƀaratomilu manwagaté gati saŋ tamuy uttama dénya diné wruha yāta tumakwani saŋ tinamuy mapa kālah-alaḥ Apa tāmbĕha tambulasiŋ kakuraŋ kurawuŋ kurapas kurahan-hana maṇḍaga riŋ raga sugwan ĕmās wwara piṇḍaṅ apiṇḍa lawan bakasĕm pakasaṅśaya haywa tamuy-tamuyan yan asömasi wantĕna saṅgiṅ irāhira hèrakĕnā sakarĕŋ mwaṅ arīṅa-riṅan Iriṅĕn tĕka dé niṅ atoṙ sahajān hibĕkī Inuman tan umāna tĕkèŋ mawĕrö wwara hantiga lumwaṅalap gĕtĕm apya mapāta rasanya rasénisi sīsyanikā Inamĕṙ nira saŋ walakas lĕkasan magaway rasa ƀaṅgi wiƀāga nikaŋ guṇaƀoga tamaṙ tama tā dadi ƀaṅga r-usiṙ suƀago matakut kuyaśā-kuyaśa-ŋ makarī sakarĕŋ makarā-kirakĕn ta ya siŋ matasak matasé kahiris ta haraḥ kuya taṅli pawèhakĕn osĕn-usĕn nda hanus hunus īku pinaṅgaṅakĕn taṅ ikān putihan ri ḍatĕŋ walikāpĕs-apĕs mwas ikā hati niŋ hyu lawan pya nikaŋ hawulāmrak inaṅsi ṅ-usīra pasāra ya satwa śaśā wana kuṙkuṭa Ugra rasottama tad warahĕn Irikaŋ hitamāṅsa hanèŋ Aji sūpakaśāstra milu-ŋ lulu kambiṅ anuŋ maharĕŋ wayawak ruti wūru-wurū prit awoṙ puyuh uttama laṇḍak iṅantya tĕmĕn rasa tuṅgal i-tiṅgiliṅ iṅgalakĕn pwa Asiŋ matasak kalalaḥ tikanaŋ kalalaḥ katĕké sira wānara wīra warĕg I-rasā kalalaḥ nira kāla nikā harĕp anta yadin tĕka riŋ paṅĕlān paṅalap ta piriŋ satapī katupaŋ kurupuk-k-ararus ḍaḍaṅan hawan iŋ warawan wulatī tatiṅan ta kaṅ anta manaṅgap atuṅgayapan paramèŋ rasa pojaraniŋ sajagat rasa kalwaṅ akĕndĕl arūm awuduk mapĕḍak malikĕt-likĕt alwat ikā gilutĕn ṅ hulu kantaka rīnuhuma-ŋ talukan tuliriŋ kupaṅan pwa ṅ-irāh-irah éraṅa saŋ mananĕk yadiyan wirasā ya rasāna wanèḥnya baniŋnya lawaṙ-lawaranya gulay-gulayanya lĕmĕŋ-lĕmĕṅanya pĕṅĕt-pĕṅĕtanya hasĕm-hasĕmanya takiḥ-takihanya sarad-saradanya kulub-kulubanya bĕnĕm-bĕnĕmanya taman sipi riŋ mahĕmuk hulam īŋ rĕcahan ta pĕcĕl-pĕcĕlan śuci taṙ pacalan cĕcĕp iŋ jruk asin nasi tāsi saménaka yan paṅinum wway ahaywa ta sanđi hana-ŋ mađu śīra jalaṇḍaka santĕn arūm tala mastaka laṇḍuga naṅka salak ya salaḥ winilaŋ ǥrĕta pūra kipiŋ tila moda tulađya paṅan paṅasī wwara puñcakatak sisilan panisil ta kukap nda kukup sagĕlista tamaṙ kĕbĕs āt Aṅinum wway atīs nda nihan ta maṅan Uwi naṅka pisaŋ waraṅan ꝑala dibya salak Inumī surasĕkṣurasārun-arun taruṇī taṅinum susu paŧya putĕṙ tan isĕp ta jukut manis énak awās luput īŋ lĕpĕt énak ikénatakan kinapuṙ-kapuran Aparan kawĕkasnya wĕkas niṅ arūm awuduk sakalé kalisālwat ikā palikĕt lakĕtan kinuñit nda kĕta t-wulati-ŋ manĕtĕk-nĕtĕk iŋ paṅĕlan Umalap ta mahā maharĕp tiru ƀāwa nikaŋ manabĕḥ murawān paṅuliŋ sĕsĕban kadi ƀāwa nikaŋ wwaṅ aboṇḍi widagđa miṅis kumayaŋ-kayaṅ aṅkĕn ulaḥnya maṅindĕlakĕn lĕṅa riŋ kawali n-taru ƀinna kisiknya ya gumyatakĕn nika maṅgurapay matama pwa ya pat mawĕrö wiratīŋ kupatay tamataṙ kagaway pabubuṙ susu śudđa putus riṅ atīs hati niŋ kĕna madya madanda ta gucꞓaka kĕmbaṅ arumpukan āpa kariḥ pakĕnā niṅ inak ya Iké ꝑala lālana saŋ wijayèŋ raṇa maṅguhakĕn śri ya ƀoga magöŋ Ikaṅ uttama ƀakti sadā ri ƀaṭāra mahéśwara hétu nikaŋ ƀuwanān kasukāna muwaḥ-muwahāta krĕta,
{basantatilaka}
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = :14:
nā liŋ nikaŋ suƀaga ƀaṇḍa si ƀaṇḍirāṅliŋ,sumwāgaté sagati saŋ tinamuy tinakwan,lāwan siraŋ ƀarata mojar-ujaṙ ya mojar,Āpan ya hapti ri siraŋ praƀu ƀrĕtya kāsiḥ*26:25:2765*

sāmpun samāpta paripūṙṇna pinūja-pūjā,saŋ wānaréśwara wiƀīṣaṇa kapwa tuṣṭa,sanđyākulĕm wulan awās ya katoñ catuṙŧī,saśrī manojña gumawaŋ gumawé ṅ-unĕŋ hyun*26:26:2766*

maṅkā naréndra tumamā ri dalĕm kaḍatwan,mwaŋ saŋ tamuy praƀu wiƀīṣaṇa wānaréndra,riŋ ratnamaṇḍapa palaṅka malit tilāmnya,ṅkā r-uṅgu saŋ tamuy aturwa kinon wisāta*26:27:2767*

saŋ rāma rāmya maduluṙ tumamèṅ umaḥ mās,sampat samodaya lawan dayitā su-sītā,r-uṅgaḥ ta riŋ grĕha tilām umaḍaŋ suganđa,pañjut ḍuḍuk jamaṇikojwala bidđanāga*26:28:2768*

saṅkā rikaŋ lawas amukti wiyoga ṅūni,saŋ kāmadéwa sumawuŋ sira yaṙ tĕka ṅkā,saŋ kāsih-āsih alulut sira toṣađāna,saṅkāna niŋ swakula wrĕdđya Anak ya donya*26:29:2769*

muṅgwiŋ tilām kadi ta mabrata lagna-lagnī,saṅkèṅ aliṅsaṅĕn asāk wĕḍihan lawan kèn,đyāyī manaḥ r-aṅĕn-aṅĕn rasa tatwa sūkṣma,pūjāpratiṣṭa gawayan nira guhyaliṅga*26:30:2770*

trus dé nirāṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn tumuju-ŋ rahasya,limpad pĕpĕk pakĕna saŋ hyaṅ awās kapaṅguḥ,suṇḍul sabīṅaniṅ alit kahiḍĕp rasanya,r-aƀyāsa yaṙ lagi-laginya makin mawās ya*26:31:2771*

ṅwaŋ yan huwus priyawiyoga muwaḥ mapaṅguḥ,tātan paḍékana lawan ṅwaṅ awahwa-wahwan,hyun kūŋ lulut tutur uśāna nahan duluṙnya,yékā mawèḥ rasa wiśéṣa ri saŋ mapaṅguḥ*26:32:2772*

Ambö nikaŋ jĕnu sumāṙ ya mamrĕdđyakĕn hyun,sĕṅsöṅ ikāṅinum-inum magawé kadaṙppān,ras-ras nikaŋ Unĕṅ agöŋ ya makon ataṅhya,dé niŋ lulut kadi pulut rumakĕt jugālwat*26:33:2773*
